nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam vyāsam vasiṣṭha naptāram śakteḥ pautram akalmaṣam parāśara ātmajam vande śuka tātam tapas nidhim vyāsāya viṣṇu rūpāya vyāsa rūpāya viṣṇave katham yuyudhire vīrāḥ kuru pāṇḍava somakāḥ pārthivāḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ nānā deśa samāgatāḥ pratyayudhyanta samare bhīṣmeṇa amitra karṣiṇā katham vā kauravāḥ sarve bhīmasene camūpatau niveśam cakrire yoddhum tat me śaṃsa mahāmate uvāca yathā yuyudhire vīrāḥ kuru pāṇḍava somakāḥ kurukṣetre tapaḥkṣetre śṛṇu tat pṛthivīpate avatīrya kurukṣetram pāṇḍavāḥ saha somakāḥ kauravān abhyavartanta jigīṣantaḥ mahā balāḥ āśaṃsantaḥ jayam yuddhe vadham vā abhimukhāḥ raṇe pūrva bhāge tu kṣetrasya sthitāḥ pratyak mukhāḥ yudhi abhiyāya ca durdharṣām dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāhinīm prāc mukhāḥ paścime bhāge nyaviśanta sa sainikāḥ samantapañcakāt bāhyam śibirāṇi sahasraśas kārayām āsa vidhivat kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śūnyā iva pṛthivī sarvā bāla vṛddha avaśeṣitā niraśva puruṣā ca āsīt ratha kuñjara varjitā yāvat tapati sūryaḥ hi jambūdvīpasya maṇḍalam tāvat eva samāvṛttam balam pārthiva sattama ekasthāḥ sarva varṇāḥ te maṇḍalam bahu yojanam paryākrāmanta deśān ca nadīḥ śailān vanāni ca teṣām yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā sarveṣām puruṣa ṛṣabha ādideśa sa vāhānām bhakṣya bhojyam anuttamam saṃjñāḥ ca vividhāḥ tāḥ tāḥ teṣām cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥ evaṃvādī veditavyaḥ pāṇḍaveyaḥ ayam iti uta abhijñānāni sarveṣām saṃjñāḥ ca ābharaṇāni ca dṛṣṭvā dhvaja agram pārthānām dhārtarāṣṭraḥ mahā manāḥ saha sarvaiḥ mahīpālaiḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavān pāṇḍureṇa ātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani dṛṣṭvā duryodhanam hṛṣṭāḥ sarve pāṇḍava sainikāḥ prahṛṣṭa vadanam tatas praviviśuḥ dadhmuḥ sarve mahā śaṅkhān bherīḥ jaghnuḥ sahasraśas tatas prahṛṣṭām svām senām abhivīkṣya atha pāṇḍavāḥ babhūvuḥ hṛṣṭa manasaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca vīryavān śrutvā sa vāhanāḥ yodhāḥ śakṛt mūtram prasusruvuḥ yathā siṃhasya nadataḥ svanam śrutvā itare mṛgāḥ traseyuḥ tadvat eva āsīt dhārtarāṣṭra balam tadā udatiṣṭhat rajaḥ bhaumam na prājñāyata kim cana antardhīyata ca ādityaḥ sainyena rajasā āvṛtaḥ vavarṣa ca atra parjanyaḥ māṃsa śoṇita vṛṣṭimān vāyuḥ tatas prādurabhūt nīcais śarkara karṣaṇaḥ vinighnan tāni anīkāni vidhaman ca eva tat rajaḥ śūnyā āsīt pṛthivī sarvā bāla vṛddha avaśeṣitā tatas te samayam cakruḥ kuru pāṇḍava somakāḥ dharmān ca sthāpayām āsuḥ yuddhānām bharata ṛṣabha yathāpuram yathāyogam na ca syāt chalanam punar niṣkrāntaḥ pṛtanā madhyāt na hantavyaḥ katham cana aśvena aśvī padātiḥ ca padātena eva bhārata yathāyogam yathāvīryam yathotsāham yathāvayas kṣīṇa śastraḥ vivarmā ca na hantavyaḥ katham cana na sūteṣu na dhuryeṣu na ca śastra upanāyiṣu na bherī śaṅkha vādeṣu prahartavyam katham cana evam te samayam kṛtvā kuru pāṇḍava somakāḥ vismayam paramam jagmuḥ prekṣamāṇāḥ parasparam niviśya ca mahātmānaḥ tatas te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ sumanasaḥ babhūvuḥ saha sainikāḥ uvāca tatas pūrva apare saṃdhye samīkṣya bhagavān ṛṣiḥ sarva veda vidām śreṣṭhaḥ vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ bhaviṣyati raṇe ghore bharatānām pitāmahaḥ vaicitravīryam rājānam sa rahasyam bravīt idam śocantam ārtam dhyāyantam putrāṇām anayam tadā uvāca rājan parīta kālāḥ te putrāḥ ca anye ca bhūmipāḥ teṣu kāla parīteṣu vinaśyatsu ca bhārata kāla paryāyam ājñāya mā sma śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ yadi tu icchasi saṃgrāme draṣṭum enam viśām pate uvāca na rocaye jñāti vadham draṣṭum brahmarṣi sattama yuddham etat tu aśeṣeṇa śṛṇuyām te tejasā uvāca tasmin an icchati draṣṭum saṃgrāmam śrotum icchati varāṇām īśvaraḥ dātā saṃjayāya varam dadau uvāca cakṣuṣā saṃjayaḥ rājan divyena eṣa samanvitaḥ prakāśam vā rahasyam vā rātrau vā yadi vā divā na enam śastrāṇi bhetsyanti na enam bādhiṣyate śramaḥ gāvalgaṇiḥ ayam jīvan yuddhāt asmāt vimokṣyate aham ca kīrtim eteṣām kurūṇām bharata ṛṣabha pāṇḍavānām ca sarveṣām prathayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ uvāca evam uktvā sa bhagavān kurūṇām prapitāmahaḥ punar eva mahā bāhum dhṛtarāṣṭram uvāca ha iha yuddhe mahā rāja bhaviṣyati mahān kṣayaḥ śyenāḥ gṛdhrāḥ ca kākāḥ ca kaṅkāḥ ca sahitāḥ balaiḥ saṃpatanti vanānteṣu samavāyān ca kurvate kravyādāḥ bhakṣayiṣyanti māṃsāni gaja vājinām khaṭākhaṭa iti vāśantaḥ bhairavam bhaya vedinaḥ kahvāḥ prayānti madhyena dakṣiṇām abhitas diśam ubhe pūrva apare saṃdhye nityam paśyāmi bhārata sarvāṇi śveta lohita paryantāḥ kṛṣṇa grīvāḥ sa vidyutaḥ tri varṇāḥ parighāḥ saṃdhau bhānum āvārayanti uta ahorātram mayā dṛṣṭam tat kṣayāya bhaviṣyati alakṣyaḥ prabhayā hīnaḥ paurṇamāsīm ca kārttikīm svapsyanti nihatāḥ vīrāḥ bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥ rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca śūrāḥ parigha bāhavaḥ antarikṣe varāhasya vṛṣadaṃśasya ca ubhayoḥ praṇādam yudhyataḥ rātrau raudram nityam pralakṣaye an āhatāḥ dundubhayaḥ praṇadanti viśām pate a yuktāḥ ca pravartante kṣatriyāṇām mahā rathāḥ kokilāḥ śatapattrāḥ ca cāṣāḥ bhāsāḥ śukāḥ tathā sārasāḥ ca mayūrāḥ ca vācaḥ muñcanti dāruṇāḥ gṛhīta śastra ābharaṇāḥ varmiṇaḥ vāji pṛṣṭha gāḥ aruṇa udayeṣu dṛśyante śataśas śalabha vrajāḥ ubhe saṃdhye prakāśete diśām dāha samanvite āsīt rudhira varṣam ca asthi varṣam ca bhārata yā ca eṣā viśrutā rājan trailokye sādhu saṃmatā arundhatī tayā api eṣa vasiṣṭhaḥ pṛṣṭhatas kṛtaḥ rohiṇīm pīḍayan eṣa sthitaḥ rājan śanaiścaraḥ anabhre ca mahā ghoram stanitam śrūyate aniśam vāhanānām ca rudatām prapatanti aśru bindavaḥ uvāca kharāḥ goṣu prajāyante ramante mātṛbhiḥ sutāḥ anārtavam puṣpa phalam darśayanti vane drumāḥ garbhiṇyaḥ rāja putryaḥ ca janayanti vibhīṣaṇān kravyādān pakṣiṇaḥ ca eva gomāyūn aparān mṛgān tri viṣāṇāḥ catur netrāḥ pañca pādāḥ dvi mehanāḥ dvi śīrṣāḥ ca dvi pucchāḥ ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ paśavaḥ aśivāḥ jāyante vivṛta āsyāḥ ca vyāharantaḥ aśivāḥ giraḥ tri padāḥ śikhinaḥ tārkṣyāḥ catur daṃṣṭrāḥ viṣāṇinaḥ tathā eva anyāḥ ca dṛśyante striyaḥ ca brahma vādinām vainateyān mayūrān ca janayatyaḥ pure tava go vatsam vaḍavā sūte śvā sṛgālam mahīpate krakarān śārikāḥ ca eva śukān ca aśubha vādinaḥ striyaḥ kāḥ cit prajāyante catasraḥ pañca kanyakāḥ tāḥ jāta mātrāḥ nṛtyanti gāyanti ca hasanti ca pṛthagjanasya kuḍakāḥ stanapāḥ stena veśmani pratimāḥ ca ālikhanti anye sa śastrāḥ kāla coditāḥ anyonyam abhidhāvanti śiśavaḥ daṇḍa pāṇayaḥ padma utpalāni vṛkṣeṣu jāyante kumudāni ca viṣvak vātāḥ ca vānti ugrāḥ rajaḥ na vyupaśāmyati abhīkṣṇam kampate bhūmiḥ arkam rāhuḥ tathā agrasat abhāvam hi viśeṣeṇa kurūṇām pratipaśyati dhūmaketuḥ mahā ghoraḥ puṣyam ākramya tiṣṭhati senayoḥ aśivam ghoram kariṣyati mahā grahaḥ maghāsu aṅgārakaḥ vakraḥ śravaṇe ca bṛhaspatiḥ bhāgyam nakṣatram ākramya sūryaputreṇa pīḍyate śukraḥ proṣṭhapade pūrve samāruhya viśām pate śyāmaḥ grahaḥ prajvalitaḥ sa dhūmaḥ saha pāvakaḥ aindram tejasvi nakṣatram jyeṣṭhām ākramya tiṣṭhati rohiṇīm pīḍayati evam ubhau ca śaśi bhāskarau citrā svāti antare ca eva dhiṣṭhitaḥ paruṣaḥ grahaḥ vakra anuvakram kṛtvā ca śravaṇe pāvaka prabhaḥ brahmarāśim samāvṛtya lohitāṅgaḥ vyavasthitaḥ pañca śīrṣāḥ yavāḥ ca eva śata śīrṣāḥ ca śālayaḥ tāḥ gāvaḥ prasnutāḥ vatsaiḥ śoṇitam prakṣaranti uta niśceruḥ apidhānebhyaḥ khaḍgāḥ prajvalitāḥ bhṛśam vyaktam paśyanti śastrāṇi saṃgrāmam samupasthitam agni varṇāḥ yathā bhāsaḥ śastrāṇām udakasya ca kavacānām dhvajānām ca bhaviṣyati mahān kṣayaḥ pṛthivī śoṇita āvartā dhvaja uḍupa samākulā kurūṇām vaiśase rājan pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhārata dikṣu prajvalita āsyāḥ ca vyāharanti mṛga dvijāḥ eka pakṣa akṣi caraṇaḥ śakuniḥ kha caraḥ niśi raudram vadati saṃrabdhaḥ śoṇitam chardayan muhur saptarṣīṇām udārāṇām samavacchādya vai prabhām viśākhayoḥ samīpa sthau bṛhaspati śanaiścarau vapūṃṣi apaharan bhāsā dhūmaketuḥ iva sthitaḥ triṣu pūrveṣu sarveṣu nakṣatreṣu viśām pate caturdaśīm pañcadaśīm bhūta pūrvām ca ṣoḍaśīm imām tu na abhijānāmi amāvāsyām trayodaśīm aparvaṇi grahau etau prajāḥ saṃkṣapayiṣyataḥ rajaḥ vṛtāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ pāṃsu varṣaiḥ samantataḥ utpāta meghāḥ raudrāḥ ca rātrau varṣanti śoṇitam māṃsa varṣam punar tīvram āsīt kṛṣṇa caturdaśīm ardharātre mahā ghoram atṛpyan tatra rākṣasāḥ pratisrotas avahat nadyaḥ saritaḥ śoṇita udakāḥ phenāyamānāḥ kūpāḥ ca nardanti vṛṣabhāḥ iva patanti ulkāḥ sa nirghātāḥ śuṣka aśani vimiśritāḥ adya ca eva niśām vyuṣṭām udaye bhānuḥ āhataḥ bhūmipāla sahasrāṇām bhūmiḥ pāsyati śoṇitam kailāsa mandarābhyām tu tathā himavataḥ gireḥ sahasraśas mahā śabdam śikharāṇi patanti ca mahā bhūtāḥ bhūmikampe caturaḥ sāgarān pṛthak vṛkṣān unmathya vānti ugrāḥ vātāḥ śarkara karṣiṇaḥ ābhagnāḥ su mahā vātaiḥ aśanībhiḥ samāhatāḥ patanti caitya vṛkṣāḥ ca grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca vāma arcīḥ śāva gandhī ca dhūma prāyaḥ khara svanaḥ sparśāḥ gandhāḥ rasāḥ ca eva viparītāḥ mahīpate dhūmāyante dhvajāḥ rājñām kampamānāḥ muhur muhur muñcanti aṅgāra varṣāṇi bheryaḥ atha paṭahāḥ tathā prāsāda śikhara agreṣu pura dvāreṣu ca eva hi gṛdhrāḥ paripatanti ugrāḥ vāmam maṇḍalam āśritāḥ pakva apakva iti su bhṛśam vāvāśyante vayāṃsi ca nilīyante dhvaja agreṣu kṣayāya pṛthivīkṣitām dhyāyantaḥ prakirantaḥ ca vālān vepathu saṃyutāḥ rudanti dīnāḥ turagāḥ mātaṃgāḥ ca sahasraśas valmīkāḥ madhukāni ca hasti aśva ratha śālāḥ tu kapotāḥ ca āśritāḥ tathā ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ utpātāḥ ghora darśanāḥ pṛthivīpāla lokānām sarve vai nāśa kārakāḥ evaṃvidham durnimittam kṣayāya pṛthivīkṣitām bhaumam divyam ca antarikṣam trividham jāyate aniśam uvāca diṣṭam etat purā manye bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ prāpsyanti puruṣa vyāghrāḥ prāṇān tyaktvā mahā āhave uvāca putreṇa dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dhyānam anvagamat param punar eva abravīt vākyam kāla vādī mahā tapāḥ asaṃśayam pārthiva indra kālaḥ saṃkṣipate jagant jñātīnām ca kurūṇām ca saṃbandhi suhṛdām tathā kṣudram jñāti vadham prāhuḥ mā kuruṣva mama apriyam kālaḥ ayam putra rūpeṇa tava jātaḥ viśām pate kulasya asya vināśāya tathā eva ca mahīkṣitām anarthaḥ rājya rūpeṇa tyajyatām asukha āvahaḥ lupta prajñaḥ pareṇa asi dharmam darśaya vai sutān labhantām pāṇḍavāḥ rājyam śamam gacchantu kauravāḥ yudhiṣṭhiram ca bhīmam ca vārayiṣyāmi saṃyuge evam bruvati vipra indre dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ ākṣipya vākyam vākya jñaḥ vākpathena api ayāt punar uvāca prasādaye tvām atula prabhāvam tvam naḥ gatiḥ darśayitā ca dhīraḥ na ca api te vaśagāḥ me mahā ṛṣe na kalmaṣam kartum iha arhase mām tvam hi dharmaḥ pavitram ca yaśaḥ kīrtiḥ dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca mānyaḥ ca asi pitāmahaḥ uvāca uvāca yāni liṅgāni saṃgrāme bhavanti vijayiṣyatām tāni sarvāṇi bhagavan śrotum icchāmi tattvāt uvāca prasanna bhās pāvakaḥ ūrdhva raśmiḥ pradakṣiṇa āvarta śikhaḥ vidhūmaḥ puṇyāḥ gandhāḥ ca āhutīnām pravānti jayasya etat bhāvinaḥ rūpam āhuḥ gambhīra ghoṣāḥ ca mahā svanāḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ mṛdaṅgāḥ ca nadanti yatra viśuddha raśmiḥ tapanaḥ śaśī ca jayasya etat bhāvinaḥ rūpam āhuḥ iṣṭāḥ vācaḥ pṛṣṭhatas vāyasānām saṃprasthitānām ca gamiṣyatām ca kalyāṇa vācaḥ śakunāḥ rājahaṃsāḥ śukāḥ krauñcāḥ śatapattrāḥ ca yatra alaṃkāraiḥ kavacaiḥ ketubhiḥ ca mukha prasādaiḥ hema varṇaiḥ ca nṝṇām bhrājiṣmatī duṣpratiprekṣaṇīyā yeṣām camūḥ te vijayanti śatrūn hṛṣṭāḥ vācaḥ tathā sattvam yodhānām yatra bhārata iṣṭaḥ vātaḥ praviṣṭasya dakṣiṇā pravivikṣataḥ paścāt saṃsādhayati artham purastāt pratiṣedhate śabda rūpa rasa sparśa gandhāḥ ca āviṣkṛtāḥ śubhāḥ sadā yodhāḥ ca hṛṣṭāḥ ca yeṣām teṣām dhruvam jayaḥ anu eva vāyavaḥ vānti tathā abhrāṇi vayāṃsi ca etāni jayamānānām lakṣaṇāni viśām pate bhavanti viparītāni mumūrṣūṇām janādhipa alpāyām vā mahatyām vā senāyām iti niścitam ekaḥ dīrṇaḥ dārayati senām su mahatīm api tam dīrṇam anudīryante yodhāḥ śūratamāḥ api durnivāratamā ca eva prabhagnā mahatī camūḥ apām iva mahā vegaḥ trastāḥ mṛga gaṇāḥ iva na eva śakyā samādhātum saṃnipāte mahā camūḥ dīrṇāḥ iti eva dīryante yodhāḥ śūratamāḥ api bhītān bhagnān ca saṃprekṣya bhayam bhūyas vivardhate prabhagnā sahasā rājan diśaḥ vibhrāmitā paraiḥ na eva sthāpayitum śakyā śūraiḥ api mahā camūḥ saṃbhṛtya mahatīm senām caturaṅgām mahīpatiḥ śaknoti na samādhātum dīrṇām indra samaḥ yudhi upāya pūrvam medhāvī yateta satata utthitaḥ mahā doṣaḥ saṃnipātaḥ tatas vyaṅgaḥ saḥ ucyate paraspareṇa saṃdṛṣṭā suraiḥ api mahā camūḥ paraspara jñāḥ saṃhṛṣ vyavadhūtāḥ su niścitāḥ pañcāśat api ye śūrāḥ mathnanti mahatīm camūm dṛṣṭvā suparṇa upacitim mahatīm api bhārata uvāca evam uktvā yayau vyāsaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dhīmate dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ api tat śrutvā dhyānam eva anvapadyata saṃjayam saṃśita ātmānam apṛcchat bharata ṛṣabha saṃjaya ime mahīpālāḥ śūrāḥ yuddha abhinandinaḥ pārthivāḥ pṛthivī hetoḥ samabhityakta jīvitāḥ manye bahu guṇā bhūmiḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya koṭayaḥ ca loka vīrāṇām sametāḥ kurujāṅgale deśānām ca parīmāṇam nagarāṇām ca saṃjaya divya buddhi pradīpena yuktaḥ tvam jñānacakṣuṣā uvāca yathāprajñam mahā prājña bhaumān vakṣyāmi te guṇān dvividhāni iha bhūtāni trasāni sthāvarāṇi ca trasānām trividhā yoniḥ aṇḍa sveda jarāyu jāḥ trasānām khalu sarveṣām śreṣṭhāḥ rājan jarāyu jāḥ jarāyu jānām pravarāḥ mānavāḥ paśavaḥ ca ye nānā rūpāṇi bibhrāṇāḥ teṣām bhedāḥ caturdaśa araṇya vāsinaḥ sapta sapta eṣām grāma vāsinaḥ siṃha vyāghra varāhāḥ ca mahiṣāḥ vāraṇāḥ tathā ṛkṣāḥ ca vānarāḥ ca eva sapta āraṇyāḥ smṛtāḥ nṛpa ete grāmyāḥ samākhyātāḥ paśavaḥ sapta sādhubhiḥ ete vai paśavaḥ rājan grāmya āraṇyāḥ caturdaśa veda uktāḥ pṛthivīpāla yeṣu yajñāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ grāmyāṇām puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ siṃhaḥ ca araṇya vāsinām sarveṣām eva bhūtānām anyonyena abhijīvanam udbhid jāḥ sthāvarāḥ proktāḥ teṣām pañca eva jātayaḥ vṛkṣa gulma latā vallyaḥ tvac sārāḥ tṛṇa jātayaḥ eṣām viṃśatiḥ eka ūnā mahābhūteṣu pañcasu caturviṃśatiḥ uddiṣṭā gāyatrī loka saṃmatā yaḥ etām veda gāyatrīm puṇyām sarva guṇa anvitām bhūmau hi jāyate sarvam bhūmau sarvam praṇaśyati bhūmiḥ pratiṣṭhā bhūtānām bhūmiḥ eva parāyaṇam uvāca nadīnām parvatānām ca nāmadheyāni saṃjaya tathā janapadānām ca ye ca anye bhūmim āśritāḥ pramāṇam ca pramāṇa jña pṛthivyāḥ api sarvaśas uvāca pañca imāni mahā rāja mahābhūtāni saṃgrahāt jagat sthitāni sarvāṇi samāni āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ bhūmiḥ apaḥ tathā vāyuḥ agniḥ ākāśam eva ca guṇa uttarāṇi sarvāṇi teṣām bhūmiḥ pradhānataḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ gandhaḥ ca pañcamaḥ bhūmyāḥ ete guṇāḥ proktāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ tattva vedibhiḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ ca api prakīrtitāḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca tejasaḥ atha guṇāḥ trayaḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca vāyoḥ tu ākāśe śabdaḥ eva ca ete pañca guṇāḥ rājan mahābhūteṣu pañcasu vartante sarva lokeṣu yeṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ yadā tu viṣamībhāvam āviśanti parasparam bhāvam na ca bhajantaḥ te nāśam gacchanti na anyathā ānupūrvyāt vinaśyanti jāyante ca anupūrvaśas sarvāṇi aparimeyāṇi tat eṣām rūpam aiśvaram tatra tatra hi dṛśyante dhātavaḥ pāñcabhautikāḥ teṣām manuṣyāḥ tarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ na tān tarkeṇa sādhayet parimaṇḍalaḥ mahā rāja dvīpaḥ asau cakra saṃsthitaḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpa phala upetaiḥ saṃpanna dhana dhānyavān lāvaṇena samudreṇa samantāt parivāritaḥ yathā ca puruṣaḥ paśyet ādarśe mukham ātmanaḥ evam sudarśana dvīpaḥ dṛśyate candra maṇḍale dvis aṃśe pippalaḥ tatra dvis aṃśe ca śaśaḥ mahān sarva oṣadhi samāvāpaiḥ sarvatas paribṛṃhitaḥ apaḥ tatas anyāḥ vijñeyāḥ eṣa saṃkṣepaḥ ucyate tatas anyaḥ ucyate ca ayam enam saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu uvāca yāvat bhūmi avakāśaḥ ayam dṛśyate śaśalakṣaṇe uvāca evam uktaḥ sa rājñā tu saṃjayaḥ vākyam abravīt prāñc āyatāḥ mahā rāja ṣaṭ ete ratna parvatāḥ sthitā samudram ākramya avarūḍhā bhavan tatas himavant hemakūṭaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca naga uttamaḥ nīlaḥ ca vaiḍūrya mayaḥ śvetaḥ ca rajata prabhaḥ sarvadhātuvinaddhaḥ ca śṛṅgavān nāma parvataḥ ete vai parvatāḥ rājan siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ teṣām antara viṣkambhaḥ yojanāni sahasraśas tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ tāni varṣāṇi bhārata vasanti teṣu sattvāni nānā jātīni sarvaśas idam tu bhāratam varṣam tatas haimavatam param tatas kiṃpuruṣa āvāsam varṣam himavantaḥ param hemakūṭāt param ca eva harivarṣam pracakṣate prāc āyataḥ mahā rāja mālyavant nāma parvataḥ āditya taruṇa ābhāsaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśa adhas kila smṛtaḥ uccais ca catura aśītiḥ yojanānām mahīpate ūrdhvam antar ca tiryak ca lokān āvṛtya tiṣṭhati tasya pārśve tu ime dvīpāḥ catvāraḥ saṃsthitāḥ prabho bhadrāśvaḥ ketumālaḥ ca jambūdvīpaḥ ca bhārata ketumālaḥ caturthaḥ ca meroḥ paścimatas sthitaḥ uttarāḥ ca eva kuravaḥ kṛta puṇya pratiśrayāḥ sa vai vicintayām āsa sauvarṇān prekṣya vāyasān meruḥ uttama madhyānām adhamānām ca pakṣiṇām a viśeṣa karaḥ yasmāt tasmāt enam tyajāmi aham tam ādityaḥ anuparyeti satatam jyotiṣām patiḥ candramāḥ ca sa nakṣatraḥ vāyuḥ ca eva pradakṣiṇam bhavanaiḥ āvṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ tatra deva gaṇāḥ rājan gandharva asura rākṣasāḥ apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃyuktāḥ śaile krīḍanti nityaśas tatra brahmā ca rudraḥ ca śakraḥ ca api sura īśvaraḥ tumburuḥ nāradaḥ ca eva viśvāvasuḥ hahā huhūḥ abhigamya amara śreṣṭhāḥ stavai stunvanti ca abhibho saptarṣayaḥ mahātmānaḥ kaśyapaḥ ca prajāpatiḥ tasmāt kuberaḥ bhagavān caturtham bhāgam aśnute tatas kalā aṃśam vittasya manuṣyebhyaḥ prayacchati karṇikāra vanam ramyam śilā jāla samudgatam tatra sākṣāt paśupatiḥ divyaiḥ bhūtaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ umāsahāyaḥ bhagavant ramate bhūtabhāvanaḥ karṇikāra mayīm mālām bibhrat pāda avalambinīm tam ugra tapasaḥ siddhāḥ suvratāḥ satya vādinaḥ paśyanti na hi durvṛttaiḥ śakyaḥ draṣṭum maheśvaraḥ tasya śailasya śikharāt kṣīra dhārā nareśvara triṃśat bāhu parigrāhyā bhīma nirghāta nisvanā puṇyā puṇyatamaiḥ juṣṭā gaṅgā bhāgīrathī śubhā tayā hi utpāditaḥ puṇyaḥ sa hradaḥ sāgara upamaḥ tām āsa purā durdharām parvataiḥ api śatam varṣa sahasrāṇām śirasā vai maheśvaraḥ jambu ṣaṇḍaḥ ca tatra eva su mahān nandana upamaḥ āyuḥ daśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tatra bhārata suvarṇa varṇāḥ ca narāḥ striyaḥ ca apsarasā upamāḥ anāmayāḥ vīta śokāḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ jāyante mānavāḥ tatra niṣṭapta kanaka prabhāḥ gandhamādana śṛṅgeṣu kuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ apsarasām saṃghaiḥ modate guhyaka adhipaḥ gandhamādana pādeṣu pareṣu apara gaṇḍikāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām parama āyuṣaḥ tatra kṛṣṇāḥ narāḥ rājan tejaḥ yuktāḥ mahā balāḥ striyaḥ ca utpala pattra ābhāḥ sarvāḥ su priya darśanāḥ nīlāt parataram śvetam śvetāt hairaṇyakam param hiraṇmayam ca śvetādreḥ param varṣam narādhipa kuru varṣam tatas rājan śṛṅgavant parvatāt param varṣam airāvatam nāma tatas śṛṅgavantaḥ param dhanuḥsaṃsthe mahā rāja dve varṣe dakṣiṇa uttare ilāvṛtam madhyamam tu pañca varṣāṇi ca eva ha āyuṣpramāṇam ārogyam dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhārata evam eṣā mahā rāja parvataiḥ pṛthivī citā hemakūṭaḥ tu su mahān kailāsaḥ nāma parvataḥ citre śilā tale ramye deva ṛṣi gaṇa pūjitaḥ hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ su mahān divyaḥ maṇi mayaḥ giriḥ tasya pārśve mahat divyam śubham kāñcana vālukam ramyam bindusaraḥ nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathīm gaṅgām uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ yūpāḥ maṇi mayāḥ tatra cityāḥ ca api hiraṇmayāḥ tatra iṣṭvā tu gataḥ siddhim sahasrākṣaḥ mahā yaśāḥ sṛṣṭvā bhūtapatiḥ yatra sarva lokān sanātanaḥ upāsyate tigma tejāḥ vṛtaḥ bhūtaiḥ samāgataiḥ nara nārāyaṇau brahmā manuḥ sthāṇuḥ ca pañcamaḥ vasvokasārā nalinī pāvanī ca sarasvatī jambūnadī ca sītā ca gaṅgā sindhuḥ ca saptamā dṛśya adṛśyā ca bhavati tatra tatra sarasvatī etāḥ divyāḥ sapta gaṅgāḥ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ rakṣāṃsi vai himavanti hemakūṭe tu guhyakāḥ sarpāḥ nāgāḥ ca niṣadhe gokarṇe ca tapodhanāḥ deva asurāṇām ca gṛham śvetaḥ parvataḥ ucyate śṛṅgavant tu mahā rāja pitṝṇām pratisaṃcaraḥ iti etāni mahā rāja sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśas bhūtāni upaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca teṣām ṛddhiḥ bahuvidhā dṛśyate daiva mānuṣī aśakyā parisaṃkhyātum śraddheyā tu bubhūṣatā yām tu pṛcchasi mā rājan divyām etām śaśa ākṛtim jambūdvīpasya sarvasya ākṛtim candra maṇḍale sa vai sudarśana dvīpaḥ dṛśyate śaśa vat vidhau pārśve śaśasya dve varṣe ubhaye dakṣiṇa uttare anyāni pañca varṣāṇi gala antam kalpitāni ca karṇau tu nāgadvīpam ca kaśyapadvīpam eva ca tāmra varṇaḥ śiraḥ rājan śrīmān malaya parvataḥ etat dvitīyam dvīpasya dṛśyate śaśa saṃsthitam uvāca meroḥ atha uttaram pārśvam pūrvam ca ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya meroḥ pārśve tathā uttare uttarāḥ kuravaḥ rājan puṇyāḥ siddha niṣevitāḥ tatra vṛkṣāḥ madhu phalāḥ nitya puṣpa phala upagāḥ sarva kāma phalāḥ tatra ke cid vṛkṣāḥ janādhipa apare kṣīriṇaḥ nāma vṛkṣāḥ tatra narādhipa ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīram ṣaṣ rasam hi amṛta upamam vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣu ābharaṇāni ca sarvā maṇi mayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣma kāñcana vālukā sarvatra sukha saṃsparśā niṣpaṅkā ca janādhipa puṣkariṇyaḥ śubhāḥ tatra sukha sparśāḥ manoharāḥ deva loka cyutāḥ sarve jāyante tatra mānavāḥ tulya rūpa guṇa upetāḥ sameṣu viṣameṣu ca mithunāni ca jāyante striyaḥ ca apsarasā upamāḥ teṣām te kṣīriṇām kṣīram pibanti amṛta saṃnibham nirāmayāḥ vīta śokāḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi daśa varṣa śatāni ca bhāruṇḍāḥ nāma śakunāḥ tīkṣṇa tuṇḍāḥ mahā balāḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ rājan vyākhyātāḥ te samāsatas meroḥ pārśvam aham pūrvam vakṣyāmi atha yathātatham bhadrāśvam nāma varṣam tu puras vai gandhamādanāt tasya pūrva abhiṣekaḥ tu bhadrāśvasya viśām pate bhadrasālavanam yatra kāla āmraḥ ca mahā drumaḥ kāla āmraḥ ca mahā rāja nitya puṣpa phalaḥ śubhaḥ tatra te puruṣāḥ śvetāḥ tejaḥ yuktāḥ mahā balāḥ striyaḥ kumuda varṇāḥ ca sundaryaḥ priya darśanāḥ candra prabhāḥ candra varṇāḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanāḥ candra śītala gātrāḥ ca nṛtta gīta viśāradāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra āyuḥ bharata ṛṣabha kāla āmra rasa pītāḥ te nityam saṃsthita yauvanāḥ sudarśanaḥ nāma mahān jambu vṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ sarva kāma phalaḥ puṇyaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitaḥ tasya nāmnā samākhyātaḥ jambūdvīpaḥ sanātanaḥ yojanānām sahasram ca śatam ca bharata ṛṣabha utsedhaḥ vṛkṣarājasya diva spṛś manuja īśvara aratnīnām sahasram ca śatāni daśa pañca ca pariṇāhaḥ tu vṛkṣasya phalānām rasa bhedinām tasyāḥ jambvāḥ phala rasaḥ nadī bhūtvā janādhipa merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā saṃprayāti uttarān kurūn pibanti tat rasam hṛṣṭāḥ janāḥ nityam janādhipa tatra jāmbūnadam nāma kanakam deva bhūṣaṇam indragopaka saṃkāśam jāyate bhāsvaram tu tat taruṇa āditya varṇāḥ ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge dīpyate tatra havyavāṭ nāmnā saṃvartakaḥ nāma kālāgniḥ bharata ṛṣabha tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge pūrve pūrva anta gaṇḍikā yojanānām sahasrāṇi pañcāśat mālyavant sthitaḥ mahārajata saṃkāśāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ rakṣaṇa artham tu bhūtānām praviśanti divākaram ṣaṣṭiḥ tāni sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiḥ eva śatāni ca ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭim eva śatāni ca āditya tāpa taptāḥ te viśanti śaśi maṇḍalam uvāca varṣāṇām ca eva nāmāni parvatānām ca saṃjaya ācakṣva me yathātattvam ye ca parvata vāsinaḥ uvāca varṣam ramaṇakam nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥ śukla abhijana saṃpannāḥ sarve su priya darśanāḥ rati pradhānāḥ ca tathā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahā rāja nityam mudita mānasāḥ dakṣiṇe śṛṅgiṇaḥ ca eva śvetasya atha uttareṇa ca varṣam hairaṇvatam nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī yatra ca ayam mahā rāja pakṣirāj pataga uttamaḥ yakṣa anugāḥ mahā rāja dhaninaḥ priya darśanāḥ mahā balāḥ tatra sadā rājan mudita mānasāḥ yakṣaḥ saḥ api mahā rāja yakṣa rāja anugautamaḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te janādhipa āyuṣpramāṇam jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca śṛṅgāṇi vai śṛṅgavantaḥ trīṇi eva manuja adhipa tatra svayaṃprabhā devī nityam vasati śāṇḍilī uttareṇa tu śṛṅgasya samudra ante janādhipa varṣam airāvatam nāma tasmāt śṛṅgavantaḥ param candramāḥ ca sa nakṣatraḥ jyotiḥ bhūtaḥ iva āvṛtaḥ padma prabhāḥ padma varṇāḥ padma pattra nibha īkṣaṇāḥ aniṣpandāḥ sugandhāḥ ca nirāhārāḥ jita indriyāḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te janādhipa āyuṣpramāṇam jīvanti narāḥ bharata sattama hariḥ vasati vaikuṇṭhaḥ śakaṭe kanaka ātmake aṣṭa cakram hi tat yānam bhūta yuktam manojavam agni varṇam mahā vegam jāmbūnada pariṣkṛtam sa prabhuḥ sarva bhūtānām vibhuḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha saṃkṣepaḥ vistaraḥ ca eva kartā kārayitā ca saḥ pṛthivī apaḥ tathā ākāśam vāyuḥ tejaḥ ca pārthiva sa yajñaḥ sarva bhūtānām āsyam tasya hutāśanaḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ saṃjayena dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ mahā manāḥ asaṃśayam sūtaputra kālaḥ saṃkṣipate jagat sṛjate ca punar sarvam na iha vidyati śāśvatam naraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva sarvajñaḥ sarva bhūta bhṛt devāḥ vaikuṇṭhaḥ iti āhuḥ vedāḥ viṣṇuḥ iti prabhum uvāca yat idam bhāratam varṣam yatra idam mūrchitam balam yatra gṛddhāḥ pāṇḍu sutāḥ yatra me sajjate manaḥ uvāca na tatra pāṇḍavāḥ gṛddhāḥ śṛṇu rājan vacaḥ mama apare kṣatriyāḥ ca api nānā janapada īśvarāḥ atra te varṇayiṣyāmi varṣam bhārata bhāratam pṛthoḥ ca rājan vainyasya tathā ikṣvākoḥ mahātmanaḥ yayāteḥ ambarīṣasya māndhātuḥ nahuṣasya ca anyeṣām ca mahā rāja kṣatriyāṇām balīyasām tat te varṣam pravakṣyāmi yathāśrutam ariṃdama śṛṇu me gadataḥ rājan yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimant ṛkṣavant api teṣām sahasraśas rājan parvatāḥ tu samīpatas abhijñātāḥ sāravantaḥ vipulāḥ citra sānavaḥ anye tatas a parijñātāḥ hrasvāḥ hrasva upajīvinaḥ āryāḥ mlecchāḥ ca kauravya taiḥ miśrāḥ puruṣāḥ vibho nadīḥ pibanti bahulāḥ gaṅgām sindhum sarasvatīm godāvarīm narmadām ca bāhudām ca mahā nadīm śatadrum candrabhāgām ca yamunām ca mahā nadīm dṛṣadvatīm vipāśām ca vipāpām sthūlavālukām nadīm vetravatīm ca eva kṛṣṇaveṇām ca nimnagām irāvatīm vitastām ca payoṣṇīm devikām api vedasmṛtīm vetasinīm tridivām iṣkumālinīm karīṣiṇīm citravahām citrasenām ca nimnagām gomatīm dhūtapāpām ca vandanām ca mahā nadīm kauśikīm tridivām kṛtyām vicitrām lohatāriṇīm rathasthām śatakumbhām ca sarayūm ca nareśvara carmaṇvatīm vetravatīm hastisomām diśam tathā śatāvarīm payoṣṇīm ca parām bhaimarathīm tathā kāverīm culukām ca api vāpīm śatabalām api nicīrām mahitām ca api suprayogām narādhipa pavitrām kuṇḍalām sindhum vājinīm puramālinīm pūrvābhirāmām vīrām ca bhīmām oghavatīm tathā palāśinīm pāpaharām mahendrām pippalāvatīm pāriṣeṇām asiknīm ca saralām bhāramardinīm puruhīm pravarām menām moghām ghṛtavatīm tathā dhūmatyām atikṛṣṇām ca sūcīm chāvīm ca kaurava sadānīrām adhṛṣyām ca kuśadhārām mahā nadīm śaśikāntām śivām ca eva tathā vīravatīm api vāstum suvāstum gaurīm ca kampanām sa hiraṇvatīm hiraṇvatīm citravatīm citrasenām ca nimnagām rathacitrām jyotirathām viśvāmitrām kapiñjalām upendrām bahulām ca eva kucarām ambuvāhinīm vainandīm piñjalām veṇṇām tuṅgaveṇām mahā nadīm vidiśām kṛṣṇaveṇṇām ca tāmrām ca kapilām api śalum suvāmām vedāśvām harisrāvām mahāpagām śīghrām ca picchilām ca eva bhāradvājīm ca nimnagām kauśikīm nimnagām śoṇām bāhudām atha candanām durgām antaḥśilām ca eva brahmamedhyām bṛhadvatīm carakṣām mahirohīm ca tathā jambunadīm api sunasām tamasām dāsīm trasām anyām varāṇasīm loloddhṛtakarām ca eva pūrṇāśām ca mahā nadīm mānavīm vṛṣabhām ca eva mahā nadyaḥ janādhipa sadānirāmayām vṛtyām mandagām mandavāhinīm brahma medhyām bṛhadvatīm etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca bahudhā brahmāṇīm ca mahāgaurīm durgām api ca bhārata citropalām citrabarhām mañjum makaravāhinīm mandākinīm vaitaraṇīm kokām ca eva mahā nadīm śuktimatīm araṇyām ca puṣpaveṇī utpalāvatīm lohityām karatoyām ca tathā eva vṛṣabhaṅginīm kumārīm ṛṣikulyām ca brahmakulyām ca bhārata sarasvatīḥ su puṇyāḥ ca sarvāḥ gaṅgāḥ ca māriṣa brahmāṇīm ca mahāgaurīm suvaśyām api bhārata mānavīm vṛṣabhām ca eva mahā nadyaḥ janādhipa viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvāḥ ca eva mahā balāḥ tathā nadyaḥ tu aprakāśāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas iti etāḥ saritaḥ rājan samākhyātāḥ yathāsmṛti tatra ime kuru pāñcālāḥ śālva mādreya jāṅgalāḥ videhāḥ māgadhāḥ siṃhāḥ mahat āyatayaḥ tathā śūrasenāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca bodhāḥ maukāḥ tathā eva ca matsyāḥ sukuṭyaḥ saubalyāḥ kuntalāḥ kāśi kośalāḥ cedi vatsāḥ karūṣāḥ ca bhojāḥ sindhupulindakāḥ uttamaujāḥ daśārṇāḥ ca mekalāḥ ca utkalaiḥ saha pāñcālāḥ kauśijāḥ ca eva ekapṛṣṭhāḥ yugaṃdharāḥ saudhāḥ madrāḥ bhujiṅgāḥ ca kāśayaḥ aparakāśayaḥ jaṭharāḥ kukkuśāḥ ca eva sudāśārṇāḥ ca bhārata govindāḥ mandakāḥ ṣaṇḍāḥ vidarbha anūpavāsikāḥ aśmakāḥ pāṃsurāṣṭrāḥ ca goparāṣṭrāḥ panītakāḥ ādirāṣṭrāḥ sukuṭṭāḥ ca balirāṣṭram ca kevalam vānarāsyāḥ pravāhāḥ ca vakrāḥ vakrabhayāḥ śakāḥ videhakāḥ māgadhāḥ ca suhmāḥ ca vijayāḥ tathā aṅgāḥ vaṅgāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca yakṛllomānaḥ eva ca mallāḥ sudeṣṇāḥ prāhūtāḥ tathā māhiṣakārṣikāḥ vāhīkāḥ vāṭadhānāḥ ca ābhīrāḥ kālatoyakāḥ aparandhrāḥ ca śūdrāḥ ca pahlavāḥ carmakhaṇḍikāḥ aṭavīśabarāḥ ca eva marubhaumāḥ ca māriṣa upāvṛśca anupāvṛśca surāṣṭrāḥ kekayāḥ tathā kuṭṭāparāntāḥ dvaidheyāḥ kākṣāḥ sāmudraniṣkuṭāḥ kaṭyāḥ ca yākāḥ sāmudra niṣka dāḥ bahirgirya aṅga maladāḥ māgadhāḥ mānavarjakāḥ mahyuttarāḥ prāvṛṣeyāḥ bhārgavāḥ ca janādhipa puṇḍrāḥ bhārgāḥ kirātāḥ ca sudoṣṇāḥ pramudāḥ tathā śakāḥ niṣādāḥ niṣadhāḥ tathā eva ānarta nairṛtāḥ dugūlāḥ pratimatsyāḥ ca kuśalāḥ kunaṭāḥ tathā tīragrāhāḥ taratoyāḥ rājikāḥ rasyakāgaṇāḥ tilakāḥ pārasīkāḥ ca madhumantaḥ prakutsakāḥ kāśmīrāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ gāndhārāḥ darśakāḥ tathā kulūtāḥ ca śaivalāḥ bāhlikāḥ tathā darvīkāḥ sa kacāḥ darvāḥ vātajāma rathoragāḥ bahuvādyāḥ ca kauravya sudāmānaḥ sumallikāḥ vadhrāḥ karīṣakāḥ ca api kulindopatyakāḥ tathā vanāyavaḥ daśāpārśvāḥ romāṇaḥ kuśabindavaḥ kacchāḥ gopālakacchāḥ ca lāṅgalāḥ paravallakāḥ kirātāḥ barbarāḥ siddhāḥ videhāḥ tāmraliṅgakāḥ oṣṭrāḥ puṇḍrāḥ sa sairandhrāḥ pārvatīyāḥ ca māriṣa atha apare janapadāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ bharata ṛṣabha draviḍāḥ keralāḥ prācyāḥ bhūṣikāḥ vanavāsinaḥ unnatyakāḥ māhiṣakāḥ vikalpāḥ mūṣakāḥ tathā karṇikāḥ kuntikāḥ ca eva saudbhidāḥ nalakālakāḥ kaukuṭṭakāḥ tathā colāḥ koṅkaṇāḥ mālavāṇakāḥ samaṅgāḥ kopanāḥ ca eva kukura aṅgada māriṣāḥ tryaṅgāḥ kekarakāḥ proṣṭhāḥ parasaṃcarakāḥ tathā mālakāḥ mallakāḥ ca eva tathā eva aparavartakāḥ kulindāḥ kulakāḥ ca eva karaṇṭhāḥ kurakāḥ tathā mūṣakāḥ stanabālāḥ ca satiyaḥ pattipañjakāḥ ādidāyāḥ sirālāḥ ca stūbakāḥ stanapāḥ tathā hṛṣīvidarbhāḥ kāntīkāḥ taṅgaṇāḥ parataṅgaṇāḥ yavanāḥ ca sa kāmbojāḥ dāruṇāḥ mleccha jātayaḥ sakṣaddruhaḥ kuntalāḥ ca hūṇāḥ pāratakaiḥ saha tathā eva maradhāḥ cīnāḥ tathā eva daśamālikāḥ kṣatriya upaniveśāḥ ca vaiśya śūdra kulāni ca śūdra ābhīra atha daradāḥ kāśmīrāḥ paśubhiḥ saha khaśikāḥ ca tukhārāḥ ca pallavāḥ giri gahvarāḥ ātreyāḥ sa bharadvājāḥ tathā eva stanayoṣikāḥ aupakāḥ ca kaliṅgāḥ ca kirātānām ca jātayaḥ kāraskarāḥ ca vaṃśāḥ ca āndhrāḥ ca dramiḍāḥ tathā colāḥ ca eva tathā pāṇḍyāḥ cerāḥ ca eva susiṃhalāḥ tāmarāḥ haṃsamārgāḥ ca tathā eva karabhañjakāḥ ete ca anye janapadāḥ prācya udīcyāḥ tathā eva ca uddeśa mātreṇa mayā deśāḥ saṃkīrtitāḥ prabho duhyet dhenuḥ kāmaduh ca bhūmiḥ samyak anuṣṭhitā tasyām gṛdhyanti rājānaḥ śūrāḥ dharma artha kovidāḥ te tyajanti āhave prāṇān rasā gṛddhāḥ tarasvinaḥ deva mānuṣa kāyānām kāmam bhūmiḥ parāyaṇam rājānaḥ bharata śreṣṭha bhoktu kāmāḥ vasuṃdharām na ca api tṛptiḥ kāmānām vidyate ca iha kasya cid tasmāt parigrahe bhūmeḥ yatante kuru pāṇḍavāḥ sāmnā dānena bhedena daṇḍena eva ca pārthiva pitā mātā ca putraḥ ca kham dyauḥ ca nara puṃgava bhūmiḥ bhavati bhūtānām samyak a chidra darśiṇī uvāca pramāṇam āyuṣaḥ sūta phalam ca api śubha aśubham anāgatam atikrāntam vartamānam ca saṃjaya uvāca kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca puṣyam ca kuru vardhana pūrvam kṛta yugam nāma tatas tretā yugam vibho saṃkṣepāt dvāparasya atha tatas puṣyam pravartate catvāri ca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām kuru sattama āyus saṃkhyā kṛta yuge saṃkhyātā rāja sattama tathā trīṇi sahasrāṇi tretāyām manuja adhipa mahā balāḥ mahāsattvāḥ prajā guṇa samanvitāḥ prajāyante ca jātāḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas ajāyanta kṛte rājan munayaḥ su tapodhanāḥ mahā utsāhāḥ mahātmānaḥ dhārmikāḥ satya vādinaḥ jātāḥ kṛta yuge rājan dhaninaḥ priya darśanāḥ āyuṣmantaḥ mahā vīrāḥ dhanurdhara varāḥ yudhi vara arhāḥ yudhi jāyante kṣatriyāḥ śūra sattamāḥ jāyante kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ tretāyām cakravartinaḥ sarva varṇāḥ mahā rāja jāyante dvāpare sati mahā utsāhāḥ mahā vīryāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ tejasā alpena saṃyuktāḥ krodhanāḥ puruṣāḥ nṛpa lubdhāḥ ca ānṛtakāḥ ca eva puṣye jāyanti bhārata īrṣyā mānaḥ tathā krodhaḥ māyā asūyā tathā eva ca puṣye bhavanti martyānām rāgaḥ lobhaḥ ca bhārata uvāca śākadvīpam ca me brūhi kuśadvīpam ca saṃjaya brūhi gāvalgaṇe sarvam rāhoḥ soma arkayoḥ tathā uvāca rājan su bahavaḥ dvīpāḥ yaiḥ idam saṃtatam jagat aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānām viśām pate ṣaṣ śatāni ca pūrṇāni viṣkambhaḥ jambu parvataḥ lāvaṇasya samudrasya viṣkambhaḥ dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ nānā janapada ākīrṇaḥ maṇi vidruma citritaḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ sāgaraḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ śākadvīpam ca vakṣyāmi yathāvat iha pārthiva śṛṇu me tvam yathānyāyam bruvataḥ kuru nandana jambūdvīpa pramāṇena dviguṇaḥ sa narādhipa viṣkambheṇa mahā rāja sāgaraḥ api vibhāgaśaḥ yathāsaṃkhyam parivṛttaḥ surā sarpiḥ payodhibhiḥ kṣīrodaḥ bharata śreṣṭha yena saṃparivāritaḥ śākadvīpasya saṃkṣepaḥ yathāvat bharata ṛṣabha uvāca śākadvīpasya saṃkṣepaḥ yathāvat iha saṃjaya uvāca tathā eva parvatāḥ rājan sapta atra maṇi bhūṣitāḥ ratna ākarāḥ tathā nadyaḥ teṣām nāmāni mama śṛṇu atīva guṇavat sarvam tatra puṇyam janādhipa prāc āyataḥ mahā rāja malayaḥ nāma parvataḥ yatas varṣam prabhavati varṣā kāle janeśvara revatī divi nakṣatram pitāmaha kṛtaḥ vidhiḥ uttareṇa tu rāja indra śyāmaḥ nāma mahā giriḥ nava megha prabhaḥ prāṃśuḥ śrīmān ujjvala vigrahaḥ yatas śyāma tvam āpannāḥ prajāḥ janapada īśvara uvāca prajāḥ katham sūtaputra saṃprāptāḥ śyāma tām iha uvāca sarveṣu eva mahā prājña dvīpeṣu kuru nandana gauraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca varṇau dvau tayoḥ varṇa antaram nṛpa śyāmaḥ yasmāt pravṛttaḥ vai tat te vakṣyāmi bhārata āste atra bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ tat kāntyā śyāma tām gataḥ teṣām yojana viṣkambhaḥ dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ varṣāṇi teṣu kauravya saṃproktāni manīṣibhiḥ mahā meruḥ mahākāśaḥ jaladaḥ kumuda uttaraḥ jala dhārāt paraḥ rājan sukumāraḥ iti smṛtaḥ raivatasya tu kaumāraḥ śyāmasya tu maṇīcakaḥ kesarasya atha modākī pareṇa tu mahā pumān śākaḥ nāma mahā rāja tasya dvīpasya madhya gaḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ pūjyate tatra śaṃkaraḥ dhārmikāḥ ca prajāḥ rājñ catvāraḥ atīva bhārata varṇāḥ sva karma niratāḥ na ca stenaḥ atra dṛśyate dīrgha āyuṣaḥ mahā rāja jarā mṛtyu vivarjitāḥ nadyaḥ puṇya jalāḥ tatra gaṅgā ca bahudhā gatiḥ sukumārī kumārī ca sītā kāverakā tathā mahānadī ca kauravya tathā maṇijalā nadī tatas pravṛttāḥ puṇya udāḥ nadyaḥ kuru kula udvaha sahasrāṇām śatāni eva yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ na tāsām nāmadheyāni parimāṇam tathā eva ca śakyate parisaṃkhyātum puṇyāḥ tāḥ hi sarit varāḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ catvāraḥ loka saṃmatāḥ magāḥ ca maśakāḥ ca eva mānasāḥ mandagāḥ tathā magāḥ brāhmaṇa bhūyiṣṭhāḥ sva karma niratāḥ nṛpa maśakeṣu tu rājanyāḥ dhārmikāḥ sarva kāma dāḥ mānaseṣu mahā rāja vaiśyāḥ karma upajīvinaḥ sarva kāma samāyuktāḥ śūrāḥ dharma artha niścitāḥ śūdrāḥ tu mandage nityam puruṣāḥ dharma śīlinaḥ na tatra rājā rāja indra na daṇḍaḥ na ca daṇḍikāḥ etāvat eva śakyam tu tasmin dvīpe prabhāṣitum etāvat eva śrotavyam śākadvīpe mahā ojasi uvāca uttareṣu tu kauravya dvīpeṣu śrūyate kathā ikṣūdaḥ ca surodaḥ ca sarpiḥ kṣīra udadhiḥ tadā dadhimaṇḍa udadhiḥ ca anyaḥ śuddha udadhiḥ atho mahān paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ sarve dvīpāḥ narādhipa sarvatas ca mahā rāja parvataiḥ parivāritāḥ parvataḥ paścimaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ nārāyaṇa nibhaḥ nṛpa tatra ratnāni divyāni svayam rakṣati keśavaḥ prajāpatim upāsīnaḥ prajānām vidadhe sukham saṃpūjyate hi plakṣaḥ ca yathā saṃpūjyate śalmaliḥ ca dvīpe śālmalike nṛpa krauñcadvīpe mahā krauñcaḥ giriḥ ratna caya ākaraḥ saṃpūjyate mahā rāja cāturvarṇyena nityadā mokṣibhiḥ saṃstutaḥ nityam prabhuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ hariḥ sudhāmā nāma durdharṣaḥ dvitīyaḥ hemaparvataḥ dyutimant nāma kauravya tṛtīyaḥ kumudaḥ giriḥ caturthaḥ puṣpavant nāma pañcamaḥ tu kuśeśayaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ harigiriḥ nāma ṣaṭ ete parvata uttamāḥ teṣām antara viṣkambhaḥ dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ audbhidam prathamam varṣam dvitīyam veṇumaṇḍalam tṛtīyam vai rathākāram caturtham pālanam smṛtam dhṛtimat pañcamam varṣam ṣaṣṭham varṣam prabhākaram saptamam kāpilam varṣam saptā ete varṣa puñjakāḥ eteṣu deva gandharvāḥ prajāḥ ca jagatīśvara avaśiṣṭeṣu varṣeṣu vakṣyāmi manuja īśvara yathāśrutam mahā rāja tat avyagra manāḥ śṛṇu krauñcadvīpe mahā rāja krauñcaḥ nāma mahā giriḥ krauñcāt paraḥ vāmanakaḥ vāmanāt andhakārakaḥ paraḥ tu dviguṇaḥ teṣām viṣkambhaḥ vaṃśa vardhana deśān tatra pravakṣyāmi tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu manonugāt paraḥ ca uṣṇaḥ deśaḥ kuru kula udvaha uṣṇāt paraḥ prāvarakaḥ prāvarāt andhakārakaḥ andhakāraka deśāt tu munideśaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ gaura prāyaḥ janādhipa ete deśāḥ mahā rāja deva gandharva sevitāḥ tam paryupāsate nityam devāḥ sarve mahā ṛṣibhiḥ vāgbhiḥ manonukūlābhiḥ pūjayantaḥ janādhipa dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānām kuru nandana ārogya āyus pramāṇābhyām dviguṇam dviguṇam tatas uktāḥ janapadāḥ yeṣu dharmaḥ ca ekaḥ pradṛśyate īśvaraḥ daṇḍam udyamya svayam eva prajāpatiḥ dvīpān etān mahā rāja rakṣan tiṣṭhati nityadā sa rājā sa śivaḥ rājan sa pitā sa pitāmahaḥ gopāyati nara śreṣṭha prajāḥ sa jaḍa paṇḍitāḥ tatas param samā nāma dṛśyate loka saṃsthitiḥ caturaśrāḥ mahā rāja trayaḥ triṃśat tu maṇḍalam diggajāḥ bharata śreṣṭha vāmana airāvata ādayaḥ tasya aham parimāṇam tu na saṃkhyātum iha utsahe asaṃbādhāḥ mahā rāja tān nigṛhṇanti te gajāḥ puṣkaraiḥ padma saṃkāśaiḥ varṣmavadbhiḥ mahā prabhaiḥ te śanais punar eva āśu vāyūn muñcanti nityaśas āgacchanti mahā rāja tatas tiṣṭhanti vai prajāḥ uvāca darśitam dvīpa saṃsthānam uttaram brūhi saṃjaya uvāca uktāḥ dvīpāḥ mahā rāja grahān mama śṛṇu tattvāt svarbhānuḥ kaurava śreṣṭha yāvat eṣa prabhāvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ mahā rāja svarbhānuḥ śrūyate grahaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi viṣkambhaḥ dvādaśa asya vai pariṇāhena ṣaṭtriṃśat vipula tvena ca anagha ṣaṣṭim āhuḥ śatāni asya budhāḥ paurāṇikāḥ tathā candramāḥ tu sahasrāṇi rājan ekādaśa smṛtaḥ viṣkambheṇa kuruśreṣṭha trayastriṃśat tu maṇḍalam ekonaṣaṣṭiḥ vaipulyāt śītaraśmeḥ mahātmanaḥ viṣkambheṇa tatas rājan maṇḍalam triṃśatam samam aṣṭapañcāśatam rājan vipula tvena ca anagha śrūyate parama udāraḥ pataṃgaḥ asau vibhāvasuḥ sa rāhuḥ chādayati etau yathākālam mahā tayā candra ādityau mahā rāja saṃkṣepaḥ ayam udāhṛtaḥ iti etat te mahā rāja pṛcchataḥ śāstra cakṣuṣā yathādṛṣṭam mayā proktam sa niryāṇam idam jagat śrīmān bhavati rājanyaḥ siddhārthaḥ sādhu saṃmataḥ yaḥ śṛṇoti mahīpāla parvaṇi idam yata vrataḥ idam tu bhāratam varṣam yatra vartāmahe vayam pūrvam pravartate puṇyam tat sarvam śrutavān asi uvāca vacanāt dhṛtarāṣṭrasya kurukṣetram jagāma ha vyāsasya vara dānena tvaramāṇaḥ tu saṃjayaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu samare rājan kṣaṇena eva samāgataḥ atha gāvalgaṇiḥ dhīmān samarāt etya saṃjayaḥ dhyāyate dhṛtarāṣṭrāya sahasā upetya duḥkhitaḥ ācaṣṭa nihatam bhīṣmam bharatānām amadhyamam hataḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ bharatānām pitāmahaḥ kakudam sarva yodhānām dhāma sarva dhanuṣmatām yasya vīryam samāśritya dyūtam putraḥ te akarot sa śete nihataḥ rājan saṃkhye bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā yaḥ sarvān pṛthivīpālān samavetān mahā mṛdhe jigāya eka rathena eva kāśi puryām mahā rathaḥ jāmadagnyam raṇe rāmam āyodhya vasu saṃbhavaḥ samudraḥ iva gāmbhīrye sahiṣṇu tve dharā samaḥ śara daṃṣṭraḥ dhanuḥ vaktraḥ khaḍga jihvaḥ durāsadaḥ nara siṃhaḥ pitā te adya pāñcālyena nipātitaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahat sainyam yam dṛṣṭvā udyantam āhave pravepata bhaya udvignam siṃham dṛṣṭvā iva go gaṇaḥ parirakṣya sa senām te daśa rātram anīka hā jagāma astam iva ādityaḥ kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram yaḥ sa śakraḥ iva akṣobhyaḥ varṣan bāṇān sahasraśas sa śete niṣṭanan bhūmau vāta rugṇaḥ iva drumaḥ uvāca katham kurūṇām ṛṣabhaḥ hataḥ bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā katham āsan ca mama putrāḥ hīnāḥ bhīṣmeṇa saṃjaya ārtiḥ parā mā āviśati yatas śaṃsasi me hatam kurūṇām ṛṣabham vīram akampyam puruṣa ṛṣabham ke tam yāntam anupreyuḥ ke ca asya āsan purogamāḥ ke śūrāḥ ratha śārdūlam acyutam kṣatriya ṛṣabham ratha anīkam gāhamānam sahasā pṛṣṭhatas anvayuḥ akarot duṣkaram karma raṇe kaurava śāsanāt kṛtinam tam durādharṣam samyak yāsyantam antike katham śāṃtanavam yuddhe pāṇḍavāḥ pratyavārayan nikṛntantam anīkāni śara daṃṣṭram tarasviṇam cāpa vyātta ānanam ghoram asi jihvam durāsadam pātayām āsa kaunteyaḥ katham tam ajitam yudhi pareṣām uttamāṅgāni pracinvantam śita iṣubhiḥ pāṇḍavānām mahat sainyam yam dṛṣṭvā udyantam āhave kālāgnim iva durdharṣam samaveṣṭata nityaśas parikṛṣya sa senām me daśa rātram anīka hā jagāma astam iva ādityaḥ kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram yaḥ sa śakraḥ iva akṣayyam varṣam śara mayam sṛjan sa śete niṣṭanan bhūmau vāta rugṇaḥ iva drumaḥ katham śāṃtanavam dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām anīkinī katham bhīṣmeṇa saṃgrāmam akurvan pāṇḍu nandanāḥ katham ca na ajayat bhīṣmaḥ droṇe jīvati saṃjaya bhīṣmaḥ praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ katham sa nidhanam gataḥ katham ca atirathaḥ tena pāñcālyena śikhaṇḍinā tam hatam samare bhīṣmam mahā ratha bala ucitam saṃjaya ācakṣva me vīram yena śarma na vidmahe māmakāḥ ke mahā iṣvāsāḥ na ajahuḥ saṃjaya acyutam duryodhana samādiṣṭāḥ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan yat śikhaṇḍi mukhāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ bhīṣmam abhyayus maurvī ghoṣa stanayitnuḥ pṛṣatka pṛṣataḥ mahān yat abhyavarṣat kaunteyān sa pāñcālān sa sṛñjayān iṣu astra sāgaram ghoram bāṇa grāham durāsadam gadā asi makara āvartam haya grāham gaja ākulam hayān gajān padātān ca rathān ca tarasā bahūn velā iva makarāvāsam ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram bhīṣmasya amita tejasaḥ pṛṣṭhatas ke parān vīrāḥ upāsedhan yata vratāḥ ke arakṣan uttaram cakram vīrāḥ vīrasya yudhyataḥ vāme cakre vartamānāḥ ke aghnan saṃjaya sṛñjayān rakṣyamāṇaḥ katham vīraiḥ gopyamānāḥ ca tena tad durjayānām anīkāni na ajayan tarasā yudhi katham prahartum api te śekuḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavāḥ tam nimagnam nara vyāghram bhīṣmam śaṃsasi saṃjaya na pāṇḍavān agaṇayat katham sa nihataḥ paraiḥ yaḥ purā vibudhaiḥ sa indraiḥ sāhāyye yuddha durmadaḥ kāṅkṣitaḥ dānavān ghnadbhiḥ pitā mama mahā vrataḥ yasmin jāte mahā vīrye śaṃtanuḥ loka śaṃkare śokam duḥkham ca dainyam ca prājahāt putra lakṣmaṇi prajñā parāyaṇam tad jñam saddharma niratam śucim veda vedāṅga tattva jñam katham śaṃsasi me hatam sarva astra vinaya upetam dāntam śāntam manasvinam hatam śāṃtanavam śrutvā manye śeṣam balam hatam yatra vṛddham gurum hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ jāmadagnyaḥ purā rāmaḥ sarva astra vid anuttamaḥ ambā artham udyataḥ saṃkhye bhīṣmeṇa yudhi nirjitaḥ hatam śaṃsasi bhīṣmam me kim nu duḥkham atas param asakṛt kṣatriya vrātāḥ saṃkhye yena vinirjitāḥ jāmadagnyaḥ tathā rāmaḥ para vīra nighātinā na hataḥ yaḥ mahā buddhiḥ sa hataḥ adya śikhaṇḍinā tasmāt nūnam mahā vīryāt bhārgavāt yuddha durmadāt tejaḥ vīrya balaiḥ bhūyāḥ śikhaṇḍī drupada ātmajaḥ yaḥ śūram kṛtinam yuddhe sarva śāstra viśāradam śaṃsa me tat yathā vṛttam yuddham bhīṣmasya pāṇḍavaiḥ ghātayitvā mahā vīryam pitaram loka dhārmikam agādhe salile magnām nāvam dṛṣṭvā iva pāragāḥ bhīṣme hate bhṛśam duḥkhāt manye śocanti putrakāḥ adri sāra mayam nūnam su dṛḍham hṛdayam mama yat śrutvā puruṣa vyāghram hatam bhīṣmam na dīryate na ca astreṇa na śauryeṇa tapasā medhayā na ca na dhṛtyā na punar tyāgāt mṛtyoḥ kaḥ cit vimucyate kālaḥ nūnam mahā vīryaḥ sarva loka duratyayaḥ yatra śāṃtanavam bhīṣmam hatam śaṃsasi saṃjaya āśaṃse aham purā trāṇam bhīṣmāt śaṃtanu nandanāt duryodhanaḥ śāṃtanavam kim tadā pratyapadyata na aham sveṣām pareṣām vā buddhyā saṃjaya cintayan śeṣam kim cit prapaśyāmi pratyanīke mahīkṣitām dāruṇaḥ kṣatra dharmaḥ ayam ṛṣibhiḥ saṃpradarśitaḥ yatra śāṃtanavam hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ vayam vā rājyam icchāmaḥ ghātayitvā pitāmaham kṣatra dharme sthitāḥ pārthāḥ na aparādhyanti putrakāḥ etat āryeṇa kartavyam kṛcchrāsu āpatsu saṃjaya parākramaḥ param śaktyā tat ca tasmin pratiṣṭhitam katham śāṃtanavam tāta pāṇḍu putrāḥ nyapātayan katham yuktāni anīkāni katham yuddham mahātmabhiḥ katham vā nihataḥ bhīṣmaḥ pitā saṃjaya mama paraiḥ duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca kitavaḥ hate bhīṣme kim abruvan yat śarīraiḥ upastīrṇām nara vāraṇa vājinām śara śakti gadā khaḍga tomara akṣām bhaya āvahām prāviśan kitavāḥ mandāḥ sabhām yudhi durāsadām prāṇa dyūte pratibhaye ke adīvyanta nara ṛṣabhāḥ ke ajayan ke jitāḥ tatra hṛta lakṣāḥ nipātitāḥ anye bhīṣmāt śāṃtanavāt tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya pitaram bhīma karmāṇam śrutvā mama duḥkham āviśat ārtim me hṛdaye rūḍhām mahatīm putra kāritām tam vimagnam nara vyāghram bhīṣmam śaṃsasi saṃjaya dṛṣṭvā vinihatam bhīṣmam manye śocanti putrakāḥ śroṣyāmi tāni duḥkhāni duryodhana kṛtāni aham saṃgrāme pṛthivīśānām mandasya a buddhi sambhavam apanītam su nītam vā tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya yat kṛtam tatra bhīṣmeṇa saṃgrāme jayam icchatā tejaḥ yuktam kṛtāstreṇa śaṃsa tat ca api aśeṣatas uvāca yaḥ ātmanaḥ duścaritāt aśubham prāpnuyāt naraḥ enasā tena na anyam saḥ upāśaṅkitum arhati mahā rāja manuṣyeṣu nindyam yaḥ sarvam ācaret nikāraḥ nikṛti prajñaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ tvad pratīkṣayā anubhūtaḥ saha amātyaiḥ kṣāntam ca su ciram vane hayānām ca gajānām ca śūrāṇām ca amita ojasām pratyakṣam yat mayā dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭam yoga balena ca śṛṇu tat pṛthivīpāla mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ diṣṭam etat purā nūnam evaṃbhāvi narādhipa namaskṛtvā pituḥ te aham pārāśaryāya dhīmate yasya prasādāt divyam me prāptam jñānam anuttamam dṛṣṭiḥ ca atīndriyā rājan dūrāt śravaṇam eva ca vyutthita utpatti vijñānam ākāśe ca gatiḥ sadā śastraiḥ asaṅgaḥ yuddheṣu vara dānāt mahātmanaḥ śṛṇu me vistareṇa idam vicitram parama adbhutam bhāratānām mahat yuddham yathā abhūt loma harṣaṇam teṣu anīkeṣu yat teṣu vyūḍheṣu ca vidhānāt duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja duḥśāsanam atha abravīt duḥśāsana rathāḥ tūrṇam yujyantām bhīṣma rakṣiṇaḥ anīkāni ca sarvāṇi śīghram tvam anucodaya ayam mā samanuprāptaḥ varṣa pūga abhicintitaḥ pāṇḍavānām sa sainyānām kurūṇām ca samāgamaḥ na atas kāryatamam manye raṇe bhīṣmasya rakṣaṇāt hanyāt guptaḥ hi asau pārthān somakān ca sa sṛñjayān abravīt ca viśuddha ātmā na aham hanyām śikhaṇḍinam śrūyate strī hi asau pūrvam tasmāt varjyaḥ raṇe mama tasmāt bhīṣmaḥ rakṣitavyaḥ viśeṣeṇa iti mama matiḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ vadhe yattāḥ sarve tiṣṭhantu māmakāḥ tathā prācyāḥ pratīcyāḥ ca dākṣiṇātya uttarāpathāḥ arakṣyamāṇam hi vṛkaḥ hanyāt siṃham mahā balam mā siṃham jambukena iva ghātayāmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā vāmam cakram yudhāmanyuḥ uttamaujāḥ ca dakṣiṇam saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena bhīṣmeṇa ca vivarjitaḥ yathā na hanyāt gāṅgeyam duḥśāsana tathā kuru tatas rajanyām vyuṣṭāyām śabdaḥ samabhavat mahān krośatām bhūmipālānām yujyatām yujyatām iti śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca bhārata gajānām bṛṃhatām ca eva yodhānām ca abhigarjatām kṣveḍita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭaiḥ tumulam sarvatas abhavat udatiṣṭhat mahā rāja sarvam yuktam aśeṣatas sūrya udaye mahat sainyam kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ tava rāja indra putrāṇām pāṇḍavānām tathā eva ca duṣpradhṛṣyāṇi ca astrāṇi sa śastra kavacāni ca tatas prakāśe sainyāni samadṛśyanta bhārata tvadīyānām pareṣām ca śastravanti mahānti ca tatra nāgāḥ rathāḥ ca eva jāmbūnada pariṣkṛtāḥ vibhrājamānāḥ dṛśyante meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ saṃnāhāḥ samadṛśyanta sveṣu anīkeṣu avasthitāḥ ratha anīkāni adṛśyanta nagarāṇi iva bhūriśas atīva śuśubhe tatra pitā te pūrṇa candra vat dhanurbhiḥ ṛṣṭibhiḥ khaḍgaiḥ gadābhiḥ śakti tomaraiḥ yodhāḥ praharaṇaiḥ śubhraiḥ sveṣu anīkeṣu avasthitāḥ gajāḥ rathāḥ padātāḥ ca turagāḥ ca viśām pate vyatiṣṭhan vāgurā ākārāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas dhvajāḥ bahuvidha ākārāḥ vyadṛśyanta samucchritāḥ svānām ca eva pareṣām ca dyutimantaḥ sahasraśas kāñcanāḥ maṇi citra aṅgāḥ jvalantaḥ iva pāvakāḥ arciṣmantaḥ vyarocanta dhvajāḥ rājñām sahasraśas saṃnaddhāḥ teṣu te vīrāḥ dadṛśuḥ yuddha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ udyataiḥ āyudhaiḥ citrāḥ tala baddhāḥ kalāpinaḥ ṛṣabha akṣāḥ manuṣya indrāḥ camū mukha gatāḥ babhuḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ śrutāyudhaḥ ca kāliṅgaḥ jayatsenaḥ ca pārthivaḥ bṛhadbalaḥ ca kauśalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ daśā ete puruṣa vyāghrāḥ śūrāḥ parigha bāhavaḥ akṣauhiṇīnām patayaḥ yajvānaḥ bhūri dakṣiṇāḥ rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca nītimantaḥ mahā balāḥ saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta sveṣu anīkeṣu avasthitāḥ baddha kṛṣṇājināḥ sarve dhvajinaḥ muñja mālinaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ duryodhanasya arthe brahma lokāya dīkṣitāḥ samṛddhāḥ daśa vāhinyaḥ parigṛhya vyavasthitāḥ ekādaśī dhārtarāṣṭrī kauravāṇām mahā camūḥ agratas sarva sainyānām yatra śāṃtanavaḥ agraṇī śveta uṣṇīṣam śveta hayam śveta varmāṇam acyutam apaśyāma mahā rāja bhīṣmam candram iva uditam śveta abhre iva tīkṣṇāṃśum dadṛśuḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ dṛṣṭvā camū mukhe bhīṣmam samakampanta pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ jṛmbhamāṇam mahā siṃham dṛṣṭvā kṣudra mṛgāḥ yathā ekādaśā etāḥ śrī juṣṭāḥ vāhinyaḥ te bhārata pāṇḍavānām tathā sapta mahā puruṣa pālitāḥ na eva naḥ tādṛśaḥ rājan dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ na ca śrutaḥ anīkānām sametānām samavāyaḥ tathāvidhaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ubhayayoḥ senayoḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā ca kuru pāṇḍavān uvāca yathā sa bhagavān vyāsa kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ abravīt dīpyamānāḥ ca saṃpetuḥ divi sapta mahā grahāḥ jvalatyā śikhayā bhūyas bhānumant uditaḥ divi vavāśire ca dīptāyām diśi gomāyu vāyasāḥ lipsamānāḥ śarīrāṇi māṃsa śoṇita bhojanāḥ ahani ahani pārthānām vṛddhaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ jayaḥ astu pāṇḍu putrāṇām iti ūcatuḥ ariṃdamau yuyudhāte tava arthāya yathā sa samayaḥ kṛtaḥ samānīya mahīpālān idam vacanam abravīt idam vaḥ kṣatriyāḥ dvāram svargāya apāvṛtam mahat eṣa vaḥ śāśvataḥ panthāḥ pūrvaiḥ pūrvataraiḥ gataḥ nābhāgaḥ hi yayātiḥ ca māndhātā nahuṣaḥ nṛgaḥ saṃsiddhāḥ paramam sthānam gatāḥ karmabhiḥ īdṛśaiḥ adharmaḥ kṣatriyasya eṣa yat vyādhi maraṇam gṛhe evam uktāḥ mahīpālāḥ bhīṣmeṇa bharata ṛṣabha sa tu vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ sa amātyaḥ saha bandhubhiḥ nyāsitaḥ samare śastram bhīṣmeṇa bharata ṛṣabha apeta karṇāḥ putrāḥ te rājānaḥ ca eva tāvakāḥ niryayuḥ siṃhanādena nādayantaḥ diśaḥ daśa śvetaiḥ chatraiḥ patākābhiḥ dhvaja vāraṇa vājibhiḥ bherī paṇava śabdaiḥ ca paṭahānām ca nisvanaiḥ ratha nemi ninādaiḥ ca babhūva ākulitā mahī kāñcana aṅgada keyūraiḥ kārmukaiḥ ca mahā rathāḥ bhrājamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta jaṅgamāḥ parvatāḥ iva tālena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ pañca tāreṇa ketunā vimala āditya saṃkāśaḥ tasthau kuru camūpatiḥ ye tvadīyāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ rājānaḥ bharata ṛṣabha putrāḥ ca tava rāja indra sa ārohā sa rathā gajaiḥ avartanta yathādeśam rājñ śāṃtanavasya te sa tu govāsanaḥ śaibyaḥ sahitaḥ sarva rājabhiḥ yayau mātaṃga rājena rāja arheṇa patākinā padma varṇaḥ tu anīkānām sarveṣām agratas sthitaḥ aśvatthāmā yayau yattaḥ siṃha lāṅgūla ketanaḥ śrutāyuḥ citrasenaḥ ca purumitraḥ viviṃśatiḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ ca eva vikarṇaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ ete sapta mahā iṣvāsāḥ droṇaputra purogamāḥ syandanaiḥ vara varṇa ābhaiḥ bhīṣmasya āsan puraḥsarāḥ bhrājamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta jāmbūnada mayāḥ dhvajāḥ jāmbūnada mayī vediḥ kamaṇḍalu vibhūṣitā tasya paurava kāliṅgau kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ syandanena mahārheṇa ketunā vṛṣabheṇa ca tat aṅga patinā guptam kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā śārada abhra caya prakhyam prācyānām abhavat balam anīka pramukhe tiṣṭhan varāheṇa mahā yaśāḥ śatam ratha sahasrāṇām tasya āsan vaśavartinaḥ aṣṭau nāga sahasrāṇi sādinām ayutāni ṣaḍ ṣaṣṭyā ratha sahasraiḥ tu nāgānām ayutena ca patiḥ sarva kaliṅgānām yayau ketumantā saha tasya parvata saṃkāśāḥ vyarocanta mahā gajāḥ yantra tomara tūṇīraiḥ patākābhiḥ ca śobhitāḥ ketumant api mātaṅgam vicitra parama aṅkuśam tejasā dīpyamānaḥ tu vāraṇa uttamam āsthitaḥ sa ratha anīkavān vyūhaḥ hasti aṅga uttama śīrṣavān droṇena vihitaḥ rājan rājñā śāṃtanavena ca tathā eva ācārya putreṇa vāhlīkena kṛpeṇa ca uvāca tatas muhūrtāt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ hṛdaya kampanaḥ aśrūyata mahā rāja yodhānām prayuyutsatām śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣaiḥ vāraṇānām ca bṛṃhitaiḥ rathānām nemi ghoṣaiḥ ca dīryati iva vasuṃdharā hayānām heṣamāṇānām yodhānām tatra garjatām kṣaṇena kham diśaḥ ca eva śabdena āpūritam tadā putrāṇām te durdharṣa pāṇḍavānām tathā eva ca tatra nāgāḥ rathāḥ ca eva jāmbūnada vibhūṣitāḥ bhrājamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ dhvajāḥ bahuvidha ākārāḥ tāvakānām narādhipa kāñcana aṅgadinaḥ rejuḥ jvalitāḥ iva pāvakāḥ svānām ca eva pareṣām ca samadṛśyanta bhārata kāñcanaiḥ kavacaiḥ vīrāḥ jvalana arka sama prabhaiḥ saṃnaddhāḥ pratyadṛśyanta grahāḥ prajvalitāḥ iva kuru yodha varāḥ rājan vicitra āyudha kārmukāḥ ṛṣabha akṣāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ camū mukha gatāḥ babhuḥ pṛṣṭhagopāḥ tu bhīṣmasya putrāḥ te narādhipa duḥśāsanaḥ durviṣahaḥ durmukhaḥ duḥsahaḥ tathā viviṃśatiḥ citrasenaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ satyavrataḥ purumitraḥ jayaḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ rathāḥ viṃśati sāhasrāḥ tathā eṣām anuyāyinaḥ abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ śālvāḥ matsyāḥ tathā ambaṣṭhāḥ trigartāḥ kekayāḥ tathā sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcya udīcya mālavāḥ dvādaśā ete janapadāḥ sarve śūrāḥ tanutyajaḥ anīkam daśa sāhasram kuñjarāṇām tarasvinām rathānām cakra rakṣāḥ ca pāda rakṣāḥ ca dantinām abhūvan vāhinī madhye śatānām ayutāni ṣaḍ pādātāḥ ca agratas agacchan dhanuḥ carma asi pāṇayaḥ adṛśyanta mahā rāja gaṅgā iva yamunā antare uvāca akṣauhiṇyaḥ daśa ekām ca vyūḍhām dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yaḥ veda mānuṣam vyūham daivam gāndharvam āsuram katham bhīṣmam sa kaunteyaḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavaḥ uvāca dhārtarāṣṭrāṇi anīkāni dṛṣṭvā vyūḍhāni pāṇḍavaḥ saṃhatān yodhayet alpān kāmam vistārayet bahūn sūcīmukham anīkam syāt alpānām bahubhiḥ saha asmākam ca tathā sainyam alpīyaḥ sutarām paraiḥ etat vacanam ājñāya mahā ṛṣeḥ vyūha pāṇḍava eṣa vyūhāmi te rājan vyūham parama durjayam acalam nāma vajra ākhyam vihitam vajrapāṇinā yaḥ sa vātaḥ iva uddhūtaḥ samare duḥsahaḥ paraiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ agratas yātu ripu sainyāni bhīṣayan tejāṃsi ripu sainyānām mṛdnan puruṣa sattamaḥ agre agraṇīḥ yāsyati naḥ yuddha upāya vicakṣaṇaḥ senā praṇetā yogyaḥ ayam devānām iva pāvakiḥ yam dṛṣṭvā pārthivāḥ sarve duryodhana purogamāḥ nivartiṣyanti saṃbhrāntāḥ siṃham kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva tam sarve saṃśrayiṣyāmaḥ prākāram akutobhayam bhīmam praharatām śreṣṭham vajrapāṇim iva amarāḥ draṣṭum ati ugra karmāṇam viṣaheta nara ṛṣabham bhīmasenaḥ gadām bibhrat vajra sāra mayīm dṛḍhām kekayāḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca cekitānaḥ ca vīryavān eta tiṣṭhanti sa amātyāḥ prekṣakāḥ te nareśvara bhīmasenam tadā rājñ darśayan sa mahā balam dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dāyādāḥ iti bībhatsuḥ abravīt bruvāṇam tu tathā pārtham sarva sainyāni māriṣa apūjayan tadā vāgbhiḥ anukūlābhiḥ āhave evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ tathā cakre dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃprayātān kurūn dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām mahā camūḥ gaṅgā iva pūrṇā stimitā syandamānā vyadṛśyata bhīmasenaḥ agraṇī teṣām dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca vīryavān samudyojya tatas paścāt rājā api akṣauhiṇī vṛtaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha putraiḥ ca saḥ abhyarakṣata pṛṣṭhatas draupadeyāḥ sa saubhadrāḥ pṛṣṭhagopāḥ tarasvinaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pāñcālyaḥ teṣām goptā mahā rathaḥ sahitaḥ pṛtanā śūraiḥ ratha mukhyaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ śikhaṇḍī tu tatas paścāt arjunena abhirakṣitaḥ pṛṣṭhagopaḥ arjunasya api yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ rājā tu madhyama anīke kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ akṣauhiṇyā ca pāñcālyaḥ yajñasenaḥ mahā manāḥ virāṭam anvayāt paścāt pāṇḍava arthe parākramī teṣām āditya candra ābhāḥ kanaka uttama bhūṣaṇāḥ nānā cihna dharāḥ rājan ratheṣu āsan mahā dhvajāḥ samutsarpya tatas paścāt dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ tvadīyānām pareṣām ca ratheṣu vividhān dhvajān śrūyate bhīma ninadaḥ nādayānaḥ diśaḥ daśa dṛṣṭvā ca bhīṣayām āsa virāvaiḥ vānara īśvaraḥ bhrū kṣepa utkṣepa vikṣepaiḥ lāṅgūlena punar kapiḥ ākāśe darśayām āsa pratiśabde mahā svanam pādātāḥ tu agratas agacchan asi śakti ṛṣṭi pāṇayaḥ aneka śata sāhasrāḥ bhīmasenasya rakṣiṇaḥ vāraṇāḥ daśa sāhasrāḥ prabhinna karaṭāmukhāḥ śūrāḥ hema mayaiḥ jālaiḥ dīpyamānāḥ iva acalāḥ sa ghaṇṭāḥ hema kakṣyābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ kṣarantaḥ iva jīmūtāḥ mada ārdrāḥ padma gandhinaḥ rājānam anvayuḥ paścāt calantaḥ iva parvatāḥ bhīmasenaḥ gadām bhīmām prakarṣan parigha upamām pracakarṣa mahat sainyam durādharṣaḥ mahā manāḥ na śekuḥ sarvatas yodhāḥ prativīkṣitum antike yam prativyūhya tiṣṭhanti pāṇḍavāḥ tava vāhinīm ajeyaḥ mānuṣe loke pāṇḍavaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ saṃdhyām tiṣṭhatsu sainyeṣu sūryasya udayanam prati prāvāt sa pṛṣataḥ vāyuḥ anabhre stanayitnumān viṣvak vātāḥ ca vānti ugrāḥ nīcais śarkara karṣiṇaḥ papāta mahatī ca ulkā prāc mukhī bharata ṛṣabha udyantam sūryam āhatya vyaśīryata mahā svanā niṣprabhaḥ abhyudiyāt sūryaḥ sa ghoṣaḥ bhūḥ cacāla ha nirghātāḥ bahavaḥ rājan dikṣu sarvāsu ca abhavan prādurāsīt rajaḥ tīvram na prājñāyata kim cana dhvajānām dhūyamānānām sahasā mātariśvanā kiṅkiṇī jāla naddhānām kāñcana sragvatām ravaiḥ mahatām sa patākānām āditya sama tejasām sarvam jhaṇajhaṇībhūtam āsīt tāla vaneṣu iva evam te puruṣa vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ yuddha nandinaḥ dṛṣṭvā agratas bhīmasenam gadā pāṇim avasthitam uvāca sūrya udaye saṃjaya ke nu pūrvam yuyutsavaḥ hṛṣyamāṇāḥ iva asan māmakāḥ vā bhīṣma netrāḥ samīke pāṇḍavāḥ vā bhīma netrāḥ tadānīm keṣām jaghanyau soma sūryau sa vāyū keṣām senām śvāpadāḥ vyābhaṣanta kānām yuvnām mukha varṇāḥ prasannāḥ sarvam hi etat brūhi tattvam yathāvat uvāca ubhe citre vana rāji prakāśe tathā eva ubhe nāga ratha aśva pūrṇe paścānmukhāḥ kuravaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sthitāḥ pārthāḥ prāc mukhāḥ yotsyamānāḥ daitya indra senā iva ca kauravāṇām deva indra senā iva ca pāṇḍavānām śukraḥ vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhatas pāṇḍavānām dhārtarāṣṭrān śvāpadāḥ vyābhaṣanta gaja indrāṇām mada gandhān ca tīvrān na sehire tava putrasya nāgāḥ samāsthitaḥ madhya gataḥ kurūṇām saṃstūyamānaḥ bandibhiḥ māgadhaiḥ ca tam sarvatas śakuniḥ pārvatīyaiḥ sārdham gāndhāraiḥ pāti gāndhāra rājaḥ bhīṣmaḥ agratas sarva sainyasya vṛddhaḥ śveta chatraḥ śveta dhanūḥ sa śaṅkhaḥ śveta uṣṇīṣaḥ pāṇḍureṇa dhvajena śvetaiḥ aśvaiḥ śveta śaila prakāśaḥ tasya sainyam dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca sarve vāhlīkānām eka deśaḥ śalaḥ ca ye ca ambaṣṭhāḥ kṣatriyāḥ ye ca sindhau tathā sauvīrāḥ pañcanadāḥ ca śūrāḥ śoṇaiḥ hayaiḥ rukmarathaḥ mahātmā droṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ adīna sattvaḥ āste guruḥ sarva rājñām paścāt camūm indraḥ iva abhirakṣan śālvāḥ matsyāḥ kekayāḥ ca api sarve gaja anīkaiḥ bhrātaraḥ yotsyamānāḥ śāradvataḥ ca uttaradhūḥ mahātmā mahā iṣvāsaḥ gautamaḥ citra yodhī mahā rathaiḥ andhaka vṛṣṇi bhojaiḥ saurāṣṭrakaiḥ nairṛtaiḥ ātta śastraiḥ bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā abhigup balam tvadīyam dakṣiṇatas abhipāti saṃśaptakānām ayutam rathānām mṛtyuḥ jayaḥ vā arjunasya iti sṛṣṭāḥ yena arjunaḥ tena rājan kṛtāstrāḥ prayātāḥ vai te trigartāḥ ca śūrāḥ sāgram śata sahasram tu nāgānām te bhārata nāge nāge ratha śatam śatam ca aśvāḥ rathe rathe aśve aśve daśa dhānuṣkāḥ dhānuṣke daśa carmiṇaḥ evam vyūḍhāni anīkāni bhīṣmeṇa te bhārata avyūhat mānuṣam vyūham daivam gāndharvam āsuram divase divase prāpte bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ agraṇī bhīṣmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām vyūhaḥ pratyak mukhaḥ yudhi ananta rūpā dhvajinī tvadīyā narendra bhīmā na tu pāṇḍavānām tām tu eva manye bṛhatīm duṣpradhṛṣyām yasyāḥ netārau keśavaḥ ca arjunaḥ ca uvāca bṛhatīm dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām dṛṣṭvā senām samudyatām viṣādam agamat rājā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vyūham bhīṣmeṇa ca abhedyam kalpitam prekṣya pāṇḍavaḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā bāho yeṣām yoddhā pitāmahaḥ akṣobhyaḥ ayam abhedyaḥ ca bhīṣmeṇa amitra karśinā kalpitaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭena vidhinā bhūri tejasā te vayam saṃśayam prāptāḥ sa sainyāḥ śatru karśana katham asmāt mahā vyūhāt udyānam naḥ bhaviṣyati atha arjunaḥ abravīt pārtham yudhiṣṭhiram amitra hā viṣaṇṇam abhisaṃprekṣya te rājan anīkinīm prajñayā abhyadhikān śūrān guṇa yuktān bahūn api tat tu te kāraṇam rājan pravakṣyāmi anasūyave nāradaḥ tam ṛṣiḥ veda bhīṣma droṇau ca pāṇḍava pitāmahaḥ kila purā mahā indra ādīn divaukasaḥ na tathā bala vīryābhyām vijayante jigīṣavaḥ yathā satya ānṛśaṃsyābhyām dharmeṇa eva udyamena ca tyaktvā adharmam ca lobham ca moham ca udyamam āsthitāḥ evam rājan vijānīhi dhruvaḥ naḥ raṇe jayaḥ yathā me nāradaḥ prāha yatas kṛṣṇaḥ tatas jayaḥ yatra kṛṣṇaḥ ca veda ātmā sarva sarva īśvaraḥ hariḥ jayaḥ tatra mahā bāho yathā me prāha nāradaḥ guṇa bhūtaḥ jayaḥ kṛṣṇe pṛṣṭhatas anveti mādhavam anyathā vijayaḥ ca asya saṃnatiḥ ca aparaḥ guṇaḥ ananta tejāḥ govindaḥ śatru pūgeṣu nirvyathaḥ puruṣaḥ sanātanatamaḥ yatas kṛṣṇaḥ tatas jayaḥ purā hi eṣa hariḥ bhūtvā vaikuṇṭhaḥ akuṇṭha sāyakaḥ tad prasādāt hi trailokyam prāptam śakra ādibhiḥ suraiḥ tasya te na vyathām kām cit iha paśyāmi bhārata yasya te jayam āśāste viśvabhuj tridaśeśvaraḥ uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā svām senām samacodayat yathā uddiṣṭāni anīkāni pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ madhye śikhaṇḍinaḥ anīkam rakṣitam savyasācinā bhīmasena mukham sainyam dhṛṣṭadyumnena pālitam bhīmasena ādibhiḥ yasya pṛtanā dikṣu pālitā anīkam dakṣiṇam rājan yuyudhānena pālitam śrīmatā sātvata agryeṇa śakreṇa iva dhanuṣmatā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kāñcana bhāṇḍa yoktram samāsthitaḥ nāga kulasya madhye samucchritam dānta śalākam asya su pāṇḍuram chatram atīva bhāti purohitāḥ śatru vadham vadantaḥ mahā ṛṣi vṛddhāḥ śrutavantaḥ eva yudhiṣṭhiram parivavruḥ sametāḥ tatas sa vastrāṇi tathā eva gāḥ ca phalāni puṣpāṇi tathā eva niṣkān kuru uttamaḥ brāhmaṇasāt mahātmā kurvan yayau śakraḥ iva amarebhyaḥ sahasra sūryaḥ śata kiṅkiṇīkaḥ parārdhya jāmbūnada hema citraḥ tam āsthitaḥ keśava saṃgṛhītam kapi dhvajam gāṇḍiva bāṇa hastaḥ anāyudhaḥ yaḥ su bhujaḥ bhujābhyām nara aśva nāgān yudhi bhasma kuryāt sa bhīmasenaḥ sahitaḥ yamābhyām vṛkodaraḥ vīra rathasya goptā samīkṣya senā agra gatam durāsadam pravivyathuḥ paṅka gatāḥ iva uṣṭrāḥ vṛkodaram vāraṇa rāja darpam yodhāḥ tvadīyāḥ bhaya vigna sattvāḥ viṣaṇṇa rūpāḥ kuru sainya mukhyā babhūvire śuṣka kaṇṭhāḥ virūpāḥ anīka madhye tiṣṭhantam rāja putram durāsadam abravīt bharata śreṣṭham guḍākeśam janārdanaḥ uvāca saḥ eṣa bhīṣmaḥ kuru vaṃśa ketuḥ yena āhṛtāḥ triṃśataḥ vāji medhāḥ etāni anīkāni mahā anubhāvam gūhanti meghāḥ iva gharmaraśmim etāni hatvā puruṣa pravīra kāṅkṣasva yuddham bharata ṛṣabheṇa uvāca dhārtarāṣṭra balam dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya samupasthitam śrī bhagavant uvāca arjunasya hita arthāya kṛṣṇaḥ vacanam abravīt śuciḥ bhūtvā mahā bāho saṃgrāma abhimukhe sthitaḥ parājayāya śatrūṇām durgā stotram udīraya uvāca avatīrya rathāt pārthaḥ stotram āha kṛtāñjaliḥ kumāri kāli kāpāli kapile kṛṣṇa piṅgale caṇḍi caṇḍe namaḥ te tāriṇi varavarṇini aṭṭa śūla praharaṇe khaḍga kheṭaka dhāriṇi mahiṣa asṛj priye nityam kauśiki pīta vāsini ume śākaṃbhari śvete kṛṣṇe kaiṭabhanāśini hiraṇyākṣi virūpākṣi su dhūmrākṣi namaḥ astu te jambūkaṭaka caityeṣu nityam saṃnihita ālaye tvam brahma vidyā vidyānām mahānidrā ca dehinām svāhākāraḥ svadhā ca eva kalā kāṣṭhā sarasvatī stutā asi tvam mahādevi viśuddhena antarātmanā kāntāra bhaya durgeṣu bhaktānām ca ālayeṣu ca tvam jambhanī mohinī ca māyā hrīḥ śrīḥ tathā eva ca saṃdhyā prabhāvatī ca eva sāvitrī jananī tathā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ dhṛtiḥ dīptiḥ candra āditya vivardhinī bhūtiḥ bhūtimatām saṃkhye vīkṣyase siddha cāraṇaiḥ uvāca tatas pārthasya vijñāya bhaktim mānava vatsalā su alpena eva tu kālena śatrūn jeṣyasi pāṇḍava naraḥ tvam asi durdharṣa nārāyaṇa sahāyavān ajeyaḥ tvam raṇe arīṇām api vajrabhṛtaḥ svayam iti evam uktvā vara dā kṣaṇena antaradhīyata kṛṣṇa arjunau eka rathau divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ yaḥ idam paṭhate stotram kalye utthāya mānavaḥ yakṣa rakṣaḥ piśācebhyaḥ na bhayam vidyate sadā na ca api ripavaḥ tebhyaḥ sarpa ādyāḥ ye ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ saṃgrāme vijayet nityam lakṣmīm prāpnoti kevalām ārogya bala saṃpannaḥ jīvet varṣa śatam tathā etat dṛṣṭam prasādāt tu mayā vyāsasya dhīmataḥ mohāt etau na jānanti nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ sarve manyu vaśa anugāḥ prāpta kālam idam vākyam kāla pāśena guṇṭhitāḥ dvaipāyanaḥ nāradaḥ ca kaṇvaḥ rāmaḥ tathā anaghaḥ avārayan tava sutam na ca asau tat gṛhītavān yatra dharmaḥ dyutiḥ kāntiḥ yatra hrīḥ śrīḥ tathā matiḥ yatas dharmaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ yatas kṛṣṇaḥ tatas jayaḥ uvāca keṣām prahṛṣṭāḥ tatra agre yodhāḥ yudhyanti saṃjaya māmakāḥ pāṇḍavānām vā tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya vācaḥ pradakṣiṇāḥ ca eva yodhānām abhigarjatām uvāca saṃhatānām anīkānām vyūḍhānām bharata ṛṣabha saṃsarpatām udīrṇānām vimardaḥ su mahān abhūt vāditra śabdaḥ tumulaḥ śaṅkha bherī vimiśritaḥ śūrāṇām raṇa śūrāṇām garjatām itaretaram anyonyam vīkṣyamāṇānām yodhānām bharata ṛṣabha kuñjarāṇām ca nadatām sainyānām ca prahṛṣyatām kṛṣṇam kamala pattra akṣam puṇya śravaṇa kīrtanam vāsudevam jagadyonim naumi nārāyaṇam harim uvāca māmakāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva kim akurvata saṃjaya śrī rāmacandrāya namaḥ śrī kṛṣṇāya namaḥ namaḥ idam śrī bhagavadgītā mālā mantrasya bhagavān vedavyāsa ṛṣiḥ chandaḥ śrī kṛṣṇa paramātmā devatā aśocyān anvaśocaḥ tvam prajñā vādān ca bhāṣase vraja 18.66ab tvām sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ kīlakam śrī kṛṣṇa prīti artham dharma artha kāma mokṣa arthe na enam dahati pāvakaḥ 2.23ab namaḥ na ca enam kledayanti āpaḥ na śoṣayati mārutaḥ iti tarjanībhyām namaḥ ayam adāhyaḥ ayam akledyaḥ aśoṣyaḥ eva ca iti madhyamābhyām namaḥ nityaḥ sarva gataḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ ayam sanātanaḥ iti anāmikābhyām namaḥ paśya mama pārtha rūpāṇi śataśas atha sahasraśas iti kaniṣṭhikābhyām namaḥ nānāvidhāni divyāni nānā varṇa ākṛtīni ca 11.5ad kara tala kara pṛṣṭhābhyām namaḥ karanyāsaḥ aṅganyāsaḥ na enam chindanti vauṣaṭ nānāvidhāni divyāni nānā varṇa ākṛtīni ca iti astrāya phaṭ aṅganyāsaḥ dhyānaṃ om pārthāya pratibodhitām bhagavantā nārāyaṇena svayam vyāsena grathitām purāṇa muninā madhye mahābhārate advaita amṛta varṣiṇīm bhagavatīm aṣṭādaśa adhyāyinīm om hṛdi vikasita padmam sūrya soma agni bimbam acala parama śāntam jyotiḥ ākāśa sāram tat bhavatu śubha daḥ me vāsudevaḥ pratiṣṭhaḥ pārthaḥ vatsaḥ sudhīḥ bhoktā dugdham gīta amṛtam mahat yena tvayā bhārata taila pūrṇaḥ prajvālitaḥ jñāna mayaḥ pradīpaḥ jñāna mudrāya kṛṣṇāya gīta amṛta duhe namaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍava anīkam vyūḍham duryodhanaḥ tadā ācāryam upasaṃgamya rājā vacanam abravīt paśya etām pāṇḍu putrāṇām ācārya mahatīm camūm vyūḍhām drupada putreṇa te śiṣyeṇa dhīmatā atra śūrāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ bhīma arjuna samāḥ yudhi yuyudhānaḥ virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ cekitānaḥ kāśi rājaḥ ca vīryavān yudhāmanyuḥ ca vikrāntaḥ uttamaujāḥ ca vīryavān naḥ tu viśiṣṭāḥ ye tān nibodha dvijottama nāyakāḥ mama sainyasya saṃjñā artham tān bravīmi te sainye mahati ye sarve netāraḥ śūra saṃmatāḥ bhavān bhīṣmaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca kṛpaḥ ca samitiṃjayaḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ mad arthe tyakta jīvitāḥ nānā śastra praharaṇāḥ sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ aparyāptam tat asmākam balam bhīṣma abhirakṣitam paryāptam tu idam eteṣām balam bhīma abhirakṣitam ayaneṣu ca sarveṣu yathābhāgam avasthitāḥ tasya saṃjanayan harṣam kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ siṃhanādam vinadya uccais śaṅkham dadhmau pratāpavān tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṇava ānaka gomukhāḥ mādhavaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca eva divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ pāñcajanyam hṛṣīkeśaḥ devadattam dhanaṃjayaḥ pauṇḍram dadhmau mahā śaṅkham bhīma karmā vṛkodaraḥ anantavijayam rājā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kāśyaḥ ca parama iṣvāsaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ virāṭaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca aparājitaḥ drupadaḥ draupadeyāḥ ca sarvaśas pṛthivīpate saubhadraḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak sa ghoṣaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām hṛdayāni vyadārayat atha vyavasthitān dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭrān kapidhvajaḥ pravṛtte śastra saṃpāte dhanuḥ udyamya pāṇḍavaḥ hṛṣīkeśam tadā vākyam idam āha mahīpate yāvat etān nirīkṣe aham yoddhu kāmān avasthitān yotsyamānān avekṣe aham ye ete atra samāgatāḥ evam uktaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ guḍākeśena bhārata bhīṣma droṇa pramukhatas sarveṣām ca mahīkṣitām uvāca pārtha paśya etān samavetān kurūn iti tatra apaśyat sthitān pārthaḥ pitṝn atha pitāmahān ācāryān mātulān bhrātṝn putrān pautrān sakhīn tathā tān samīkṣya sa kaunteyaḥ sarvān bandhūn avasthitān kṛpayā parayā āviṣṭaḥ viṣīdan idam abravīt dṛṣṭvā imān sva janān kṛṣṇa yuyutsūn samavasthitān sīdanti mama gātrāṇi mukham ca pariśuṣyati vepathuḥ ca śarīre me romaharṣaḥ ca jāyate gāṇḍīvam sraṃsate hastāt tvac ca eva paridahyate nimittāni ca paśyāmi viparītāni keśava na kāṅkṣe vijayam kṛṣṇa na ca rājyam sukhāni ca yeṣām arthe kāṅkṣitam naḥ rājyam bhogāḥ sukhāni ca te ime avasthitāḥ yuddhe prāṇān tyaktvā dhanāni ca ācāryāḥ pitaraḥ putrāḥ tathā eva ca pitāmahāḥ mātulāḥ śvaśurāḥ pautrāḥ syālāḥ saṃbandhinaḥ tathā nihatya dhārtarāṣṭrān naḥ kā prītiḥ syāt janārdana pāpam eva āśrayet asmān hatvā etān ātatāyinaḥ tasmāt na arhāḥ vayam hantum dhārtarāṣṭrān sa bāndhavān kula kṣaya kṛtam doṣam mitra drohe ca pātakam katham na jñeyam asmābhiḥ pāpāt asmāt nivartitum kula kṣaya kṛtam doṣam prapaśyadbhiḥ janārdana kula kṣaye praṇaśyanti kula dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ adharma abhibhavāt kṛṣṇa praduṣyanti kulastriyaḥ strīṣu duṣṭāsu vārṣṇeya jāyate varṇa saṃkaraḥ patanti pitaraḥ hi eṣām lupta piṇḍa udaka kriyāḥ doṣaiḥ etaiḥ kula ghnānām varṇa saṃkara kārakaiḥ utsādyante jāti dharmāḥ kula dharmāḥ ca śāśvatāḥ utsanna kula dharmāṇām manuṣyāṇām janārdana yadi mām apratīkāram aśastram śastra pāṇayaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ raṇe hanyuḥ tat me kṣemataram bhavet visṛjya sa śaram cāpam śoka saṃvigna mānasaḥ uvāca tam tathā kṛpayā āviṣṭam aśru pūrṇa ākula īkṣaṇam viṣīdantam idam vākyam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca katham bhīṣmam aham saṃkhye droṇam ca madhusūdana iṣubhiḥ pratiyotsyāmi pūjā arhau ari sūdana gurūn a hatvā hi mahā anubhāvān śreyaḥ bhoktum bhaikṣam api iha loke hatvā artha kāmān tu gurūn iha eva bhuñjīya bhogān rudhira pradigdhān yān eva hatvā na jijīviṣāmaḥ te avasthitāḥ pramukhe dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kārpaṇya doṣa upahata svabhāvaḥ pṛcchāmi tvām dharma saṃmūḍha cetāḥ yat śreyaḥ syāt niścitam brūhi tat me śiṣyaḥ te aham śādhi mām tvām prapannam na hi prapaśyāmi mama apanudyāt yat śokam ucchoṣaṇam indriyāṇām avāpya bhūmau asapatnam ṛddham rājyam surāṇām api ca ādhipatyam uvāca evam uktvā hṛṣīkeśam guḍākeśaḥ paraṃtapa na yotsye iti govindam uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva ha tam uvāca hṛṣīkeśaḥ prahasan iva bhārata śrī bhagavān uvāca a śocyān anvaśocaḥ tvam prajñā vādān ca bhāṣase gatāsūn agatāsūn ca na anuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ tvam mānuṣyeṇa upahata antarātmā viṣāda moha abhibhavāt visaṃjñaḥ kṛpā gṛhītaḥ samavekṣya bandhūn na tu eva aham jātu na āsam na tvam na ime janādhipāḥ mātrā sparśāḥ tu kaunteya śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkha dāḥ āgama apāyinaḥ anityāḥ tān titikṣasva bhārata antavantaḥ ime dehāḥ nityasya uktāḥ śarīriṇaḥ na jāyate mriyate vā kadā cit na ayam bhūtvā bhavitā vā na bhūyas ajaḥ nityaḥ śāśvataḥ ayam purāṇaḥ na hanyate hanyamāne śarīre vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni yathā vihāya navāni gṛhṇāti naraḥ aparāṇi tathā śarīrāṇi vihāya jīrṇāni anyāni saṃyāti navāni dehī na enam chindanti śastrāṇi na enam dahati pāvakaḥ na ca enam kledayanti āpaḥ na śoṣayati mārutaḥ nityaḥ sarva gataḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ ayam sanātanaḥ tathā api tvam mahā bāho na enam śocitum arhasi avyakta ādīni bhūtāni vyakta madhyāni bhārata āścarya vat ca enam anyaḥ śṛṇoti śrutvā api enam veda na ca eva kaḥ cit tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni na tvam śocitum arhasi sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pārtha labhante yuddham īdṛśam tatas svadharmam kīrtim ca hitvā pāpam avāpsyasi akīrtim ca api bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti te avyayām saṃbhāvitasya ca akīrtiḥ maraṇāt atiricyate bhayāt raṇāt uparatam maṃsyante tvām mahā rathāḥ yeṣām ca tvam bahu mataḥ bhūtvā yāsyasi lāghavam avācya vādān ca bahūn vadiṣyanti tava ahitāḥ hataḥ vā prāpsyasi svargam jitvā vā bhokṣyase mahīm tasmāt uttiṣṭha kaunteya yuddhāya kṛta niścayaḥ sukha duḥkhe same kṛtvā lābha alābhau jaya ajayau eṣā te abhihitā sāṃkhye buddhiḥ yoge tu imām śṛṇu bahu śākhāḥ hi anantāḥ ca buddhayaḥ avyavasāyinām yām imām puṣpitām vācam pravadanti a vipaścitaḥ veda vāda ratāḥ pārtha na anyat asti iti vādinaḥ kriyā viśeṣa bahulām bhoga aiśvarya gatim prati bhoga aiśvarya prasaktānām tayā apahṛta cetasām tāvān sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ karmaṇi eva adhikāraḥ te mā phaleṣu kadā cana yoga sthaḥ kuru karmāṇi saṅgam tyaktvā dhanaṃjaya buddhau śaraṇam anviccha kṛpaṇāḥ phala hetavaḥ karma jam buddhi yuktāḥ hi phalam tyaktvā manīṣiṇaḥ śruti vipratipannā te yadā sthāsyati niścalā sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā samādhi sthasya keśava sthita dhīḥ kim prabhāṣeta kim āsīta vrajeta kim śrī bhagavān uvāca prajahāti yadā kāmān sarvān pārtha manaḥ gatān ātmani eva ātmanā tuṣṭaḥ sthita prajñaḥ tadā ucyate duḥkheṣu anudvigna manāḥ sukheṣu vigata spṛhaḥ na abhinandati na dveṣṭi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā yadā saṃharate ca ayam kūrmaḥ aṅgāni iva sarvaśas indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā tāni sarvāṇi saṃyamya yuktaḥ āsīta mad paraḥ vaśe hi yasya indriyāṇi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā dhyāyataḥ viṣayān puṃsaḥ saṅgaḥ teṣu upajāyate saṅgāt saṃjāyate kāmaḥ kāmāt krodhaḥ abhijāyate krodhāt bhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohāt smṛti vibhramaḥ smṛti bhraṃśāt buddhi nāśaḥ buddhi nāśāt praṇaśyati prasāde sarva duḥkhānām hāniḥ asya upajāyate na ca abhāvayataḥ śāntiḥ aśāntasya kutas sukham indriyāṇām hi caratām yat manaḥ anuvidhīyate tat asya harati prajñām vāyuḥ nāvam iva ambhasi tasmāt yasya mahā bāho nigṛhītāni sarvaśas indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā yā niśā sarva bhūtānām tasyām jāgarti saṃyamī yasyām jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyataḥ muneḥ āpūryamāṇam acala pratiṣṭham samudram āpaḥ praviśanti yadvat tadvat kāmāḥ yam praviśanti sarve sa śāntim āpnoti na kāma kāmī vihāya kāmān yaḥ sarvān pumān carati niḥspṛhaḥ eṣā brāhmī sthitiḥ pārtha na enām prāpya vimuhyati vyāmiśreṇa eva vākyena buddhim mohayasi iva me śrī bhagavān uvāca loke asmin dvividhā niṣṭhā purā proktā mayā anagha jñāna yogena sāṃkhyānām karma yogena yoginām na karmaṇām anārambhāt naiṣkarmyam puruṣaḥ aśnute na hi kaḥ cit kṣaṇam api jātu tiṣṭhati a karma kṛt kāryate hi avaśaḥ karma sarvaḥ prakṛti jaiḥ guṇaiḥ indriya arthān vimūḍha ātmā mithyā ācāraḥ saḥ ucyate śarīra yātrā api ca te na prasidhyet akarmaṇaḥ saha yajñāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā purā uvāca prajāpatiḥ devān bhāvayata anena te devāḥ bhāvayantu vaḥ iṣṭān bhogān hi vaḥ devāḥ dāsyante yajña bhāvitāḥ yajña śiṣṭa āśinaḥ santaḥ mucyante sarva kilbiṣaiḥ bhuñjate te tu agham pāpāḥ ye pacanti ātma kāraṇāt evam pravartitam cakram na anuvartayati iha yaḥ aghāyuḥ indriya ārāmaḥ mogham pārtha sa jīvati yaḥ tu ātma ratiḥ eva syāt ātma tṛptaḥ ca mānavaḥ na ca asya sarva bhūteṣu kaḥ cit artha vyapāśrayaḥ tasmāt asaktaḥ satatam kāryam karma samācara mama vartma anuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśas saṃkarasya ca kartā syām upahanyām imāḥ prajāḥ saktāḥ karmaṇi a vidvāṃsaḥ yathā kurvanti bhārata kuryāt vidvān tathā asaktaḥ cikīrṣuḥ loka saṃgraham na buddhi bhedam janayet ajñānām karma saṅginām prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi sarvaśas ahaṃkāra vimūḍha ātmā kartāham iti manyate prakṛteḥ guṇa saṃmūḍhāḥ sajjante guṇa karmasu mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasya adhyātma cetasā ye me matam idam nityam anutiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ sarva jñāna vimūḍhān tān viddhi naṣṭān acetasaḥ sadṛśam ceṣṭate svasyāḥ prakṛteḥ jñānavān api prakṛtim yānti bhūtāni nigrahaḥ kim kariṣyati śreyān svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ para dharmāt su anuṣṭhitāt atha kena prayuktaḥ ayam pāpam carati pūruṣaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca mahā aśanaḥ mahā pāpmā viddhi enam iha vairiṇam śrī bhagavant uvāca kim ātmakaḥ kim ācāraḥ tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ eṣa sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śatruḥ dehinām indriyaiḥ saha ahaṃkāraḥ abhimāna ātmā dustaraḥ pāpa karmabhiḥ saḥ eṣa kaluṣaḥ kṣudraḥ chidra prekṣī dhanaṃjaya rajaḥ pravṛttaḥ moha ātmā manuṣyāṇām upadravaḥ āvṛtam jñānam etena jñāninaḥ nitya vairiṇā kāmarūpeṇa kaunteya duṣpūreṇa analena ca pāpmānam prajahihi enam jñāna vijñāna nāśanam indriyāṇi parāṇi āhuḥ indriyebhyaḥ param manaḥ evam buddheḥ param buddhvā saṃstabhya ātmānam ātmanā jahi śatrum mahā bāho kāmarūpam durāsadam śrī bhagavān uvāca evam paraṃparā prāptam imam rājarṣayaḥ viduḥ sa kālena iha mahatā yogaḥ naṣṭaḥ paraṃtapa saḥ eva ayam mayā te adya yogaḥ proktaḥ purātanaḥ katham etat vijānīyām tvam ādau proktavan iti śrī bhagavān uvāca ajaḥ api san avyaya ātmā bhūtānām īśvaraḥ api san prakṛtim svām adhiṣṭhāya saṃbhavāmi ātma māyayā paritrāṇāya sādhūnām vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām vīta rāga bhaya krodhāḥ mad mayāḥ mām upāśritāḥ bahavaḥ jñāna tapasā pūtāḥ mad bhāvam āgatāḥ mama vartma anuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśas kāṅkṣantaḥ karmaṇām siddhim yajantaḥ iha devatāḥ cāturvarṇyam mayā sṛṣṭam guṇa karma vibhāgaśaḥ na mām karmāṇi limpanti na me karma phale spṛhā evam jñātvā kṛtam karma pūrvaiḥ api mumukṣubhiḥ kuru karma eva tasmāt tvam pūrvaiḥ pūrvataram kṛtam tat te karma pravakṣyāmi yat jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt akarmaṇaḥ ca boddhavyam gahanā karmaṇaḥ gatiḥ yasya sarve samārambhāḥ kāma saṃkalpa varjitāḥ jñāna agni dagdha karmāṇam tam āhuḥ paṇḍitam budhāḥ tyaktvā karma phala āsaṅgam nitya tṛptaḥ nirāśrayaḥ śārīram kevalam karma kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam yadṛcchā lābha saṃtuṣṭaḥ dvaṃdva atītaḥ vimatsaraḥ yajñāya ācarataḥ karma samagram pravilīyate śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi anye saṃyama agniṣu juhvati śabda ādīn viṣayān anye indriya agniṣu juhvati sarvāṇi indriya karmāṇi prāṇa karmāṇi ca apare ātma saṃyama yoga agnau juhvati jñāna dīpite dravya yajñāḥ tapaḥ yajñāḥ yoga yajñāḥ tathā apare svādhyāya jñāna yajñāḥ ca yatayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ apāne juhvati prāṇam prāṇe apānam tathā apare prāṇa apāna gatī ruddhvā prāṇāyāma parāyaṇāḥ apare niyata āhārāḥ prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati sarve api ete yajña vidaḥ yajña kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ yajña śiṣṭa amṛta bhujaḥ yānti brahma sanātanam evam bahuvidhāḥ yajñāḥ vitatāḥ brahmaṇaḥ mukhe karma jān viddhi tān sarvān evam jñātvā vimokṣyase śreyāḥ dravya mayāt yajñāt jñāna yajñaḥ paraṃtapa sarvam karma akhilam pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate upadekṣyanti te jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśiṇaḥ yat jñātvā na punar moham evam yāsyasi pāṇḍava yena bhūtāni aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasi ātmani atha u mayi sarvam jñāna plavena eva vṛjinam saṃtariṣyasi jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā śraddhāvān labhate jñānam tad paraḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ jñānam labdhvā parām śāntim acireṇa adhigacchati ajñaḥ ca aśraddadhānaḥ ca saṃśaya ātmā vinaśyati na ayam lokaḥ asti na paraḥ na sukham saṃśaya ātmanaḥ yoga saṃnyasta karmāṇam jñāna saṃchinna saṃśayam tasmāt ajñāna saṃbhūtam hṛd stham jñāna asinā ātmanaḥ chittvā enam saṃśayam yogam ātiṣṭha uttiṣṭha bhārata saṃnyāsam karmaṇām kṛṣṇa punar yogam ca śaṃsasi śrī bhagavān uvāca saṃnyāsaḥ karmayogaḥ ca niḥśreyasa karau ubhau jñeyaḥ sa nitya saṃnyāsī yaḥ na dveṣṭi na kāṅkṣati sāṃkhya yogau pṛthak bālāḥ pravadanti na paṇḍitāḥ ekam sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati saṃnyāsaḥ tu mahā bāho duḥkham āptum ayogataḥ paśyan śṛṇvan spṛśan jighran aśnan gacchan svapan śvasan brahmaṇi ādhāya karmāṇi saṅgam tyaktvā karoti yaḥ yuktaḥ karma phalam tyaktvā śāntim āpnoti naiṣṭhikīm sarva karmāṇi manasā saṃnyasya āste sukham vaśī ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam tena muhyanti jantavaḥ jñānena tu tat ajñānam yeṣām nāśitam ātmanaḥ teṣām āditya vat jñānam prakāśayati tat param tad buddhayaḥ tad ātmānaḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ gacchanti apunarāvṛttim jñāna nirdhūta kalmaṣāḥ śuni ca eva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ sama darśinaḥ iha eva taiḥ jitaḥ sargaḥ yeṣām sāmye sthitam manaḥ nirdoṣam hi samam brahma tasmāt brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ śaknoti iha eva yaḥ soḍhum prāk śarīravimokṣaṇāt labhante brahma nirvāṇam ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ chinna dvaidhāḥ yata ātmānaḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ kāma krodha viyuktānām yatīnām yata cetasām sparśān kṛtvā bahis bāhyān cakṣuḥ ca eva antare bhruvoḥ prāṇa apānau samau kṛtvā nāsā abhyantara cāriṇaḥ suhṛdam sarva bhūtānām jñātvā mām śāntim ṛcchati śrī bhagavān uvāca anāśritaḥ karma phalam kāryam karma karoti yaḥ sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca na niragniḥ na ca akriyaḥ yam saṃnyāsam iti prāhuḥ yogam tam viddhi pāṇḍava yoga ārūḍhasya tasya eva śamaḥ kāraṇam ucyate sarva saṃkalpa saṃnyāsī yoga ārūḍhaḥ tadā ucyate uddharet ātmanā ātmānam na ātmānam avasādayet jita ātmanaḥ praśāntasya paramātmā samāhitaḥ śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkheṣu tathā māna avamānayoḥ jñāna vijñāna tṛpta ātmā kūṭasthaḥ vijita indriyaḥ yuktaḥ iti ucyate yogī sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ sādhuṣu api ca pāpeṣu sama buddhiḥ viśiṣyate yogī yuñjīta satatam ātmānam rahasi sthitaḥ ekākī yata citta ātmā nirāśīḥ aparigrahaḥ śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ na ati ucchritam na ati nīcam caila ajina kuśa uttaram upaviśya āsane yuñjyāt yogam ātma viśuddhaye samam kāya śiraḥ grīvam dhārayan acalam sthiraḥ saṃprekṣya nāsikā agram svam diśaḥ ca anavalokayān praśānta ātmā vigata bhīḥ brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ yuñjan evam sadā ātmānam yogī niyata mānasaḥ śāntim nirvāṇa paramām mad saṃsthām adhigacchati yadā viniyatam cittam ātmani eva avatiṣṭhate yathā dīpaḥ nivāta sthaḥ na iṅgate sā upamā smṛtā yatra ca eva ātmanā ātmānam paśyan ātmani tuṣyati yam labdhvā ca aparam lābham manyate na adhikam tatas tam vidyāt duḥkha saṃyoga viyogam yoga saṃjñitam saṃkalpa prabhavān kāmān tyaktvā sarvān aśeṣatas śanais śanais uparamet buddhyā dhṛti gṛhītayā ātma saṃstham manaḥ kṛtvā na kim cit api cintayet yuñjan evam sadā ātmānam yogī vigata kalmaṣaḥ sarva bhūta stham ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani īkṣate yoga yukta ātmā sarvatra sama darśanaḥ tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati sukham vā yadi vā duḥkham sa yogī paramaḥ mataḥ etasya aham na paśyāmi cañcala tvāt sthitim sthirām cañcalam hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavat dṛḍham śrī bhagavān uvāca asaṃśayam mahā bāho manaḥ durnigraham calam asaṃyata ātmanā yogaḥ duṣprāpaḥ iti me matiḥ vaśya ātmanā tu yatatā śakyaḥ avāptum upāyataḥ lipsamānaḥ satām mārgam pramūḍhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pathini a prāpya yoga saṃsiddhim kām gatim kṛṣṇa gacchati apratiṣṭhaḥ mahā bāho vimūḍhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pathi etat mama saṃśayam kṛṣṇa chettum arhasi aśeṣatas śrī bhagavān uvāca prāpya puṇya kṛtām lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ śucīnām śrīmatām gehe yoga bhraṣṭaḥ abhijāyate prayatnāt yatamānaḥ tu yogī saṃśuddha kilbiṣaḥ yoginām api sarveṣām mad gatena antarātmanā phalitāḥ śālayaḥ samyak vṛṣṭi mātre avalokite śrī bhagavān uvāca mayi āsakta manāḥ pārtha yogam yuñjan mad āśrayaḥ asaṃśayam samagram mām yathā jñāsyasi tat śṛṇu jñānam te aham sa vijñānam idam vakṣyāmi aśeṣatas yat jñātvā na iha bhūyas anyat jñātavyam avaśiṣyate manuṣyāṇām sahasreṣu kaḥ cit yatati siddhaye yatatām api siddhānām kaḥ cit mām vetti tattvāt ahaṃkāraḥ iti iyam me bhinnā prakṛtiḥ aṣṭadhā jīva bhūtām mahā bāho yayā idam dhāryate jagat etad yonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇi iti upadhāraya mayi sarvam idam protam sūtre maṇi gaṇāḥ iva praṇavaḥ sarva vedeṣu śabdaḥ khe pauruṣam nṛṣu puṇyaḥ gandhaḥ pṛthivyām ca tejaḥ ca asmi vibhāvasau jīvanam sarva bhūteṣu tapaḥ ca asmi tapasviṣu bījam mām sarva bhūtānām viddhi pārtha sanātanam balam balavatām ca aham kāma rāga vivarjitam ye ca eva sāttvikāḥ bhāvāḥ rājasāḥ tāmasāḥ ca ye mohitam na abhijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayam daivī hi eṣā guṇa mayī mama māyā duratyayā na mām duṣkṛtinaḥ mūḍhāḥ prapadyante nara adhamāḥ māyayā apahṛta jñānāḥ āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ caturvidhāḥ
