bhajante mām janāḥ sukṛtinaḥ arjuna ārtaḥ jijñāsuḥ artha arthī jñānī ca bharata ṛṣabha teṣām jñānī nitya yuktaḥ eka bhaktiḥ viśiṣyate udārāḥ sarve eva ete jñānī tu ātmā eva me matam āsthitaḥ sa hi yukta ātmā mām eva anuttamām gatim bahūnām janmanām ante jñānavān mām prapadyate kāmaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ hṛta jñānāḥ prapadyante anya devatāḥ tam tam niyamam āsthāya prakṛtyā niyatāḥ svayā yaḥ yaḥ yām yām tanum bhaktaḥ śraddhayā arcitum icchati tasya tasya acalām śraddhām tām eva vidadhāmi aham sa tayā śraddhayā yuktaḥ tasyāḥ rādhanam īhate siddhān yānti siddha vratāḥ bhūtān bhūta yajaḥ yānti pitṝn yānti pitṛ vratāḥ yānti na aham prakāśaḥ sarvasya yoga māyā samāvṛtaḥ mūḍhaḥ ayam na abhijānāti lokaḥ mām ajam avyayam veda aham samatītāni vartamānāni ca arjuna bhaviṣyāṇi ca bhūtāni mām tu veda na kaḥ cana sarva bhūtāni saṃmoham sarge yānti paraṃtapa yeṣām tu anta gatam pāpam janānām puṇya karmaṇām te dvaṃdva moha nirmuktāḥ bhajante mām dṛḍha vratāḥ jarā maraṇa mokṣāya mām āśritya yatanti ye sa adhibhūta adhidaivam mām sa adhiyajñam ca ye viduḥ prayāṇa kāle api ca mām te viduḥ yukta cetasaḥ sādhana icchā samucitām yena āśām paripūrayet prayāṇa kāle ca katham jñeyaḥ asi niyata ātmabhiḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca adhibhūtam kṣaraḥ bhāvaḥ puruṣaḥ ca adhidaivatam yaḥ prayāti sa mad bhāvam yāti na asti atra saṃśayaḥ paramam puruṣam divyam yāti pārtha anucintayan kavim purāṇam anuśāsitāram aṇoḥ aṇīyāṃsam anusmaret yaḥ mūrdhni ādhāya ātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthitaḥ yoga dhāraṇām yaḥ prayāti tyajan deham sa yāti paramām gatim an anya cetāḥ satatam yaḥ mām smarati nityaśas mām upetya punarjanma duḥkha ālayam aśāśvatam na āpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ saṃsiddhim paramām gatāḥ rātrim yuga sahasra antām te ahorātra vidaḥ janāḥ bhūta grāmaḥ saḥ eva ayam bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate yaḥ sa sarveṣu bhūteṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati yatra kāle tu anāvṛttim āvṛttim ca eva yoginaḥ prayātāḥ yānti tam kālam vakṣyāmi bharata ṛṣabha agniḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam dhūmaḥ rātriḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ dakṣiṇāyanam śukla kṛṣṇe gatī hi ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate ekayā yāti anāvṛttim anyayā āvartate punar na ete sṛtī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaḥ cana vedeṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu ca eva śrī bhagavān uvāca jñānam vijñāna sahitam yat jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣāḥ dharmasya asya paraṃtapa mad sthāni sarva bhūtāni na ca aham teṣu avasthitaḥ bhūta bhṛt na ca bhūta sthaḥ mama ātmā bhūta bhāvanaḥ sarvagaḥ sarvavaḥ ca ādyaḥ sarva kṛt sarva darśanaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva darśī ca sarva ātmā sarvatomukhaḥ yathā ākāśa sthitaḥ nityam vāyuḥ sarvatragaḥ mahān tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mad sthāni iti upadhāraya evam hi sarva bhūteṣu carāmi anabhilakṣitaḥ sarva bhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtim yānti māmakām prakṛtim svām avaṣṭabhya visṛjāmi punar punar bhūta grāmam imam kṛtsnam avaśam prakṛtyāḥ vaśāt na ca mām tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjaya udāsīna vat āsīnam asaktam teṣu karmasu mayā adhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram avajānanti mām mūḍhāḥ mānuṣīm tanum āśritam mogha āśāḥ mogha karmāṇaḥ mogha jñānāḥ vicetasaḥ rākṣasīm āsurīm ca eva prakṛtim mohinīm śritāḥ mahātmānaḥ tu mām pārtha daivīm prakṛtim āśritāḥ satatam kīrtayantaḥ mām yatantaḥ ca dṛḍha vratāḥ jñāna yajñena ca api anye yajantaḥ mām upāsate pitā aham asya jagataḥ mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ gatiḥ bhartā prabhuḥ sākṣī nivāsaḥ śaraṇam suhṛd prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ sthānam nidhānam bījam avyayam tapāmi aham aham varṣam nigṛhṇāmi utsṛjāmi ca traividyāḥ mām somapāḥ pū pāpāḥ yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā svar gatim prārthayante te tam bhuktvā svarga lokam viśālam kṣīṇe puṇye martya lokam viśanti evam trayī dharmam anuprapannā gata āgatam kāma kāmāḥ labhante an anyāḥ cintayantaḥ mām ye janāḥ paryupāsate teṣām nitya abhiyuktānām yogakṣemam vahāmi aham aham hi sarva yajñānām bhoktā ca prabhuḥ eva ca yānti deva vratāḥ devān pitṝn yānti pitṛ vratāḥ bhūtāni yānti bhūta ijyāḥ yānti mad yājinaḥ api mām saṃnyāsa yoga yukta ātmā vimuktaḥ mām upaiṣyasi kṣipram bhavati dharma ātmā śaśvat śāntim nigacchati mām hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye api syuḥ pāpa yonayaḥ striyaḥ vaiśyāḥ tathā śūdrāḥ te api yānti parām gatim kim punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyāḥ bhaktāḥ rājarṣayaḥ tathā mām eva eṣyasi yuktvā evam ātmānam mad parāyaṇaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca bhūyas eva mahā bāho śṛṇu me paramam vacaḥ yat te aham prīyamāṇāya vakṣyāmi hita kāmyayā na me viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ prabhavam na mahā ṛṣayaḥ aham ādiḥ hi devānām mahā ṛṣīṇām ca sarvaśas asaṃmūḍhaḥ sa martyeṣu sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate buddhiḥ jñānam asaṃmohaḥ kṣamā satyam damaḥ śamaḥ ahiṃsā sama tā tuṣṭiḥ tapaḥ dānam yaśaḥ ayaśaḥ bhavanti bhāvāḥ bhūtānām mattaḥ eva pṛthagvidhāḥ mad bhāvāḥ mānasāḥ jātāḥ yeṣām loke imāḥ prajāḥ etām vibhūtim yogam ca mama yaḥ vetti tattvataḥ iti matvā bhajante mām budhāḥ bhāva samanvitāḥ teṣām satata yuktānām bhajatām prīti pūrvakam teṣām eva anukampā artham aham ajñāna jam tamaḥ nāśayāmi ātma bhāva sthaḥ jñāna dīpena bhāsvatā puruṣam śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum āhuḥ tvām ṛṣayaḥ sarve deva ṛṣiḥ nāradaḥ tathā vaktum arhasi aśeṣeṇa divyāḥ hi ātma vibhūtayaḥ yābhiḥ vibhūtibhiḥ lokān imān tvam vyāpya tiṣṭhasi katham vidyām aham yogin tvām sadā paricintayan vistareṇa ātmanaḥ yogam vibhūtim ca janārdana bhūyas kathaya tṛptiḥ hi śṛṇvataḥ na asti me amṛtam śrī bhagavān uvāca prādhānyāt kuruśreṣṭha na asti antaḥ vistarasya me aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarva bhūta āśaya sthitaḥ aham ādiḥ ca madhyam ca bhūtānām antaḥ eva ca ādityānām aham viṣṇuḥ jyotiṣām raviḥ aṃśumān marīciḥ marutām asmi nakṣatrāṇām aham śaśī vedānām sāmavedaḥ asmi devānām asmi vāsavaḥ indriyāṇām manaḥ ca asmi bhūtānām asmi cetanā rudrāṇām śaṃkaraḥ ca asmi vitteśaḥ yakṣa rakṣasām vasūnām pāvakaḥ ca asmi meruḥ śikhariṇām aham purodhasām ca mukhyam mām viddhi pārtha bṛhaspatim senā nīnām aham skandaḥ sarasām asmi sāgaraḥ mahā ṛṣīṇām bhṛguḥ aham girām asmi ekam akṣaram yajñānām japa yajñaḥ asmi sthāvarāṇām himālayaḥ aśvatthaḥ sarva vṛkṣāṇām deva ṛṣīṇām ca nāradaḥ gandharvāṇām citrarathaḥ siddhānām kapilaḥ muniḥ uccaiḥśravasam aśvānām viddhi mām amṛta udbhavam airāvatam gaja indrāṇām narāṇām ca narādhipam āyudhānām aham vajram dhenūnām asmi kāmaduh prajanaḥ ca asmi kandarpaḥ sarpāṇām asmi vāsukiḥ anantaḥ ca asmi nāgānām varuṇaḥ yādasām aham pitṝṇām aryamā ca asmi yamaḥ saṃyamatām aham prahlādaḥ ca asmi daityānām kālaḥ kalayatām aham mṛgāṇām ca mṛgendraḥ aham vainateyaḥ ca pakṣiṇām pavanaḥ pavatām asmi rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām aham jhaṣāṇām makaraḥ ca asmi srotasām asmi jāhnavī sargāṇām ādiḥ antaḥ ca madhyam ca eva aham arjuna adhyātma vidyā vidyānām vādaḥ pravadatām aham akṣarāṇām akāraḥ asmi dvaṃdvaḥ sāmāsikasya ca aham eva akṣayaḥ kālaḥ dhātā aham viśvatomukhaḥ mṛtyuḥ sarva haraḥ ca aham udbhavaḥ ca bhaviṣyatām kīrtiḥ śrīḥ vāc ca nārīṇām smṛtiḥ medhā dhṛtiḥ kṣamā bṛhatsāma tathā sāmnām gāyatrī chandasām aham māsānām mārgaśīrṣaḥ aham ṛtūnām kusumākaraḥ oṣadhīnām yavaḥ ca asmi dhātūnām asmi kāñcanam sarvāsām tṛṇa jātīnām darbhaḥ aham pāṇḍu nandana vṛṣṇīnām vāsudevaḥ asmi pāṇḍavānām dhanaṃjayaḥ munīnām api aham vyāsaḥ kavīnām uśanāḥ kaviḥ daṇḍaḥ damayatām asmi nītiḥ asmi jigīṣatām maunam ca eva asmi guhyānām jñānam jñānavatām aham yat ca api sarva bhūtānām bījam tat aham arjuna na tat asti vinā yat syāt mayā bhūtam carācaram na antaḥ asti mama divyānām vibhūtīnām paraṃtapa eṣa tu uddeśataḥ proktaḥ vibhūteḥ vistaraḥ mayā viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam eka aṃśena sthitaḥ jagat bhava apyayau hi bhūtānām śrutau vistaraśaḥ mayā draṣṭum icchāmi te rūpam aiśvaram puruṣottama śrī bhagavān uvāca paśya mama pārtha rūpāṇi śataśas atha sahasraśas nānāvidhāni divyāni nānā varṇa ākṛtīni ca paśya ādityān vasūn rudrān aśvinau marutaḥ tathā bahūni a dṛṣṭa pūrvāṇi paśya āścaryāṇi bhārata mama dehe guḍākeśa yat ca anyat draṣṭum icchasi na tu mām śakyase draṣṭum anena eva sva cakṣuṣā uvāca darśayām āsa pārthāya paramam rūpam aiśvaram yadi bhās sadṛśī sā syāt bhāsaḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ apaśyat devadevasya śarīre pāṇḍavaḥ tadā tatas sa vismaya āviṣṭaḥ hṛṣṭa romā dhanaṃjayaḥ praṇamya śirasā devam kṛtāñjaliḥ abhāṣata paśyāmi devān tava deva dehe sarvān tathā bhūta viśeṣa saṃghān brahmāṇam īśam kamalāsana stham ṛṣīn ca sarvān uragān ca divyān na antam na madhyam na punar tava ādim paśyāmi viśveśvara viśvarūpa kirīṭinam gadinam cakriṇam ca tejaḥ rāśim sarvatas dīptimantam paśyāmi tvām durnirīkṣyam samantāt dīpta anala arka dyutim aprameyam paśyāmi tvām dīpta hutāśa vaktram sva tejasā viśvam idam tapantam dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ idam antaram hi vyāptam tvayā ekena diśaḥ ca sarvāḥ dṛṣṭvā adbhutam rūpam idam tava ugram lokatrayam pravyathitam mahātman amī hi tvā sura saṃghāḥ viśanti ke cit bhītāḥ prāñjalayaḥ gṛṇanti svasti iti uktvā mahā ṛṣi siddha saṃghāḥ stuvanti tvām stutibhiḥ puṣkalābhiḥ rudra ādityāḥ vasavaḥ ye ca sādhyāḥ viśve aśvinau marutaḥ ca ūṣmapāḥ ca gandharva yakṣa asura siddha saṃghāḥ vīkṣante tvā vismitāḥ ca eva sarve rūpam mahat te bahu vaktra netram mahā bāho bahu bāhu ūru pādam bahu udaram bahu daṃṣṭra karālam dṛṣṭvā lokāḥ pravyathitāḥ tathā aham nabhaḥ spṛśam dīptam aneka varṇam vyātta ānanam dīpta viśāla netram dṛṣṭvā hi tvām pravyathita antarātmā dhṛtim na vindāmi śamam ca viṣṇo daṃṣṭra karālāni ca te mukhāni dṛṣṭvā eva kāla anala saṃnibhāni amī ca tvām dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ sarve saha eva avanipāla saṃghaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ sūtaputraḥ tathā asau saha asmadīyaiḥ api yodha mukhyaiḥ vaktrāṇi te tvaramāṇāḥ viśanti daṃṣṭra karālāni bhayānakāni sahasra sūryāta saṃnibhāni tathā jagat grāsa kṛtakṣaṇāni nānā rūpaiḥ puruṣaiḥ vadhyamānā yaudhiṣṭhirāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca yodhāḥ śastraiḥ kṛttāḥ vividhaiḥ sarve eva tathā hi ime tvad śarīram praviṣṭāḥ ke cit vilagnāḥ daśana antareṣu saṃdṛśyante cūrṇitaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ tathā tava amī nara loka vīrāḥ viśanti vaktrāṇi abhivijvalanti yathā pradīptam jvalanam pataṃgāḥ tathā eva nāśāya viśanti lokāḥ tava api vaktrāṇi samṛddha vegāḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca ṛte api tvā na bhaviṣyanti sarve ye avasthitāḥ pratyanīkeṣu yodhāḥ tasmāt tvam uttiṣṭha yaśaḥ labhasva jitvā śatrūn bhuṅkṣva rājyam samṛddham droṇam ca bhīṣmam ca jayadratham ca karṇam tathā anyān api yodha vīrān mayā hatān tvam jahi mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ yudhyasva jetāsi raṇe sapatnān uvāca etat śrutvā vacanam keśavasya kṛtāñjaliḥ vepamānaḥ kirīṭī namaskṛtvā bhūyas eva āha kṛṣṇam sa gadgadam bhīta bhītaḥ praṇamya sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyā jagat prahṛṣyati anurajyate ca rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśaḥ dravanti sarve namasyanti ca siddha saṃghāḥ tvam ādidevaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ tvam asya viśvasya param nidhānam vāyuḥ yamaḥ agniḥ varuṇaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ prajāpatiḥ tvam prapitāmahaḥ ca anādimān apratima prabhāvaḥ a jānatā mahimānam tava idam mayā pramādāt praṇayena vā api yat ca avahāsa artham asatkṛtaḥ asi vihāra śayyā āsana bhojaneṣu tasmāt praṇamya praṇidhāya kāyam prasādaye tvām aham īśam īḍyam divyāni karmāṇi te adbhutāni pūrvāṇi pūrve api ṛṣayaḥ smaranti dhātā vidhātā ca vibhuḥ bhavaḥ ca kim vā aśakyam paratas kīrtayiṣye na te guṇānām parimāṇam asti imāni karmāṇi tava adbhutāni na te guṇānām parimāṇam asti na tejasaḥ ca api balasya viṣṇo adṛṣṭa pūrvam hṛṣitaḥ asmi dṛṣṭvā bhayena ca pravyathitam manaḥ me kirīṭinam gadinam cakra hastam icchāmi tvām draṣṭum aham tathā eva śrī bhagavān uvāca mayā prasannena tava arjuna idam rūpam param darśitam ātma yogāt evaṃrūpaḥ śakyaḥ aham nṛ loke draṣṭum tvat anyena kuru pravīra mā te vyathā mā ca vimūḍha bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭvā rūpam ghoram īdṛś mama idam vyapeta bhīḥ prīta manāḥ punar tvam uvāca iti arjunam vāsudevaḥ tathā uktvā svakam rūpam darśayām āsa bhūyas āśvāsayām āsa ca bhītam enam bhūtvā punar saumya vapūḥ mahātmā dṛṣṭvā idam mānuṣam rūpam te saumyam janārdana idānīm asmi saṃvṛttaḥ sa cetāḥ prakṛtim gataḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca su durdarśam idam rūpam dṛṣṭavan asi yat mama devāḥ api asya rūpasya nityam darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ śakyaḥ evaṃvidhaḥ draṣṭum dṛṣṭavan asi mām yathā jñātum draṣṭum ca tattvena praveṣṭum ca paraṃtapa nirvairaḥ sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ sa mām eti pāṇḍava evam satata yuktāḥ ye bhaktāḥ tvām paryupāsate ye ca api akṣaram avyaktam teṣām ke yoga vittamāḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca mayi āveśya manaḥ ye mām nitya yuktāḥ upāsate śraddhayā parayā upetāḥ te me yuktatamāḥ matāḥ ye tu sarvāṇi karmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya mad pare teṣām aham samuddhartā mṛtyu saṃsāra sāgarāt bhavāmi nacirāt pārtha mayi āveśita cetasām nivasiṣyasi mayi eva atas ūrdhvam na saṃśayaḥ śreyaḥ hi jñānam abhyāsāt jñānāt dhyānam viśiṣyate a dveṣṭā sarva bhūtānām maitraḥ karuṇaḥ eva ca nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ sama duḥkha sukhaḥ kṣamī saṃtuṣṭaḥ satatam yogī yata ātmā dṛḍha niścayaḥ anapekṣaḥ śuciḥ dakṣaḥ udāsīnaḥ gata vyathaḥ yaḥ na hṛṣyati na dveṣṭi na śocati na kāṅkṣati śubha aśubha parityāgī bhaktimān yaḥ sa me priyaḥ samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā māna avamānayoḥ śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkheṣu samaḥ saṅga vivarjitaḥ śraddadhānāḥ mad paramāḥ bhaktāḥ te atīva me priyāḥ prakṛtim puruṣam ca eva kṣetram kṣetrajñam eva ca etat veditum icchāmi jñānam jñeyam ca keśava śrī bhagavān uvāca prakṛtim puruṣam ca eva kṣetram kṣetrajñam eva ca etat te kathayiṣyāmi jñānam jñeyam ca bhārata kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ jñānam yat tat jñānam matam mama sa ca yaḥ yad prabhāvaḥ ca tat samāsena me śṛṇu ṛṣibhiḥ bahudhā gītam chandobhiḥ vividhaiḥ pṛthak indriyāṇi daśa ekam ca pañca ca indriya gocarāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham saṃghātaḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ etat kṣetram samāsena sa vikāram udāhṛtam ācārya upāsanam śaucam sthairyam ātma vinigrahaḥ janma mṛtyu jarā vyādhi duḥkha doṣa anudarśanam asaktiḥ anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ putra dāra gṛha ādiṣu nityam ca sama citta tvam iṣṭa aniṣṭa upapattiṣu adhyātma jñāna nitya tvam tattva jñāna artha darśanam etat jñānam iti proktam ajñānam yat atas anyathā jñeyam yat tat pravakṣyāmi yat jñātvā amṛtam aśnute sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sūkṣma tvāt tat avijñeyam dūra stham ca antike ca tat bhūta bhartṛ ca tat jñeyam grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca jñānam jñeyam jñāna gamyam hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam iti kṣetram tathā jñānam jñeyam ca uktam samāsatas prakṛtim puruṣam ca eva viddhi anādī ubhau api vikārān ca guṇān ca eva viddhi prakṛti saṃbhavān kārya kāraṇa kartṛ tve hetuḥ prakṛtiḥ ucyate puruṣaḥ sukha duḥkhānām bhoktṛ tve hetuḥ ucyate puruṣaḥ prakṛti sthaḥ hi bhuṅkte prakṛti jān guṇān upadraṣṭā anumantā ca bhartā bhoktā maheśvaraḥ yaḥ evam vetti puruṣam prakṛtim ca guṇaiḥ saha dhyānena ātmani paśyanti ke cit ātmānam ātmanā te api ca atitaranti eva mṛtyum śruti parāyaṇāḥ yāvat saṃjāyate kim cit sattvam sthāvara jaṅgamam samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantam parameśvaram na hinasti ātmanā ātmānam tatas yāti parām gatim prakṛtyā eva ca karmāṇi kriyamāṇāni sarvaśas yaḥ paśyati tathā ātmānam akartāram sa paśyati anādi tvāt nirguṇa tvāt paramātmā ayam avyayaḥ yathā sarva gatam saukṣmyāt ākāśam na upalipyate yathā prakāśayati ekaḥ kṛtsnam lokam imam raviḥ kṣetram kṣetrī tathā kṛtsnam prakāśayati bhārata kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ evam antaram jñānacakṣuṣā śrī bhagavān uvāca param bhūyas pravakṣyāmi jñānānām jñānam uttamam yat jñātvā munayaḥ sarve parām siddhim itas gatāḥ idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ saṃbhavaḥ sarva bhūtānām tatas bhavati bhārata tāsām brahma mahat yoniḥ aham bīja pradaḥ pitā sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ prakṛti saṃbhavāḥ sukha saṅgena badhnāti jñāna saṅgena ca anagha rajaḥ rāga ātmakam viddhi tṛṣṇā saṅga samudbhavam jñānam āvṛtya tu tamaḥ pramāde sañjayati uta jñānam yadā tadā vidyāt vivṛddham sattvam iti uta lobhaḥ pravṛttiḥ ārambhaḥ karmaṇām aśamaḥ spṛhā tathā pralīnaḥ tamasi mūḍha yoniṣu jāyate karmaṇaḥ su kṛtasya āhuḥ sāttvikam nirmalam phalam sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānam rajasaḥ lobhaḥ eva ca ūrdhvam gacchanti sattva sthāḥ madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥ na anyam guṇebhyaḥ kartāram yadā draṣṭā anupaśyati guṇān etān atītya trīn dehī deha samudbhavān kimācāraḥ katham ca etān trīn guṇān ativartate śrī bhagavān uvāca prakāśam ca pravṛttim ca moham eva ca pāṇḍava na dveṣṭi saṃpravṛttāni na nivṛttāni kāṅkṣati udāsīna vat āsīnaḥ guṇaiḥ yaḥ na vicālyate sama duḥkha sukhaḥ svasthaḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ māna avamānayoḥ tulyaḥ tulyaḥ mitra ari pakṣayoḥ sarva ārambha parityāgī guṇa atītaḥ saḥ ucyate śrī bhagavān uvāca ūrdhva mūlam adhas śākham aśvattham prāhuḥ avyayam adhas ca ūrdhvam prasṛtāḥ tasya śākhāḥ guṇa pravṛddhāḥ viṣaya pravālāḥ adhas ca mūlāni anusaṃtatāni karma anubandhīni manuṣya loke aśvattham enam su virūḍha mūlam asaṅga śastreṇa dṛḍhena chittvā tam eva ca ādyam puruṣam prapadye yatas pravṛttiḥ prasṛtā purāṇī nirmāna mohāḥ jita saṅga doṣāḥ adhyātma nityāḥ vinivṛtta kāmāḥ dvaṃdvaiḥ vimuktāḥ sukha duḥkha saṃjñaiḥ gacchanti amūḍhāḥ padam avyayam tat na tat bhāsayate sūryaḥ na śaśāṅkaḥ na pāvakaḥ mama eva aṃśaḥ jīva loke jīva bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni indriyāṇi prakṛti sthāni karṣati śarīram yat avāpnoti yat ca api utkrāmati īśvaraḥ gṛhītvā etāni saṃyāti vāyuḥ gandhān iva āśayāt śrotram cakṣuḥ sparśanam ca rasanam ghrāṇam eva ca adhiṣṭhāya manaḥ ca ayam viṣayān upasevate utkrāmantam sthitam vā api bhuñjānam vā guṇa anvitam vimūḍhāḥ na anupaśyanti paśyanti jñāna cakṣuṣaḥ gām āviśya ca bhūtāni dhārayāmi aham ojasā puṣṇāmi ca oṣadhīḥ sarvāḥ somaḥ bhūtvā rasa ātmakaḥ aham vaiśvānaraḥ bhūtvā prāṇinām deham āśritaḥ prāṇa apāna samāyuktaḥ pacāmi annam caturvidham sarvasya ca aham hṛdi saṃniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam ca dvau imau puruṣau loke kṣaraḥ ca akṣaraḥ eva ca kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭasthaḥ akṣaraḥ ucyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yasmāt kṣaram atītaḥ aham akṣarāt api ca uttamaḥ yaḥ mām evam asaṃmūḍhaḥ jānāti puruṣottamam etat buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārata śrī bhagavān uvāca dānam damaḥ ca yajñaḥ ca svādhyāyaḥ tapaḥ ārjavam ahiṃsā satyam akrodhaḥ tyāgaḥ śāntiḥ apaiśunam dayā bhūteṣu a loluptvam mārdavam hrīḥ acāpalam tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adrohaḥ na atimāni tā ajñānam ca abhijātasya pārtha saṃpadam āsurīm daivī saṃpad vimokṣāya nibandhāya āsurī matā mā śucaḥ saṃpadam daivīm abhijātaḥ asi pāṇḍava daivaḥ vistaraśaḥ proktaḥ āsuram pārtha mama śṛṇu pravṛttim ca nivṛttim ca janāḥ na viduḥ āsurāḥ na śaucam na api ca ācāraḥ na satyam teṣu vidyate asatyam apratiṣṭham te jagat āhuḥ anīśvaram etām dṛṣṭim avaṣṭabhya naṣṭa ātmānaḥ alpabuddhayaḥ prabhavanti ugra karmāṇaḥ kṣayāya jagantaḥ ahitāḥ kāmam āśritya duṣpūram dambha māna mada anvitāḥ mohāt gṛhītvā asat grāhān pravartante aśuci vratāḥ cintām aparimeyām ca pralaya antām upāśritāḥ kāma upabhoga paramāḥ etāvat iti niścitāḥ āśā pāśa śataiḥ baddhāḥ kāma krodha parāyaṇāḥ īhante kāma bhoga artham anyāyena artha saṃcayān asau mayā hataḥ śatruḥ haniṣye ca aparān api īśvaraḥ aham aham bhogī siddhaḥ aham balavān sukhī āḍhyaḥ abhijanavān asmi kaḥ anyaḥ asti sadṛśaḥ mayā yakṣye dāsyāmi modiṣye iti ajñāna vimohitāḥ aneka citta vibhrāntāḥ moha jāla samāvṛtāḥ ātma saṃbhāvitāḥ stabdhāḥ dhana māna mada anvitāḥ ahaṃkāram balam darpam kāmam krodham ca saṃśritāḥ mām ātma para deheṣu pradviṣantaḥ abhyasūyakāḥ tān aham dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu nara adhamān kṣipāmi ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu āsurīm yonim āpannāḥ mūḍhāḥ janmani janmani trividham narakasya idam dvāram nāśanam ātmanaḥ ācarati ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ tatas yāti parām gatim yaḥ śāstra vidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ tasmāt śāstram pramāṇam te kārya akārya vyavasthitau jñātvā śāstra vidhāna uktam karma kartum iha arhasi ye śāstra vidhim utsṛjya yajante śraddhayā anvitāḥ teṣām niṣṭhā tu kā kṛṣṇa sattvam āho rajaḥ tamaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca trividhā bhavati śraddhā dehinām sā svabhāva jā sāttvikā rājasā ca eva tāmasā ca iti tām śṛṇu yajante sāttvikāḥ devān yakṣa rakṣāṃsi rājasāḥ pretān bhūta gaṇān ca anye yajante tāmasāḥ janāḥ a śāstra vihitam ghoram tapyante ye tapaḥ janāḥ dambha ahaṃkāra saṃyuktāḥ kāma rāga bala anvitāḥ karśayantaḥ śarīra stham bhūta grāmam acetasaḥ mām ca eva antar śarīra stham tān viddhi āsura niścayān yajñaḥ tapaḥ tathā dānam teṣām bhedam imam śṛṇu rasyāḥ snigdhāḥ sthirāḥ hṛdyāḥ āhārāḥ sāttvika priyāḥ kaṭu amla lavaṇa ati uṣṇa tīkṣṇa rūkṣa vidāhinaḥ āhārāḥ rājasasya iṣṭāḥ duḥkha śoka āmaya pradāḥ yātayāmam gata rasam pūti paryuṣitam ca yat a phala ākāṅkṣibhiḥ yajñaḥ vidhi dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ ijyate yaṣṭavyam eva iti manaḥ samādhāya sa sāttvikaḥ ijyate bharata śreṣṭha tam yajñam viddhi rājasam vidhi hīnam a sṛṣṭa annam mantra hīnam a dakṣiṇam śraddhā virahitam yajñam tāmasam paricakṣate deva dvija guru prājña pūjanam śaucam ārjavam brahmacaryam ahiṃsā ca śārīram tapaḥ ucyate svādhyāya abhyasanam ca eva vāc mayam tapaḥ ucyate a phala ākāṅkṣibhiḥ yuktaiḥ sāttvikam paricakṣate mūḍha grāheṇa ātmanaḥ yat pīḍayā kriyate tapaḥ parasya utsādana artham vā tat tāmasam udāhṛtam dātavyam iti yat dānam dīyate anupakāriṇe deśe kāle ca pātre ca tat dānam sāttvikam smṛtam dīyate ca parikliṣṭam tat dānam rājasam smṛtam a deśa kāle yat dānam apātrebhyaḥ ca dīyate asatkṛtam avajñātam tat tāmasam udāhṛtam brāhmaṇāḥ tena vedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca vihitāḥ purā tasmāt om iti udāhṛtya yajña dāna tapaḥ kriyāḥ tat iti an abhisaṃdhāya phalam yajña tapaḥ kriyāḥ dāna kriyāḥ ca vividhāḥ kriyante mokṣa kāṅkṣibhiḥ aśraddhayā hutam dattam tapaḥ taptam kṛtam ca yat tyāgasya ca hṛṣīkeśa pṛthak keśiniṣūdana śrī bhagavān uvāca kāmyānām karmaṇām nyāsam saṃnyāsam kavayaḥ vid sarva karma phala tyāgam prāhuḥ tyāgam vicakṣaṇāḥ tyājyam doṣavat iti eke karma prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ niścayam śṛṇu mama tatra tyāge bharata sattama tyāgaḥ hi puruṣa vyāghra trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ yajñaḥ dānam tapaḥ ca eva pāvanāni manīṣiṇām etāni api tu karmāṇi saṅgam tyaktvā phalāni ca mohāt tasya parityāgaḥ tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ sa kṛtvā rājasam tyāgam na eva tyāga phalam labhet saṅgam tyaktvā phalam ca eva sa tyāgaḥ sāttvikaḥ mataḥ na dveṣṭi akuśalam karma kuśale na anuṣajjate tyāgī sattva samāviṣṭaḥ medhāvī chinna saṃśayaḥ na hi dehabhṛtā śakyam tyaktum karmāṇi aśeṣatas aniṣṭam iṣṭam miśram ca trividham karmaṇaḥ phalam bhavati atyāginām pretya na tu saṃnyāsinām kva cit pañca etāni mahā bāho kāraṇāni nibodha mama sāṃkhye kṛtānte proktāni siddhaye sarva karmaṇām adhiṣṭhānam tathā kartā karaṇam ca pṛthagvidham vividhāḥ ca pṛthak ceṣṭāḥ daivam ca eva atra pañcamam nyāyyam vā viparītam vā pañca ete tasya hetavaḥ tatra evam sati kartāram ātmānam kevalam tu yaḥ jñānam jñeyam parijñātā trividhā karma codanā procyate guṇa saṃkhyāne yathāvat śṛṇu tāni api sarva bhūteṣu yena ekam bhāvam avyayam īkṣate pṛthaktvena tu yat jñānam nānā bhāvān pṛthagvidhān vetti sarveṣu bhūteṣu tat jñānam viddhi rājasam niyatam saṅga rahitam a rāga dveṣataḥ kṛtam yat tu kāma īpsunā karma sa ahaṃkāreṇa vā punar kriyate bahula āyāsam tat rājasam udāhṛtam anubandham kṣayam hiṃsām an apekṣya ca pauruṣam mukta saṅgaḥ an ahaṃvādī dhṛti utsāha samanvitaḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ayuktaḥ prākṛtaḥ stabdhaḥ śaṭhaḥ naikṛtikaḥ alasaḥ viṣādī dīrghasūtrī ca kartā tāmasaḥ ucyate buddheḥ bhedam dhṛtyāḥ ca eva guṇāt trividham śṛṇu procyamānam aśeṣeṇa pṛthaktvena dhanaṃjaya pravṛttim ca nivṛttim ca kārya akārye bhaya abhaye bandham mokṣam ca yā vetti buddhiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasī sarva arthān viparītān ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī dhṛtyā yayā dhārayate manaḥ prāṇa indriya kriyāḥ yogena avyabhicārinyā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī yayā tu dharma kāma arthān dhṛtyā dhārayate arjuna prasaṅgena phala ākāṅkṣī dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha rājasī yayā svapnam bhayam śokam viṣādam madam eva ca na vimuñcati durmedhāḥ dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī sukham tu idānīm trividham śṛṇu mama bharata ṛṣabha pariṇāme viṣam iva tat sukham rājasam smṛtam na tat asti pṛthivyām vā divi deveṣu vā punar brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām śūdrāṇām ca paraṃtapa śamaḥ damaḥ tapaḥ śaucam kṣāntiḥ ārjavam eva ca jñānam vijñānam āstikyam brahma karma svabhāva jam śauryam tejaḥ dhṛtiḥ dākṣyam yuddhe ca api apalāyanam dānam īśvara bhāvaḥ ca kṣatra karma svabhāva jam kṛṣi gorakṣya vāṇijyam vaiśya karma svabhāva jam yatas pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam śreyān svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ para dharmāt su anuṣṭhitāt sarva ārambhāḥ hi doṣeṇa dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ naiṣkarmya siddhim paramām saṃnyāsena adhigacchati samāsena eva kaunteya niṣṭhā jñānasya yā parā buddhyā viśuddhayā yuktaḥ dhṛtya ātmānam niyamya ca śabda ādīn viṣayān tyaktvā rāga dveṣau vyudasya ca vivikta sevī laghu āśī yata vāc kāya mānasaḥ dhyāna yoga paraḥ nityam vairāgyam samupāśritaḥ ahaṃkāram balam darpam kāmam krodham parigraham brahma bhūtaḥ prasanna ātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣati bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān yaḥ ca asmi tattvāt tatas mām tattvataḥ jñātvā viśate tad anantaram sarva karmāṇi api sadā kurvāṇaḥ mad vyapāśrayaḥ mad prasādāt avāpnoti śāśvatam padam avyayam atha ced tvam ahaṃkārāt na śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasi īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā tad prasādāt parām śāntim sthānam prāpsyasi śāśvatam iti te jñānam ākhyātam guhyāt guhyataram mayā vimṛśya etat aśeṣeṇa yathā icchasi tathā kuru sarva guhyatamam bhūyas śṛṇu mama paramam vacaḥ iṣṭaḥ asi me dṛḍham iti tatas vakṣyāmi te hitam aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ idam te na atapaskāya na abhaktāya kadā cana na ca aśuśrūṣave vācyam na ca mām yaḥ abhyasūyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ adhyeṣyate ca yaḥ imam dharmyam saṃvādam āvayoḥ jñāna yajñena tena aham iṣṭaḥ syām iti mama matiḥ śraddhāvān anasūyaḥ ca śṛṇuyāt api yaḥ naraḥ saḥ api muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇya karmaṇām kaccit ajñāna saṃmohaḥ pranaṣṭaḥ te dhanaṃjaya naṣṭaḥ mohaḥ smṛtiḥ labdhā tvad prasādāt mayā acyuta uvāca saṃvādam imam aśrauṣam adbhutam roma harṣaṇam yogam yogeśvarāt kṛṣṇāt sākṣāt kathayataḥ svayam rājan saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya saṃvādam imam adbhutam keśava arjunayoḥ puṇyam hṛṣyāmi ca muhur muhur tat ca saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya rūpam atyadbhutam hareḥ vismayaḥ mama mahān rājan hṛṣyāmi ca punar punar yatra yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ yatra pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ sukham bandha vimuktiḥ syāt iti gītārtha saṃgraha ṣaḍ śatāni saviṃśāni ślokānām prāha keśavaḥ arjunaḥ saptapañcāśat saptaṣaṣṭiḥ tu saṃjayaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ślokam ekam gītāyāḥ mānam ucyate uvāca gītā su gītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstra vistaraiḥ yā ca iyam padmanābhasya mukha padmāt viniḥsṛtā sarva śāstra mayī gītā sarva deva mayaḥ hariḥ gaṅgā gītā ca gāyatrī govinda iti hṛdi sthite bhārata amṛta sarvasva gītāyāḥ mathitasya ca śrī bhagavant uvāca jñāna jñāna yoga vinirmuc tat jñānam brūhi keśava sarvatas jyotiḥ jyotis ākāśam sarva bhūta guṇa anvitam ātma dehe mayā sṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ kṣetram eva ca pramāṇam veda tattvānām sāṃkhya ādīni abhiyoginām teṣām na vidyate niṣṭhā sarvaiḥ pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ saha kathitam ca mayā jñānam devānām api durlabham suṣumṇā dakṣiṇe mārge darśitā viśva rūpiṇā aprakāśam idam praśnam yat mayā kathay tava na agniḥ vāyuḥ na ca ākāśam na kṣitiḥ na api vā jalam manaḥ buddhi ahaṃkāram guh artham kathitam tava anityaḥ nitya tām yāti yadā bhāvam na paśyati śūnyam nirañjana ākāram nirvāṇam dhruvam avyayam puruṣam nirguṇam sākṣāt sarvatas ca eva tiṣṭhati daśamam ca aṅgulam vyāpya ca āśā bāhyam vyavasthitam jīvaḥ yatra pralīyeta sā kalā ṣoḍaśī smṛtā tat cintyam tena vai jñānam tat atra ādyāḥ upāsate brahmaṇā eva hi vikhyātam vedānteṣu prakāśitam āhutiḥ sā parā jñeyā sā ca saṃdhyā pratiṣṭhitā gāyatrī gāyatrī tad parā jñeyā ajapā nāma viśrutā tām kalām yaḥ abhijānāti sa kalā jñaḥ abhidhīyate yām jñātvā mucyate jantuḥ garbha janma jarā ādibhiḥ parijñānena mucyante narāḥ pātaka kilbiṣaiḥ iḍā iḍā bhagavatī gaṅgā piṅgalā yamunā nadī iḍā vai vaiṣṇavī nāḍī brahmanāḍī tu piṅgalā suṣumṇā ca aiśvarā nāḍī tridhā prāṇa vahā smṛ brahmā viṣṇuḥ mahādevaḥ recakaḥ pūra kumbhakaḥ iḍā vai gārhapatyaḥ tu piṅgalā āhavanīyakaḥ suṣumṇā dakṣiṇa agniḥ tu hi etat agni trayam smṛtam śivaḥ binduḥ śivaḥ devaḥ ghargharā amṛta varcasā nikhilam pūrayet deham viṣa dāha jvara apaham sarpa sarpa vat kuṭila kuṭila ākāra suṣumṇā veṣṭitām tanum makāra veṣṭitām kṛtvā mātṛ vat pariyojayet sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiras mukham nirmalam vimala ākāram śuddha sphaṭika saṃnibham jīvaḥ jīvati jīvena na asti jīvam ajīvitam śrī bhagavant uvāca ākāśam pibate nityam sa jīvaḥ tena jīvati kākīmukham kakāra antam makāram cetanā anugam tāvat paśyet khaga ākāram khakāram tu vicintayet ātmānam kha mayam kṛtvā na kim cit api cintayet ūrdhva śūnyam adhas śūnyam madhyeśūnyam nirāmayam puṇya pāpa harāḥ ca eva ye ca anye pañca daivatāḥ pāpam dah jñāna agniḥ puṇya soma sūrya saṃtoṣam samidhā amṛtam indriyāṇi paśum kṛtvā yaḥ yajeta sa dīkṣitaḥ sakale sakala dṛṣṭa pāraḥ api bhāvam yuñjati yuñjati niṣkale darśanam na asti svabhāvaḥ bhāvam yuñjati tālumūle ca lampāyām trikūṭam tripatha antaram ekam tattvam vijānīyāt vighnasya āyatanam mahat gītāḥ su gītāḥ kartavyāḥ kim anyaiḥ śāstra saṃgrahaiḥ yāḥ purā padmanābhasya mukha padmāt viniḥsṛtāḥ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate sarva tīrtha tīrtha mayā gaṅgā sarva pāpa kṣayaṃkarā gītā gaṅgā ca gāyatrī govindaḥ hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ tasmāt guṇa sahasreṇa viṣṇoḥ nirvacanam yathā etat puṇyam pāpa haram dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam śrī śrī bhagavant uvāca jñāna yoga vinirmuktam vinirmuc tat jñānam brūhi keśava sarvatas jyotiḥ jyotis ākāśam sarva bhūta guṇa anvitam ātman deha mad sṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ kṣetram eva ca pramāṇam veda tattvānām sāṃkhya ādīni abhiyoginām teṣām na vidyate niṣṭhā sarvaiḥ pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ saha kathitam ca mayā jñānam devānām api durlabham aprakāśam idam praśnam yat mayā kathitam tava vāc vāc mayam sarva śāstrāṇām ati sūkṣmam carācaram na na agniḥ vāyuḥ na ca ākāśam na kṣitiḥ na api vā jalam manaḥ buddhi ahaṃkāra guh artham artha kathitam tava anityaḥ nitya tām yāti yadā bhāvam na paśyati śūnya nirañjana nirañjana nirañjana nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇa nirvāṇ puruṣam nirguṇam sākṣāt sarvatas ca eva tiṣṭhati daśamam ca aṅgulam vyāpya ca āśā bāhyam vyavasthitam jīvaḥ yatra pralīyeta sā kalā ṣoḍaśī smṛtā tat cintyam tena vai jñānam tat atra ādyāḥ upāsate brahmaṇā eva hi vikhyātam vedānteṣu prakāśitam āhutiḥ sā parā jñeyā sā ca saṃdhyā pratiṣṭhitā gāyatrī gāyatrī tad parā jñeyā ajapā nāma viśrutā tām kalām yaḥ abhijānāti sa kalā jñaḥ abhidhīyate yām yad jñātvā mucyate jantuḥ garbha janma jarā ādibhiḥ parijñānena mucyante narāḥ pātaka kilbiṣaiḥ iḍā bhagavatī gaṅgā piṅgalā yamunā nadī iḍā iḍā vai vaiṣṇavī nāḍī brahmanāḍī tu piṅgalā suṣumṇā suṣumṇā ca aiśvarā nāḍī tridhā prāṇa vahā smṛtā brahmā brahman viṣṇuḥ mahādevaḥ recakaḥ pūra kumbhakaḥ iḍā iḍā vai gārhapatyaḥ tu piṅgalāhavanīyakaḥ suṣumṇā dakṣiṇa agniḥ tu hi etat agni trayam smṛtam śivaḥ binduḥ śivaḥ devaḥ ghargharā amṛta varcasā nikhilam pūrayet deham viṣa dāha jvara apaham sarpa sarpa vat kuṭila kuṭila ākāra suṣumṇā veṣṭitām tanum makāra veṣṭitām kṛtvā mātṛ vat pariyojayet sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi akṣi śiras mukham nirmalam vimala ākāram śuddha sphaṭika saṃnibham śrī śrī bhagavant uvāca jīvaḥ jīvati jīvena sa jīvaḥ kena jīvati ākāśam pibate nityam sa jīvaḥ tena jīvati kākīmukham kakāra antam makāram cetanā anugam tāvat paśyet khaga ākāram khakāram tu vicintayet ātmānam kha mayam kṛtvā na kim cit api cintayet ūrdhva śūnyam adhas śūnyam madhyeśūnyam nirāmayam saṃprāpte samprāp jñāna vijñāne jñā ca hṛdi saṃsthite labdha śānta pade bhāve na yogaḥ na ca dhāraṇā veda veda ādau yaḥ suraḥ proktaḥ veda ante ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ nā nāvā arthī bhavet tāvat yāvat pāram na gacchati uttīrṇe tu pare pāre kim nāvā vai prayojanam dūra dūra sthaḥ na api dūra sthaḥ piṇḍa sthaḥ piṇḍa varjitaḥ amala nirmala sūkṣmaḥ sarva vyāpī nirañjanaḥ akṣarāṇi samātrāṇi sarve bindu samāśritāḥ śrī śrī bhagavant uvāca oṃkāra dhvani nādena vāyuḥ saṃharaṇa antikam śrī śrī bhagavant uvāca tat tālu kaṇṭheṣu anunāsikam ca arepha jātam śubham ūṣma varjitam na duṣkarāṇām kurute kadā cit ākāśam api an ākāśam puruṣa tve pratiṣṭhitam śabdam guṇam iva ākāśam niḥśabdam brahma ca ucyate indriyāṇām nirodhena dehe paśyanti mānavāḥ dehe naṣṭe kutas buddhiḥ jñānam vijñānam eva ca jñānam jñāna vijñāna yuj ca rakṣaṇīyam prayatna gītāḥ su gītāḥ kṛ kim anyaiḥ śāstra saṃgrahaiḥ yāḥ purā padmanābhasya mukha padma viniḥsṛtāḥ gītāgaṅgā udakam pītvā punarjanma na vidyate sarva tīrtha mayī maya gaṅgā sarva pāpa kṣayaṃkarī gakāra gakāra pūrvāḥ catvāraḥ rakṣanti mahataḥ bhayāt gītā gaṅgā ca gāyatrī govindaḥ hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ snātaḥ vā yadi vā a snātaḥ śuciḥ vā yadi vā aśuciḥ yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣam sa bāhya abhyantara śuci gītā sāram paṭhet yaḥ tu viṣṇu loke mahīyate etat puṇyam pāpa haram dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam uvāca prabodhitaḥ sa tu tadā viṣṇunā viśvamūrtinā avināśi svarūpam ca dṛṣṭvā tattvena phālgunaḥ kṛtrimam tu jagat rūpam jñātvā yuddha udyataḥ abhavat devadattam samāyujya śastrāṇi jagṛhe punar tatas dhanaṃjayam dṛṣṭvā bāṇa gāṇḍīva dhāriṇam punar eva mahā nādam vyasṛjanta mahā rathāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ somakāḥ ca eva ye ca eṣām anuyāyinaḥ dadhmuḥ ca muditāḥ śaṅkhān vīrāḥ sāgara saṃbhavān tatas bheryaḥ ca peśyaḥ ca krakacāḥ goviṣāṇikāḥ atha devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ pitaraḥ ca janeśvara siddha cāraṇa saṃghāḥ ca samīyuḥ te didṛkṣayā ṛṣayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ puraskṛtya śatakratum samīyuḥ tatra sahitāḥ draṣṭum tat vaiśasam mahat te sene stimite ca āstām vīkṣamāṇe parasparam tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya su samudyate avaruhya rathāt tūrṇam padbhyām eva kṛtāñjaliḥ avatīrya rathāt tūrṇam bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ anvayāt bhītam yudhiṣṭhiram matvā bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān vāsudevaḥ ca bhagavant pṛṣṭhatas anujagāma ha sātyakiḥ ca arjunaḥ ca eva abhimanyuḥ ca vīryavān yathāmukhyāḥ ca rājānaḥ tam anvājagmuḥ utsukāḥ daṃśiteṣu ari sainyeṣu bhrātṝn utsṛjya pārthiva kva evam gamiṣyasi śreṣṭha tyaktvā asmān durbalaḥ yathā rājā hi tvam mahā bāho vāgyataḥ manyumān iva uvāca evam ābhāṣyamāṇaḥ api bhrātṛbhiḥ kuru nandana na uvāca vāgyataḥ kim cit gacchati eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tān uvāca mahā prājñaḥ vāsudevaḥ mahā manāḥ eṣa bhīṣmam tathā droṇam gautamam śalyam eva ca śrūyate hi purākalpe gurūn an anumānya yaḥ yaḥ tu yuddhe samutpanne gurūn dṛṣṭvā atha daṃśitān evam bruvati kṛṣṇe tu dhārtarāṣṭra camūm prati hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt niḥśabdāḥ tu apare abhavan dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram dūrāt dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥ mithas saṃkathayām cakruḥ na īśaḥ asti kula pāṃsanaḥ vyaktam bhītaḥ iva abhyeti rājā asau bhīṣmam antikāt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sa sodaryaḥ śaraṇa artham prayācakaḥ dhanaṃjaye katham nāthe pāṇḍave ca vṛkodare hṛṣṭāḥ sumanasaḥ bhūtvā cailāni dudhuvuḥ pṛthak yudhiṣṭhiram sa sodaryam sahitam keśavena ha niḥśabdam abhavat tūrṇam punar eva viśām pate kim nu vakṣyati rājā asau kim bhīṣmaḥ prativakṣyati kim nu vakṣyati rājā asau dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kim nu vakṣyati bhīṣmaḥ asau bharatānām dhuraṃdharaḥ kim bhīmaḥ samara ślāghī kim nu kṛṣṇa arjunau iti vivakṣitam kim asya iti saṃśayaḥ su mahān abhūt ubhayoḥ senayoḥ rājan yudhiṣṭhira kṛte tadā sa vigāhya camūm śatroḥ śara śakti samākulām bhīṣmam eva abhyayāt tūrṇam bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ tam uvāca tatas pādau karābhyām pīḍya pāṇḍavaḥ bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam rājā yuddhāya samupasthitam uvāca anujānīhi mām tāta āśiṣaḥ ca prayojaya jayeyam ca ripūn sarvān anujñātaḥ tvayā anagha yudhyantam mām raṇe vīra tvam anujñātum arhasi uvāca yadi evam na abhigacchethāḥ yudhi mām pṛthivīpate śapeyam tvām mahā rāja parābhāvāya bhārata vriyatām ca varaḥ pārtha kim asmattaḥ abhikāṅkṣasi evam gate mahā rāja na tava asti parājayaḥ uvāca mantrayasva mahā prājña hita eṣī mama nityaśas uvāca uvāca uvāca vijayeta pumān kaḥ cit api sākṣāt śatakratuḥ uvāca jaya upāyam bravīhi tvam ātmanaḥ samare paraiḥ uvāca na śatrum tāta paśyāmi samare yaḥ jayeta mām uvāca prayāt punar mahā bāhuḥ ācāryasya ratham prati paśyatām sarva sainyānām madhyena bhrātṛbhiḥ saha sa droṇam abhivādya atha kṛtvā ca eva pradakṣiṇam uvāca vācā durdharṣam ātma niḥśreyasam vacaḥ jayeyam ca ripūn sarvān anujñātaḥ tvayā dvija uvāca yadi mām na abhigacchethāḥ yuddhāya kṛta niścayaḥ śapeyam tvām mahā rāja parābhāvāya sarvaśas tat yudhiṣṭhira tuṣṭaḥ asmi pūjitaḥ ca tvayā anagha karavāṇi ca te kāmam brūhi yat te abhikāṅkṣitam yotsyāmi kauravasya arthe te āśāsyaḥ jayaḥ mayā uvāca uvāca aham ca tvā abhijānāmi raṇe śatrūn vijeṣyasi yatas dharmaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ yatas kṛṣṇaḥ tatas jayaḥ uvāca pṛcchāmi tvām dvijaśreṣṭha śṛṇu me yat vivakṣitam uvāca uvāca hanta tasmāt mahā bāho vadha upāyam vada ātmanaḥ ācārya praṇipatya eṣa pṛcchāmi tvām namaḥ astu te uvāca na śatrum tāta paśyāmi yaḥ mām hanyāt raṇe sthitam yudhyamānam su saṃrabdham śara varṣa ogha varṣiṇam hanyāt mām yudhi yodhānām satyam etat bravīmi te śastram ca aham raṇe jahyām śrutvā su mahat apriyam śraddheya vākyāt puruṣāt etat satyam bravīmi te uvāca etat śrutvā mahā rāja bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ anumānya tam ācāryam prāyāt śāradvatam prati saḥ abhivādya kṛpam rājā kṛtvā ca api pradakṣiṇam uvāca durdharṣatamam vākyam vākya viśāradaḥ anumānaye tvām yotsyāmi guro vigata kalmaṣaḥ jayeyam ca ripūn sarvān anujñātaḥ tvayā anagha uvāca yadi mām na abhigacchethāḥ yuddhāya kṛta niścayaḥ śapeyam tvām mahā rāja parābhāvāya sarvaśas kim te karomi vai kāmam brūhi pāṇḍava nandana uvāca hanta pṛcchāmi te tasmāt ācārya śṛṇu mama vacaḥ uvāca tam gautamaḥ pratyuvāca vijñāya asya vivakṣitam āśāsiṣye sadā utthāya satyam etat bravīmi te anumānya kṛpam rājā prayayau yena madra rāj sa śalyam abhivādya atha kṛtvā ca abhipradakṣiṇam uvāca rājā durdharṣam ātma niḥśreyasam vacaḥ anumānaye tvām yotsyāmi guro vigata kalmaṣaḥ jayeyam ca mahā rāja anujñātaḥ tvayā ripūn uvāca yadi mām na abhigacchethāḥ yuddhāya kṛta niścayaḥ śapeyam tvām mahā rāja parābhāvāya vai raṇe tuṣṭaḥ asmi pūjitaḥ ca asmi yat kāṅkṣasi tat astu te brūhi ca eva param vīra kena arthaḥ kim dadāmi te uvāca uvāca uvāca tvām hi yokṣyati sūta tve sūtaputrasya mātula duryodhanaḥ raṇe śūram iti mama naiṣṭhikā matiḥ uvāca uvāca nirjagāma mahā sainyāt bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ tatas enam uvāca idam pāṇḍava arthe gadāgrajaḥ śrutam me karṇa bhīṣmasya dveṣāt kila na yotsyasi dhārtarāṣṭrasya sāhāyyam yadi paśyasi ced samam uvāca na vipriyam kariṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya keśava tyakta prāṇam hi mām viddhi duryodhana hita eṣiṇam uvāca tat śrutvā vacanam kṛṣṇaḥ saṃnyavartata bhārata yudhiṣṭhira purogaiḥ ca pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgataḥ atha sainyasya madhye tu prākrośat pāṇḍava agrajaḥ yaḥ asmān vṛṇoti tat aham varaye sāhya kāraṇāt prīta ātmā dharmarājānam kuntī putram yudhiṣṭhiram aham yotsyāmi miṣataḥ saṃyuge dhārtarāṣṭra jān tvad arthe mahā rāja yadi mām vṛṇuṣe anagha uvāca yuyutso vāsudevaḥ ca vayam ca sarvaśas na bhaviṣyanti te bālāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ na saṃśayaḥ vṛṇomi tvām mahā bāho yudhyasva mama kāraṇāt tvayi piṇḍaḥ ca tantuḥ ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dṛśyate na bhaviṣyati durbuddhiḥ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ ati amarṣaṇaḥ uvāca jagāma pāṇḍu putrāṇām senām viśrāvya dundubhim tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ saha anujaiḥ tatas vyūham yathāpūrvam pratyavyūhanta te punar avādayan dundubhīn ca śataśas ca eva puṣkarān siṃhanādān ca vividhān vineduḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ ratha sthān puruṣa vyāghrān pāṇḍavān prekṣya pārthivāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna ādayaḥ sarve punar jahṛṣire mudā gauravam pāṇḍu putrāṇām mānyān mānayatām ca tān dṛṣṭvā mahīkṣitaḥ tatra pūjayām cakrire bhṛśam sauhṛdam ca kṛpām ca eva prāpta kālam mahātmanām dayām ca jñātiṣu parām nṛpāḥ sādhu sādhu iti sarvatra niśceruḥ stuti saṃhitāḥ vācaḥ puṇyāḥ kīrtimatām manaḥ hṛdaya harṣiṇīḥ mlecchāḥ ca āryāḥ ca ye tatra dadṛśuḥ śuśruvuḥ tadā vṛttam tat pāṇḍu putrāṇām ruruduḥ te sa gadgadāḥ tatas jaghnuḥ mahā bherīḥ śataśas ca eva puṣkarān śaṅkhān ca go kṣīra nibhān dadhmuḥ hṛṣṭāḥ manasvinaḥ kṛṣṇam kamala pattra akṣam puṇya śravaṇa kīrtanam vāsudevam jagadyonim naumi nārāyaṇam harim uvāca evam vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu māmakeṣu itareṣu ca ke pūrvam prāharan tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tathā uvāca bhīṣmam pramukhatas kṛtvā prayayau saha senayā tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve bhīmasena purogamāḥ bhīṣmeṇa yuddham icchantaḥ prayayuḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ kṣveḍāḥ kilakilā śabdāḥ krakacāḥ goviṣāṇikāḥ bherī mṛdaṅga murajāḥ haya kuñjara nisvanāḥ mahānti anīkāni mahā samucchraye samāgame pāṇḍava dhārtarāṣṭrayoḥ cakampire śaṅkha mṛdaṅga nisvanaiḥ prakampitāni iva vanāni vāyunā narendra nāga aśva ratha ākulānām abhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrte babhūva ghoṣaḥ tumulaḥ camūnām vāta uddhutānām iva sāgarāṇām bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ prāṇadat go vṛṣaḥ yathā śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣam vāraṇānām ca bṛṃhitam siṃhanādam ca sainyānām bhīmasena ravaḥ abhyabhūt hayānām heṣamāṇānām anīkeṣu sahasraśas jīmūtasya iva nadataḥ śakra aśani sama svanam vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛt mūtram prasusruvuḥ śabdena tasya vīrasya siṃhasya iva itare mṛgāḥ vibhīṣayan te sutān tava senām samabhyayāt tam āyāntam mahā iṣvāsam sodaryāḥ paryavārayan chādayantaḥ śara vrātaiḥ meghāḥ iva divākaram duḥśāsanaḥ ca atirathaḥ tathā durmarṣaṇaḥ nṛpa viviṃśatiḥ citrasenaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ ādadānāḥ ca nārācān nirmukta āśīviṣa upamān atha tān draupadī putrāḥ saubhadraḥ ca mahā rathaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān pratiyayuḥ ardayantaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ vajraiḥ iva mahā vegaiḥ śikharāṇi dharābhṛtām tāvakānām pareṣām ca na āsīt kaḥ cit parāṅmukhaḥ lāghavam droṇa śiṣyāṇām apaśyam bharata ṛṣabha nimittavedhinām rājñ śarān utsṛjatām bhṛśam na upaśāmyati nirghoṣaḥ dhanuṣām kūjatām tathā viniśceruḥ śarāḥ dīptāḥ jyotīṃṣi iva nabhastalāt sarve tu anye mahīpālāḥ prekṣakāḥ iva bhārata dadṛśuḥ darśanīyam tam bhīmam jñāti samāgamam tatas te jāta saṃrambhāḥ paraspara kṛta āgasaḥ śuśubhāte raṇe atīva paṭe citra gate iva tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve pragṛhīta śarāsanāḥ saha sainyāḥ samāpetuḥ putrasya te śāsanāt teṣām ādhāvatām tatra gaja aśva kalilaḥ mahān siṃhanāda rava unmiśraḥ śaṅkha bherī samākulaḥ sa ghoṣavān śara grāhaḥ dhanuḥ nāgaḥ asi kacchapaḥ vyāvalgita purovātaḥ āsīt kṣubdha abdhi vat svanaḥ yudhiṣṭhireṇa ca ādiṣṭāḥ pārthivāḥ te sahasraśas ubhayayoḥ senayoḥ tīvraḥ sainyānām sa samāgamaḥ antardhīyata ca ādityaḥ sainyena rajasā āvṛtaḥ prayuddhānām prabhagnānām punar āvartatām api na atra svānām pareṣām vā viśeṣaḥ samajāyata uvāca prāvartata mahā ghoram rājñām deha avakartanam kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca saṃgrāme vijigīṣ siṃhānām iva saṃhrādaḥ divam urvīm ca nādayan āsīt kilakilā śabdaḥ tala śaṅkha ravaiḥ saha jajñire siṃhanādāḥ ca śūrāṇām pratigarjatām talatra abhihatāḥ ca eva jyā śabdāḥ bharata ṛṣabha pattīnām pāda śabdāḥ ca vājinām ca mahā svanāḥ tottra aṅkuśa nipātāḥ ca āyudhānām ca nisvanāḥ ghaṇṭā śabdāḥ ca nāgānām anyonyam abhidhāvatām te manaḥ krūram ādhāya samabhityakta jīvitāḥ svayam śāṃtanavaḥ rājan abhyadhāvat dhanaṃjayam pragṛhya kārmukam ghoram kāla daṇḍa upamam raṇe arjunaḥ api dhanuḥ gṛhya gāṇḍīvam loka viśrutam abhyadhāvata tejasvī gāṅgeyam raṇa mūrdhani gāṅgeyaḥ tu raṇe pārtham viddhvā na akampayat balī tathā eva pāṇḍavaḥ rājan bhīṣmam na akampayat yudhi sātyakiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam kṛtavarmā ca sātyakim tau śara ācita sarva aṅgau śuśubhāte mahā balau vasante puṣpa śabalau puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau tatas kosalakaḥ rājā saubhadrasya viśām pate bṛhadbalam mahā rāja vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ atha aparābhyām bhallābhyām pītābhyām ari mardanaḥ anyonyam ca śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kruddhau rājan tatakṣatuḥ māninam samare dṛptam kṛta vairam mahā ratham anyonyam śara varṣābhyām vavṛṣāte raṇa ajire vismayaḥ sarva bhūtānām samapadyata bhārata tasya mādrī sutaḥ ketum sa śaram ca śarāsanam atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārdayat yuga īṣām cicchide bāṇaiḥ dhvajam ca eva nyapātayat vivyādha śara varṣeṇa yatamānam mahā āhave śareṇa bhṛśa tīkṣṇena pātayām āsa sārathim trāsayetām śaraiḥ ghoraiḥ kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ svayam rājā madra rājānam abhyayāt tasya madra adhipaḥ cāpam dvidhā ciccheda māriṣa tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas madra īśvaram rājā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ chādayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya droṇaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ parāsu karaṇam dṛḍham śaram ca eva mahā ghoram kāla daṇḍam iva aparam atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sāyakān ca caturdaśa tau anyonyam su saṃkruddhau cakratuḥ su bhṛśam raṇam pratyudyayau mahā rāja tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tayoḥ samabhavat yuddham ghora rūpam viśām pate dṛptayoḥ samare tūrṇam vṛtra vāsavayoḥ iva vāhlīkam tu raṇe kruddham kruddha rūpaḥ viśām pate abhyadravat ameya ātmā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā rathaḥ vāhlīkaḥ tu tatas rājan dhṛṣṭaketum amarṣaṇam cedi rājaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ vāhlīkam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ samīyatuḥ su saṃkruddhau aṅgāraka budhau iva rākṣasam krūra karmāṇam krūra karmā ghaṭotkacaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasam tam mahā balam navatyā sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ dārayām āsa bhārata bahudhā vārayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ śikhaṇḍī samare rājñ drauṇim abhyudyayau balī aśvatthāmā tatas kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍinam avasthitam nārācena su tīkṣṇena bhṛśam viddhvā vyakampayat śikhaṇḍī api tatas rājñ droṇaputram atāḍayat sāyakena su pītena tīkṣṇena niśitena ca bhagadattam raṇe śūram virāṭaḥ vāhinīpatiḥ virāṭaḥ bhagadattena śara varṣeṇa tāḍitaḥ abhyavarṣat su saṃkruddhaḥ meghaḥ vṛṣṭyā iva acalam bhagadattaḥ tatas tūrṇam virāṭam pṛthivīpatim bṛhatkṣatram tu kaikeyam kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yayau tam kṛpaḥ śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata gautamam kekayaḥ kruddhaḥ śara vṛṣṭyā abhyapūrayat tau anyonyam hayān hatvā vinikṛtya vai abhyudyayau saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ hṛṣṭa rūpam paraṃtapa īkṣitṛ prīti jananam śukra aṅgārakayoḥ iva suśarmāṇam nara vyāghram cekitānaḥ mahā rathaḥ abhyadravat su saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍava arthe parākramī suśarmā tu mahā rāja cekitānam mahā ratham mahatā śara varṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyuge cekitānaḥ api saṃrabdhaḥ suśarmāṇam mahā āhave śakuniḥ prativindhyam tu parākrāntam parākramī yaudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ saubalam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vyadārayat mahā prājñaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sudakṣiṇam tu rāja indra kāmbojānām mahā ratham śrutakarmā tatas kruddhaḥ kāmbojānām mahā ratham irāvān atha saṃkruddhaḥ śrutāyuṣam amarṣaṇam śrutāyuḥ tu atha saṃkruddhaḥ phālguneḥ samare hayān sa senam sa sutam vīram saṃsasajjatuḥ āhave tatra adbhutam apaśyāma āvantyānām parākramam kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca gāndhārān pañca māriṣa sa sainyāḥ te sa sainyān ca yodhayām āsuḥ āhave vīrabāhuḥ ca te putraḥ vairāṭim ratha sattamam uttaram yodhayām āsa vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ulūkam tu śatānīkaḥ śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ āvṛṇot uttaraḥ ca api tam dhīram vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ulūkaḥ ca api tam bāṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ lomavāhibhiḥ evam dvaṃdva sahasrāṇi ratha vāraṇa vājinām padātīnām ca samare tava teṣām ca saṃkulam aśvaḥ aśvam samabhipretya padātiḥ ca padātinam śūrāṇām samare tatra samāsādya parasparam tatra devarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ cāraṇāḥ ca samāgatāḥ tatas danti sahasrāṇi rathānām ca api māriṣa aśva oghāḥ puruṣa oghāḥ ca viparītam samāyayuḥ uvāca rājan śata sahasrāṇi tatra tatra tadā tadā na bhrātā bhrātaram tatra svasrīyam na ca mātulaḥ mātulam na ca svasrīyaḥ na sakhāyam sakhā tathā āviṣṭāḥ iva yudhyante pāṇḍavāḥ kurubhiḥ saha ratha anīkam nara vyāghrāḥ ke cid abhyapatan rathaiḥ ratha īṣāḥ ca ratha īṣābhiḥ kūbarāḥ ratha kūbaraiḥ saṃhatāḥ saṃhataiḥ ke cid paraspara jighāṃsavaḥ prabhinnāḥ tu mahā kāyāḥ saṃnipatya gajāḥ gajaiḥ bahudhā adārayan kruddhāḥ viṣāṇaiḥ itaretaram sa tomara patākaiḥ ca vāraṇāḥ para vāraṇaiḥ abhinītāḥ ca śikṣābhiḥ tottra aṅkuśa samāhatāḥ su prabhinnāḥ prabhinnānām saṃmukha abhimukhāḥ yayuḥ samyak praṇītāḥ nāgāḥ ca prabhinna karaṭāmukhāḥ ṛṣṭi tomara nārācaiḥ nirviddhāḥ vara vāraṇāḥ gajānām pādarakṣāḥ tu vyūḍha uraskāḥ prahāriṇaḥ ṛṣṭibhiḥ ca dhanurbhiḥ ca vimalaiḥ ca paraśvadhaiḥ gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva bhindipālaiḥ sa tomaraiḥ āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ ca eva nistriṃśaiḥ vimalaiḥ śitaiḥ pragṛhītaiḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ dhāvamānāḥ tatas tatas vyadṛśyanta mahā rāja paraspara jighāṃsavaḥ rājamānāḥ ca nistriṃśāḥ saṃsiktāḥ nara śoṇitaiḥ pratyadṛśyanta śūrāṇām anyonyam abhidhāvatām avakṣipta avadhūtānām asīnām vīra bāhubhiḥ saṃjajñe tumulaḥ śabdaḥ patatām para marmasu gadā musala rugṇānām bhinnānām ca vara asibhiḥ danti dantau abhinnānām mṛditānām ca dantibhiḥ tatra tatra nara oghāṇām krośatām itaretaram śuśruvuḥ dāruṇāḥ vācaḥ pretānām iva bhārata hayaiḥ api haya ārohāḥ cāmara āpīḍa dhāribhiḥ taiḥ vimuktāḥ mahā prāsāḥ jāmbūnada vibhūṣaṇāḥ āśugāḥ vimalāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetuḥ bhujaga upamāḥ śirāṃsi ādadire vīrāḥ rathinām aśva sādinaḥ rathī jaghāna saṃprāpya bāṇa gocaram āgatān naga megha pratīkāśāḥ ca ākṣipya turagān gajāḥ pādaiḥ eva avamṛdnanta mattāḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇāḥ pāṭyamāneṣu kumbheṣu pārśveṣu api ca vāraṇāḥ prāsaiḥ vinihatāḥ ke cid vineduḥ parama āturāḥ sa aśva ārohān hayān ke cid unmathya vara vāraṇāḥ sa aśva ārohān viṣāṇa agraiḥ utkṣipya turagān dvipāḥ sa aśva ārohān hayān jaghnuḥ karaiḥ sa caraṇaiḥ tathā ke cit ākṣipya kariṇaḥ sa aśvān api rathān karaiḥ vikarṣantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ samīyuḥ sarva śabda gāḥ pratimāneṣu gātreṣu pārśveṣu abhi ca vāraṇān muktāḥ tu rathibhiḥ bāṇāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ su tejanāḥ te nipetuḥ akuṇṭha agrāḥ nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu ca āśugāḥ vimalāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetuḥ bhujaga upamāḥ nara aśva kāyān nirbhidya lauhāni kavacāni ca nipetuḥ vimalāḥ śaktyaḥ vīra bāhubhiḥ arpitāḥ mahā ulkā pratimāḥ ghorāḥ tatra tatra viśām pate vidarśayantaḥ saṃpetuḥ khaḍga carma paraśvadhaiḥ śaktibhiḥ dāritāḥ ke cid saṃchinnāḥ ca paraśvadhaiḥ hastibhiḥ mṛditāḥ ke cid kṣuṇṇāḥ ca anye turaṃgamaiḥ ratha nemi nikṛttāḥ ca nikṛttāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ putrān anye pitṝn anye bhrātṝn ca saha bāndhavaiḥ mātulān bhāgineyān ca parān api ca saṃyuge vikīrṇa antrāḥ su bahavaḥ bhagna sakthāḥ ca bhārata bāhubhiḥ su bhuja ācchinnaiḥ pārśveṣu ca vidāritāḥ krandantaḥ samadṛśyanta tṛṣitāḥ jīvita īpsavaḥ tṛṣṇā parigatāḥ ke cid alpa sattvāḥ viśām pate rudhira ogha pariklinnāḥ kliśyamānāḥ ca bhārata vyanindan bhṛśam ātmānam tava putrān ca saṃgatān apare kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ kṛta vairāḥ parasparam nirdaśya daśanaiḥ ca api krodhāt chadān tarjayitvā su saṃhṛṣṭāḥ yāvat prāṇasya dhāraṇam apare kliśyamānāḥ tu vraṇa ārtāḥ śara pīḍitāḥ niṣkūjāḥ samapadyanta dṛḍha sattvāḥ mahā balāḥ anye tu virathāḥ śūrāḥ ratham anyasya saṃyuge prārthayānāḥ nipatitāḥ saṃkṣuṇṇāḥ vara vāraṇaiḥ aśobhanta mahā rāja puṣpitāḥ iva kiṃśukāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ anīkeṣu bahavaḥ bhairava svanāḥ svasrīyaḥ mātulam ca api svasrīyam ca api mātulaḥ sakhāyam ca sakhā rājan saṃbandhī bāndhavam tathā evam yuyudhire tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhīṣmam āsādya pārthānām vāhinī samakampata ketunā pañca tāreṇa tālena bharata ṛṣabha babhau bhīṣmaḥ tadā rājñ candramāḥ iva meruṇā uvāca gata pūrvāhṇa bhūyiṣṭhe tasmin ahani dāruṇe durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ viviṃśatiḥ bhīṣmam jugupuḥ āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vijagāhe mahā rathaḥ cedi kāśi karūṣeṣu pāñcāleṣu ca bhārata bhīṣmasya bahudhā tālaḥ caran ketuḥ adṛśyata śirāṃsi ca tadā bhīṣmaḥ bāhūn ca api saha āyudhān dhanūṃṣi rathinām bhīṣmaḥ sa utsedhāni śirāṃsi ca bāhūn api tathā ca ūrūn rathān ca vipula dhvajān ekaikena tu mātaṃgāḥ nārācena mahātmanā tāḍitāḥ sahasā jagmuḥ pṛthivīm parvata upamāḥ ke cit ārta svaram cakruḥ nāgāḥ marmaṇi tāḍitāḥ durādharṣaḥ tu śatrūṇām manāṃsi samakampayat hayān ca sa haya ārohān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ maṇḍalāni ca vīthīḥ ca go mūtrāṇi ca bhārata anyān ca su bahūn mārgān rathena ratha kovidaḥ vismāpayan śatru saṃghān vyacarat jāhnavīsutaḥ saṃyuktam ratham āsthāya prāyāt bhīṣma ratham prati jāmbūnada vicitreṇa karṇikāreṇa ketunā abhyavarṣata bhīṣmam ca tān ca eva ratha sattamān sa tālaketoḥ tīkṣṇena ketum āhatya pattriṇā bhīṣmeṇa yuyudhe vīraḥ tasya ca anucaraiḥ saha kṛtavarmāṇam ekena śalyam pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ pūrṇa āyata visṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena ca jahāra sāratheḥ kāyāt śiraḥ saṃnata parvaṇā viviṃśatiḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ sarva āvaraṇa bhedibhiḥ kṛpasya niśita agreṇa tān ca tīkṣṇa mukhaiḥ śaraiḥ labdha lakṣya tayā karṣṇeḥ sarve bhīṣma mukhāḥ rathāḥ diśaḥ paryapatat cāpam gāṇḍīvam iva ghoṣavat tam āsādya mahā vegaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ vivyādha samare tūrṇam ārjunim para vīra hā sārathim ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna yata vrataḥ tathā eva kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ ca māriṣa viviṃśatiḥ tathā rājan sarve viddhvā mahā rathāḥ viddhvā na akampayat kārṣṇim mainākam iva parvatam sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūraḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi kārṣṇiḥ pañca rathān prati tatas teṣām mahā astrāṇi saṃvārya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ nanāda balavān kārṣṇiḥ bhīṣmāya visṛjan śarān yatamānasya samare bhīṣmam ardayataḥ śaraiḥ parākrāntasya tasya eva bhīṣmaḥ api prāhiṇot śarān sa tān ciccheda samare bhīṣma cāpa cyutān śarān sa rājataḥ mahā skandhaḥ tālaḥ hema vibhūṣitaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaḥ anadat dhṛṣṭaḥ saubhadram abhiharṣayan atha bhīṣmaḥ mahā astrāṇi divyāni ca bahūni ca prāduścakre mahā raudraḥ kṣaṇe tasmin mahā balaḥ avākirat ameya ātmā śarāṇām nata parvaṇām tatas daśa mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ virāṭaḥ saha putreṇa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ bhīmaḥ ca kekayāḥ ca eva sātyakiḥ ca viśām pate javena āpatatām teṣām bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ raṇe pāñcālyam tribhiḥ ānarchat sātyakim niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata visṛṣṭena kṣureṇa niśitena ca papāta bhīmasenasya bhīṣmeṇa mathitaḥ rathāt bhīmasenaḥ tribhiḥ viddhvā bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam raṇe kṛpam ekena vivyādha kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ pragṛhīta agra hastena vairāṭiḥ api dantinā śalyaḥ nivārayām āsa vegam apratimam raṇe tasya kruddhaḥ sa nāga indraḥ bṛhataḥ sādhu vāhinaḥ padā yugam adhiṣṭhāya jaghāna caturaḥ hayān sa hata aśve rathe tiṣṭhan madra adhipatiḥ āyasīm uttara anta karīm śaktim cikṣepa bhujaga upamām tayā bhinna tanutrāṇaḥ praviśya vipulam tamaḥ bhinna marmā śara vrātaiḥ chinna hastaḥ sa vāraṇaḥ bhīmam ārta svaram kṛtvā papāta ca mamāra ca etat īdṛśakam kṛtvā madra rājaḥ mahā rathaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam bhāsvaram kṛtavarmaṇaḥ uttaram nihatam dṛṣṭvā vairāṭiḥ bhrātaram śubham kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitam dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitam śvetaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāṭ iva sa visphārya mahat cāpam śakra cāpa upamam balī abhyadhāvat jighāṃsan vai śalyam madra adhipam balī mahatā ratha vaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥ muñcan bāṇa mayam varṣam prāyāt śalya ratham prati tāvakānām rathāḥ sapta samantāt paryavārayan madra rājam abhīpsantaḥ mṛtyoḥ daṃṣṭra antaram gatam tathā rukmarathaḥ rājan śalya putraḥ pratāpavān vinda anuvindau āvantyau kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ saindhavaḥ ca jayadrathaḥ nānā varṇa vicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca mahātmanām visphāritāni dṛśyante toyadeṣu iva vidyutaḥ te tu bāṇa mayam varṣam śveta mūrdhani apātayan dhanūṃṣi teṣām ācchidya mamarda pṛtanāpatiḥ nikṛttāni eva tāni sma samadṛśyanta bhārata sapta ca eva pṛṣatkān ca śvetasya upari apātayan tatas punar ameya ātmā bhallaiḥ sapta āśugaiḥ nicakarta mahā bāhuḥ teṣām cāpāni dhanvinām te nikṛtta mahā cāpāḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ ratha śaktīḥ parāmṛśya vineduḥ bhairavān ravān tatas tāḥ jvalitāḥ sapta mahā indra aśani nisvanāḥ tatas samādāya śaram sarva kāya vidāraṇam prāhiṇot bharata śreṣṭha śvetaḥ rukmaratham prati tatas rukmarathaḥ rājan sāyakena dṛḍha āhataḥ niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalam ca āviśat mahat tam visaṃjñam vimanasam tvaramāṇaḥ tu sārathiḥ tatas anyān ṣaṭ samādāya śvetaḥ hema vibhūṣitān teṣām ṣaṇṇām mahā bāhuḥ dhvaja śīrṣāṇi apātayat hayān ca teṣām nirbhidya sārathīn ca paraṃtapa śaraiḥ ca etān samākīrya prāyāt śalya ratham prati dṛṣṭvā senāpatim tūrṇam yāntam śalya ratham prati tatas bhīṣmam puraskṛtya tava putraḥ mahā balaḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca vyatiṣikta ratha dvipam kaikeye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣate uvāca vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ evam śvete mahā iṣvāse prāpte śalya ratham prati kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ ca kim akurvata saṃjaya uvāca bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kim vā tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ rājan śata sahasrāṇi tatas kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ śvetam senāpatim śūram puraskṛtya mahā rathāḥ śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya trātum aicchat mahā rathāḥ jighāṃsantam yudhām śreṣṭham tadā āsīt tumulam mahat tāvakānām pareṣām ca yathā yuddham avartata tatra akarot rathopasthān śūnyān śāṃtanavaḥ bahūn prākṛntat uttamāṅgāni śaraiḥ ārchat ratha uttamān tena ājau preṣitāḥ rājan śarāḥ śata sahasraśas kṣatriya anta karāḥ saṃkhye mahā vegāḥ mahā balāḥ śirāṃsi pātayām āsuḥ vīrāṇām śataśas raṇe gajān kaṇṭaka saṃnāhān vajreṇa iva śiloccayān rathāḥ ratheṣu saṃsaktāḥ vyadṛśanta viśām pate yuvānam nihatam vīram lambamānam sa kārmukam udīrṇāḥ ca hayāḥ rājan vahantaḥ tatra tatra ha baddha khaḍga niṣaṅgāḥ ca vidhvasta śirasaḥ hatāḥ śataśas patitāḥ bhūmau vīra śayyāsu śerate paraspareṇa dhāvantaḥ patitāḥ punar utthitāḥ pīḍitāḥ punar anyonyam luṭhantaḥ raṇa mūrdhani sa cāpān sa niṣaṅgān ca jātarūpa pariṣkṛtān visrabdha hata vīrāḥ ca śataśas paripīḍitāḥ hata sārathiḥ api uccais papāta kāṣṭha vat rathaḥ dhanuḥ kūjita vijñānam tatra āsīt pratiyudhyataḥ gātra sparśena yodhānām vyajñāsta paripanthinam yudhyamānam śaraiḥ rājan siñjinī dhvajinī ravāt anyonyam vīra saṃśabdaḥ na aśrūyata bhaṭaiḥ kṛtaḥ śabdāyamāne saṃgrāme paṭahe karṇa dāriṇi na aśrauṣīt nāma gotra uktim kīrtanam ca parasparam bhīṣma cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ ārtānām yudhyatām mṛdhe paraspareṣām vīrāṇām manāṃsi samakampayan pitā putram ca samare na abhijānāti kaḥ cana ākṣiptaḥ syandanāt vīraḥ sa sārathiḥ ajihmagaiḥ evam ca samare sarve vīrāḥ ca virathīkṛtāḥ tena tena sma dṛśyante dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ ahataḥ kaḥ api na eva āsīt bhīṣme nighnati śātravān śvetaḥ kurūṇām akarot svayam tasmin mahā āhave rāja putrān ratha udārān avadhīt śata saṃghaśas ciccheda rathinām bāṇaiḥ śirāṃsi bharata ṛṣabha sa aṅgadāḥ bāhavaḥ ca eva dhanūṃṣi ca samantataḥ ratha īṣām ratha cakrāṇi tūṇīrāṇi yugāni ca chatrāṇi ca mahārhāni patākāḥ ca viśām pate haya oghāḥ ca ratha oghāḥ ca nara oghāḥ ca eva bhārata vāraṇāḥ śataśas ca eva hatāḥ śvetena bhārata avaśiṣṭāḥ tathā paścāt vibhum paśyāma dhṛṣṇavaḥ bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam yuddhe sthitāḥ paśyāma sarvaśas adīnaḥ dīna samaye bhīṣmaḥ naḥ mahā āhave ādadānaḥ iva prāṇān savitā śiśirātyaye sa mumoca mahā iṣvāsaḥ śara saṃghān anekaśas te vadhyamānāḥ bhīṣmeṇa prajahuḥ tam mahā balam sva yūthāt iva te yūthāt muktam bhūmiṣu dāruṇam tam ekam upalabhya ekaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ paraṃtapa pātayām āsa sainyāni pāṇḍavānām viśām pate dṛṣṭvā senāpatim bhīṣmaḥ tvaritaḥ śvetam abhyayāt sa bhīṣmam śara jālena mahatā samavākirat śvetam ca api tathā bhīṣmaḥ śara oghaiḥ samavākirat bhīṣmaḥ śvetaḥ ca yuyudhe paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ eka ahnā nirdahet bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm pitāmaham tatas dṛṣṭvā śvetena vimukhīkṛtam praharṣam pāṇḍavāḥ jagmuḥ putraḥ te vimanāḥ bhavat sa sainyaḥ pāṇḍava anīkam abhyadravata saṃyuge durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ viśām pate bhīṣmam jugupuḥ āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥ dṛṣṭvā tu pārthivaiḥ sarvaiḥ duryodhana purogamaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vadhyamānāni saṃyuge śvetaḥ gāṅgeyam utsṛjya tava putrasya vāhinīm nāśayām āsa vegena vāyuḥ vṛkṣān iva ojasā drāvayitvā camūm rājan vairāṭiḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ nigṛhya kārmukam śvetaḥ bhīṣmam vivyādha sapta śvetaḥ śāṃtanavam bhūyas śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tam pratyavidhyat daśabhiḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā vairāṭiḥ samare kruddhaḥ bhṛśam āyamya kārmukam ājaghāna tatas bhīṣmam śvetaḥ kṣatriya nandanaḥ saṃprahasya tatas śvetaḥ parisaṃlihan dhanuḥ ciccheda bhīṣmasya navabhiḥ daśadhā śaraiḥ saṃdhāya viśikham ca eva śaram loma pravāhinam unmamātha tatas tālam dhvaja śīrṣam mahātmanaḥ ketum nipatitam dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya tanayāḥ tava pāṇḍavāḥ ca api saṃhṛṣṭāḥ dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yutāḥ bhīṣmasya patitam ketum dṛṣṭvā tālam mahātmanaḥ yatnāt bhīṣmam parīpsadhvam rakṣamāṇāḥ samantataḥ mā naḥ prapaśyamānānām śvetāt mṛtyum avāpsyati bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śūraḥ tathā satyam bravīmi vaḥ rājñaḥ tu vacanam śrutvā tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ vāhlīkaḥ kṛtavarmā ca śalaḥ śalyaḥ ca bhārata jalasaṃdhaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca citrasenaḥ viviṃśatiḥ tvaramāṇāḥ tvarā kāle parivārya samantataḥ śastra vṛṣṭim su tumulām śvetasya upari apātayan tān kruddhaḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ avārayat ameya ātmā darśayan pāṇi lāghavam sa nivārya tu tān sarvān kesarī kuñjarān iva mahatā śara varṣeṇa bhīṣmasya dhanuḥ ācchinat tatas anyat dhanuḥ ādāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yudhi śvetam vivyādha rāja indra kaṅka pattraiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas senāpatiḥ kruddhaḥ bhīṣmam bahubhiḥ āyasaiḥ tatas pravyathitaḥ rājā bhīṣmam dṛṣṭvā nivāritam niṣṭhānakaḥ ca su mahān tava sainyasya ca abhavat tam vīram vāritam dṛṣṭvā śvetena śara vikṣatam dhvajam unmathitam dṛṣṭvā tām ca senām nivāritām śvetam prati mahā rāja vyasṛjat sāyakān bahūn tān āvārya raṇe śvetaḥ bhīṣmasya rathinām varaḥ utsṛjya kārmukam rājan gāṅgeyaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ tatra saṃdhāya vipulān bhallān sapta śilā śitān caturbhiḥ ca jaghāna aśvān śvetasya pṛtanāpateḥ hata aśva sūtāt sa rathāt avaplutya mahā balaḥ viratham rathinām śreṣṭham śvetam dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ tāḍayām āsa niśitaiḥ śara saṃghaiḥ samantataḥ sa tāḍyamānaḥ samare bhīṣma cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ sva rathe dhanuḥ utsṛjya śaktim jagrāha kāñcanīm tatas śaktim raṇe śvetaḥ jagrāha ugrām mahā bhayām kāla daṇḍa upamām ghorām mṛtyoḥ iva svasām śvasan abravīt ca tadā śvetaḥ bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam raṇe tiṣṭha idānīm su saṃrabdhaḥ paśya mām puruṣaḥ bhava evam uktvā mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhīṣmam yudhi parākramī tatas śaktim ameya ātmā cikṣepa bhujaga upamām pāṇḍava arthe parākrāntaḥ tava anartham cikīrṣati hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt putrāṇām te viśām pate dṛṣṭvā śaktim mahā ghorām mṛtyoḥ daṇḍa sama prabhām jvalantīm antarikṣe tām jvālābhiḥ iva saṃvṛtām aṣṭabhiḥ navabhiḥ bhīṣmaḥ śaktim ciccheda pattribhiḥ utkṛṣṭa hema vikṛtām nikṛttām niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā vairāṭiḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ gadām jagrāha saṃhṛṣṭaḥ bhīṣmasya nidhanam prati krodhena rakta nayanaḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ tasya vegam a saṃvārya matvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavān prahāra vipramokṣa artham sahasā dharaṇīm gataḥ śvetaḥ krodha samāviṣṭaḥ bhrāmayitvā tu tām gadām tayā bhīṣma nipātinyā sa rathaḥ bhasmasāt kṛtaḥ viratham rathinām śreṣṭham bhīṣmam dṛṣṭvā ratha uttamāḥ abhyadhāvanta sahitāḥ śalya prabhṛtayaḥ rathāḥ etasmin antare bhīṣmaḥ śuśrāva vipulām giram ākāśāt īritām divyām ātmanaḥ hita saṃbhavām bhīṣma bhīṣma mahā bāho śīghram yatnam kuruṣva vai eṣa hi asya jaye kālaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ viśvayoninā saṃprahṛṣṭa manāḥ bhūtvā vadhe tasya manaḥ dadhe viratham rathinām śreṣṭham śvetam dṛṣṭvā padātinam sātyakiḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ kaikeyaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca abhimanyuḥ ca vīryavān etān āpatataḥ sarvān droṇa śalya kṛpaiḥ saha avārayat ameya ātmā vāri vegān iva acalaḥ sa niruddheṣu sarveṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu śvetaḥ khaḍgam atha ākṛṣya bhīṣmasya dhanuḥ ācchinat tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam tvaramāṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ pitā te bharata śreṣṭha śvetam dṛṣṭvā mahā rathaiḥ abhyavartata gāṅgeyaḥ śvetam senāpatim drutam āpatantam tatas bhīṣmaḥ bhīmasenam pratāpavān ājaghne viśikhaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā senānyam sa mahā rathaḥ ājaghne bharata śreṣṭhaḥ tribhiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sātyakim ca śatena ājau bharatānām pitāmahaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca viṃśatyā kaikeyam ca api pañcabhiḥ tān ca sarvān mahā iṣvāsān pitā devavrataḥ tava tatas śaram mṛtyu samam bhāra sādhanam uttamam vikṛṣya balavān bhīṣmaḥ samādhatta durāsadam brahmāstreṇa su saṃyuktam tam śaram lomavāhinam dadṛśuḥ deva gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ jagāma dharaṇīm bāṇaḥ mahā aśaniḥ iva jvalan astam gacchan yathā ādityaḥ prabhām ādāya sa tvaraḥ evam jīvitam ādāya śveta dehāt jagāma ha tam bhīṣmeṇa nara vyāghram tathā vinihatam yudhi prapatantam apaśyāma gireḥ śṛṅgam iva cyutam aśocan pāṇḍavāḥ tatra kṣatriyāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ ca sutāḥ tubhyam kuravaḥ ca api sarvaśas tatas duḥśāsanaḥ rājan śvetam dṛṣṭvā nipātitam tasmin hate mahā iṣvāse bhīṣmeṇa āhava śobhinā prāvepanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ śikhaṇḍi pramukhāḥ rathāḥ tatas dhanaṃjayaḥ rājan vārṣṇeyaḥ ca api sarvaśas avahāram śanais cakruḥ nihate vāhinīpatau tatas avahāraḥ sainyānām te teṣām ca bhārata tāvakānām pareṣām ca nardatām ca muhur muhur pārthāḥ vimanasaḥ bhūtvā nyaviśanta mahā rathāḥ uvāca śvete senāpatau tāta saṃgrāme nihate paraiḥ kim akurvan mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha senāpatim samākarṇya śvetam yudhi nipātitam tad artham yatatām ca api pareṣām prapalāyinām manaḥ prīṇāti me vākyam jayam saṃjaya śṛṇvataḥ kṛtam vairam sadā tena pituḥ putreṇa dhīmatā tasya udvega bhayāt ca api saṃśritaḥ pāṇḍavān purā sarvam balam parityajya durgam saṃśritya tiṣṭhati pāṇḍavānām pratāpena durgam deśam niveśya ca sapatnān satatam bādhan ārya vṛttim anuṣṭhitaḥ āścaryam vai sadā teṣām purā rājñām su durmatiḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhire bhaktaḥ katham saṃjaya sūditaḥ prakṣiptaḥ saṃmataḥ kṣudraḥ putraḥ me puruṣa adhamaḥ na yuddham rocayet bhīṣmaḥ na ca ācāryaḥ katham cana na kṛpaḥ na ca gāndhārī na aham saṃjaya rocaye na vāsudevaḥ vārṣṇeyaḥ dharmarājaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ vāryamāṇaḥ mayā nityam gāndhāryā vidureṇa ca jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa vyāsena ca mahātmanā duḥśāsanasya ca tathā pāṇḍavān anvasūyata tasya aham vyasanam ghoram manye prāptam tu saṃjaya saṃkruddhaḥ kṛṣṇa sahitaḥ pārthaḥ kim akarot yudhi sa hi śūraḥ ca kaunteyaḥ kṣiprakārī ca pāṇḍavaḥ manye śaraiḥ śarīrāṇi pramathiṣyati vidviṣām amogha krodha saṃkalpam dṛṣṭvā vaḥ kim abhūt manaḥ vajra saṃsparśa rūpāṇām astrāṇām nyāsa kāri tā sa khaḍga ākṣepa hastaḥ tu ghoṣam cakre mahā rathaḥ sa saṃjaya mahā prājñaḥ drupadasya ātmajaḥ balī manye manaḥ prajajvāla pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām teṣām krodham cintayan tu ahaḥsu ca niśāsu ca uvāca gata pūrvāhṇa bhūyiṣṭhe tasmin ahani dāruṇe tāvakānām pareṣām ca punar yuddham avartata śvetam tu nihatam dṛṣṭvā virāṭasya camūpatim kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitam dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitam śaṅkhaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāṭ iva abhyadhāvat jighāṃsan vai śalyam madra adhipam balī mahatā ratha vaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥ sṛjan bāṇa mayam varṣam prāyāt śalya ratham prati tāvakānām rathāḥ sapta samantāt paryavārayan madra rājam parīpsantaḥ mṛtyoḥ daṃṣṭra antaram gatam tāla mātram dhanuḥ gṛhya śaṅkham abhyadravat raṇe tam udyatam udīkṣya atha mahā iṣvāsam mahā balam saṃtrastā pāṇḍavā senā vāta vega hatā iva nauḥ tatra arjunaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ śaṅkhasya āsīt puraḥsaraḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt yodhānām yudhi yudhyatām atha śalyaḥ gadā pāṇiḥ avatīrya mahā rathāt sa hata aśvāt rathāt tūrṇam khaḍgam ādāya vidrutaḥ bībhatsoḥ syandanam prāpya tatas śāntim avindata tatas bhīṣma rathāt tūrṇam utpatanti patatriṇaḥ pāñcālān atha matsyam ca drupadam senayā vṛtam pāñcālān atha matsyān ca kekayān ca prabhadrakān bhīṣmaḥ praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ pātayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥ utsṛjya samare tūrṇam pāṇḍavam savyasācinam abhyadravata pāñcālyam drupadam senayā vṛtam priyam saṃbandhinam rājan śarān avakiran bahūn atiṣṭhata raṇe bhīṣmaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ na śekuḥ pāṇḍaveyasya yodhāḥ bhīṣmam nirīkṣitum vīkṣām cakruḥ samantāt te pāṇḍavāḥ bhaya pīḍitāḥ trātāram na adhyagacchanta gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva sā tu yaudhiṣṭhirā senā gāṅgeya śara pīḍitā hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt pāṇḍu sainyeṣu bhārata tatas bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ nityam maṇḍala kārmukaḥ mumoca bāṇān dīpta agrān ahīn āśīviṣān iva śaraiḥ ekāyanīkurvan diśaḥ sarvāḥ yata vrataḥ jaghāna pāṇḍava rathān ādiśya ādiśya bhārata prāpte ca astam dinakare na prājñāyata kim cana bhīṣmam ca dṛṣṭvā pārthāḥ mahā āhave uvāca bhīṣme ca yudhi saṃrabdhe hṛṣṭe duryodhane tathā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ sarvaiḥ ca eva janeśvaraiḥ śucā paramayā yuktaḥ cintayānaḥ parājayam vārṣṇeyam abravīt rājan dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam kṛṣṇa paśya mahā iṣvāsam bhīṣmam bhīma parākramam śaraiḥ dahantam sainyam mama grīṣme kakṣam iva analam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahā rāja dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam atha abravīt katham enam mahātmānam śakṣyāmaḥ prativīkṣitum etam hi puruṣa vyāghram dhanuṣmantam mahā balam dṛṣṭvā vipradrutam sainyam madīyam mārgaṇa āhatam śakyaḥ jetum yamaḥ kruddhaḥ vajrapāṇiḥ ca saṃyuge varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛt ca api kuberaḥ vā gadā dharaḥ na tu bhīṣmaḥ mahā tejāḥ śakyaḥ jetum mahā balaḥ saḥ aham evam gate magnaḥ bhīṣma agādha jale a plavaḥ ātmanaḥ buddhi daurbalyāt bhīṣmam āsādya keśava na tu imān pṛthivīpālān dātum bhīṣmāya mṛtyave kṣapayiṣyati senām mama kṛṣṇa bhīṣmaḥ mahā astra vid yathā analam prajvalitam pataṃgāḥ samabhidrutāḥ kṣayam nītaḥ asmi vārṣṇeya rājya hetoḥ parākramī bhrātaraḥ ca eva mama vīrāḥ karśitāḥ śara pīḍitāḥ mad kṛte bhrātṛ sauhārdāt rājyāt bhraṣṭāḥ tathā sukhāt jīvitasya hi śeṣeṇa tapaḥ tapsyāmi duścaram na ghātayiṣyāmi raṇe mitrāṇi imā keśava ghātayati aniśam bhīṣmaḥ pravarāṇām prahāriṇām kim nu kṛtvā kṛtam me syāt brūhi mādhava māciram ekaḥ bhīmaḥ param śaktyā yudhyati eṣa mahā bhujaḥ gadayā vīra ghātinyā yathotsāham mahāmanāḥ na alam eṣa kṣayam kartum para sainyasya māriṣa nirdahyamānān bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā divyāni astrāṇi bhīṣmasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ dhakṣyanti kṣatriyān sarvān prayuktāni punar punar kṛṣṇa bhīṣmaḥ su saṃrabdhaḥ sahitaḥ sarva pārthivaiḥ kṣapayiṣyati naḥ nūnam yādṛśaḥ asya parākramaḥ sa tvam paśya mahā iṣvāsam yogīṣvara mahā ratham yaḥ bhīṣmam śamayet saṃkhye dāva agnim jaladaḥ yathā te prasādāt govinda pāṇḍavāḥ nihata dviṣaḥ sva rājyam anusaṃprāptāḥ modiṣyanti sa bāndhavāḥ evam uktvā tatas pārthaḥ dhyāyan āste mahā manāḥ śoka ārtam pāṇḍavam jñātvā duḥkhena hata cetasam mā śucaḥ bharata śreṣṭha na tvam śocitum arhasi yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ sarva lokasya dhanvinaḥ aham ca priya kṛt rājan sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ virāṭa drupadau vṛddhau dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ tvad prasādam pratīkṣante tvad bhaktāḥ ca viśām pate eṣa te pārṣataḥ nityam hita kāmaḥ priye rataḥ senāpatyam anuprāptaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā balaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahā bāho bhīṣmasya nidhanam kila sa tvam puruṣa śārdūla śārdūla sama vikrama etat śrutvā tatas rājā dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā ratham abravīt samitau tasyām vāsudevasya śṛṇvataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna nibodha idam yat tvā vakṣyāmi māriṣa bhavān senāpatiḥ mahyam vāsudevena saṃmataḥ kārttikeyaḥ yathā nityam devānām abhavat purā tathā tvam api pāṇḍūnām senā nīḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha sa tvam puruṣa śārdūla vikramya jahi kauravān aham ca tvā anuyāsyāmi bhīmaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca māriṣa mādrī putrau ca sahitau draupadeyāḥ ca daṃśitāḥ ye ca anye pṛthivīpālāḥ pradhānāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha etāvat uktvā nṛpatiḥ sahadevam abhāṣata abhiṣekasya saṃbhārān kṣipram ānaya vai javāt prādurāsīt tatas dhaumyaḥ saṃbhārān gṛhya bhārata tatas uddharṣayan sarvān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ abhyabhāṣata aham droṇa antakaḥ pārtha vihitaḥ śambhunā purā raṇe bhīṣmam tathā droṇam kṛpam śalyam jayadratham atha utkruṣṭam mahā iṣvāsaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ yuddha durmadaiḥ tat śrutvā jahṛṣuḥ pārthāḥ pārthivāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ tam abravīt tatas pārthaḥ pārṣatam pṛtanāpatim vyūhaḥ krauñca aruṇaḥ nāma sarva śatru nibarhaṇaḥ yam bṛhaspatiḥ indrāya tadā devāsure abravīt tam yathāvat prativyūha para anīka vināśanam a dṛṣṭa pūrvam rājānaḥ paśyantu kurubhiḥ saha tathā uktaḥ sa nṛdevena viṣṇuḥ vajrabhṛtā iva śāsanāt puruhūtasya nirmitaḥ viśvakarmaṇā indrāyudha savarṇābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ ākāśa gaḥ iva ākāśe gandharvanagara upamaḥ nṛtyamānaḥ iva ābhāti ratha caryāsu māriṣa tena ratnavatā pārthaḥ sa ca gāṇḍīvadhanvanā babhūva parama upetaḥ svayambhuḥ iva bhānunā śiraḥ abhūt drupadaḥ rājā mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ kuntibhojaḥ ca caidyaḥ ca cakṣuṣi āstām janeśvara dāśārṇakāḥ prayāgāḥ ca dāśeraka gaṇaiḥ saha anūpa gāḥ kirātāḥ ca grīvāyām bharata ṛṣabha paṭaccaraiḥ ca huṇḍaiḥ ca rājan pauravakaiḥ tathā niṣādaiḥ sahitaḥ ca api pṛṣṭham āsīt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pakṣau tu bhīmasenaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ piśācāḥ daradāḥ ca eva puṇḍrāḥ kuṇḍīviṣaiḥ saha maḍakāḥ laḍakāḥ ca eva taṅgaṇāḥ parataṅgaṇāḥ bāhlikāḥ tittirāḥ ca eva colāḥ pāṇḍyāḥ ca bhārata ete janapadāḥ rājan dakṣiṇam pakṣam āśritāḥ agniveṣyāḥ jagattuṇḍāḥ paladāśāḥ ca bhārata śabarāḥ tumbupāḥ ca eva vatsāḥ ca saha nākulaiḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca vāmam pārśvam samāśritāḥ rathānām ayutam pakṣau śiraḥ ca niyutam tathā pṛṣṭham arbudam eva āsīt sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ grīvāyām niyutam ca api sahasrāṇi ca saptatiḥ pakṣa koṭi prapakṣeṣu pakṣa anteṣu ca vāraṇāḥ jagmuḥ parivṛtāḥ rājñ calantaḥ iva parvatāḥ jaghanam pālayām āsa virāṭaḥ saha kekayaiḥ kāśirājaḥ ca śaibyaḥ ca rathānām ayutaiḥ tribhiḥ evam etam mahā vyūham vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ sūrya udayanam icchantaḥ sthitāḥ yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ evam te puruṣa vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ trasanti iva hi cetāṃsi yodhānām bharata ṛṣabha uvāca dṛṣṭvā agratas bhīmasenam gadā pāṇim avasthitam yuyutsavaḥ hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ tathā asan kim māmakāḥ bhīṣma netrāḥ samīyuḥ kim pāṇḍavāḥ bhīma netrāḥ tadānīm keṣām jaghanyau soma sūryau su vāyuḥ keṣām senām śvāpadāḥ vyāhareyuḥ keṣām yuvnām mukha varṇāḥ prasannāḥ uvāca ubhe citre vana rājī prakāśe ubhe sene nāga ratha aśva pūrṇe paścānmukhāḥ kauravāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tathā pāṇḍavāḥ prāc mukhāḥ yotsyamānāḥ sura indra senā iva ca pāṇḍavānām vavau vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhatas pāṇḍavānām tathā vāyuḥ sanmukhaḥ tāvakānām gaja indrāṇām mada gandhā suvarṇa kakṣam jāta balam prabhinnam samāsthitaḥ madhya gataḥ kurūṇām saṃstūyamānaḥ rathibhiḥ māgadhaiḥ ca tathā sauvarṇā sraj bhrājate ca uttamāṅge tam sarvatas śakuniḥ pārvatīyaḥ sārdham gāndhāraiḥ pāti gāndhāra rājaḥ śveta chattraḥ śveta kacaḥ sa śaṅkhaḥ śveta uṣṇīṣaḥ pāṇḍureṇa dhvajena śvetaḥ rathaḥ śaila sama prakāśaḥ bāhlikānām ca atirathaḥ mahātmā mahā iṣvāsāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sthitāḥ yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ teṣām āditya varṇāni vimalāni mahānti ca śveta chatrāṇi aśobhanta vāraṇeṣu ratheṣu ca uvāca vyūḍham dṛṣṭvā mahā ghoram pārthena amita tejasā ācāryam upasaṃgamya kṛpam śalyam ca māriṣa saumadattim vikarṇam ca aśvatthāmānam eva ca duḥśāsana ādīn bhrātṝn ca sa sarvān eva bhārata anyān ca su bahūn śūrān yuddhāya samupāgatān prāha idam vacanam kāle harṣayan tanayaḥ tava nānā śastra praharaṇāḥ sarve śastra astra vedinaḥ ekaikaśas samarthāḥ hi yūyam sarve mahā rathāḥ pāṇḍu putrān raṇe hantum sa sainyān kim saṃhatāḥ aparyāptam tat naḥ balam bhīṣma abhirakṣitam paryāptam tu idam eteṣām balam pārthiva sattamāḥ saṃsthānāḥ śūrasenāḥ ca veṇikāḥ kukurāḥ tathā ārevakāḥ trigartāḥ ca madrakāḥ yavanāḥ tathā śatruṃjayena sahitāḥ tathā duḥśāsanena ca citrasenena sahitāḥ sahitāḥ bhīṣmam eva abhirakṣantu saha sainya puraskṛtāḥ tatas droṇaḥ ca bhīṣmaḥ ca te putraḥ ca māriṣa avyūhanta mahā vyūham pāṇḍūnām pratibādhane bhīṣmaḥ sainyena mahatā samantāt parivāritaḥ yayau prakarṣan mahatīm vāhinīm surarāj iva tam anvayāt mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān kuntalaiḥ ca daśārṇaiḥ ca māgadhaiḥ ca viśām pate gāndhārāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ vikarṇaiḥ ca tathā śarmila kosalaiḥ daradaiḥ cūcupaiḥ ca eva tathā kṣudraka mālavaiḥ abhyarakṣata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ saubaleyasya vāhinīm bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyaḥ bhagadattaḥ ca māriṣa vinda anuvindau āvantyau vāmam pārśvam apālayan saumadattiḥ suśarmā ca kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ śatāyuḥ ca śrutāyuḥ ca dakṣiṇam pārśvam āsthitāḥ aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ ca eva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ mahatyā senayā sārdham senā pṛṣṭhe vyavasthitāḥ pṛṣṭhagopāḥ tu tasya āsan nānādeśyāḥ janeśvarāḥ ketumant vasudānaḥ ca putraḥ kāśyasya tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve hṛṣṭāḥ yuddhāya bhārata dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādān ca nādayan teṣām śrutvā tu hṛṣṭānām kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ siṃhanādam vinadya uccais śaṅkham dadhmau pratāpavān tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca peśyaḥ ca vividhāḥ paraiḥ pāñcajanyam hṛṣīkeśaḥ devadattam dhanaṃjayaḥ pauṇḍram dadhmau mahā śaṅkham bhīma karmā vṛkodaraḥ anantavijayam rājā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca dharma ātmā mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau kāśirājaḥ ca śaibyaḥ ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ virāṭaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ pāñcālyaḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ draupadyāḥ pañca ca ātmajāḥ sarve dadhmuḥ mahā śaṅkhān siṃhanādān ca nedire sa ghoṣaḥ su mahān tatra vīraiḥ taiḥ samudīritaḥ evam ete mahā rāja prahṛṣṭāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ uvāca evam vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu māmakeṣu itareṣu ca katham praharatām śreṣṭhāḥ saṃprahāram pracakrire uvāca samam vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu saṃnaddhāḥ rucira dhvajāḥ tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham yathā ayudhyanta tat śṛṇu apāram iva saṃdṛśya sāgara pratimam balam abravīt tāvakān sarvān yudhyadhvam iti daṃśitāḥ te manaḥ krūram āsthāya samabhityakta jīvitāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca vyatiṣakta ratha dvipam muktāḥ tu rathibhiḥ bāṇāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ su tejanāḥ saṃnipetuḥ akuṇṭha agrāḥ nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu ca tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme dhanuḥ udyamya daṃśitaḥ abhipatya mahā bāhuḥ bhīṣmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ kekaye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣate eteṣu nara vīreṣu cedi matsyeṣu ca abhitas vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīt vyatikaraḥ mahān sādita dhvaja nāgāḥ ca hata pravara vājinaḥ viprayāta ratha anīkāḥ samapadyanta pāṇḍavāḥ arjunaḥ tu nara vyāghraḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmam mahā ratham vārṣṇeyam abravīt kruddhaḥ yāhi yatra pitāmahaḥ eṣa bhīṣmaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ vārṣṇeya mama vāhinīm eṣa droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca janārdana dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca sahitāḥ duryodhana purogamāḥ pāñcālān nihaniṣyanti rakṣitāḥ dṛḍhadhanvanā saḥ aham bhīṣmam gamiṣyāmi sainya hetoḥ janārdana eṣa tvā prāpaye vīra pitāmaha ratham prati evam uktvā tatas śaurī ratham tam loka viśrutam prāpayām āsa bhīṣmāya ratham prati janeśvara cañcat bahu patākena balākā varṇa vājinā lāṅgūla āsphoṭa śabdena svanayānaḥ nabhastalam piṅga akṣaiḥ dṛṣṭipātaiḥ ca bhīṣayan ari sainikān vinighnan kaurava anīkam śūrasenān ca pāṇḍavaḥ āyāt śarān nudan śīghram suhṛd śoṣa vināśanaḥ trāsayānam raṇe śūrān pātayantam ca sāyakaiḥ sahasā pratyudīyāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ arjunam kaḥ hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānam anyaḥ kuru pitāmahāt droṇa vaikartanābhyām vā rathaḥ saṃyātum arhati tatas bhīṣmaḥ mahā rāja kauravāṇām pitāmahaḥ arjunam saptasaptatyā nārācānām samāvṛṇot droṇaḥ ca pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaḥ pañcāśatā śaraiḥ duryodhanaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā śalyaḥ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ drauṇiḥ ṣaṣṭyā nara vyāghraḥ vikarṇaḥ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ saindhavaḥ navabhiḥ ca api śakuniḥ ca api pañcabhiḥ vikarṇaḥ daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ rājñ vivyādha pāṇḍavam sa taiḥ viddhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa bhīṣmam pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ droṇam ṣaṣṭyā nara vyāghraḥ vikarṇam ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ śalyam ca daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tāvadbhiḥ ca jayadratham ārtāyanim tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ rājānam ca api pañcabhiḥ tam sātyakiḥ virāṭaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ tatas droṇam mahā iṣvāsam gāṅgeyasya priye ratam abhyavarṣata pāñcālyaḥ saṃyuktaḥ saha somakaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ tūrṇam vivyādha pāṇḍavam aśītyā niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ tatas akrośanta tāvakāḥ teṣām tu ninadam śrutvā prahṛṣṭānām prahṛṣṭa vat teṣām tu ratha siṃhānām madhyam prāpya dhanaṃjayaḥ cikrīḍa dhanuṣā rājñ lakṣyam kṛtvā mahā rathān kṣatriyāṇām śirāṃsi ugraiḥ kṛntan śastraiḥ mahā rathaḥ śūnyān kṛtvā rathopasthān vyacarat phalgunaḥ tadā tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhīṣmam āha janeśvaraḥ pīḍyamānam svakam sainyam dṛṣṭvā pārthena saṃyuge eṣa pāṇḍu sutaḥ tāta kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ balī yatatām sarva sainyānām mūlam naḥ parikṛntati tvayi jīvati gāṅgeye droṇe ca rathinām vare na yudhyati raṇe pārtham hita kāmaḥ sadā mama ubhau śveta hayau rājan saṃsaktau dṛśya pārthivāḥ siṃhanādān bhṛśam cakruḥ śaṅkha śabdān ca bhārata parivārya raṇe bhīṣmam sthitāḥ yuddhāya māriṣa tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya dhanaṃjayam gāṅgeyaḥ tu raṇe pārtham ānarchat navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śara sahasreṇa su prayuktena pāṇḍavaḥ arjunaḥ samara ślāghī bhīṣmasya avārayat diśaḥ vārayām āsa pārthasya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tathā nirviśeṣam ayudhyetām kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇaḥ bhīṣma cāpa vimuktāni śara jālāni saṃghaśas śīryamāṇāni adṛśyanta bhinnāni arjuna sāyakaiḥ tathā eva arjuna muktāni śara jālāni bhāgaśas arjunaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmam ārchat śitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīṣmaḥ api samare pārtham vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ ratha īṣām ratha cakre ca cikrīḍatuḥ ariṃdamau tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmaḥ praharatām varaḥ vāsudevam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare bhīṣma cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ nirviddhaḥ madhusūdanaḥ virarāja raṇe rājñ sa puṣpaḥ iva kiṃśukaḥ gāṅgeya sārathim saṃkhye nirbibheda tribhiḥ śaraiḥ na aśaknutām tadā anyonyam abhisaṃdhātum āhave maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gata pratyāgatāni ca adarśayetām bahudhā sūta sāmarthya lāghavāt rājan antara mārga sthau sthitau āstām muhur muhur ubhau siṃha rava unmiśram śaṅkha śabdam pracakratuḥ dāritā sahasā bhūmiḥ cakampa ca nanāda ca balinaḥ samare śūrau anyonya sadṛśau ubhau cihna mātreṇa bhīṣmam tu prajajñuḥ tatra kauravāḥ tathā pāṇḍu sutāḥ pārtham cihna mātreṇa jajñire tayoḥ nṛ varayoḥ rājan dṛśya tādṛś parākramam ubhau hi śara jālena tau adṛśyau babhūvatuḥ prakāśau ca punar tūrṇam babhūvatuḥ ubhau raṇe tatra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ cāraṇāḥ ca saha ṛṣibhiḥ anyonyam pratyabhāṣanta tayoḥ dṛṣṭvā parākramam na etādṛśāni yuddhāni bhaviṣyanti katham cana na api śakyaḥ raṇe jetum bhīṣmaḥ pārthena dhīmatā gāṅgeya arjunayoḥ saṃkhye stava yuktāḥ viśām pate tvadīyāḥ tu tatas yodhāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ ca bhārata droṇa pāñcālyayoḥ rājan mahān āsīt samāgamaḥ uvāca katham droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālyaḥ ca api pārṣataḥ diṣṭam eva param manye pauruṣāt api saṃjaya yatra śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ na atarat yudhi pāṇḍavam bhīṣmaḥ hi samare kruddhaḥ hanyāt lokān cara acarān sa katham pāṇḍavam yuddhe na atarat saṃjaya ojasā uvāca śṛṇu rājñ sthiraḥ bhūtvā yuddham etat su dāruṇam na śakyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ jetum devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ droṇaḥ tu niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apātayat tasya atha caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ sāyaka uttamaiḥ pīḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas droṇam navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha prahasan vīraḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tatas punar ameya ātmā bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa dhṛṣṭadyumnam amarṣaṇam ādade ca śaram ghoram pārṣatasya vadham prati śakra aśani sama sparśam mṛtyu daṇḍam iva aparam hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt sarva sainyasya bhārata tam iṣum saṃdhitam dṛṣṭvā bhāradvājena saṃyuge tatra adbhutam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnasya pauruṣam tam ca dīptam śaram ghoram āyāntam
