mṛtyum ātmanaḥ ciccheda śara vṛṣṭim ca bhāradvāje mumoca ha tatas uccukruśuḥ sarve pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha dhṛṣṭadyumnena tat karma kṛtam dṛṣṭvā su duṣkaram tatas śaktim mahā vegām svarṇa vaiḍūrya bhūṣitām droṇasya nidhana ākāṅkṣī cikṣepa sa parākramī tām āpatantīm sahasā śaktim kanaka bhūṣaṇām śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi droṇam prati janeśvara śara varṣam tatas tam tu saṃnivārya mahā yaśāḥ sa chinna dhanvā samare gadām gurum mahā yaśāḥ droṇāya preṣayām āsa girisāra mayīm balī sā gadā vegavat muktā prāyāt droṇa jighāṃsayā lāghavāt vyaṃsayām āsa gadām hema vibhūṣitām vyaṃsayitvā gadām tām ca preṣayām āsa pārṣate bhallān su niśitān pītān svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā manāḥ droṇam yudhi parākramya śaraiḥ vivyādha pañcabhiḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ avākirat ameya ātmā vṛṣṭyā meghaḥ iva acalam sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apātayat atha asya caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pātayām āsa samare siṃhanādam nanāda ca gadā pāṇiḥ avārohat khyāpayan pauruṣam mahat tām asya viśikhaiḥ tūrṇam pātayām āsa bhārata abhidudrāva vegena droṇasya vadha kāṅkṣayā āmiṣa arthī yathā siṃhaḥ vane mattam iva dvipam lāghavam ca astra yogam ca balam bāhuvoḥ ca bhārata yat enam śara varṣeṇa vārayām āsa pārṣatam na śaśāka tatas gantum balavān api saṃyuge tatra sthitam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā ratham vārayāṇam śara oghān ca carmaṇā kṛtahasta vat tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sahasā abhyapatat balī sāhāyya kārī samare pārṣatasya mahātmanaḥ sa droṇam niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ rājñ vivyādha sapta pārṣatam ca tadā tūrṇam anyam āropayat ratham tatas sā mahatī senā kaliṅgānām janeśvara bhīmam abhyudyayau tūrṇam te putrasya śāsanāt pāñcālyam abhisaṃtyajya droṇaḥ api rathinām varaḥ kaliṅgānām ca samare bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥ uvāca tathā pratisamādiṣṭaḥ kaliṅgaḥ vāhinīpatiḥ carantam gadayā vīram daṇḍa pāṇim iva antakam uvāca mahatyā senayā guptaḥ prāyāt bhīma ratham prati tām āpatantīm sahasā kaliṅgānām mahā camūm ratha nāga aśva kalilām pragṛhīta mahā āyudhām bhīmasenaḥ kaliṅgānām ārchat bhārata vāhinīm ketumantam ca naiṣādam āyāntam saha cedibhiḥ tatas śrutāyuḥ saṃkruddhaḥ rājñā ketumantā saha āsasāda raṇe bhīmam vyūḍha anīkeṣu cediṣu rathaiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ kaliṅgānām janādhipaḥ ayutena gajānām ca niṣādaiḥ saha ketumant bhīmasenam raṇe rājan samantāt paryavārayat cedi matsya karūṣāḥ ca bhīmasena purogamāḥ abhyavartanta sahasā niṣādān saha rājabhiḥ sarve kaliṅgakāḥ ca eva saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣu babhūva su mahān śabdaḥ sāgarasya iva garjataḥ anyonyasya tadā yodhāḥ nikṛntantaḥ viśām pate mahīm cakruḥ citām sarvām śaśa śoṇita saṃnibhām yodhān ca svān parān vā api na abhyajānan jighāṃsayā svān api ādadate svāḥ ca śūrāḥ samara durjayāḥ vimardaḥ su mahān āsīt alpānām bahubhiḥ saha kaliṅgaiḥ saha cedīnām niṣādaiḥ ca viśām pate kṛtvā puruṣakāram tu yathāśakti mahā balāḥ sarvaiḥ kaliṅgaiḥ āsannaḥ saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣu sva bāhu balam āsthāya na nyavartata pāṇḍavaḥ śitaiḥ avākiran bāṇaiḥ kaliṅgānām varūthinīm kaliṅgaḥ tu mahā iṣvāsaḥ putraḥ ca asya mahā rathaḥ śakradevaḥ iti khyātaḥ jaghnatuḥ pāṇḍavam śaraiḥ yodhayām āsa kāliṅgān sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ aśvān jaghāna samare bhīmasenasya sāyakaiḥ tam dṛṣṭvā viratham tatra bhīmasenam ariṃdamam śakradevaḥ abhidudrāva śitaiḥ avakiran śaraiḥ vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi tapānte jaladaḥ yathā hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ śakradevāya cikṣepa sarva śaikyāyasīm gadām hatam ātma sutam dṛṣṭvā kaliṅgānām janādhipaḥ ayutena gajānām ca niṣādaiḥ parivāritaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ gurum tyaktvā mahā gadām nistriṃśam cikīrṣuḥ karma dāruṇam carma ca apratimam rājan ārṣabham puruṣa ṛṣabha prāhiṇot bhīmasenāya vadha ākāṅkṣī janeśvaraḥ tam āpatantam vegena preritam niśitam śaram bhīmasenaḥ dvidhā rājñ ciccheda vipula asinā udakrośat ca saṃhṛṣṭaḥ trāsayānaḥ varūthinīm tomarān prāhiṇot śīghram caturdaśa śilā śitān tān aprāptān mahā bāhuḥ kha gatān eva pāṇḍavaḥ ciccheda sahasā rājñ asambhrāntaḥ vara asinā bhānumant tu tatas bhīmam śara varṣeṇa chādayan na tam sa mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ siṃhanādam mahā raṇe tena śabdena vitrastā kaliṅgānām varūthinī na bhīmam samare mene mānuṣam bharata ṛṣabha sa asiḥ vegāt avaplutya dantābhyām vāraṇa uttamam āruroha tatas madhyam nāga rājasya māriṣa tatas mumoca kāliṅgaḥ śaktim tām akarot dvidhā saḥ antara āyudhinam hatvā rāja putram ariṃdamaḥ ārugṇaḥ sindhu vegena sānumān iva parvataḥ khaḍga pāṇiḥ adīna ātmā atiṣṭhat bhuvi daṃśitaḥ sa cacāra bahūn mārgān abhītaḥ pātayan gajān aśva vṛndeṣu nāgeṣu ratha anīkeṣu padātīnām ca saṃgheṣu vinighnan śoṇita ukṣitaḥ chindan teṣām śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca mahā javaḥ khaḍgena śita dhāreṇa saṃyuge gaja yodhinām padātiḥ ekaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śatrūṇām bhaya vardhanaḥ mohayām āsa ca tadā kāla antaka yama upamaḥ padātibhiḥ padātīn ca aśvān aśvaiḥ gajān gajaiḥ mūḍhāḥ ca te tam eva ājau vinadantaḥ samādravan vibhujya kṣudhitāḥ nādam vidravanti diśaḥ daśa bhramantam kāla rūpeṇa bhīmasenam mahā balam nikṛtya rathinām ājau ratha īṣāḥ ca yugāni ca bhīmasenaḥ caran mārgān su bahūn pratyadṛśyata bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutam prasṛtam sṛtam saṃpātam samudīryam ca darśayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ ke cit agra asinā chinnāḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanā viyodhāḥ svāni anīkāni jaghnuḥ bhārata vāraṇāḥ gajān ca gaja yantṝn ca gaja hastān ca bhārata chinnān ca tomarān cāpān mahāmātra śirāṃsi ca paristomāni citrāṇi kakṣyāḥ ca kanaka ujjvalāḥ graiveyāṇi atha śaktīḥ ca patākāḥ kaṇapān tathā tūṇīrāṇi atha yantrāṇi vicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca agnikuṇḍāni śubhrāṇi tottrān ca eva aṅkuśaiḥ saha ghaṇṭāḥ ca vividhāḥ rājan hema garbhān tsarūn api patataḥ patitān ca eva paśyāmaḥ saha sādibhiḥ chinna gātra avara karaiḥ nihataiḥ ca api vāraṇaiḥ āsīt tasmin samāstīrṇā patitaiḥ bhūḥ nagaiḥ iva vimṛdya evam mahā nāgān mamarda aśvān nara ṛṣabhaḥ aśva āroha varān ca api pātayām āsa bhārata khalīnāni atha yoktrāṇi kaśāḥ ca kanaka ujjvalāḥ paristomāḥ ca prāsāḥ ca ṛṣṭayaḥ ca mahā dhanāḥ kavacāni atha carmāṇi citrāṇi āstaraṇāni ca sa cakre vasudhām kīrṇām śabalaiḥ kusumaiḥ iva āplutya rathinaḥ kān cit parāmṛśya mahā balaḥ ākṣipya anyāni apātayat khaḍgena anyān ca ciccheda pātayām āsa khaḍgena sa dhvajān api pāṇḍavaḥ mārgān ca carataḥ citrān vyasmayanta raṇe janāḥ nijaghāna padā kān cit ākṣipya anyān apothayat khaḍgena anyān ca ciccheda nādena anyān ca bhīṣayan ūru vegena ca api anyān pātayām āsa bhū tale apare ca enam ālokya bhayāt pañcatvam āgatāḥ evam sā bahulā senā kaliṅgānām tarasviṇām parivārya raṇe bhīṣmam bhīmasenam upādravat śrutāyuṣam abhiprekṣya bhīmasenaḥ samabhyayāt tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya kaliṅgaḥ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ kaliṅga bāṇa abhihataḥ tottra arditaḥ iva dvipaḥ atha aśokaḥ samādāya ratham hema pariṣkṛtam bhīmam saṃpādayām āsa rathena ratha sārathiḥ tam āruhya ratham tūrṇam kaunteyaḥ śatru sūdanaḥ kaliṅgam abhidudrāva tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tatas śrutāyuḥ balavān bhīmāya niśitān śarān preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ darśayan pāṇi lāghavam sa kārmuka vara utsṛṣṭaiḥ navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ samāhataḥ bhṛśam rājñ kaliṅgena mahā yaśāḥ saṃcukrudhe bhṛśam bhīmaḥ daṇḍa āhataḥ iva uragaḥ kaliṅgam avadhīt pārthaḥ bhīmaḥ sapta āyasaiḥ kṣurābhyām cakrarakṣau ca kaliṅgasya mahā balau tatas punar ameya ātmā nārācaiḥ niśitaiḥ tribhiḥ tatas kaliṅgāḥ saṃkruddhāḥ bhīmasenam amarṣaṇam anīkaiḥ bahu sāhasraiḥ kṣatriyāḥ samavārayan tatas śakti gadā khaḍga tomara ṛṣṭi paraśvadhaiḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca tatas rājñ bhīmasenam avākiran saṃnivārya sa tām ghorām śara vṛṣṭim samutthitām gadām ādāya tarasā pariplutya mahā balaḥ papāta śatru sainyeṣu kesarī iva mahā balaḥ bhīmaḥ saptaśatān vīrān anayat yama sādanam gadayā muktayā rājan pātayām āsa dantinaḥ ratham rathena saṃcūrṇya turaṅgam turageṇa tu padātinam padātena preṣayām āsa mṛtyave ratheṣu sa padāteṣu vāyunā iva mahā analaḥ yathā mṛgāṇām madhye tu kesarī iva nakhagrahaḥ evam bhramati sainyeṣu bhīma karmā vṛkodaraḥ evam sa tāni anīkāni kaliṅgānām punar punar bibheda samare vīraḥ prekṣya bhīṣmam mahā vratam hata ārohāḥ ca mātaṃgāḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanā mṛdnantaḥ svāni anīkāni vinadantaḥ śara āturāḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śaṅkham prādhmāpayat balī khaḍga āsakta mahā bhujaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ mahā ghoṣam sarva kāliṅga sainyānām manāṃsi samakampayat bhīmena sahasā rājñ bhramamāṇena saṃyuge mohaḥ ca api kaliṅgānām āviveśa paraṃtapa prākampanta ca sainyāni vāhanāni ca sarvaśas mārgān bahūn vicaratā dhāvatā ca tatas tatas dhāvatā hasti mārgeṣu muhur āpatatā punar kaliṅgānām sa sainyānām saṃmohaḥ samajāyata kṣobhyamāṇam asaṃbādham grāheṇa iva mahat saraḥ trāsiteṣu ca vīreṣu bhīmena adbhuta karmaṇā punar āvartamāneṣu vidravatsu ca saṃghaśas sarva kāliṅga yodheṣu pāṇḍūnām dhvajinīpatiḥ abravīt svāni anīkāni yudhyadhvam iti pārṣataḥ senāpati vacaḥ śrutvā śikhaṇḍi pramukhāḥ gaṇāḥ bhīmam eva abhyavartanta ratha anīkaiḥ prahāribhiḥ dharmarājaḥ ca tān sarvān upajagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ mahatā megha varṇena nāga anīkena pṛṣṭhatas evam saṃcodya sarvāṇi svāni anīkāni pārṣataḥ bhīmasenasya jagrāha pārṣṇim sat puruṣa ucitām bhīma sātyakayoḥ anyaḥ prāṇebhyaḥ priya kṛttamaḥ bhīmasenam mahā bāhum pārṣataḥ para vīra hā nanarda bahudhā rājan hṛṣṭaḥ ca āsīt paraṃtapaḥ śaṅkham dadhmau ca samare siṃhanādam nanāda ca sa ca pārāvata aśvasya rathe hema pariṣkṛte kovidāra dhvajam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaḥ samāśvasat dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā kaliṅgaiḥ samabhidrutam bhīmasenam ameya ātmā trāṇa āyājau samabhyayāt tau dūrāt sātyakiḥ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumna vṛkodarau pārtha pārṣatayoḥ pārṣṇim jagrāha puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ etat caturdaśe varṣe bhīmaḥ dṛṣṭvā raṇa ajiram viśeṣeṇa gajān rājñ param toṣam upāgamat sa kṛtvā kadanam tatra pragṛhīta śarāsanaḥ āsthitaḥ raudram ātmānam jaghāna samare parān kaliṅga prabhavām ca eva māṃsa śoṇita kardamām antareṇa kaliṅgānām pāṇḍavānām ca vāhinīm saṃtatāra su dustārām bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ bhīmasenam tathā dṛṣṭvā prākrośan tāvakāḥ nṛpa kālaḥ ayam bhīma rūpeṇa kaliṅgaiḥ saha yudhyate tatas śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ śrutvā tam ninadam raṇe abhyayāt tvaritaḥ bhīmam vyūḍha anīkaḥ samantataḥ tam sātyakiḥ bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ parivārya ca te sarve gāṅgeyam rabhasam raṇe yatamānān mahā iṣvāsān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ tatas śara sahasreṇa saṃnivārya mahā rathān hayān kāñcana saṃnāhān bhīmasya nyahanat śaraiḥ hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān śaktim cikṣepa tarasā gāṅgeyasya ratham prati aprāptām eva tām śaktim pitā devavrataḥ tava tridhā ciccheda samare sā pṛthivyām aśīryata tatas śaikyāyasīm gurum pragṛhya balavat gadām bhīṣmam eva abhyayāt tūrṇam jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍava ṛṣabhaḥ sātyakaḥ api tatas tūrṇam bhīmasya priya kāmyayā asinā tīkṣṇa dhāreṇa yodhān chittvā mahā āhave sārathim kuruvṛddhasya pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ vātāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ apanītaḥ raṇa ajirāt sa hatvā sarva kāliṅgān senā madhye vyatiṣṭhata dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tam āropya sva rathe rathinām varaḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām apovāha yaśasvinam saṃpūjyamānaḥ pāñcālyaiḥ matsyaiḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha dhṛṣṭadyumnam pariṣvajya sameyāt atha sātyakim atha abravīt bhīmasenam sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ praharṣayan yadu vyāghraḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥ diṣṭyā kaliṅga rājaḥ ca rāja putraḥ ca ketumant śakradevaḥ ca kāliṅgaḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca mṛdhe hatāḥ sva bāhu bala vīryeṇa nāga aśva ratha saṃkulaḥ mahā puruṣa bhūyiṣṭhaḥ vīra yodha niṣevitaḥ mahā vyūhaḥ kaliṅgānām ekena mṛditaḥ tvayā evam uktvā śineḥ naptā dīrghabāhuḥ ariṃdamaḥ bhīma ca punar āviṣṭaḥ sātvatena narottama praharṣam atulam lebhe bhīmaḥ sātyakinā saha uvāca gata aparāhṇa bhūyiṣṭhe tasmin ahani bhārata ratha nāga aśva pattīnām sādinām ca mahā kṣaye droṇaputreṇa śalyena kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā sa loka viditān aśvān nijaghāna mahā balaḥ drauṇeḥ pāñcāla dāyādaḥ śitaiḥ daśabhiḥ āśugaiḥ tatas śalya ratham tūrṇam āsthāya hata vāhanaḥ drauṇiḥ pāñcāla dāyādam abhyavarṣat atha iṣubhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tu saṃsaktam drauṇinā dṛśya bhārata saubhadraḥ abhyapatat tūrṇam vikiran niśitān śarān sa śalyam pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ aśvatthāmānam aṣṭabhiḥ vivyādha puruṣa ṛṣabha ārjunim tu tatas tūrṇam drauṇiḥ vivyādha pattriṇā śalyaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ ca eva kṛpaḥ ca niśitaiḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ pañcāśatā rājan kṣiprahastaḥ abhyavidhyata muṣṭideśe mahā rāja tatas uccukruśuḥ janāḥ anyat ādattavān citram kārmukam vegavattaram tau tatra samare hṛṣṭau kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇau anyonyam viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ jaghnatuḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhau tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā putram mahā ratham pīḍitam te pautreṇa prāyāt tatra janeśvaraḥ ārjunim ratha vaṃśena samantāt paryavārayan sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūraiḥ śūraḥ yudhi su durjayaiḥ saubhadram atha saṃsaktam tatra dṛṣṭvā dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ bhīṣma droṇa purogamāḥ abhyavartanta rājānaḥ sahitāḥ savyasācinam uddhūtam sahasā bhaumam nāga aśva ratha sādibhiḥ divākara patham prāpya rajaḥ tīvram adṛśyata tāni nāga sahasrāṇi bhūmipāla śatāni ca tasya bāṇa patham prāpya na abhyavartanta sarvaśas praṇeduḥ sarva bhūtāni babhūvuḥ timirāḥ diśaḥ kurūṇām anayaḥ tīvraḥ samadṛśyata dāruṇaḥ na api antarikṣam na diśaḥ na bhūmiḥ na ca bhāskaraḥ prajajñe bharata śreṣṭha śara saṃghaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ sādita dhvaja nāgāḥ tu hata aśvāḥ rathinaḥ bhṛśam vipradruta rathāḥ ke cid dṛśyante ratha yūthapāḥ virathāḥ rathinaḥ ca anye dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ tatra tatra eva dṛśyante sa āyudhāḥ sa aṅgadaiḥ bhujaiḥ haya ārohāḥ hayān tyaktvā gaja ārohāḥ ca dantinaḥ patitāḥ pātyamānāḥ ca dṛśyante arjuna tāḍitāḥ sa gadān udyatān bāhūn sa khaḍgān ca viśām pate sa prāsān ca sa tūṇīrān sa śarān sa śarāsanān sa aṅkuśān sa patākān ca tatra tatra arjunaḥ nṛṇām parighāṇām pravṛdh mudgarāṇām ca māriṣa prāsānām bhindipālānām nistriṃśānām ca saṃyuge paraśvadhānām tīkṣṇānām tomarāṇām ca bhārata varmaṇām ca apaviddhānām kavacānām ca bhū tale dhvajānām carmaṇām ca eva vyajanānām ca sarvaśas chatrāṇām hema daṇḍānām cāmarāṇām ca bhārata pratodānām kaśānām ca yoktrāṇām ca eva māriṣa rāśayaḥ ca atra dṛśyante vinikīrṇāḥ raṇa kṣitau yaḥ arjunam samare śūram pratyudyāyāt katham cana yaḥ yaḥ hi samare pārtham pati udyāti viśām pate sa sa vai viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ para lokāya nīyate teṣu vidravamāṇeṣu tava yodheṣu sarvaśas rorūyamāṇaḥ dṛśyeta dhvaja agre vānara īśvaraḥ dṛṣṭyā bhīṣayate śatrūn stabdha karṇaḥ mahā kapiḥ tat prabhagnam balam dṛṣṭvā pitā devavrataḥ tava abravīt samare śūram bhāradvājam smayan iva eṣa pāṇḍu sutaḥ vīraḥ kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ balī yathā asya dṛśyate rūpam kāla antaka yama upamam na nivartayitum ca api śakyā iyam mahatī camūḥ anyonya prekṣayā paśya dravati iyam varūthinī śara vrātāḥ pradṛśyanta pannaga ābhāḥ samantataḥ diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva vyāptāḥ hi ārjuna sāyakaiḥ eṣa ca astam giri śreṣṭham bhānumant pratipadyate tatra avahāram saṃprāptam manye aham puruṣa ṛṣabha śrāntāḥ bhītāḥ ca naḥ yodhāḥ na yotsyanti katham cana evam uktvā tatas bhīṣmaḥ droṇam ācārya sattamam avahāram atho cakre tāvakānām mahā rathaḥ tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ jayam prāpya sa somakāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva praṇeduḥ ca punar punar prayayuḥ śibirāya eva dhanaṃjaya puraskṛtāḥ vāditra ghoṣaiḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pranṛtyantaḥ mahā rathāḥ tatas avahāraḥ sainyānām te teṣām ca bhārata uvāca prabhātāyām tu śarvaryām bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tatas anīkāni anusaṃyāne vyādideśa atha bhārata gāruḍam ca mahā vyūham cakre śāṃtanavaḥ tadā putrāṇām te jaya ākāṅkṣī bhīṣmaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ cakṣuṣī ca bharadvājaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ ca eva śīrṣam āstām yaśasvinau bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyaḥ bhagadattaḥ ca māriṣa madrakāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ tathā pañcanadāḥ ca ye jayadrathena sahitāḥ grīvāyām saṃniveśitāḥ pṛṣṭhe duryodhanaḥ rājā sodaraiḥ sa anugaiḥ vṛtaḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau kāmbojaḥ ca śakaiḥ saha puccham āsan mahā rāja śūrasenāḥ ca sarvaśas māgadhāḥ ca kaliṅgāḥ ca dāśeraka gaṇaiḥ saha dakṣiṇam pakṣam āsādya sthitāḥ vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ kānanāḥ ca vikuñjāḥ ca muktāḥ tathā bṛhat balena sahitāḥ vāmam pakṣam upāśritāḥ vyūḍham dṛṣṭvā tu tat sainyam savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ tāvakānām tu tam vyūham pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ ardhacandreṇa vyūhena vyūham tam ati dāruṇam dakṣiṇam śṛṅgam āsthāya bhīmasenaḥ vyarocata nānā śastra ogha saṃpannaiḥ nānādeśyaiḥ nṛpaiḥ vṛtaḥ tat anu eva virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ tad anantaram eva āsīt nīlaḥ nīlāyudhaiḥ saha nīlāt anantaram ca eva dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā rathaḥ cedi kāśi karūṣaiḥ ca pauravaiḥ ca abhisaṃvṛtaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāñcālāḥ ca prabhadrakāḥ tathā eva dharmarājaḥ api gaja anīkena saṃvṛtaḥ tatas tu sātyakiḥ rājan draupadyāḥ pañca ca ātmajāḥ abhimanyuḥ tatas tūrṇam irāvant ca tatas param bhaimaseniḥ tatas rājñ kekayāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ tatas abhūt dvipadām śreṣṭhaḥ vāmam pārśvam upāśritaḥ tatra anu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ vāma śṛṅge vyavasthitaḥ evam etat mahā vyūham pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ vadha artham te putrāṇām tad pakṣam ye ca saṃgatāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca nighnatām itaretaram haya oghāḥ ca ratha oghāḥ ca tatra tatra viśām pate saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante nighnamānāḥ parasparam dhāvatām ca ratha oghānām nighnatām ca pṛthak pṛthak diva spṛś nara vīrāṇām nighnatām itaretaram saṃprahāre su tumule tava teṣām ca bhārata uvāca tatas vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu tāvakeṣu itareṣu ca te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kālena iva yuga kṣaye dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ raṇe yattāḥ pāṇḍavān pratyayodhayan prārthayānāḥ yaśaḥ dīptam mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam ekāgra manasaḥ bhūtvā pāṇḍavānām varūthinīm pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravaiḥ ca eva na prajñāyata kim cana udatiṣṭhat rajaḥ bhaumam chādayānam divākaram diśaḥ pratidiśaḥ vā api tatra jajñuḥ katham cana anumānena saṃjñābhiḥ nāma gotraiḥ ca saṃyuge rakṣitaḥ satya saṃdhena bhāradvājena dhīmatā tathā eva pāṇḍaveyānām rakṣitaḥ savyasācinā mahā vyūhaḥ bhīmena ca su rakṣitaḥ senā agrāt abhiniṣpatya prāyudhyan tatra mānavāḥ haya ārohaiḥ haya ārohāḥ pātyante sma mahā āhave ṛṣṭibhiḥ vimala agrābhiḥ prāsaiḥ api ca saṃyuge rathī rathinam āsādya śaraiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ gaja ārohāḥ gaja ārohān nārāca śara tomaraiḥ saṃsaktāḥ pātayām āsuḥ tava teṣām ca saṃghaśas keśa pakṣe parāmṛśya jahāra samare śiraḥ vemuḥ ca rudhiram vīrāḥ niḥśvasantaḥ samantataḥ kaḥ cit kari viṣāṇa sthaḥ vīraḥ raṇa viśāradaḥ patti saṃghāḥ raṇe pattīn bhindipāla paraśvadhaiḥ nyapātayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ paraspara kṛta āgasaḥ sa gajam pātayām āsa gajī ca rathinam rathāt padātī rathinam saṃkhye rathī ca api padātinam gaja ārohāḥ haya ārohān pātayām cakrire tadā nistriṃśaiḥ niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ pātitāḥ samadṛśyanta taiḥ ca api gaja yodhinaḥ patti saṃghāḥ haya ārohaiḥ sādi saṃghāḥ ca pattibhiḥ pātyamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta śataśas atha sahasraśas śaktibhiḥ kavacaiḥ citraiḥ kaṇapaiḥ aṅkuśaiḥ api nistriṃśaiḥ vimalaiḥ ca api svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śaraiḥ tathā bhūḥ bhāti bharata śreṣṭha sraj dāmaiḥ iva citritā agamya rūpā pṛthivī māṃsa śoṇita kardamā praśaśāma rajaḥ bhaumam vyukṣitam raṇa śoṇitaiḥ diśaḥ ca vimalāḥ sarvāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ janeśvara cihna bhūtāni jagantaḥ vināśa arthāya bhārata pratyadṛśyanta rathinaḥ dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ tatas droṇaḥ ca bhīṣmaḥ ca saindhavaḥ ca jayadrathaḥ purumitraḥ vikarṇaḥ ca śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ ete samara durdharṣāḥ siṃha tulya parākramāḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkāni babhañjuḥ sma punar punar sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca draupadeyāḥ ca bhārata tāvakān tava putrān ca sahitān sarva rājbhiḥ drāvayām āsuḥ ājau te tridaśāḥ dānavān iva tathā te samare anyonyam nighnantaḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ rakta ukṣitāḥ ghora rūpāḥ virejuḥ dānavāḥ iva vyadṛśyanta mahāmātrāḥ grahāḥ iva nabhastale abhyayāt pāṇḍavān yuddhe rākṣasam ca ghaṭotkacam tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve mahatyā senayā saha droṇa bhīṣmau raṇe śūrau pratyudyayuḥ ariṃdamau kirīṭī tu yayau kruddhaḥ samarthān pārthiva uttamān tatas pravavṛte bhūyas saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca samare vijigīṣatām uvāca tatas te pārthivāḥ kruddhāḥ phalgunam vīkṣya saṃyuge atha enam ratha vṛndena koṣṭakīkṛtya bhārata śaktīḥ ca vimalāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ gadāḥ ca parighaiḥ saha prāsān paraśvadhān ca eva mudgarān musalān api śastrāṇām atha tām vṛṣṭim śalabhānām iva āyatim rurodha sarvatas pārthaḥ śaraiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ tatra tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā bībhatsoḥ ati mānuṣam deva dānava gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ sātyakim ca abhimanyum ca mahatyā senayā saha gāndhārāḥ samare śūrāḥ rurudhuḥ saha saubalāḥ abhimanyoḥ ratham tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ vyadhametām śitaiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ droṇa bhīṣmau raṇe yattau dharmarājasya vāhinīm nāśayetām śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka pattra paricchadaiḥ tatas dharmasutaḥ rājā mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau miṣatām sarva sainyānām droṇa anīkam upādravan yathā devāsuram yuddham pūrvam āsīt su dāruṇam rājānam pratyudīyetām bhīmasena ghaṭotkacau hṛdi avidhyat pṛṣatkena prahasan iva pāṇḍavaḥ tam visaṃjñam atho jñātvā tvaramāṇaḥ asya sārathiḥ apovāha raṇāt rājñ tatas sainyam abhidyata tatas tām kauravīm senām dravamāṇām samantataḥ nighnan bhīmaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ anuvavrāja pṛṣṭhatas pārṣataḥ ca ratha śreṣṭhaḥ dharmaputraḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ droṇasya paśyataḥ sainyam gāṅgeyasya ca paśyataḥ jaghnatuḥ viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ para anīka viśātanaiḥ na aśaknutām vārayitum bhīṣma droṇau mahā rathau vāryamāṇam hi bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca viśām pate saubalām samare senām śātayetām samantataḥ śuśubhāte tadā tau tu śaineya kuru puṃgavau vavarṣa śara varṣeṇa dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ vāryamāṇam mahā rāja bhīṣma droṇa kṛpa ādibhiḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā samāśvasya viśām pate tatra tatra nyavartanta kṣatriyāṇām mahā rathāḥ tān nivṛttān samīkṣya eva tatas anye api itare janāḥ punar āvartatām teṣām vegaḥ āsīt viśām pate saṃnivṛttān tatas tān tu dṛṣṭvā rājā suyodhanaḥ abravīt tvaritaḥ gatvā bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam vacaḥ pitāmaha nibodha idam yat tvā vakṣyāmi bhārata droṇe ca astra vidām śreṣṭhe sa putre sa suhṛd jane kṛpe ca eva mahā iṣvāse dravati iyam varūthinī na pāṇḍavāḥ pratibalāḥ te rājan katham cana tathā droṇasya saṃgrāme drauṇeḥ ca eva kṛpasya ca anugrāhyāḥ pāṇḍu sutāḥ nūnam tava pitāmaha yathā imām kṣamase vīra vadhyamānām varūthinīm na yotsye pāṇḍavān saṃkhye na api pārṣata sātyakī yadi na aham parityājyaḥ yuvābhyām iha saṃyuge vikrameṇa anurūpeṇa yudhyetām puruṣa ṛṣabhau abravīt tanayam te krodhāt udvṛtya cakṣuṣī bahuśas hi mayā rājan tathyam uktam hitam vacaḥ ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ yuddhe devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ yat tu śakyam mayā kartum vṛddhena adya nṛpa uttama kariṣyāmi yathāśakti prekṣa idānīm sa bāndhavaḥ adya pāṇḍu sutān sarvān sa sainyān saha bandhubhiḥ miṣataḥ vārayiṣyāmi sarva lokasya paśyataḥ dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktāḥ bherīḥ ca jaghnire bhṛśam pāṇḍavāḥ api tatas rājñ śrutvā tam ninadam mahat dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān ca bherīḥ ca murajān ca vyanādayan uvāca pratijñāte tu bhīṣmeṇa tasmin yuddhe su dāruṇe pāṇḍūn āvārayiṣye iti katham yuyudhire nṛpāḥ bhīṣmaḥ kim akarot tatra pāṇḍaveyeṣu saṃjaya pitāmahe vā pāñcālāḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca gata pūrvāhṇa bhūyiṣṭhe tasmin ahani bhārata paścimām diśam āsthāya sthite ca api divākare jayam prāpteṣu hṛṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu abhyayāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm mama pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham anayāt tava bhārata dhanuṣām kūjatām tatra talānām mahān samabhavat śabdaḥ girīṇām iva dīryatām sthitaḥ asmi praharasva iti śabdāḥ śrūyanta sarvaśas kāñcaneṣu tanutreṣu kirīṭeṣu dhvajeṣu ca śilānām iva śaileṣu patitānām abhūt svanaḥ patitāni uttamāṅgāni bāhavaḥ ca vibhūṣitāḥ vyaceṣṭanta mahīm prāpya śataśas atha sahasraśas hṛta uttamāṅgāḥ ke cid tu tathā eva udyata kārmukāḥ pragṛhīta āyudhāḥ ca api tasthuḥ puruṣa sattamāḥ prāvartata mahā vegā nadī rudhira vāhinī mātaṃga aṅga śilā raudrā māṃsa śoṇita kardamā vara aśva nara nāgānām śarīra prabhavā tadā para loka arṇava mukhī gṛdhra gomāyu modinī na dṛṣṭam na śrutam ca api yuddham etādṛśam nṛpa yathā te sutānām ca pāṇḍavānām ca bhārata gajaiḥ ca patitaiḥ nīlaiḥ giri śṛṅgaiḥ iva āvṛtam vikīrṇaiḥ kavacaiḥ citraiḥ dhvajaiḥ chatraiḥ ca māriṣa śuśubhe tat raṇa sthānam śaradi iva nabhastalam vinirbhinnāḥ śaraiḥ ke cid anta pīḍā vikarṣiṇaḥ abhītāḥ samare śatrūn abhyadhāvanta daṃśitāḥ mā mām parityaja iti anye cukruśuḥ patitāḥ raṇe ādhāva abhyehi mā gaccha kim bhītaḥ asi kva yāsyasi tatra bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ nityam maṇḍala kārmukaḥ mumoca bāṇān dīpta agrān ahīn āśīviṣān iva śaraiḥ ekāyanīkurvan diśaḥ sarvāḥ yata vrataḥ jaghāna pāṇḍava rathān ādiśya ādiśya bhārata tam ekam samare śūram pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā aneka śata sāhasram samapaśyanta lāghavāt māyā kṛta ātmānam iva bhīṣmam tatra sma menire pūrvasyām diśi tam dṛṣṭvā pratyañci dadṛśuḥ janāḥ udīcyām ca enam ālokya dakṣiṇasyām punar prabho evam sa samare vīraḥ gāṅgeyaḥ pratyadṛśyata na ca enam pāṇḍaveyānām kaḥ cit śaknoti vīkṣitum viśikhān eva paśyanti bhīṣma cāpa cyutān bahūn kurvāṇam samare karma sūdayānam ca vāhinīm vyākrośanta raṇe tatra vīrāḥ bahuvidham bahu amānuṣeṇa rūpeṇa carantam pitaram tava śalabhāḥ iva rājānaḥ patanti vidhi coditāḥ bhīṣma agnim abhi saṃkruddham vināśāya sahasraśas na hi moghaḥ śaraḥ kaḥ cit āsīt bhīṣmasya saṃyuge nara nāga aśva kāyeṣu bahu tvāt laghu vedhinaḥ gaja kaṅkaṭa saṃnāham vajreṇa iva acala uttamam dvau trīn api gaja ārohān piṇḍitān varmitān api nārācena su tīkṣṇena nijaghāna pitā tava muhūrta dṛṣṭaḥ sa mayā pātitaḥ bhuvi dṛśyate evam sā dharmarājasya vadhyamānā mahā camūḥ bhīṣmeṇa atula vīryeṇa vyaśīryata sahasradhā prakīryata mahā senā śara varṣa abhitāpitā yatamānā api te vīrāḥ dravamāṇān mahā rathān na aśaknuvan vārayitum bhīṣma bāṇa prapīḍitāḥ mahā indra sama vīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahā camūḥ āviddha nara nāga aśvam patita dhvaja kūbaram anīkam pāṇḍu putrāṇām hāhā bhūtam acetanam jaghāna atra pitā putram putraḥ ca pitaram tathā priyam sakhim ca ākrande sakhiḥ daiva balātkṛtaḥ vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍu putrasya sainikāḥ prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārata dadṛśe pāṇḍu putrasya sainyam ārta svaram tadā prabhajyamānam tat sainyam dṛṣṭvā devakī nandanaḥ ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pārtha yaḥ kāṅkṣitaḥ tvayā yat tvayā kathitam vīra purā rājñām samāgame bhīṣma droṇa mukhān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikān sa anubandhān haniṣyāmi ye mām yotsyanti saṃyuge bībhatso paśya sainyam svam bhajyamānam samantataḥ dravataḥ ca mahīpālān sarvān yaudhiṣṭhire bale dṛṣṭvā hi samare bhīṣmam vyātta ānanam iva antakam bhaya ārtāḥ saṃpraṇaśyanti siṃham kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca vāsudevam dhanaṃjayaḥ codaya aśvān yatas bhīṣmaḥ vigāhya etat bala arṇavam pātayiṣyāmi durdharṣam kuruvṛddham pitāmaham tatas aśvān rajata prakhyān codayām āsa mādhavaḥ yatas bhīṣma rathaḥ rājan duṣprekṣyaḥ raśmimant iva dṛṣṭvā pārtham mahā bāhum bhīṣmāya udyantam āhave tatas bhīṣmaḥ kuru śreṣṭhaḥ siṃha vat vinadan muhur dhanaṃjaya ratham tūrṇam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat śara varṣeṇa mahatā saṃchannaḥ na prakāśate codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣma sāyakaiḥ pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuḥ chittvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ nimeṣa antara mātreṇa sajyam cakre pitā tava tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavam śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥ sādhu pārtha mahā bāho sādhu bho pāṇḍu nandana iti pārtham praśasya atha pragṛhya anyat mahat dhanuḥ mumoca samare vīraḥ śarān pārtha ratham prati moghān kurvan śarān tasya maṇḍalāni acarat laghu tathā api bhīṣmaḥ su dṛḍham vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sarva gātreṣu māriṣa śuśubhāte nara vyāghrau tau bhīṣma śara vikṣatau go vṛṣau iva nardantau viṣāṇa ullikhita aṅkitau punar ca api su saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ yudhi saṃrabdhaḥ bhīṣmaḥ vyāvārayat diśaḥ pārthaḥ api samare kruddhaḥ bhīṣmasya avārayat diśaḥ bhīṣmaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ pārthasya avārayat diśaḥ vārṣṇeyam ca śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kampayām āsa roṣitaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ tu samare dṛṣṭvā bhīṣma parākramam saṃprekṣya ca mahā bāhuḥ pārthasya mṛdu yuddha tām bhīṣmam ca śara varṣāṇi sṛjantam aniśam yudhi varān varān vinighnantam pāṇḍu putrasya sainikān yuga antam iva kurvāṇam bhīṣmam yaudhiṣṭhire bale amṛṣyamāṇaḥ bhagavant keśavaḥ para vīra hā eka ahnā hi raṇe bhīṣmaḥ nāśayet deva dānavān kim u pāṇḍu sutān yuddhe sa balān sa padānugān ete ca kauravāḥ tūrṇam prabhagnān dṛśya somakān ādravanti raṇe hṛṣṭāḥ harṣayantaḥ pitāmaham saḥ aham bhīṣmam nihanmi adya pāṇḍava arthāya daṃśitaḥ bhāram etam vineṣyāmi pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām kartavyam na abhijānāti raṇe bhīṣmasya gauravāt preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ śarān pārtha ratham prati teṣām bahu tvāt hi bhṛśam śarāṇām diśaḥ atha sarvāḥ pihitāḥ babhūvuḥ na ca antarikṣam na diśaḥ na bhūmiḥ na bhāskaraḥ adṛśyata raśmimālī vavuḥ ca vātāḥ tumulāḥ sa dhūmāḥ diśaḥ ca sarvāḥ kṣubhitāḥ babhūvuḥ droṇaḥ vikarṇaḥ atha jayadrathaḥ ca bhūriśravāḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ ca śrutāyuḥ ambaṣṭha patiḥ ca rājā vinda anuvindau ca sudakṣiṇaḥ ca prācyāḥ ca sauvīra gaṇāḥ ca sarve vasātayaḥ kṣudraka mālavāḥ ca kirīṭinam tvaramāṇā abhisasruḥ nideśa gāḥ śāṃtanavasya rājñaḥ kirīṭinam saṃparivāryamāṇam śineḥ naptā vāraṇa yūthapaiḥ ca tatas tu dṛṣṭvā arjuna vāsudevau padāti nāga aśva rathaiḥ samantāt abhidrutau śastrabhṛtām variṣṭhau śini pravīraḥ abhisasāra tūrṇam sa tāni anīkāni mahā dhanuṣmān śini pravīraḥ sahasā abhipatya cakāra sāhāyyam atha arjunasya viṣṇuḥ yathā vṛtra niṣūdanasya viśīrṇa nāga aśva ratha dhvaja ogham bhīṣmeṇa vitrāsita sarva yodham yudhiṣṭhira anīkam abhidravantam provāca saṃdṛśya śinipravīraḥ kva kṣatriyāḥ yāsyatha na eṣa dharmaḥ satām purastāt kathitaḥ purāṇaiḥ mā svām pratijñām jahata pravīrāḥ svam vīra dharmam paripālayadhvam pārthasya dṛṣṭvā mṛdu yuddha tām ca amṛṣyamāṇaḥ sa tatas mahātmā yaśasvinam sarva daśārha bhartā uvāca śaineyam abhipraśaṃsan dṛṣṭvā kurūn āpatataḥ samantāt bhīṣmam rathāt paśya nipātyamānam droṇam ca saṃkhye sa gaṇam mayā adya na asau rathaḥ sātvata kauravāṇām kruddhasya mucyeta raṇe adya kaḥ cit tasmāt aham gṛhya rathāṅgam ugram prāṇam hariṣyāmi mahāvratasya nihatya bhīṣmam sa gaṇam tathā ājau droṇam ca śaineya ratha pravīram prītim kariṣyāmi dhanaṃjayasya rājñaḥ ca bhīmasya tathā aśvinoḥ ca nihatya sarvān dhṛtarāṣṭra putrān tad pakṣiṇaḥ ye ca narendra mukhyāḥ rājyena rājānam ajātaśatrum saṃpādayiṣyāmi aham adya hṛṣṭaḥ iti idam uktvā sa mahā anubhāvaḥ sasmāra cakram niśitam purāṇam saṃkampayan gām caraṇaiḥ mahātmā vegena kṛṣṇaḥ prasasāra bhīṣmam mada andham ājau samudīrṇa darpaḥ siṃhaḥ jighāṃsan iva vāraṇa indram vyālambi pīta anta paṭaḥ cakāśe ghanaḥ yathā khe acira bhā pinaddhaḥ yathā ādi padmam taruṇa arka varṇam rarāja nārāyaṇa nābhi jātam tat kṛṣṇa kopa udaya sūrya buddham kṣura anta tīkṣṇa agra sujāta pattram tasya eva deha ūru saraḥ prarūḍham rarāja nārāyaṇa bāhu nālam sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhṛśam vineduḥ kṣayam kurūṇām iti cintayitvā tam āpatantam pragṛhīta cakram samīkṣya devam dvipadām variṣṭham asaṃbhramāt kārmuka bāṇa pāṇī rathe sthitaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ abhyuvāca asaṃbhramam tat vicakarṣa dorbhyām mahā dhanuḥ gāṇḍiva tulya ghoṣam uvāca bhīṣmaḥ tam ananta pauruṣam govindam ājau avimūḍha cetāḥ ehi ehi deveśa jagannivāsa namaḥ astu te śārṅga ratha aṅga pāṇe prasahya mām pātaya loka nātha ratha uttamāt bhūta śaraṇya saṃkhye saṃbhāvitaḥ asmi andhaka vṛṣṇi nātha lokaiḥ tribhiḥ vīra te abhiyānāt śrutvā vacaḥ śāṃtanavasya kṛṣṇo durdyūta devī nṛpatiḥ nivāryaḥ dharma atigaḥ yaḥ kula pāṃsanaḥ syāt bhīṣmaḥ tat ākarṇya yadu pravīram rājā param daivatam iti uvāca dharmāt kurūṇām adhipaḥ tadānīm kleśāya daivāt viparīta buddhiḥ vaktā bhṛśam syāt sa tu kim bravītu jagrāha pīna uttama lamba bāhum bāhvoḥ harim vyāyata pīna bāhuḥ nigṛhyamāṇaḥ ca tat ādidevaḥ bhṛśam sa roṣaḥ kila nāma yogī ādāya vegena jagāma viṣṇuḥ jiṣṇum mahā vātaḥ iva eka vṛkṣam pārthaḥ tu viṣṭabhya balena pādau bhīṣma antikam tūrṇam abhidravantam balāt nijagrāha kirīṭamālī pade atha rājan daśame kathaṃ cit avasthitam ca praṇipatya kṛṣṇam prītaḥ arjunaḥ kāñcana citra mālī uvāca kopam pratisaṃhara iti gatiḥ bhavān keśava pāṇḍavānām antam kariṣyāmi yathā kurūṇām tvayā aham indrānuja saṃprayuktaḥ tatas pratijñām samayam ca tasmai janārdanaḥ prīta manāḥ niśamya tatas pratijñām samavāpya bhīṣmaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ stutyam atha akarot vai sa tān abhīṣūn punar ādadānaḥ pragṛhya śaṅkham dviṣatām nihantā vinādayām āsa tatas diśaḥ ca sa pāñcajanyasya raveṇa śauriḥ vyāviddha niṣka aṅgada kuṇḍalam tam rajaḥ vikīrṇa āñcita pakṣma netram viśuddha daṃṣṭram pragṛhīta śaṅkham vicukruśuḥ prekṣya kuru pravīrāḥ mṛdaṅga bherī paṭaha praṇādāḥ nemi svanāḥ dundubhi nisvanāḥ ca sa siṃhanādāḥ ca babhūvuḥ ugrāḥ sarveṣu anīkeṣu tatas kurūṇām gāṇḍīva ghoṣaḥ stanayitnu kalpaḥ jagāma pārthasya nabhaḥ diśaḥ ca jagmuḥ ca bāṇāḥ vimalāḥ prasannāḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ pāṇḍava cāpa muktāḥ tam kauravāṇām adhipaḥ balena bhīṣmeṇa bhūriśravasā ca sārdham abhyudyayau udyata bāṇa pāṇiḥ kakṣam didhakṣan iva dhūmaketuḥ atha arjunāya prajahāra bhallān bhūriśravāḥ sapta suvarṇa puṅkhān duryodhanaḥ tomaram ugra vegam śalyaḥ gadām śāṃtanavaḥ ca śaktim sa saptabhiḥ sapta śara pravekān saṃvārya bhūriśravasā visṛṣṭān tatas śubhām āpatatīm sa śaktim vidyutprabhām śāṃtanavena muktām gadām ca madra adhipa bāhu muktām dvābhyām śarābhyām nicakarta vīraḥ tatas bhujābhyām balavat vikṛṣya citram dhanuḥ gāṇḍivam aprameyam tena uttama astreṇa tatas mahātmā sarvāṇi anīkāni mahā dhanuṣmān śara ogha jālaiḥ vimala agni varṇaiḥ nivārayām āsa kirīṭamālī bhīṣmam śaraiḥ saṃparivārya saṃkhye śalyam ca viddhvā navabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ śilīmukhāḥ pārtha dhanuḥ pramuktāḥ rathān dhvaja agrāṇi dhanūṃṣi bāhūn nikṛtya dehān viviśuḥ pareṣām narendra nāga indra turaṃgamāṇām tatas diśaḥ ca anudiśaḥ ca pārthaḥ śaraiḥ su dhāraiḥ niśitaiḥ vitatya gāṇḍīva śabdena manāṃsi teṣām kirīṭamālī vyathayām cakāra antarhitāḥ gāṇḍiva nisvanena bhabhūvuḥ ugrāḥ ca raṇa praṇādāḥ gāṇḍīva śabdam tam atho viditvā virāṭa rāja pramukhāḥ nṛ vīrāḥ pāñcāla rājaḥ drupadaḥ ca vīraḥ tam deśam ājagmuḥ adīna sattvāḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni tu tāvakāni yatas yatas gāṇḍiva jaḥ praṇādaḥ punar punar dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samagrāḥ tasmin su ghora nṛpa saṃprahāra han pravīra sa ratha sa sūta gajāḥ ca nārāca nipāta taptāḥ mahā patākāḥ śubha rukma kakṣyāḥ parīta sattvāḥ sahasā nipetuḥ kirīṭinā bhinna tanutra kāyāḥ dṛḍha āhatāḥ pattribhiḥ ugra vegaiḥ pārthena bhallaiḥ niśitaiḥ śita agraiḥ padāti saṃghāḥ ca rathāḥ ca saṃkhye hayāḥ ca nāgāḥ ca dhanaṃjayena bāṇa āhatāḥ tūrṇam apeta sattvāḥ viṣṭabhya gātrāṇi nipetuḥ urvyām tatas śara oghaiḥ niśitaiḥ kirīṭinā tatas śara oghaiḥ niśitaiḥ kirīṭī pravartayām āsa nadīm su ghorām nṛ nāga vāji kṣata lohita udām vegena sā atīva pṛthu pravāhā prasusrutā bhairava ārāva rūpā pareta nāga aśva śarīra rodhā prabhūta rakṣas gaṇa bhūta sev śiras kapāla ākula keśa śādvala śarīra saṃghāta sahasra vāhinī viśīrṇa nānā kavaca ūrmi saṃkulā nara aśva nāga asthi nikṛtta śarkarā vināśa pātālavatī bhaya āvahā tām kaṅka mālā vṛta gṛdhra kahvaiḥ kravyāda saṃghaiḥ ca tarakṣubhiḥ ca upeta kūlām dadṛśuḥ samantāt krūrām mahā vaitaraṇī prakāśām pravartitām arjuna bāṇa saṃghaiḥ medaḥ vasā asṛj pravahām su bhīmām hata pravīrām ca tathā eva dṛṣṭvā senām kurūṇām atha phalgunena te cedi pāñcāla karūṣa matsyāḥ pārthāḥ ca sarve sahitāḥ praṇeduḥ jaya pragalbhāḥ puruṣa pravīrāḥ saṃtāpayantaḥ kuru yodha vīrān hata pravīrāṇi balāni dṛṣṭvā kirīṭinā śatru bhaya āvahena vitrāsya senām dhvajinī patīnām siṃhaḥ mṛgāṇām iva yūtha saṃghān dṛṣṭvā tadā bhārata vṛṣṇi siṃhau vinedatuḥ tau ati harṣa yuktau gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca janārdanaḥ ca tatas ravim saṃhṛta raśmi jālam dṛṣṭvā bhṛśam śastra parikṣata aṅgāḥ atha apayānam kuravaḥ sa bhīṣmāḥ sa droṇa duryodhana bāhlikāḥ ca cakruḥ niśām saṃdhi gatām samīkṣya vibhāvasoḥ lohita rāji yuktām rarāja ca ārakta diś antarālam sa śoṇam atyartharathāṅga nāmnaḥ hṛdaḥ prabhinnāt iva śoṇita oghaiḥ avāpya kīrtim ca yaśaḥ ca loke vijitya śatrūn ca dhanaṃjayaḥ api yayau narendraiḥ saha sodaraiḥ ca samāpta karmā śibiram niśāyām tatas prajajñe tumula kurū niśā mukha ghorataraḥ praṇādaḥ raṇe rathānām ayutam nihatya hatāḥ gajāḥ saptaśatā arjunena prācyāḥ ca sauvīra gaṇāḥ ca sarve nipātitāḥ kṣudraka mālavāḥ ca śrutāyuḥ ambaṣṭha patiḥ ca rājā tathā eva durmarṣaṇa citrasenau droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ saindhava bāhlikau ca bhūriśravāḥ śalya śalau ca rājan anye ca yodhāḥ śataśas sametāḥ sva bāhu vīrya ji sa bhīṣmāḥ kirīṭin loka mahat rathena saṃveṣṭitaḥ pāṇḍava bāṇa bhinnaḥ iti bruvantaḥ śibirāṇi jagmuḥ sarve gaṇāḥ bhārata ye tvadīyāḥ ulkā sahasraiḥ ca su saṃpradīptaiḥ vibhrājamānaiḥ ca tathā pradīpaiḥ kirīṭi vitrāsita sarva yodhā cakre niveśam dhvajinī kurūṇām bhagnena darpeṇa mahā rathānām uvāca vyuṣṭām niśām bhārata bhāratānām anīkinīnām pramukhe mahātmā tasmin anīka pramukhe viṣaktā dodhūyamānāḥ ca mahā patākāḥ su rakta pīta asita pāṇḍura ābhāḥ mahā gaja skandha gatāḥ virejuḥ sā vāhinī śāṃtanavena rājñā mahā rathaiḥ vāraṇa vājibhiḥ ca tatas raṇāya abhimukhī prayātā prati arjunam śāṃtanava abhiguptā senā mahā ugrā sahasā kurūṇām vegaḥ yathā bhīmaḥ iva āpagāyāḥ atas param vyūham acintya rūpam niveśayām āsa mahā dhanuṣmān tam vyāla nānāvidha gūḍha sāram gaja aśva pādāta ratha ogha pakṣam vyūham mahā megha samam mahātmā dadarśa dūrāt kapi rāja ketuḥ nārāyaṇena indraḥ iva abhiguptaḥ śaśī iva sūryeṇa sameyivān yathā tathā mahātmā saha keśavena varūthinīnām pramukhe rarāja yathā mahā indraḥ asura vāhinīnām nārāyaṇena indraḥ iva abhiguptaḥ śaśī iva sūryeṇa sameyivān yathā tathā mahātmā saha keśavena su upaskaram sa uttarabandhura iṣam yattam yadūnām ṛṣabheṇa saṃkhye tam vyūha rājam dadṛśuḥ tvadīyāḥ catur catur vyāla sahasra kīrṇam yathā hi pūrve ahani dharmarājñā vyūhaḥ kṛtaḥ kaurava nandanena tathā tathā uddeśam upetya tasthuḥ pāñcāla mukhyaiḥ saha cedi mukhyāḥ tathā na bhūtaḥ bhuvi mānuṣeṣu na dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ na ca saṃśrutaḥ ca śaṅkha svanāḥ dundubhi nisvanāḥ ca sarveṣu anīkeṣu sa siṃhanādāḥ tatas sa bāṇāni mahā svanāni visphāryamāṇāni dhanūṃṣi vīraiḥ kṣaṇena bherī paṇava praṇādān antardadhuḥ śaṅkha mahā svanāḥ ca mahā vitāna avatata prakāśam ālokya vīrāḥ sahasā abhipetuḥ rathī rathena abhihataḥ sa sūtaḥ papāta sa aśvaḥ sa rathaḥ sa ketuḥ gajaḥ gajena abhihataḥ papāta padātinā ca abhihataḥ padātiḥ āvartamānāni abhivartamānaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kṣatāni adbhuta darśanāni prāsaiḥ ca khaḍgaiḥ ca samāhatāni sat aśva vṛndāni sat aśva vṛndaiḥ suvarṇa tārā gaṇa bhūṣitāni śarāvarāṇi prahitāni vīraiḥ vidāryamāṇāni paraśvadhaiḥ ca prāsaiḥ ca khaḍgaiḥ ca nipetuḥ urvyām gajaiḥ viṣāṇaiḥ vara hasta rugṇāḥ ke cit sa sūtāḥ rathinaḥ prapetuḥ gaja ṛṣabhāḥ ca api ratha ṛṣabheṇa nipetire bāṇa hatāḥ pṛthivyām gaja ogha vega uddhata sāditānām ārta svaram sādi padāti yuvnām viṣāṇa gātra avara tāḍitānām saṃbhrānta nāga aśva rathe prasūte mahā bhaye sādi padāti yuvnām mahā rathaiḥ saṃparivāryamāṇam dadarśa bhīṣmaḥ kapi rāja ketum tam pañca tāla ucchrita tāla ketuḥ sat aśva vega uddhata vīrya yātaḥ mahā astra bāṇa aśani dīpta mārgam kirīṭinam śāṃtanavaḥ abhyadhāvat kṛpaḥ ca śalyaḥ ca viviṃśatiḥ ca duryodhanaḥ saumadattiḥ ca rājan teṣām mahā astrāṇi mahā rathānām asakta karmā vinihatya kārṣṇiḥ tatas sa tūrṇam rudhira uda phenām kṛtvā nadīm ripūṇām jagāma saubhadram atītya bhīṣmaḥ mahā ratham pārtham adīna sattvaḥ tatas prahasya adbhuta darśanena gāṇḍīva nirhvāda mahā svanena vipāṭha jālena mahā astra jālam vināśayām āsa kirīṭamālī bhīṣmam mahātmā abhivavarṣa tūrṇam śara ogha jālaiḥ vimalaiḥ ca bhallaiḥ mahā astra jālam kapi rāja ketoḥ viśīryamāṇam dadṛśuḥ tvadīyā evaṃvidham kārmuka bhīma nādam adīna vat sat puruṣa uttamābhyām dadarśa lokaḥ kuru sṛñjayāḥ ca tat dvairatham bhīṣma dhanaṃjayābhyām uvāca drauṇiḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalyaḥ citrasenaḥ ca māriṣa saṃsaktam ati tejobhiḥ tam ekam dadṛśuḥ janāḥ pañcabhiḥ manuja vyāghraiḥ gajaiḥ siṃha śiśum yathā babhūva sadṛśaḥ kārṣṇeḥ na astre na api ca lāghave dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ raṇe yattaḥ siṃhanādam atho anadat pīḍayānam ca tat sainyam pautram te viśām pate dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ rāja indra samantāt paryavārayan dadarśa rājan pāñcālyaḥ senāpatiḥ ariṃdamaḥ dhvajinīm dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām dīna śatruḥ adīna vat sa drauṇim iṣuṇā ekena viddhvā śalyam ca pañcabhiḥ dhvajam sāṃyamaneḥ ca api saḥ aṣṭābhiḥ apavarjayat rukma daṇḍām mahā śaktim preṣitām saumadattinā śitena uraga saṃkāśām pattriṇā vijahāra tām śalyasya ca mahā ghorān asyataḥ śataśas śarān nivārya arjuna dāyādaḥ jaghāna samare hayān bhūriśravāḥ ca śalyaḥ ca drauṇiḥ sāṃyamaniḥ śalaḥ na abhyavartanta saṃrabdhāḥ kārṣṇeḥ bāhu bala āśrayāt pañcatriṃśati sāhasrāḥ tava putreṇa coditāḥ saha putram jighāṃsantam parivavruḥ kirīṭinam dadarśa rājñ pāñcālyaḥ senāpatiḥ amitra jit sa vāraṇa ratha oghānām sahasraiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtaḥ vājibhiḥ pattibhiḥ ca eva vṛtaḥ śata sahasraśas pārāvata aśvam sa ratham āsthāya para vīra hā yayau tat madraka anīkam kekayān ca paraṃtapaḥ tena kīrtimatā guptam anīkam dṛḍhadhanvanā saḥ arjunam pramukhe yāntam pāñcālyaḥ kuru nandana tribhiḥ śāradvatam bāṇaiḥ jatru deśe samarpayat tatas sa madrakān hatvā daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ ekaḥ jaghāna aśvam bhallena kṛtavarmaṇaḥ damanam ca api dāyādam pauravasya mahātmanaḥ jaghāna vipula agreṇa nārācena paraṃtapaḥ tatas sāṃyamani putraḥ pāñcālyam yuddha durmada avidhyat triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca asya sārathim saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ parisaṃlihan bhallena bhṛśa tīkṣṇena nicakarta asya kārmukam aśvān ca asya avadhīt rājan ubhau tau pārṣṇisārathī putraḥ sāṃyamaneḥ putram pāñcālyasya mahātmanaḥ sa saṃgṛhya mahā ghoram nistriṃśa varam āyasam bhrānta āvaraṇa nistriṃśam kāla utsṛṣṭam iva antakam apaśyan pāṇḍavāḥ tatra dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ śita nistriṃśa hastasya śarāvaraṇa dhāriṇaḥ bāṇa vegam atītasya ratha abhyāśam upeyivasaḥ tasya rājan sa nistriṃśam su prabham ca śarāvaram tam nihatya gadā agreṇa lebhe sa paramam yaśaḥ putraḥ pāñcāla rājasya mahātmā bhīma vikramaḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt te sainyasya māriṣa tatas sāṃyamaniḥ kruddhaḥ dṛṣṭvā nihatam ātmajam dadṛśuḥ sarva rājānaḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tathā tatas sāṃyamaniḥ kruddhaḥ pārṣatam para vīra hā tathā eva pārṣatam śūram śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ uvāca nityam hi māmakān tāta hatān eva hi śaṃsasi avyagrān ca prahṛṣṭān ca nityam śaṃsasi pāṇḍavān vibhagnān ca praṇaṣṭān ca nityam śaṃsasi māmakān hīnān puruṣakāreṇa māmakān adya saṃjaya patitān pātyamānān ca hatān eva ca śaṃsasi yudhyamānān yathāśakti ghaṭamānān jayam prati pāṇḍavāḥ vijayanti eva jīyante ca eva māmakāḥ saḥ aham tīvrāṇi duḥkhāni duryodhana kṛtāni ca aśrauṣam satatam tāta duḥsahāni bahūni ca tam upāyam na paśyāmi jīyeran yena pāṇḍavāḥ māmakāḥ vā jayam yuddhe prāpnuyuḥ yena saṃjaya uvāca kṣayam manuṣya dehānām gaja vāji ratha kṣayam śṛṇu rājan sthiraḥ bhūtvā tava eva apanayaḥ mahān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu śalyena pīḍitaḥ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ pīḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ madra adhipatim āyasaiḥ nyavārayata yat tūrṇam śalyam samiti śobhanam na antaram dadṛśe kaḥ cit tayoḥ saṃrabdhayoḥ raṇe tatas śalyaḥ mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge atha enam śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata girim jalāgame yadvat jaladāḥ jala dhāriṇaḥ tatas madra adhipa ratham kārṣṇiḥ prāpya ati kopanaḥ ārtāyanim ameya ātmā vivyādha viśikhaiḥ tribhiḥ tatas tu tāvakāḥ rājan parīpsantaḥ raṇe madra rāja ratham tūrṇam parivārya avatasthire duryodhanaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca duḥśāsana viviṃśatī ete madra adhipa ratham pālayantaḥ sthitāḥ raṇe tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ draupadeya abhimanyuḥ ca mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau dhārtarāṣṭrān daśa rathān daśa eva pratyavārayan nānā rūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjantaḥ viśām pate abhyavartanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca prekṣakāḥ rathinaḥ abhavan śastrāṇi aneka rūpāṇi visṛjantaḥ mahā rathāḥ te yattāḥ jāta saṃrambhāḥ sarve anyonyam jighāṃsavaḥ anyonya spardhayā rājan jñātayaḥ saṃgatāḥ mithas samāgatāḥ mahā rāja jñātayaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ mahā astrāṇi vimuñcantaḥ samāpetuḥ amarṣaṇāḥ duryodhanaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā raṇe vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ caturbhiḥ tvaritaḥ bhṛśam durmarṣaṇaḥ ca viṃśatyā citrasenaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ viviṃśatiḥ pañcabhiḥ ca tribhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tathā vikarṇaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ purumitraḥ ca pañcabhiḥ madra adhipaḥ tribhiḥ ca eva vikarṇaḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tān pratyavidhyat rāja indra pārṣataḥ śatru tāpanaḥ ekaikam pañcaviṃśatyā darśayan pāṇi lāghavam mādrī putrau tu samare mātulam mātṛ nandanau tatas śalyaḥ mahā rāja svasrīyau rathinām varau atha duryodhanam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ vidhitsuḥ kalahasya antam gadām jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ tam udyata gadam dṛṣṭvā kailāsam iva śṛṅgiṇam bhīmasenam mahā bāhum putrāḥ te prādravan bhayāt anīkam daśa sāhasram kuñjarāṇām tarasviṇām māgadham puratas kṛtvā bhīmasenam samabhyayāt āpatantam ca tam dṛṣṭvā gaja anīkam vṛkodaraḥ gadā pāṇiḥ avārohat rathāt siṃhaḥ iva unnadan ghoraḥ pratibhayaḥ ca āsīt pinākī iva pinākadhṛk nirmathyamānām kruddhena pragṛhya mahatīm gadām adrisāra mayīm gurum pragṛhya mahatīm gadām abhyadhāvat gaja anīkam vyādita āsyaḥ iva antakaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sa vajraḥ iva vāsavaḥ vipradhvastāḥ gajāḥ rājan madam tyaktvā bhayam gatāḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ pṛṣṭham bhīmasya rakṣantaḥ śara varṣeṇa vāraṇān nākuliḥ tu śatānīkaḥ samare śatru pūga hā pāṇḍavāḥ gaja yodhinām śirobhiḥ prapatadbhiḥ ca bāhubhiḥ ca vibhūṣitaiḥ aśma vṛṣṭiḥ iva ābhāti pāṇibhiḥ ca saha aṅkuśaiḥ hṛta uttamāṅgāḥ skandheṣu gajānām gaja yodhinaḥ adṛśyanta acala agreṣu drumāḥ bhagna śikhāḥ iva dhṛṣṭadyumna hatān anyān apaśyāma mahā gajān patitān pātyamānān ca pārṣatena mahātmanā jaghāna eka iṣuṇā vīraḥ saubhadraḥ para vīra hā tasya āvarjita nāgasya kārṣṇiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ vigāhya tat gaja anīkam bhīmasenaḥ api pāṇḍavaḥ eka prahāra abhihatān bhīmasenena kuñjarān bhagna dantān bhagna kaṭān bhagna sakthān ca vāraṇān bhagna pṛṣṭhān bhagna kumbhān nihatān parvata upamān nadataḥ sīdataḥ ca anyān vimukhān samare gajān vimūtrān bhagna saṃvignān tathā viśakṛtaḥ aparān bhīmasenasya mārgeṣu gatāsūn parvata upamān apaśyāma hatān nāgān niṣṭanantaḥ tathā apare vihvalantaḥ gatāḥ bhūmim śailāḥ iva dharā tale mārgeṇa gacchamānasya bhīmasya ubhaya pārśvatas dṛśyante patitāḥ nāgāḥ vajreṇa iva śiloccayāḥ medas rudhira digdha aṅgaḥ vasā majjā samukṣitaḥ vyacarat samare bhīmaḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ gajānām rudhira aktām tām gadām bibhrat vṛkodaraḥ ghoraḥ pratibhayaḥ ca āsīt pinākī iva pinākadhṛk sahasā prādravan śiṣṭāḥ mṛdnantaḥ te vāhinīm tam hi vīram mahā iṣvāsāḥ saubhadra pramukhāḥ rathāḥ śoṇita aktām gadām bibhrat ukṣitaḥ gaja śoṇitaiḥ kṛtāntaḥ iva raudra ātmā bhīmasenaḥ vyadṛśyata vyāyacchamānam gadayā dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata nṛtyamānam apaśyāma nṛtyantam iva śaṃkaram yama daṇḍa upamām gurum indra aśani sama svanām apaśyāma mahā rāja raudrām viśasanīm gadām vimiśrām keśa majjābhiḥ pradigdhām rudhireṇa ca mārutiḥ śūla hastasya purā iva abhighnataḥ paśūn yathā paśūnām saṃghātam yaṣṭyā pālaḥ prakālayet tathā bhīmaḥ gaja anīkam gadayā paryakālayat gadayā vadhyamānāḥ te mārgaṇaiḥ ca samantataḥ svāni anīkāni mṛdnantaḥ prādravan kuñjarāḥ tava mahā vātaḥ iva abhrāṇi vidhamitvā sa vāraṇān atiṣṭhat tumule bhīmaḥ śmaśāne iva śūlabhṛt uvāca tatas sarvāṇi anīkāni te putrasya śāsanāt āpatantam su duṣpāram samudram iva parvaṇi ratha nāga aśva kalilam śaṅkha dundubhi nāditam udīrṇām pṛthivīm sarvām sa aśvām sa ratha kuñjarām asaṃbhramam bhīmasenaḥ gadayā samatāḍayat sa saṃvārya bala oghān tān gadayā rathinām varaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca eva putrāḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ draupadeya abhimanyuḥ ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahā rathaḥ tatas śaikyāyasīm gurvīm pragṛhya mahatīm gadām avadhīt tāvakān yodhān daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ pothayan ratha vṛndāni vāji vṛndāni ūru vegena saṃkarṣan ratha jālāni pāṇḍavaḥ pramardayan gajān sarvān naḍvalāni iva kuñjaraḥ sādinaḥ ca aśva pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ bhūmau ca eva padātinaḥ gadayā vyadhamat sarvān vātaḥ vṛkṣān iva ojasā sā vai majjā vasā māṃsaiḥ pradigdhā rudhireṇa ca adṛśyata mahā raudrā gadā nāga aśva ghātinī raṇa aṅgaṇam tat abhavat mṛtyoḥ āghāta saṃnibham yama daṇḍa upamām ugrām indra aśani sama svanām dadṛśuḥ bhīmasenasya raudrām viśasanīm gadām gadā māruta vegaḥ abhūt viṣphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ babhau rūpam mahā ghoram kālasya iva yuga kṣaye tam tathā mahatīm senām drāvayantam punar punar dṛṣṭvā mṛtyum iva āyāntam sarve vimanasaḥ abhavan yatas yatas prekṣate sma gadām udyamya pāṇḍavaḥ grasamānam anīkāni vyādita āsyam iva antakam tam tathā bhīma karmāṇam pragṛhīta mahā gadam dṛṣṭvā vṛkodaram bhīṣmaḥ sahasā eva samabhyayāt chādayan śara varṣeṇa parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān tam āyāntam tathā dṛṣṭvā vyātta ānanam iva antakam bhīṣmam bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ pratyudīyāt amarṣaṇaḥ tam yāntam aśvaiḥ rajata prakāśaiḥ śarān dhamantam dhanuṣā dṛḍhena na aśaknuvan vārayitum tadānīm sarve gaṇāḥ bhārata ye tvadīyāḥ avidhyat enam niśitaiḥ śara agraiḥ alambuṣaḥ anvāgatam vṛṣṇi varam niśamya madhye ripūṇām parivartamānam prāvartayantam kuru puṃgavān ca punar punar ca praṇadantam ājau yodhāḥ tvadīyāḥ śara varṣaiḥ avarṣan na aśaknuvan vārayitum variṣṭham madhyaṃdine sūryam iva ātapantam na tatra kaḥ cit a viṣaṇṇaḥ āsīt ṛte rājan somadattasya putrāt dṛṣṭvā rathān svān vyapanīyamānān pratyudyayau sātyakim yoddhum icchan uvāca tatas bhūriśravāḥ rājan sātyakim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ kauravam sātyakiḥ ca eva śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve sātyakim rabhasam raṇe vivyādha niśitaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ kaṅka pattraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sva ratham su mahā balaḥ āruroha ratha śreṣṭham viśokam ca idam abravīt ete mahā rathāḥ śūrāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ mahā balāḥ saphalaḥ sūta adya iha yaḥ aham paśyāmi sodarān yatra aśoka samutkṣiptāḥ reṇavaḥ ratha nemibhiḥ tatra tiṣṭhati saṃnaddhaḥ svayam rājā suyodhana bhrātaraḥ ca asya saṃnaddhāḥ kula putrāḥ mada utkaṭāḥ etān adya haniṣyāmi paśyataḥ te na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt mama aśvān saṃgrāme yattaḥ saṃyaccha sārathe vivyādha daśabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ tam tu duryodhanaḥ ṣaṣṭyā viddhvā bhīmam mahā balam muṣṭideśe śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ tribhiḥ rājā hasan iva bhīmaḥ tu prekṣya yantāram viśokam saṃyuge tadā pīḍitam viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ te putreṇa dhanvinā amṛṣyamāṇaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ dhanuḥ divyam parāmṛśat sa niṣaṇṇaḥ rathopasthe mūrchām abhijagāma ha tam dṛṣṭvā vyathitam bhīmam abhimanyu purogamāḥ na amṛṣyanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ tatas tu tumulām vṛṣṭim śastrāṇām tigma tejasām pātayām āsuḥ avyagrāḥ putrasya te mūrdhani pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām bhīmasenaḥ mahat balaḥ śalyam ca pañcaviṃśatyā śaraiḥ vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ rukma puṅkhaiḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sa viddhaḥ vyapayāt raṇāt senāpatiḥ suṣeṇaḥ ca jalasaṃdhaḥ sulocanaḥ visṛjantaḥ bahūn bāṇān krodha saṃrakta locanāḥ putrān tu tava saṃprekṣya bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ vilihan vīraḥ paśu madhye vṛkaḥ yathā senāpateḥ kṣurapreṇa śiraḥ ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ saṃprahṛṣya ca hṛṣṭa ātmā tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ mahā bhujaḥ suṣeṇam ca tatas hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyave vicitram ca tathā hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyave ugrasya sa śirastrāṇam śiraḥ candra upamam bhuvi pātayām āsa bhallena kuṇḍalābhyām vibhūṣitam bhīmabāhum ca saptatyā sa aśva ketum sa sārathim nināya samare bhīmaḥ para lokāya māriṣa tatas su locanam bhīmaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahā mṛdhe miṣatām sarva sainyānām anayat yama sādanam putrāḥ tu tava tam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasena parākramam śeṣāḥ ye anye abhavan tatra te bhīmasya bhaya arditāḥ vipradrutāḥ diśaḥ rājan vadhyamānāḥ mahātmanā tatas abravīt śāṃtanavaḥ sarvān eva mahā rathān eṣa bhīmaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān mahā rathān yathā prāgryān yathā jyeṣṭhān yathā śūrān ca saṃgatān nipātayati ugra dhanvā tam pramathnīta pārthivāḥ evam uktāḥ tatas sarve dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥ āpatan eva ca raṇe bhīmasenam śilā śitaiḥ adṛśyam samare cakre jīmūtaḥ iva bhāskaram abhimanyu mukhāḥ tatra na amṛṣyanta mahā rathāḥ bhīmasya ācchādanam saṃkhye sva bāhu balam āśritāḥ te enam śara varṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan gajam ca śara vṛṣṭyā tam bibhiduḥ te samantataḥ sa śastra vṛṣṭyā abhihataḥ prādravat dviguṇam padam prāgjyotiṣa gajaḥ rājan nānā liṅgaiḥ su tejanaiḥ saṃjāta rudhira utpīḍaḥ prekṣaṇīyaḥ abhavat raṇe abhyadhāvata tān sarvān kāla utsṛṣṭaḥ iva antakaḥ dviguṇam javam āsthāya kampayan caraṇaiḥ mahīm tasya tat su mahat rūpam dṛṣṭvā sarve mahā rathāḥ ājaghāna nara vyāghra śareṇa nata parvaṇā saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ tena rājñā mahā rathaḥ mūrchayā abhiparīta aṅgaḥ dhvaja yaṣṭim upāśritaḥ tān tu bhītān samālakṣya bhīmasenam ca mūrchitam nanāda balavat nādam bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān sa kṛtvā dāruṇām māyām bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinīm adṛśyata nimeṣa ardhāt ghora rūpam samāśritaḥ airāvatam samāruhya svayam māyā mayam kṛtam kailāsa giri saṃkāśam vajrapāṇiḥ iva abhyayāt tasya ca anye api diṅnāgāḥ babhūvuḥ anuyāyinaḥ añjanaḥ vāmanaḥ ca eva mahāpadmaḥ ca suprabhaḥ trayaḥ ete mahā nāgāḥ rākṣasaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ kāma rūpa dharāḥ ca eva bhavanti bahu rūpakāḥ praṇamya vikacaḥ pādau agṛhṇāt pitaram tadā mātuḥ ca parama iṣvāsaḥ tau ca nāma asya cakratuḥ ghaṭotkacasya ukta pūrvam mātā tam pratyabhāṣata sa hi sṛṣṭaḥ maghavnā karṇa hetoḥ mahātmanā tejaḥ vīrya bala upetāḥ mahā bala parākramāḥ preṣitāḥ ca mahā rāja rākṣasaiḥ ca caturdiśam ghaṭotkacaḥ tu svam nāgam codayām āsa tam tatas te ca anye coditāḥ nāgāḥ rākṣasaiḥ taiḥ mahā balaiḥ paripetuḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ catur daṃṣṭrāḥ caturdiśam bhagadattasya tam nāgam viṣāṇaiḥ te abhyapīḍayan saṃpīḍyamānaḥ taiḥ nāgaiḥ vedanā ārtaḥ śara āturaḥ nyavartata mahā ghoṣaḥ bhīmasena śara arditaḥ śrutvā bhīṣmaḥ abravīt droṇam rājānam ca suyodhanam eṣa yudhyati saṃgrāme haiḍimbena durātmanā rākṣasaḥ ca mahā māyaḥ sa ca rājā atikopanaḥ śrūyate hi eṣa hṛṣṭānām pāṇḍavānām mahā svanaḥ arakṣyamāṇaḥ samare kṣipram prāṇān vimokṣyate te tvaradhvam mahā vīryāḥ kim cireṇa prayāmahe mahān hi vartate raudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ bhaktaḥ ca kula putraḥ ca śūraḥ ca pṛtanāpatiḥ yuktam tasya paritrāṇam kartum asmābhiḥ acyutāḥ bhīṣmasya tat vacaḥ śrutvā bhāradvāja purogamāḥ sahitāḥ sarva rājānaḥ bhagadatta parīpsayā tān prayātān samālokya yudhiṣṭhira purogamāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham pṛṣṭhatas anuyayuḥ parān tāni anīkāni atha ālokya rākṣasa indraḥ pratāpavān nanāda su mahā nādam visphoṭam aśaneḥ iva tasya tam ninadam śrutvā dṛṣṭvā nāgān ca yudhyataḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ bhūyas bhāradvājam abhāṣata bala vīrya samāviṣṭaḥ sa sahāyaḥ ca sāṃpratam labdha lakṣyaḥ prahārī ca vayam ca śrānta vāhanāḥ pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca divasam kṣata vikṣatāḥ idānīm yudhi nirjetum na śakyaḥ asau sa rākṣasaḥ tat na me rocate yuddham pāṇḍavaiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ ghuṣyatām avahāraḥ adya śvas yotsyāmaḥ paraiḥ saha pitāmaha vacaḥ śrutvā tathā cakruḥ sma kauravāḥ upāyena apayānam te ghaṭotkaca bhaya arditāḥ kauraveṣu nivṛtteṣu pāṇḍavāḥ jita kāśinaḥ pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca puraskṛtya ghaṭotkacam vrīḍamānāḥ niśā kāle pāṇḍaveyaiḥ parājitāḥ śara vikṣata gātrāḥ ca pāṇḍu putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ pūjayantaḥ tadā anyonyam mudā paramayā yutāḥ nadantaḥ vividhān nādān tūrya svana vimiśritān siṃhanādān ca kurvāṇāḥ vimiśrān śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ ghaṭṭayantaḥ ca marmāṇi te putrasya māriṣa kampayantaḥ ca putrāṇām te cetāṃsi bhūmipa putrāḥ ca te rāja indra tathā eva śara vikṣatāḥ prayātāḥ śibirāya eva niśā kāle paraṃtapāḥ muhūrtam cintayām āsa bāṣpa śoka samākulaḥ tatas kṛtvā vidhim sarvam śibirasya yathāvidhi uvāca śrutvā pāṇḍu kumārāṇām karma devaiḥ su duṣkaram putrāṇām ca parābhavam śrutvā saṃjaya sarvaśas yatra bhīṣma mukhān śūrān astra jñān yodha sattamān pāṇḍavānām anīkāni yodhayanti prahāriṇaḥ kena avadhyāḥ mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍu putrāḥ mahā balāḥ kena datta varāḥ tāta kim vā jñānam vidanti te yena kṣayam na gacchanti divi tārā gaṇāḥ iva punar punar na mṛṣyāmi hatam sainyam sma pāṇḍavaiḥ mayi eva daṇḍaḥ patati daivāt parama dāruṇaḥ yathā a vadhyāḥ pāṇḍu sutāḥ yathā vadhyāḥ ca mama sutāḥ na hi pāram prapaśyāmi duḥkhasya asya katham cana putrāṇām vyasanam manye dhruvam prāptam su dāruṇam ghātayiṣyati mama putrān sarvān bhīmaḥ na saṃśayaḥ na hi paśyāmi tam vīram yaḥ me rakṣet sutān raṇe dhruvam vināśaḥ samare putrāṇām mama saṃjaya tasmāt mama kāraṇam sūta yuktim ca eva viśeṣataḥ duryodhanaḥ api yat cakre dṛṣṭvā svān vimukhān raṇe drauṇiḥ vā api mahā iṣvāsaḥ vikarṇaḥ vā mahā balaḥ niścayaḥ vā api kaḥ teṣām tadā hi āsīt mahātmanām vimukheṣu mahā prājña mama putreṣu saṃjaya uvāca śṛṇu rājan avahitaḥ śrutvā ca eva avadhāraya na eva mantra kṛtam kim cit na eva māyām tathāvidhām na vai vibhīṣakām kām cit rājan kurvanti pāṇḍavāḥ dharmeṇa sarva kāryāṇi kīrtitāni iti bhārata ārabhante sadā pārthāḥ prārthayānāḥ mahat yaśaḥ tena avadhyāḥ raṇe pārthāḥ jaya yuktāḥ ca pārthiva tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ pāpeṣu abhiratāḥ sadā niṣṭhurāḥ hīna karmāṇaḥ tena hīyanti saṃyuge su bahūni nṛśaṃsāni putraiḥ te janeśvara nikṛtāni iha pāṇḍūnām nīcaiḥ iva yathā naraiḥ sarvam ca tat an ādṛtya putrāṇām tava kilbiṣam sa apahnavāḥ sadā eva āsan pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja tasya pāpasya satatam kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ saṃprāptam su mahat ghoram phalam kiṃpāka saṃnibham sa tat bhuṅkṣva mahā rāja sa putraḥ sa suhṛd janaḥ na avabudhyasi yat rājan vāryamāṇaḥ suhṛd janaiḥ vidureṇa atha bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā tathā mayā ca api asakṛt vāryamāṇaḥ na gṛhṇasi putrāṇām matam āsthāya jitān manyasi pāṇḍavān śṛṇu bhūyas yathātattvam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi kāraṇam bharata śreṣṭha pāṇḍavānām jayam prati tat te aham kathayiṣyāmi yathāśrutam ariṃdama duryodhanena saṃpṛṣṭaḥ etam artham pitāmahaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn raṇe sarvān nirjitān su mahā rathān śoka saṃmūḍha hṛdayaḥ niśā kāle sma kauravaḥ pitāmaham mahā prājñam vinayena upagamya ha tvam ca droṇaḥ ca śalyaḥ ca kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ tathā eva ca kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ bhūriśravāḥ vikarṇaḥ ca bhagadattaḥ ca vīryavān mahā rathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kula putrāḥ tanutyajaḥ trayāṇām api lokānām paryāptāḥ iti mama matiḥ pāṇḍavānām samastāḥ ca na tiṣṭhanti parākrame tatra me saṃśayaḥ jātaḥ tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan vacaḥ mahyam yat tvām vakṣyāmi kaurava kriyatām pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham śamaḥ bharata sattama bhuñja imām pṛthivīm rājan bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sukhī durhṛdaḥ tāpayan sarvān nandayan ca api bāndhavān tat idam samanuprāptam yat pāṇḍūn avamanyase yaḥ ca hetuḥ avadhya tve teṣām akliṣṭa karmaṇām tam śṛṇuṣva mahā rāja mama kīrtayataḥ prabho na asti lokeṣu tat bhūtam bhavitā naḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ jayet pāṇḍavān saṃkhye pālitān śārṅgadhanvanā purāṇa gītam dharma jña tat śṛṇuṣva yathātatham purā kila surāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ ca samāgatāḥ madhye teṣām samāsīnaḥ prajāpatiḥ apaśyata dhyānena āvedya tam brahmā kṛtvā ca niyataḥ añjalim namaścakāra hṛṣṭa ātmā paramam parameśvaram ṛṣayaḥ tu atha devāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā brahmāṇam utthitam jagāda jagataḥ sraṣṭā param parama dharma vid viśvāvasuḥ viśvamūrtiḥ viśveśaḥ viṣvaksenaḥ viśvakarmā vaśī ca viśveśvaraḥ vāsudevaḥ asi tasmāt yoga ātmānam daivatam tvām upaimi viśvāvāsaḥ viśvamūrtiḥ viṣvaksenaḥ janārdanaḥ yogeśvara namaḥ te astu saṃsāra arṇava tāraṇa padmagarbha viśāla akṣa jaya loka īśvara īśvara nārāyaṇa su duṣpāra jaya śārṅga dhanus dhara harivāsa viśām īśa viśvāvāsa amita avyaya asaṃkhyeya ātma bhāva jña jaya gambhīra kāma da kṛta kārya kṛta prajña dharma jña vijaya ajaya guhya ātman sarva bhūta ātman sphuṭa saṃbhūta saṃbhava ātma bhūta mahābhūta karma ātman jaya karma da pādau tava dharā devī diśaḥ bāhuḥ divam śiraḥ mūrtiḥ te aham surāḥ kāyaḥ candra ādityau ca cakṣuṣī balam tapaḥ ca satyam ca dharmaḥ kāma ātmajaḥ prabho tejaḥ agniḥ pavanaḥ śvāsaḥ apaḥ te sveda saṃbhavāḥ aśvinau śravaṇau nityam devī jihvā sarasvatī vedāḥ saṃskāra niṣṭhāḥ hi tvayi idam jagat āśritam na saṃkhyām na parīmāṇam na tejaḥ na parākramam na balam yoga yogi īśa jānīmaḥ te na saṃbhavam arcayāmaḥ sadā viṣṇo parameśam maheśvaram ṛṣayaḥ deva gandharvāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa pannagāḥ piśācāḥ mānuṣāḥ ca eva mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpāḥ evamādi mayā sṛṣṭam pṛthivyām tvad prasāda jam padmanābha viśāla akṣa kṛṣṇa duḥsvapna nāśana tvam gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām tvam netā tvam jagat mukham tasmāt bhava viśāla akṣa yadu vaṃśa vivardhanaḥ dharma saṃsthāpana arthāya daiteyānām vadhāya ca jagantaḥ dhāraṇa arthāya vijñāpyam kuru mama prabho sṛṣṭvā saṃkarṣaṇam devam svayam ātmānam ātmanā kṛṣṇa tvam ātmanā asrākṣīḥ pradyumnam ca ātma sambhavam aniruddhaḥ asṛjat mām vai brahmāṇam loka dhāriṇam tasmāt yācāmi lokeśa catur ātmānam ātmanā vibhajya bhāgaśas ātmānam vraja mānuṣa tām vibho dharmam sthāpya yaśaḥ prāpya yogam prāpsyasi tattvāt tvām hi brahmarṣayaḥ loke devāḥ ca amita vikrama sarva bhūta īśvaram devam yogam yogeśvaram prabhum sthita ca sarve tvayi bhūta saṃghāḥ kṛ āśrayam tvām vara dam su bāhu uvāca tatas sa bhagavant devaḥ lokānām parama īśvaraḥ brahmānam pratyuvāca idam snigdha gambhīrayā girā vāgbhiḥ stutaḥ variṣṭhābhiḥ śrotum icchāma tam vayam tena asmi kṛta saṃvādaḥ prasannena sura ṛṣabhāḥ mānuṣam lokam ātiṣṭha vāsudeva iti śrutaḥ asurāṇām vadha arthāya saṃbhavasva mahī tale ṭī ṭī vāsudevaḥ iti śrutaḥ vāsudeva gṛhe sākṣāt saṃgrāme nihatāḥ ye te daitya dānava rākṣasāḥ te ime nṛṣu saṃbhūtāḥ ghora rūpāḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām vadha artha bhagavant nareṇa sahita vaśī mānuṣīm yonim āsthāya cariṣyati mahī tale nara nārāyaṇau yau tau purāṇau ṛṣi sattamau sahitau mānuṣe loke saṃbhūtau amita dyutī mūḍhāḥ tu etau na jānanti nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī na avajñeyaḥ mahā vīryaḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ etat puruṣa saṃjñam vai purāṇam rūpam uttamam etat puruṣa saṃjñam vai gīyate jñāyate na ca etat paramakam satyam kīrtitam viśvakarmaṇā na avajñeyaḥ vāsudevaḥ mānuṣaḥ ayam iti prabhuḥ yaḥ ca mānuṣa mātraḥ ayam iti brūyāt su manda dhīḥ hṛṣīkeśam avajñānāt tam āhuḥ puruṣa adhamam yoginam tam mahātmānam praviṣṭam mānuṣīm tanum avamanyet vāsudevam tam āhuḥ tāmasam janāḥ devam carācara ātmānam śrīvatsa aṅkam su varcasam padmanābham na jānāti tam āhuḥ tāmasam janāḥ kirīṭa kaustubha dharam mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaram evam viditvā tattva artham lokānām īśvara īśvaraḥ evam uktvā sa bhagavān sarvān deva gaṇān purā kathām tām brahmaṇā gītām śrutvā prītāḥ divam yayuḥ etat śrutam mayā tāta ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām vāsudevam kathayatām samavāye purātanam jāmadagnyasya rāmasya mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥ vyāsa nāradayoḥ ca api śrutam śruta viśārada vāsudevam mahātmānam lokānām īśvara īśvaram yasya asau ātmajaḥ brahmā sarvasya jagataḥ pitā mā gaccha saṃyugam tena vāsudevena dhīmatā mā pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham iti tat ca mohāt na budhyase manye tvām rākṣasam krūram tathā ca asi tamaḥ vṛtaḥ yasmāt dviṣasi govindam pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam nara nārāyaṇau devau na anyaḥ dviṣyāt hi mānavaḥ tasmāt bravīmi te rājan eṣa vai śāśvataḥ avyayaḥ sarva loka mayaḥ nityaḥ śāstā dhātā dharaḥ dhruvaḥ lokān dhārayate yaḥ trīn carācara guruḥ prabhuḥ yoddhā jayaḥ ca jetā ca sarva prakṛtiḥ īśvaraḥ dhṛtāḥ pāṇḍu sutāḥ rājñ jayaḥ ca eṣām bhaviṣyati śreyaḥ yuktām sadā buddhim pāṇḍavānām dadhāti yaḥ saḥ eṣa śāśvataḥ devaḥ sarva guhya mayaḥ śivaḥ vāsudevaḥ iti jñeyaḥ yat mām pṛcchasi bhārata brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ ca kṛta lakṣaṇaiḥ sātvatam vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṃkarṣaṇena yaḥ saḥ eṣa sarva asura martya lokam samudra kakṣyā antaritāḥ purīḥ ca yuge yuge mānuṣam ca eva vāsam punar punar sṛjate vāsudevaḥ tasya āgamam pratiṣṭhām ca jñātum icche pitāmaha uvāca vāsudevaḥ mahat bhūtam saṃbhūtam saha daivataiḥ na param puṇḍarīkākṣāt dṛśyate bharata ṛṣabha nāradasya ca deva ṛṣeḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya ca asitaḥ devalaḥ ca api vālakhilyāḥ tapodhanāḥ sarva bhūtāni bhūtātmā mahātmā puruṣottamaḥ sa sṛṣṭvā pṛthivīm devaḥ sarva loka īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ apsu vai śayanam cakre mahātmā puruṣottamaḥ mukhatas saḥ agnim asṛjat prāṇāt vāyum atha api ca sarasvatīm ca vedān ca manasaḥ sasṛje acyutaḥ eṣa lokān sasarja ādau devān ca ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ saha nidhanam ca eva mṛtyum ca prajānām prabhavaḥ avyayaḥ eṣa kartā ca kāryam ca pūrvadevaḥ svayamprabhuḥ ubhe saṃdhye diśaḥ kham ca niyamam ca janārdanaḥ ṛṣīn ca eva hi govindaḥ tapaḥ ca eva anu kalpayat sraṣṭāram jagantaḥ ca api mahātmā prabhuḥ avyayaḥ agra jam sarva bhūtānām saṃkarṣaṇam akalpayat tasmāt nārāyaṇaḥ jajñe devadevaḥ sanātanaḥ tasmāt pitāmahaḥ jātaḥ tasmāt jātāḥ tu imāḥ prajāḥ śeṣam ca akalpayat devam anantam iti yam viduḥ yaḥ dhārayati bhūtāni dharām ca imām sa parvatām harantam brahmaṇaḥ vedān jaghāna brahmaṇaḥ pitā tasya tāta vadhāt eva deva dānava mānavāḥ madhusūdanam iti āhuḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca janārdanam eṣa mātā pitā ca eva sarveṣām prāṇinām hariḥ param hi puṇḍarīkākṣāt na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati mukhataḥ asṛjat brāhmaṇān bāhubhyām kṣatriyān tathā vaiśyān ca api ūroḥ rājñ śūdrān padbhyām tathā eva ca brahma bhūtam amāvāsyām paurṇamāsyām tathā eva ca yoga bhūtam paricaran keśavam mahat āpnuyāt keśavaḥ paramam tejaḥ sarva loka pitāmahaḥ evam āhuḥ hṛṣīkeśam munayaḥ vai narādhipa evam enam vijānīhi ācāryam pitaram gurum kṛṣṇaḥ yasya prasīdeta lokāḥ tena akṣayāḥ jitāḥ yaḥ ca eva enam bhaya sthāne keśavam śaraṇam vrajet sadā naraḥ paṭhan ca idam svastimān sa sukhī bhavet ye ca kṛṣṇam prapadyante te na muhyanti mānavāḥ bhaye mahati ye magnāḥ pāti nityam janārdanaḥ etat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ jñātvā yāthātathyena bhārata sarva ātmanā mahātmānam keśavam jagat īśvaram prapannaḥ śaraṇam rājan yogānām īśvaram prabhum uvāca śṛṇu ca idam mahā rāja brahma bhūta stavam mama sādhyānām api devānām devadeva īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ loka bhāvana bhāva jñaḥ iti tvām nāradaḥ abravīt bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca mārkaṇḍeyaḥ abhyuvāca ha yajñānām ca eva yajñam tvām tapaḥ ca tapasām api devānām api devam ca tvām āha bhagavān bhṛguḥ purāṇe bhairavam rūpam viṣṇo bhūtapate iti vai vāsudevaḥ vasūnām tvam śakram sthāpayitā tathā pūrve prajā nisargeṣu dakṣam āhuḥ prajāpatim sraṣṭāram sarva bhūtānām aṅgirāḥ tvām tatas abravīt śirasā te divam vyāptam bāhubhyām pṛthivī dhṛtā jaṭharam te trayaḥ lokāḥ puruṣaḥ asi sanātanaḥ evam tvām abhijānanti tapasā bhāvitāḥ narāḥ ātma darśana tṛptānām ṛṣīṇām ca api sattamaḥ rājarṣīṇām udārāṇām āhaveṣu anivartinām eṣa te vistaraḥ tāta saṃkṣepaḥ ca prakīrtitaḥ purāṇapuruṣasya iha yad artham nṛṣu saṃbhavaḥ uvāca puṇyam śrutvā etat ākhyānam mahā rāja sutaḥ tava keśavam bahu mene sa pāṇḍavān ca mahā rathān tam abravīt mahā rāja bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punar māhātmyam te śrutam rājan keśavasya mahātmanaḥ nārāyaṇam ca saṃgrāme avadhyau tau yatas smṛtau dharmarājaḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca mādrī putraḥ ca pāṇḍavau ete api avadhyāḥ kathitāḥ purāṇe parama ṛṣiṇā yad artham nṛṣu saṃbhūtau nara nārāyaṇau ubhau yathā ca pāṇḍavāḥ rājan agamyāḥ yudhi kasya cid prītimān hi dṛḍham kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍaveṣu yaśasviṣu tasmāt bravīmi rāja indra śamaḥ bhavatu pāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthivīm bhuṅkṣva sahitaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ balibhiḥ vaśī nara nārāyaṇau devau avajñāya naśiṣyasi evam uktvā tava pitā tūṣṇīm āsīt viśām pate vyasarjayat ca rājānam śayanam ca viveśa ha rājā api śibiram prāyāt praṇipatya mahātmane śiśye ca śayane śubhre tām rātrim bharata ṛṣabha uvāca vyuṣitāyām ca śarvaryām udite ca divākare tasyām rātrau vyatītāyām niryayuḥ kuru puṃgavāḥ puraskṛtya mahātmānam bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam yudhi abhyadhāvan ca saṃkruddhāḥ paraspara jigīṣavaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca rājan durmantrite te vyūhau ca vyūhya saṃrabdhāḥ saṃprayuddhāḥ prahāriṇaḥ arakṣat makara vyūham bhīṣmaḥ rājan samantataḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan arakṣan vyūham ātmanaḥ ajātaśatruḥ śatrūṇām manāṃsi samakampayat yathāvyūham śāṃtanavaḥ saḥ anvavartata tat punar mahatā ratha vaṃśena saṃvṛtaḥ rathinām varaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā prodyatān saṃkhye pāṇḍavāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ netre śikhaṇḍī durdharṣaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ śīrṣam tasya bhavat vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ vidhunvan gāṇḍivam pārthaḥ grīvāyām abhavat tadā akṣauhiṇyā samagrā yā vāma pakṣaḥ abhavat tadā mahātmā drupadaḥ śrīmān saha putreṇa saṃyuge dakṣiṇaḥ ca abhavat pakṣaḥ kaikeyaḥ akṣauhiṇī patiḥ pṛṣṭhatas draupadeyāḥ ca saubhadraḥ ca api vīryavān pṛṣṭhe samabhavat śrīmān svayam rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhrātṛbhyām sahitaḥ dhīmān yamābhyām cāru vikramaḥ bhīṣmam āsādya saṃgrāme chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ tatas bhīṣmaḥ mahā astrāṇi pātayām āsa bhārata mohayan pāṇḍu putrāṇām vyūḍham sainyam mahā āhave bhīṣmam śara sahasreṇa vivyādha raṇa mūrdhani parisaṃvārya ca astrāṇi bhīṣma muktāni saṃyuge svena anīkena hṛṣṭena yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhāradvājam abhāṣata pūrvam dṛṣṭvā vadham ghoram balasya balinām varaḥ bhrātṝṇām ca vadham yuddhe smaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ ācārya satatam tvam hi hita kāmaḥ mama anagha vayam hi tvām samāśritya bhīṣmam ca eva pitāmaham devān api raṇe jetum prārthayāmaḥ na saṃśayaḥ kim u pāṇḍu sutān yuddhe hīna vīrya parākramān sa tathā kuru bhadram te yathā vadhyanti pāṇḍavāḥ uvāca tatra rājānam saṃkruddhaḥ iva niḥśvasan bāliśaḥ tvam na jānīṣe pāṇḍavānām parākramam na śakyāḥ hi yathā jetum pāṇḍavāḥ hi mahā balāḥ yathābalam yathāvīryam karma kuryām aham hi te abhinat pāṇḍava anīkam prekṣamāṇasya sātyakeḥ sātyakiḥ tu tadā droṇam vārayām āsa bhārata śaineyam tu raṇe kruddhaḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān saṃrakṣan sātyakim rājan droṇāt śastrabhṛtām varāt tatas droṇaḥ ca bhīṣmaḥ ca tathā śalyaḥ ca māriṣa bhīmasenam raṇe kruddhāḥ chādayām cakrire śaraiḥ tatra abhimanyuḥ saṃkruddhaḥ draupadeyāḥ ca māriṣa vivyadhuḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sarvān tān udyata āyudhān bhīṣma droṇau ca saṃkruddhau āpatantau mahā balau pratyudyayau śikhaṇḍī tu mahā iṣvāsaḥ mahā āhave abhyavarṣat śaraiḥ tūrṇam chādayānaḥ divākaram śikhaṇḍinam samāsādya bharatānām pitāmahaḥ rakṣamāṇaḥ tatas bhīṣmam te putreṇa coditaḥ śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya droṇam śastrabhṛtām varam jugopa bhīṣmam āsādya prārthayānaḥ mahat yaśaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan puraskṛtya dhanaṃjayam bhīṣmam eva abhyavartanta jaye kṛtvā dṛḍhām matim jayam ca kāṅkṣatām nityam yaśaḥ ca parama adbhutam uvāca akarot tumulam yuddham bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā pūrvāhṇe tat mahā raudram rājñām yuddham avartata kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca mukhya śūra vināśanam abhavat tumulaḥ śabdaḥ saṃspṛśan gaganam mahat nadadbhiḥ ca mahā nāgaiḥ heṣamāṇaiḥ ca vājibhiḥ bherī śaṅkha ninādaiḥ ca tumulaḥ samapadyata yuyutsavaḥ te vikrāntāḥ vijayāya mahā balāḥ śirasām pātyamānānām samare niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ aśma vṛṣṭiḥ iva ākāśe babhūva bharata ṛṣabha kuṇḍala uṣṇīṣa dhārīṇi jātarūpa ujjvalāni ca patitāni sma dṛśyante śirāṃsi bharata ṛṣabha sa hasta ābharaṇaiḥ ca anyaiḥ abhavat chāditā mahī mukhaiḥ ca candra saṃkāśaiḥ rakta anta nayanaiḥ śubhaiḥ gaja vāji manuṣyāṇām sarva gātraiḥ ca bhūpate āsīt sarvā samākīrṇā muhūrtena vasuṃdharā sa saṃprahāraḥ tumulaḥ kaṭukaḥ śoṇita udakaḥ prāvartata kurūṇām ca pāṇḍavānām ca bhārata vavarṣuḥ śara varṣāṇi kṣatriyāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ krośanti kuñjarāḥ tatra śara varṣa pratāpitāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca saṃyuge bharata uttama saṃrabdhānām ca vīrāṇām dhīrāṇām amita ojasām dhanuḥ jyā tala śabdena na prājñāyata kim cana śara śakti gadābhiḥ te khaḍgaiḥ ca amita tejasaḥ babhramuḥ kuñjarāḥ ca atra śaraiḥ viddhāḥ niraṅkuśāḥ aśvāḥ ca paryadhāvanta hata ārohāḥ diśaḥ daśa utpatya nipatanti anye śara ghāta prapīḍitāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca yodhānām bharata ṛṣabha bahūnām uttamāṅgānām kārmukāṇām tathā eva ca gadānām parighānām ca hastānām ca ūrubhiḥ saha pādānām bhūṣaṇānām ca keyūrāṇām ca saṃghaśas rāśayaḥ sma pradṛśyante bhīṣma bhīma parākrame aśvānām kuñjarāṇām ca rathānām ca ativartatām saṃghātāḥ sma pradṛśyante tatra tatra viśām pate gadābhiḥ asibhiḥ prāsaiḥ bāṇaiḥ ca nata parvabhiḥ jaghnuḥ parasparam tatra kṣatriyāḥ kāla coditāḥ muṣṭibhiḥ jānubhiḥ ca eva talaiḥ ca eva viśām pate anyonyam jaghnire vīrāḥ tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha patitaiḥ pātyamānaiḥ ca viceṣṭadbhiḥ ca bhū tale bhīṣme yudhi parākrānte bhīmasenena bhārata prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇita ogha taraṃgiṇī madhye ca mahatī senā keśa śaivala śādvalā viceruḥ tatra saṃgrāme nistriṃśa vara dhāriṇaḥ virathāḥ rathinaḥ ca atra nistriṃśa vara dhāriṇaḥ puraskṛtya raṇe bhīṣmam pāṇḍavān abhyavartata tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya vṛkodaram bhīṣmam abhyadravan kruddhāḥ raṇe rabhasa vāhanāḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmeṇa saṃsaktān bhrātṝn anyān ca pārthivān pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣam dhanuṣaḥ gāṇḍivasya ca dhvajam ca dṛṣṭvā pārthasya sarvān naḥ bhayam āviśat siṃha lāṅgūlam ākāśe jvalantam iva parvatam asajjamānam vṛkṣeṣu dhūmaketum iva utthitam bahu varṇam ca citram ca divyam vānara lakṣaṇam apaśyāma mahā rāja dhvajam gāṇḍiva dhanvanaḥ vidyutam megha madhya sthām bhrājamānām iva ambare dadṛśuḥ gāṇḍivam yodhāḥ rukma pṛṣṭham mahā rathe aśuśruma bhṛśam ca asya śakrasya iva abhigarjataḥ diśaḥ saṃplāvayan sarvāḥ śara varṣaiḥ samantataḥ abhyadhāvata gāṅgeyam bhairava astraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ diśam prāñcam pratyañcam ca na jānīmaḥ astra mohitāḥ kāṃdiś bhūtāḥ śrānta patrāḥ hata astrāḥ hatacetasaḥ teṣām ārta ayanam abhūt bhīṣmaḥ śaṃtanavaḥ raṇe sādinaḥ ca aśva pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ bhūmau ca api padātayaḥ vihvalāḥ pratyadṛśyanta na jānanti diśaḥ nṛpa śrutvā gāṇḍīva nirghoṣam visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ atha kāmboja mukhyaiḥ tu bṛhadbhiḥ śīghra gāmibhiḥ gopānām bahu sāhasraiḥ balaiḥ govāsanaḥ vṛtaḥ tatas kāmboja mukhyāḥ ca te haṃsa patha karṇikāḥ madra sauvīra gāndhāraiḥ trigartaiḥ ca viśām pate sarva kāliṅga mukhyaiḥ ca kaliṅga adhipatiḥ vṛtaḥ nāgāḥ nara gaṇa oghāḥ ca duḥśāsana puraḥsarāḥ haya āroha varāḥ ca eva tava putreṇa coditāḥ pāṇḍavān samare jagmuḥ tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha cedi kāśi padātaiḥ ca rathaiḥ pāñcāla sṛñjayaiḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sahitāḥ sarve dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ rathibhiḥ vāraṇaiḥ aśvaiḥ padātaiḥ ca samīritam ghoram āyodhanam jajñe mahā abhra sadṛśam rajaḥ tomara prāsa nārāca gaja aśva ratha yodhinām balena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ samasajjat kirīṭinā āvantyaḥ kāśirājena bhīmasenena saindhavaḥ ajātaśatruḥ madrāṇām ṛṣabheṇa yaśasvinā vikarṇaḥ sahadevena citrasenaḥ śikhaṇḍinā matsyāḥ duryodhanam jagmuḥ śakunim ca viśām pate drupadaḥ cekitānaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca dhṛṣṭaketum abhidrutau evam prajavita aśvāni bhrānta nāga rathāni ca nirabhre vidyutaḥ tīvrāḥ diśaḥ ca rajasā āvṛtāḥ prādurāsan mahā ulkāḥ ca sa nirghātāḥ viśām pate pravavau ca mahā vātaḥ pāṃsu varṣam papāta ca prakāśam cakruḥ ākāśe udyata asibhiḥ uttamaiḥ rajasā ca abhibhūtānām astra jālaiḥ ca tudyatām vīra bāhu visṛṣṭānām sarva āvaraṇa bhedinām saṃghātaḥ śara jālānām tumulaḥ samapadyata prakāśam cakruḥ ākāśam udyatāni bhuja uttamaiḥ nakṣatra vimala ābhāni śastrāṇi bharata ṛṣabha ārṣabhāṇi vicitrāṇi rukma jāla āvṛtāni ca sūrya varṇaiḥ ca nistriṃśaiḥ pātyamānāni sarvaśas dikṣu sarvāsu adṛśyanta śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca bhagna cakra akṣa nīḍāḥ ca nipātita mahā dhvajāḥ hata aśvāḥ pṛthivīm jagmuḥ tatra tatra mahā rathāḥ paripetuḥ hayāḥ ca atra ke cid śastra kṛta vraṇāḥ śara āhatāḥ bhinna dehāḥ baddha yoktrāḥ haya uttamāḥ adṛśyanta sa sūtāḥ ca sa aśvāḥ sa ratha yodhinaḥ ekena balinā rājan vāraṇena hatāḥ rathāḥ saṃnipāte bala oghānām vītam ādadire gajāḥ babhūva āyodhanam channam nārāca abhihataiḥ gajaiḥ saṃnipāte bala oghānām preṣitaiḥ vara vāraṇaiḥ nipetuḥ yudhi saṃbhagnāḥ sa yodhāḥ sa dhvajāḥ rathāḥ vyadṛśyanta mahā rāja saṃbhagnāḥ ratha kūbarāḥ viśīrṇa ratha jālāḥ ca keśeṣu ākṣipya dantibhiḥ druma śākhāḥ iva āvidhya niṣpiṣṭāḥ rathinaḥ raṇe ratheṣu ca rathān yuddhe saṃsaktān vara vāraṇāḥ vikarṣantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃpetuḥ sarva śabda gāḥ teṣām tathā karṣatām ca gajānām rūpam ābabhau saraḥsu nalinī jālam viṣaktam iva karṣatām evam saṃchāditam tatra babhūva āyodhanam mahat sādibhiḥ ca padātaiḥ ca sa dhvajaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ uvāca śikhaṇḍī saha matsyena virāṭena viśām pate bhīṣmam āśu mahā iṣvāsam āsasāda su durjayam droṇam kṛpam vikarṇam ca mahā iṣvāsān mahā balān rājñaḥ ca anyān raṇe śūrān bahūn ārchat dhanaṃjayaḥ saindhavam ca mahā iṣvāsam sa amātyam saha bandhubhiḥ prācyān ca dākṣiṇātyān ca bhūmipān bhūmipa ṛṣabha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahā rāja gaja anīkam mahā rathaḥ mādrī putraḥ tu nakulaḥ śūraḥ saṃkrandanaḥ yudhi trigartānām ratha udāraiḥ samasajjata pāṇḍavaḥ nākuliḥ ca śatānīkaḥ samare ratha puṃgavaḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca saubhadraḥ ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca samare rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ putrāṇām te ratha anīkam pratyudyātāḥ su durjayāḥ senāpatiḥ ameya ātmā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā balaḥ evam ete mahā iṣvāsāḥ tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sametya samare śūrāḥ saṃprahāram pracakrire kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ ca nijaghnuḥ itaretaram sa patākāḥ rathāḥ rejuḥ vaiyāghra parivāraṇāḥ sametānām ca samare jigīṣūṇām parasparam babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ siṃhānām iva nardatām tatra adbhutam apaśyāma saṃprahāram su dāruṇam yam akurvan raṇe vīrāḥ sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ saha na eva kham na diśaḥ rājan na sūryam śatru tāpana vidiśaḥ vā api apaśyāma śaraiḥ muktaiḥ samantataḥ śaktīnām vimala agrāṇām tomarāṇām tathā asyatām nistriṃśānām ca pītānām nīlotpala nibhāḥ prabhāḥ kavacānām vicitrāṇām bhūṣaṇānām prabhāḥ tathā kham diśaḥ pradiśaḥ ca eva bhāsayām āsuḥ ojasā vapurbhiḥ ca narendrāṇām candra sūrya sama prabhaiḥ virarāja tadā rājñ tatra tatra raṇa aṅgaṇam ratha siṃhāsana vyāghrāḥ samāyāntaḥ ca saṃyuge bhīṣmaḥ tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ bhīmasenam mahā balam tatas bhīṣma vinirmuktāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ tasya śaktim mahā vegām bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ kruddha āśīviṣa saṃkāśām preṣayām āsa bhārata tām āpatatīm sahasā rukma daṇḍām durāsadām ciccheda samare bhīṣmaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ apāsya tu dhanuḥ chinnam bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ ānarchat bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam yudhi sātyakiḥ tu tatas tūrṇam bhīṣmam āsādya saṃyuge ākarṇa prahitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ tigma tejanaiḥ tatas saṃdhāya vai tīkṣṇam śaram parama dāruṇam vārṣṇeyasya rathāt bhīṣmaḥ pātayām āsa sārathim tasya aśvāḥ pradrutāḥ rājan nihate ratha sārathau hāhākāraḥ ca saṃjajñe pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām iti āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ yuyudhāna ratham prati etasmin eva kāle tu bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punar vyahanat pāṇḍavīm senām āsurīm iva vṛtrahā te vadhyamānāḥ bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ saha āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā bhīṣmam eva abhidudruvuḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhāḥ ca api pārthāḥ śāṃtanavam raṇe tathā eva tāvakāḥ rājan bhīṣma droṇa mukhāḥ parān uvāca virāṭaḥ atha tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhīṣmam ārchat mahā ratham vivyādha turagān ca asya tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ mahā rathaḥ tam pratyavidhyat daśabhiḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śaraiḥ rukma puṅkhaiḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtahastaḥ mahā balaḥ drauṇiḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvānam bhīma dhanvā mahā rathaḥ avidhyat iṣubhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ dṛḍha hastaḥ stanāntare avidhyat ca bhṛśam tīkṣṇaiḥ pattribhiḥ śatru karśanaḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena kārmuka chedam āhave avidhyat phalgunam rājñ navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vāsudevam ca saptatyā vivyādha parama iṣubhiḥ tatas krodha abhitāmra akṣaḥ saha kṛṣṇena phalgunaḥ dīrgham uṣṇam ca niḥśvasya cintayitvā muhur muhur dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇa amitra karśanaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvā saṃkruddhaḥ śitān saṃnata parvṇaḥ jīvitānta karān ghorān samādatta śilīmukhān taiḥ tūrṇam samare avidhyat drauṇim balavatām varam tasya te kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave tasya tat su mahat karma śaśaṃsuḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ yat kṛṣṇābhyām sametābhyām na apatrapata saṃyuge astra grāmam sa saṃhāram droṇāt prāpya su durlabham mama ayam ācārya sutaḥ droṇasya ati priyaḥ sutaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ ca viśeṣeṇa mānanīyaḥ mama iti ca samāsthāya matim vīraḥ bībhatsuḥ śatru tāpanaḥ kṛpām cakre ratha śreṣṭhaḥ bhāradvāja sutam prati drauṇim tyaktvā tatas yuddhe kaunteyaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ yuyudhe tāvakān nighnan tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī duryodhanaḥ tu daśabhiḥ gārdhra pattraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ bhīmasenam mahā iṣvāsam rukma puṅkhaiḥ samarpayat bhīmasenaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ parāsu karaṇam dṛḍham citram kārmukam ādatta śarān ca niśitān daśa tasya kāñcana sūtraḥ tu śaraiḥ parivṛtaḥ maṇiḥ na amṛṣyata yathā nāgaḥ tala śabdam samīritam tatas śaraiḥ mahā rāja rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ bhīmam vivyādha saṃkruddhaḥ trāsayānaḥ varūthinīm putrau te deva saṃkāśau vyarocetām mahā balau nṛtyan iva raṇe vīraḥ ārtim naḥ samajījanat tam pratyavidyat daśabhiḥ citrasenaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ sa viddhaḥ vikṣaran raktam śatru saṃvāraṇam mahat bhittvā ca asya tanutrāṇam śareṇa urasi atāḍayat tatas te tāvakāḥ vīrāḥ rāja putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ tān ca sarvān śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ jaghāna parama astra vid tat tasya caritam dṛṣṭvā pautraḥ te viśām pate lakṣmaṇaḥ abhyapatat tūrṇam sātvatī putram āhave abhimanyuḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ lakṣmaṇam śubha lakṣaṇam vivyādha viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sārathim ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ tathā eva lakṣmaṇaḥ rājan saubhadram niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya aśvān caturaḥ hatvā sārathim ca mahā balaḥ abhyadravata saubhadraḥ lakṣmaṇam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hata aśve tu rathe tuṣṭhan lakṣmaṇaḥ para vīra hā tām āpatatīm sahasā ghora rūpām durāsadām abhimanyuḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ciccheda bhujaga upamām hayaḥ hayam gajaḥ nāgam vīraḥ vīram viśām pate abhyadravan jighāṃsantaḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ tāvakāḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ mukta keśāḥ vikavacāḥ virathāḥ chinna kārmukāḥ bāhubhiḥ samayudhyanta sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ saha tatas bhīṣmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām uvāca vikṛṣya cāpam samare bhāra sādhanam uttamam prāmuñcat puṅkha saṃyuktān śarān āśīviṣa upamān tasya vikṣipataḥ cāpam śarān anyān ca muñcataḥ ādadānasya bhūyas ca saṃdadhānasya ca aparān kṣipataḥ ca śarān asya raṇe śatrūn vinighnataḥ rathānām ayutam tasya preṣayām āsa bhārata tān tu sarvān mahā iṣvāsān sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ jaghāna parama iṣvāsaḥ divyena astreṇa vīryavān sa kṛtvā dāruṇam karma pragṛhīta śarāsanaḥ āsasāda tatas vīraḥ bhūriśravasam āhave sa hi saṃdṛśya senām tām yuyudhānena pātitām abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ kurūṇām kīrti vardhanaḥ vyasṛjat vajra saṃkāśān śarān āśīviṣa upamān sahasraśas mahā rāja darśayan pāṇi lāghavam śarān tān mṛtyu saṃsparśān sātyakeḥ tu padānugāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānasya sutāḥ daśa mahā balāḥ mahā rathāḥ samākhyātāḥ citra varma āyudha dhvajāḥ samāsādya mahā iṣvāsam bhūriśravasam āhave ūcuḥ sarve su saṃrabdhāḥ yūpaketum mahā raṇe asmān vā tvam parājitya yaśaḥ prāpnuhi saṃyuge vayam vā tvām parājitya prītim dāsyāmahe pituḥ evam uktaḥ tadā śūraiḥ tān uvāca mahā balaḥ vīrya ślāghī nara śreṣṭhaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā samupasthitān yudhyadhvam sahitāḥ yattāḥ nihaniṣyāmi vaḥ raṇe evam uktāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ te vīrāḥ kṣiprakāriṇaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa abhyavarṣan ariṃdamam aparāhṇe mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ tumulaḥ abhavat ekasya ca bahūnām ca sametānām raṇa ajire tam ekam rathinām śreṣṭham śara varṣaiḥ avākiran prāvṛṣi iva mahā śailam siṣicuḥ jaladāḥ nṛpa taiḥ tu muktān śara oghān tān yama daṇḍa aśani prabhān asaṃprāptān asaṃprāptān ciccheda āśu mahā rathaḥ visṛjya śara vṛṣṭim tām daśa rājan mahā rathāḥ saumadattiḥ tatas kruddhaḥ teṣām cāpāni bhārata ciccheda daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ nimeṣeṇa mahā rathaḥ atha eṣām chinna dhanuṣām bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ciccheda samare rājñ śirāṃsi niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān raṇe putrān mahā balān vārṣṇeyaḥ vinadan rājan
