bhūriśravasam abhyayāt āropayat ratham tūrṇam paśyatām sarva dhanvinām tasmin tathā vartamāne raṇe bhīṣmam mahā ratham ayodhayanta saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ bharata ṛṣabha lohitāyati ca āditye tvaramāṇaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ pañcaviṃśati sāhasrān nijaghāna mahā rathān te hi duryodhana ādiṣṭāḥ tadā pārtha nibarhaṇe saṃprāpya eva gatāḥ nāśam śalabhāḥ iva pāvakam tatas matsyāḥ kekayāḥ ca dhanurveda viśāradāḥ sarveṣām eva sainyānām pramohaḥ samajāyata saṃdhyā kāle mahā rāja sainyānām śrānta vāhanaḥ pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca paraspara samāgame te sene bhṛśa saṃvigne yayatuḥ svam niveśanam tatas sva śibiram gatvā nyaviśan tatra bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sārdham kuravaḥ ca yathāvidhi uvāca vihṛtya ca tatas rājan sahitāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ vyatītāyām tu śarvaryām punar yuddhāya niryayuḥ tatra śabdaḥ mahān āsīt tava teṣām ca bhārata yujyatām ratha mukhyānām ca eva dantinām saṃnahyatām padātīnām hayānām ca eva bhārata tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā dhṛṣṭadyumnam abhāṣata vyūham vyūha mahā bāho makaram śatru tāpanam vyādideśa mahā rāja rathinaḥ rathinām varaḥ śiraḥ abhūt drupadaḥ tasya pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ cakṣuṣī sahadevaḥ ca nakulaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ tuṇḍam āsīt mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ saubhadraḥ draupadeyāḥ ca rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ sātyakiḥ dharmarājaḥ ca vyūha grīvām samāsthitāḥ pṛṣṭham āsīt mahā rāja virāṭaḥ vāhinīpatiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahitaḥ mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca vāmam pārśvam samāśritāḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ nara vyāghraḥ karakarṣaḥ ca vīryavān dakṣiṇam pakṣam āśritya sthitāḥ vyūhasya rakṣaṇe pādayoḥ tu mahā rāja sthitaḥ śrīmān mahā rathaḥ kuntibhojaḥ śatānīkaḥ mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ śikhaṇḍī tu mahā iṣvāsaḥ somakaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ balī evam etat mahā vyūham vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ sūrya udaye mahat rāja punar yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ vyūham dṛṣṭvā tu tat sainyam pitā devavrataḥ te tasya tuṇḍe mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhāradvājaḥ vyarocata aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ ca eva cakṣuḥ āstām nareśvara kṛtavarmā tu sahitaḥ kāmboja āraṭṭa bāhlikaiḥ śirasi āsīt nara śreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva dhanuṣmatām grīvāyām śūrasenaḥ tu tava putraḥ ca māriṣa urasi abhūt nara śreṣṭha mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe ca āstām mahā iṣvāsau āvantyau sa padānugau vāmam pakṣam samāśritya daṃśitaḥ samavasthitaḥ tuṣārāḥ yavanāḥ ca eva śakāḥ ca saha cūcupaiḥ dakṣiṇam pakṣam āśritya sthitāḥ vyūhasya bhārata śrutāyuḥ ca śatāyuḥ ca saumadattiḥ ca māriṣa vyūhasya jaghane tasthuḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ parasparam tatas yuddhāya saṃjagmuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kauravaiḥ saha pratīyuḥ rathinaḥ nāgān nāgāḥ ca rathinaḥ yayuḥ haya ārohāḥ haya ārohān rathinaḥ ca api sādinaḥ sārathim ca rathī rājñ kuñjarān ca mahā raṇe hasti ārohāḥ ratha ārohān rathinaḥ ca api sādinaḥ rathinaḥ pattibhiḥ sārdham sādinaḥ ca api pattibhiḥ śuśubhe pāṇḍavā senā nakṣatraiḥ iva śarvarī tathā bhīṣma kṛpa droṇa śalya duryodhana ādibhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ tu kaunteyaḥ droṇam dṛṣṭvā parākramī vivyādha samare rājñ marmāṇi uddiśya vīryavān dṛḍha āhataḥ tatas bhīmaḥ bhāradvājasya saṃyuge sārathim preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanam prati sa saṃgṛhya svayam vāhān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān vyadhamat pāṇḍavām senām tūla rāśim iva analaḥ te vadhyamānāḥ droṇena bhīṣmeṇa ca narottama sṛñjayāḥ kekayaiḥ sārdham palāyana parāḥ abhavan āsīt vyatikaraḥ ghoraḥ tava teṣām ca bhārata tat adbhutam apaśyāma tāvakānām paraiḥ saha pratisaṃvārya ca astrāṇi te anyonyasya viśām pate yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva kauravāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ uvāca vyūḍham evam yathāśāstram amogham ca eva saṃjaya puṣṭam naḥ atyantam abhikāmam ca naḥ sadā na ati vṛddham abālam ca na kṛśam na ca pīvaram laghu vṛtta āyata prāyam sāra gātram anāmayam prāsa ṛṣṭi tomareṣu ājau parigheṣu āyaseṣu ca bhindipāleṣu musaleṣu ca sarvaśas kampaneṣu ca cāpeṣu kaṇapeṣu ca sarvaśas kṣepaṇīṣu ca citrāsu muṣṭi yuddheṣu kovidam aparokṣam ca vidyāsu vyāyāmeṣu kṛta śramam nāga aśva ratha yāneṣu bahuśas su parīkṣitam parīkṣya ca yathānyāyam vetanena upapāditam na goṣṭhyā na upacāreṇa na ca bandhu nimittatas na sauhṛda balaiḥ ca api na akulīna parigrahaiḥ samṛddha janam āryam ca tuṣṭa satkṛta bāndhavam kṛta upakāra bhūyiṣṭham yaśasvi ca manasvi ca lokapāla upamaiḥ tāta pālitam loka viśrutaiḥ bahubhiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ guptam pṛthivyām loka saṃmataiḥ asmān abhigataiḥ kāmāt sa balaiḥ sa padānugaiḥ mahā udadhim iva āpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥ apakṣaiḥ pakṣa saṃkāśaiḥ rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam nānā yodha jalam bhīmam vāhana ūrmi taraṃgiṇam kṣepaṇī asi gadā śakti śara prāsa samākulam dhvaja bhūṣaṇa saṃbādham ratna paṭṭena saṃci droṇa bhīṣma abhisaṃguptam guptam ca kṛtavarmaṇā kṛpa duḥśāsanābhyām ca jayadratha mukhaiḥ tathā bhagadatta vikarṇābhyām drauṇi saubala bāhlikaiḥ na etādṛśam samudyogam dṛṣṭavantaḥ atha mānuṣāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vā mahābhāgāḥ purāṇāḥ bhuvi saṃjaya īdṛśaḥ hi bala oghaḥ tu yuktaḥ śastra astra saṃpadā yatra īdṛśam balam ghoram na atarat yudhi pāṇḍavān atha vā pāṇḍava arthāya devāḥ tatra samāgatāḥ āsīt yathāgatam tāta yena dṛṣṭam idam purā purā dhātrā yathā sṛṣṭam tat tathā na tat anyathā uvāca ātma doṣāt tvayā rājan prāptam vyasanam īdṛśam yāni tvam dṛṣṭavan rājan dharma saṃkara kārite tava doṣāt purā vṛttam dyūtam etat viśām pate tava doṣeṇa yuddham ca pravṛttam saha pāṇḍavaiḥ tvam eva adya phalam bhuṅkṣva kṛtvā kilbiṣam ātmanā iha vā pretya vā rājan tvayā prāptam yathātatham tasmāt rājñ sthiraḥ bhūtvā prāpya idam vyasanam mahat śṛṇu yuddham yathāvṛttam śaṃsataḥ mama māriṣa bhīmasenaḥ tu niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhittvā mahā camūm āsasāda tatas vīraḥ sarvān duryodhana anujān duḥśāsanam durviṣaham duḥsaham durmadam jayam cārucitram suvarmāṇam duṣkarṇam karṇam eva ca etān anyān ca su bahūn samīpa sthān mahā rathān dhārtarāṣṭrān su saṃkruddhān dṛṣṭvā bhīmaḥ mahā balaḥ bhīṣmeṇa samare guptām praviveśa mahā camūm jīva grāham nigṛhṇīmaḥ vayam enam narādhipāḥ sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ pārthaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ kṛta niścayaiḥ prajā saṃharaṇe sūryaḥ krūraiḥ iva mahā grahaiḥ saṃprāpya madhyam vyūhasya na bhī pāṇḍavam āviśat tatas śata sahasrāṇi rathinām sarvaśas prabho sa teṣām pravarān yodhān hasti aśva ratha sādinaḥ jaghāna samare śūraḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān a cintayan teṣām vyavasitam jñātvā bhīmasenaḥ jighṛkṣatām samastānām vadhe rājñ matim cakre mahāmanāḥ tatas ratham samutsṛjya gadām ādāya pāṇḍavaḥ uvāca sārathim bhīmaḥ sthīyatām iti bhārata yāvat enān haniṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrān saha anugān jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām tam bala ogha mahā arṇavam gadayā bhīmasenena tāḍitāḥ vāraṇa uttamāḥ bhinna kumbhāḥ mahā kāyāḥ bhinna pṛṣṭhāḥ tathā eva ca bhinna gātrāḥ sahārohāḥ śerate parvatāḥ iva rathāḥ ca bhagnāḥ tilaśas sa yodhāḥ śataśas raṇe aśvāḥ ca sādinaḥ ca eva pādātaiḥ saha bhārata antakāle prajāḥ sarvāḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ bhīmasene praviṣṭe tu dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api pārṣataḥ vidārya mahatīm senām tāvakānām nara ṛṣabhaḥ āsasāda ratham śūnyam bhīmasenasya saṃyuge ratham ca śūnyam saṃprekṣya bhīmam prati vicetanaḥ dṛṣṭvā viśokam samare bhīmasenasya sārathim dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja durmanāḥ gata cetanaḥ apṛcchat bāṣpa saṃruddhaḥ nisvanām vācam īrayan mama prāṇaiḥ priyatamaḥ kva bhīmaḥ iti duḥkhitaḥ viśokaḥ tam uvāca idam dhṛṣṭadyumnam kṛtāñjaliḥ saṃsthāpya mām iha balī pāṇḍaveyaḥ pratāpavān praviṣṭaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām etat bala mahā arṇavam mām uktvā puruṣa vyāghra prīti yuktam idam vacaḥ pratipālaya mām sūta niyamya aśvāt muhūrtakam yāvat etān nihanmi āśu ye ime mad vadha udyatāḥ abhyadhāvat gadā pāṇiḥ tat balam sa mahā balaḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā gadā hastam pradhāvantam mahā balam sarveṣām eva sainyānām saṃgharṣaḥ samajāyata bhittvā rājan mahā vyūham praviveśa sakhiḥ te viśokasya vacaḥ śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api pārṣataḥ pratyuvāca tatas sūtam raṇa madhye mahā balaḥ bhīmasenam raṇe hitvā sneham utsṛjya pāṇḍavaiḥ yadi yāmi vinā bhīmam kim mām kṣatram vadiṣyati yaḥ sahāyān parityajya svastimān āvrajet gṛhān mama bhīmaḥ sakhā ca eva saṃbandhī ca mahā balaḥ bhaktaḥ asmān bhaktimān ca aham tam api ari niṣūdanam saḥ aham tatra gamiṣyāmi yatra yātaḥ vṛkodaraḥ nighnantam mām arīn paśya dānavān iva vāsavam sa dadarśa tatas bhīmam dahantam ripu vāhinīm vātam vṛkṣān iva balāt prabhañjantam raṇe nṛpān te hanyamānāḥ samare rathinaḥ sādinaḥ tathā hāhākāraḥ ca saṃjajñe te sainyasya māriṣa tatas kṛtāstrāḥ te sarve parivārya vṛkodaram abhītāḥ samavartanta śastra vṛṣṭyā samantataḥ abhidrutam śastrabhṛtām variṣṭham samantataḥ pāṇḍavam loka vīraiḥ abhidrutam śastrabhṛtām variṣṭham ca samantataḥ lokapāla samam vīra loka vīraiḥ ca pāṇḍavam sainyena ghoreṇa su saṃgatena dṛṣṭvā balī pārṣataḥ bhīmasenam āśvāsayan pārṣataḥ bhīmasenam gadā hastam kālam iva antakāle niḥśalyam enam ca cakāra tūrṇam āropayat ca ātma ratham mahātmā bhṛśam pariṣvajya ca bhīmasenam āśvāsayām āsa ca śatru madhye dṛṣṭvā raṇe vākyam idam babhāṣe tam yāta sarve sahitāḥ nihantum mā vaḥ ripuḥ prārthayatām anīkam ṛchan etam kṣudra karma ati hīnam sainyam ca vidhvaṃsayate pṛṣatkaiḥ śrutvā tu vākyam tam amṛṣyamāṇāḥ jyeṣṭha ājñayā coditāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ pragṛhya citrāṇi dhanūṃṣi vīrāḥ jyā nemi ghoṣaiḥ pravikampayantaḥ śaraiḥ avarṣan drupadasya putram yathā ambudāḥ bhūdharam vāri jālaiḥ nihatya tān ca api śaraiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ na vivyathe samare citra yodhī samabhyudīrṇān ca te ātmajān tathā niśāmya vīrān abhitas sthitān raṇe pramohanam droṇadattam mahātmā prayojayām āsa udāra karmā tatas vyamuhyanta raṇe nṛ vīrāḥ pramohana astra āhata buddhi sattvāḥ pradudruvuḥ kuravaḥ ca eva sarve sa vāji nāgāḥ sa rathāḥ samantāt parīta kālān iva naṣṭa saṃjñān moha upetān tava putrān niśamya etasmin eva kāle tu bhīmaḥ praharatām varaḥ viśramya ca tadā rājan pītvā amṛta rasam jalam punar saṃnahya sahasā yodhayām āsa saṃyuge dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahitaḥ kālayām āsa bhārata etasmin eva kāle tu droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ drupadam tribhiḥ āsādya śaraiḥ vivyādha dāruṇaiḥ jitvā tu drupadam droṇaḥ śaṅkham dadhmau pratāpavān tasya śaṅkha svanam śrutvā vitresuḥ sarva somakāḥ atha śuśrāva tejasvī droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ pramohana astreṇa raṇe mohitān ātmajān te tatas droṇaḥ rāja gṛddhī tvaritaḥ abhiyayau raṇāt tatra apaśyat mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca bhīmam ca vicarantau mahā raṇe moha āviṣṭān ca te putrān apaśyat sa mahā rathaḥ tatas prajñā astram ādāya mohana astram vyaśātayat atha pratyāgata prāṇāḥ tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prāha samāhūya sva sainikān gacchantu padavīm śaktyāḥ bhīma pārṣatayoḥ yudhi saubhadra pramukhāḥ vīrāḥ rathāḥ dvādaśa daṃśitāḥ vijñāya samare śīghram praviśadhvam ratha arṇavam te evam samanujñātāḥ śūrāḥ vikrānta yodhinaḥ bāḍham iti evam uktvā tu sarve puruṣa māninaḥ kekayāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca vīryavān abhimanyum puraskṛtya mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ te kṛtvā samare vyūham sūcīmukham ariṃdamāḥ bibhiduḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām tat ratha anīkam āhave tān prayātān mahā iṣvāsān abhimanyu purogamān bhīmasena bhaya āviṣṭā dhṛṣṭadyumna vimohitā na saṃdhārayitum śaktā te senā janādhipa mada mūrchā anvitā ātmānam pramadā iva adhvani sthitā te abhiyātāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ tau ca dṛṣṭvā mahā iṣvāsān abhimanyu purogamān dṛṣṭvā ca sahasā āyāntam pāñcālyaḥ gurum ātmanaḥ na aśaṃsata vadham vīraḥ putrāṇām te pārṣataḥ tasya abhipatataḥ tūrṇam bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān anyān ca śataśas bāṇān preṣayām āsa pārṣate atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya pārṣataḥ para vīra hā droṇam vivyādha saptatyā rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tasya droṇaḥ punar cāpam ciccheda amitra karśanaḥ hayān ca caturaḥ tūrṇam caturbhiḥ sāyaka uttamaiḥ vaivasvata kṣayam ghoram preṣayām āsa vīryavān sārathim ca asya bhallena preṣayām āsa mṛtyave dharmarāja puram rājñ preṣayām āsa vai dvijaḥ hata aśvāt sa rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ tatas sa ratha nāga aśvā samakampata vāhinī paśyataḥ bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca paśyataḥ tat prabhagnam balam dṛṣṭvā droṇena amita tejasā na aśaknuvan vārayitum samastāḥ te mahā rathāḥ vadhyamāna tu tat sainyam droṇena niśā śaraiḥ tathā dṛṣṭvā ca tat sainyam jahṛṣe ca balam tava dṛṣṭvā ācāryam ca saṃkruddham dahantam ripu vāhinīm cukruśuḥ sarvatas yodhāḥ sādhu sādhu iti bhārata uvāca ekībhūtāḥ punar ca eva tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ sametya samare bhīmam yodhayām āsuḥ udyatāḥ pragṛhya ca mahā vegam parāsu karaṇam dṛḍham citram śarāsanam saṃkhye śaraiḥ vivyādha te sutān nārācena su tīkṣṇena bhṛśam marmaṇi atāḍayat sa tathā abhihataḥ rājā na acalat giri rāj iva duryodhana anujāḥ sarve śūrāḥ saṃtyakta jīvitāḥ saṃsmṛtya mantritam pūrvam nigrahe bhīmakarmaṇaḥ niścayam manasā kṛtvā nigrahītum pracakramuḥ tān āpatataḥ eva ājau bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ ca tejasvī nārācena samarpayat citrasenam mahā rāja te putram mahā yaśāḥ tathā itarān te sutān tāḍayām āsa bhārata tatas saṃsthāpya samare svāni anīkāni sarvaśas abhimanyu prabhṛtayaḥ te dvādaśa mahā rathāḥ preṣitāḥ dharmarājena bhīmasena padānugāḥ dṛṣṭvā ratha sthān tān śūrān sūrya agni sama tejasaḥ sarvān eva mahā iṣvāsān bhrājamānān śriyā vṛtān mahā āhave dīpyamānān suvarṇa kavaca ujjvalān tatyajuḥ samare bhīmam tava putrāḥ mahā balāḥ tān na amṛṣyata kaunteyaḥ jīvamānāḥ gatāḥ iti anvīya ca punar sarvān te putrān apīḍayat pārṣatena ca saṃprekṣya tava sainye mahā rathāḥ kekayāḥ draupadī sutāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā samare kruddhāḥ duryodhana prabhṛtayaḥ pragṛhīta śarāsanāḥ bhṛśam aśvaiḥ prajavitaiḥ prayayuḥ yatra te rathāḥ aparāhṇe tatas rājan prāvartata mahān raṇaḥ tāvakānām ca balinām pareṣām ca eva bhārata atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samācinot hata aśvam ratham utsṛjya vikarṇaḥ tu mahā rathaḥ ārjuniḥ śara jālena chādayām āsa bhārata durjayaḥ atha vikarṇaḥ ca kārṣṇim pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ vivyadhāte na ca akampat kārṣṇiḥ meruḥ iva acalaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tu samare kekayān pañca māriṣa sāyakaiḥ niśitaiḥ rājñ ājaghāna pṛthak pṛthak taiḥ ca api viddhaḥ śuśubhe rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ bhīṣmaḥ api samare rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm kālayām āsa balavān pālaḥ paśu gaṇān iva tatas gāṇḍīva nirghoṣaḥ prādurāsīt viśām pate dakṣiṇena varūthinyāḥ pārthasya arīn vinighnataḥ kurūṇām ca api sainyeṣu pāṇḍavānām ca bhārata śoṇita udam ratha āvartam gaja dvīpam haya ūrmiṇam chinna hastāḥ vikavacāḥ videhāḥ ca nara uttamāḥ patitāḥ tatra dṛśyante śataśas atha sahasraśas bhūḥ bhāti bharata śreṣṭha parvataiḥ ācitā yathā tatra adbhutam apaśyāma tava teṣām ca bhārata na tatra āsīt pumān kaḥ cit yaḥ yoddhum na abhikāṅkṣati evam yuyudhire vīrāḥ prārthayānāḥ mahat yaśaḥ tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham kāṅkṣamāṇāḥ jayam yudhi uvāca tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya nṛ vīram dṛḍha vairiṇam ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ varṣa pūga abhikāṅkṣitaḥ adya tvām nihaniṣyāmi yadi na utsṛjase raṇam adya kuntyāḥ parikleśam vana vāsam ca kṛtsnaśas yat tvam durodaraḥ bhūtvā pāṇḍavān avamanyase a cintya pāṇḍavān kāmāt yatheṣṭam kṛtavan asi yācamānam ca yat mohāt dāśārham avamanyase ulūkasya samādeśam yat dadāsi ca hṛṣṭa vat samīkariṣye tat pāpam yat purā kṛtavān asi evam uktvā dhanuḥ ghoram vikṛṣya udbhrāmya ca asakṛt samādāya śarān ghorān mahā aśani sama prabhān ṣaḍviṃśat tarasā kruddhaḥ mumoca āśu suyodhane jvalita agni śikhā ākārān vajra kalpān a jihma gān tatas asya kārmukam dvābhyām sūtam dvābhyām ca vivyadhe dvābhyām ca su vikṛṣṭābhyām śarābhyām ari mardanaḥ rathāt ca sa dhvajaḥ śrīmān nānā ratna vibhūṣitaḥ jvalantam sūrya saṃkāśam nāgam maṇi mayam śubham dhvajam kuru pateḥ chinnam dadṛśuḥ sarva pārthivāḥ ājaghāna raṇe bhīmaḥ smayan iva mahā rathaḥ tatas tu rājā sindhūnām ratha śreṣṭhaḥ jayadrathaḥ duryodhanasya jagrāha pārṣṇim sat puruṣa ucitām kṛpaḥ ca rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ kauravyam amita ojasam dhṛṣṭaketuḥ tatas rājñ abhimanyuḥ ca vīryavān citrasenaḥ sucitraḥ ca citrāśvaḥ citradarśanaḥ aṣṭau ete mahā iṣvāsāḥ sukumārāḥ yaśasvinaḥ ājaghāna tatas tūrṇam abhimanyuḥ mahā manāḥ ekaikam pañcabhiḥ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vajra mṛtyu pratīkāśaiḥ vicitra āyudha niḥsṛtaiḥ vavarṣuḥ mārgaṇaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ girim merum iva ambudāḥ sa pīḍyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstraḥ yuddha durmadaḥ yathā devāsure yuddhe vajrapāṇiḥ mahā asurān vikarṇasya tatas bhallān preṣayām āsa bhārata caturdaśa ratha śreṣṭhaḥ ghorān āśīviṣa upamān sa taiḥ vikarṇasya rathāt pātayām āsa vīryavān dhvajam sūtam hayān ca asya chittvā nṛtyan iva āhave punar ca anyān śarān pītān akuṇṭha agrān śilā śitān preṣayām āsa saubhadraḥ vikarṇāya mahā balaḥ te vikarṇam samāsādya kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ bhittvā deham gatāḥ bhūmim jvalantaḥ iva pannagāḥ te śarāḥ hema puṅkha agrāḥ vyadṛśyanta mahī tale vikarṇam vīkṣya nirbhinnam tasya eva anye sahodarāḥ abhiyātvā tathā eva āśu ratha sthān sūrya varcasaḥ durmukhaḥ śrutakarmāṇam viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ aśvān jāmbūnadaiḥ jālaiḥ pracchannān vāta raṃhasaḥ jaghāna ṣaḍbhiḥ āsādya sārathim ca abhyapātayat sa hata aśve rathe tiṣṭhan śrutakarmā mahā rathaḥ śaktim cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ mahā ulkām jvalitām iva vidārya prāviśat bhūmim dīpyamānā su tejanā visaṃjñam prekṣya te sarve bhrātaraḥ paryavārayan tam dṛṣṭvā viratham tatra sutasomaḥ mahā balaḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām ratham āropayat svakam śrutakīrtiḥ tathā vīraḥ jayatsenam sutam te tasya vikṣipataḥ cāpam śrutakīrteḥ mahātmanaḥ kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena prahasan iva bhārata tam dṛṣṭvā chinna dhanvānam śatānīkaḥ sahodaram śatānīkaḥ tu samare dṛḍham visphārya kārmukam nanāda su mahā nādam prabhinnaḥ iva vāraṇaḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ tūrṇam jayatsenam śilīmukhaiḥ atha anyena su tīkṣṇena sarva āvaraṇa bhedinā śatānīkaḥ jayatsenam vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam mumoca asmai śitān bāṇān tīkṣṇān āśīviṣa upamān samādatta śitān bāṇān śatānīkaḥ mahā balaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca āmantrya duṣkarṇam bhrātuḥ agratas mumoca niśitān bāṇān jvalitān pannagān iva tatas asya dhanuḥ ekena dvābhyām sūtam ca māriṣa aśvān manojavān ca asya kalmāṣān vīta kalmaṣaḥ jaghāna niśitaiḥ tūrṇam sarvān dvādaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ duṣkarṇam samare kruddhaḥ vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam duṣkarṇam nihatam dṛṣṭvā pañca rājñ mahā rathāḥ jighāṃsantaḥ śatānīkam sarvatas paryavārayan chādyamānam śara vrātaiḥ śatānīkam yaśasvinam abhyadhāvanta saṃrabdhāḥ kekayāḥ pañca sodarāḥ tān abhyāpatataḥ prekṣya tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ śatruṃjayaḥ śatru sahaḥ sarve kruddhāḥ yaśasvinaḥ pratyudyātāḥ mahā rāja kekayān bhrātaraḥ samam nānā varṇa vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtaiḥ vara cāpa dharāḥ vīrāḥ vicitra kavaca dhvajāḥ viviśuḥ te param sainyam siṃhāḥ iva vanāt vanam anyonya āgaskṛtām rājan yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam tatas śāṃtanavaḥ kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nāśayām āsa senām vai bhīṣmaḥ teṣām mahātmanām pāñcālānām ca sainyāni śaraiḥ ninye yama kṣayam evam bhittvā mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm kṛtvā avahāram sainyānām yayau sva śibiram nṛpa nāśayām āsatuḥ vīrau dhṛṣṭadyumna vṛkodarau kauravāṇām anīkāni śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ dharmarājaḥ api saṃprekṣya dhṛṣṭadyumna vṛkodarau mūrdhni ca etau upāghrāya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śibiram yayau arjunaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca kauravāṇām anīkinīm hatvā vidrāvya ca śaraiḥ śibirāya eva jagmatuḥ uvāca atha śūrāḥ mahā rāja paraspara kṛta āgasaḥ jagmuḥ sva śibirāṇi eva rudhireṇa samukṣitāḥ saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta bhūyas yuddha cikīrṣayā visravat śoṇita akta aṅgaḥ papraccha idam pitāmaham sainyāni raudrāṇi bhayānakāni vyūḍhāni samyak bahula dhvajāni vidārya hatvā ca nipīḍya śūrāḥ te pāṇḍavānām tvaritāḥ ratha oghāḥ praviśya bhīmena nibarhitaḥ asmi ghoraiḥ śaraiḥ mṛtyu daṇḍa prakāśaiḥ kruddham tam udvīkṣya bhayena rājñ saṃmūrchitaḥ na alabham śāntim adya icche prasādāt tava satya saṃdha prāptum jayam pāṇḍaveyān ca hantum tam pratyuvāca avimanāḥ manasvī gaṅgāsutaḥ śastrabhṛtām variṣṭhaḥ pareṇa yatnena vigāhya senām sarva ātmanā aham tava rāja putra icchāmi dātum vijayam sukham ca na ca ātmānam chādaye aham tvad arthe ete tu raudrāḥ bahavaḥ mahā rathāḥ yaśasvinaḥ śūratamāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ ye pāṇḍavānām samare sahāyāḥ jita klamāḥ krodha viṣam vamanti te na iha śakyāḥ sahasā vijetum vīrya unnaddhāḥ kṛta vairāḥ tvayā ca aham hi etān pratiyotsyāmi rājñ sarva ātmanā jīvitam tyajya vīra raṇe te arthāya mahā anubhāva na jīvitam rakṣyatamam mama adya sarvān te arthāya sa deva daityān lokān daheyam kim śatrūn te iha tat pāṇḍavān yodhayiṣyāmi rājan priyam ca te sarvam aham kariṣye sarvāṇi sainyāni tatas prahṛṣṭaḥ nirgacchata iti āha nṛpān ca sarvān tad ājñayā tāni viniryayuḥ drutam ratha aśva pādāta gaja ayutāni sthitāni nāga aśva padātimanti virejuḥ ājau te rājan balāni vṛndaiḥ sthitāḥ ca api su saṃprayuktāḥ cakāśire danti gaṇāḥ samantāt śastra astra vidbhiḥ naradeva yodhaiḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ sainya gaṇāḥ tvadīyāḥ rathaiḥ ca pādāta gaja aśva saṃghaiḥ prayādbhiḥ ājau vidhivat praṇunnaiḥ samuddhatam vai taruṇa arka varṇam rajaḥ babhau chādayat sūrya raśmīn rejuḥ patākāḥ ratha danti saṃsthā vāta īritāḥ bhrāmyamāṇāḥ samantāt dhanūṃṣi visphārayatām nṛpāṇām babhūva śabdaḥ tumulaḥ ati ghoraḥ tat ugra nādam bahu rūpa varṇam te ātmajānām samudīrṇam evam uvāca abravīt bharata śreṣṭhaḥ saṃpraharṣa karam vacaḥ aham droṇaḥ ca śalyaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau bāhlikaḥ saha bāhlikaiḥ trigarta rājaḥ ca balī māgadhaḥ ca su durjayaḥ rathāḥ ca bahu sāhasrāḥ śobhamānāḥ mahā dhvajāḥ deśa jāḥ ca hayāḥ rājan su ārūḍhāḥ haya sādibhiḥ gaja indrāḥ ca mada udvṛttāḥ prabhinna karaṭāmukhāḥ padātāḥ ca tathā śūrāḥ nānā praharaṇa āyudhāḥ avaśyam tu mayā rājñ te vācyam hitam sadā aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jetum devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ vāsudeva sahāyāḥ ca mahā indra sama vikramāḥ pāṇḍavān vā raṇe jeṣye mām vā jeṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ evam uktvā dadau ca asmai viśalyakaraṇīm śubhām oṣadhīm vīrya saṃpannām viśalyaḥ ca bhavat tadā tatas prabhāte vimale svena anīkena vīryavān avyūhata svayam vyūham bhīṣmaḥ vyūha viśāradaḥ maṇḍalam manuja śreṣṭha nānā śastra samākulam saṃpūrṇam yodha mukhyaiḥ ca tathā danti padātibhiḥ aśva vṛndaiḥ mahadbhiḥ ca ṛṣṭi tomara dhāribhiḥ nāge nāge rathāḥ sapta sapta ca aśvāḥ rathe rathe anu aśvam daśa dhānuṣkāḥ dhānuṣke sapta carmiṇaḥ evaṃvyūham mahā rāja te sainyam mahā rathaiḥ sthitam raṇāya mahate bhīṣmeṇa yudhi pālitam daśa aśvānām sahasrāṇi dantinām ca tathā eva ca rathānām ayutam ca api putrāḥ ca te daṃśitāḥ citrasena ādayaḥ śūrāḥ abhyarakṣan pitāmaham rakṣyamāṇaḥ ca taiḥ śūraiḥ gopyamānāḥ ca tena te saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta rājānaḥ ca mahā balāḥ vyabhrājata śriyā juṣṭaḥ yathā śakraḥ triviṣṭape tatas śabdaḥ mahān āsīt putrāṇām te bhārata ratha ghoṣaḥ ca tumulaḥ vāditrāṇām ca nisvanaḥ bhīṣmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām vyūḍhaḥ pratyak mukhaḥ yudhi maṇḍalaḥ su mahā vyūhaḥ durbhedyaḥ amitra ghātinām sarvatas śuśubhe rājan raṇe arīṇām durāsadaḥ maṇḍalam tu samālokya vyūham parama dāruṇam svayam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā vyūham vajram atha akarot tathā vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu yathāsthānam avasthitāḥ rathinaḥ sādinaḥ ca eva siṃhanādam atha anadan bibhitsavaḥ tatas vyūham niryayuḥ yuddha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ itaretaratas śūrāḥ saha sainyāḥ prahāriṇaḥ bhāradvājaḥ yayau matsyam drauṇiḥ ca api śikhaṇḍinam svayam duryodhanaḥ rājā pārṣatam samupādravat nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca rājan madra īśam īyatuḥ citrasenam vikarṇam ca tathā durmarṣaṇam vibho prāgjyotiṣam mahā iṣvāsam haiḍimbaḥ rākṣasa uttamaḥ bhūriśravāḥ raṇe yattaḥ dhṛṣṭaketum ayodhayat śrutāyuṣam tu rājānam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śeṣāḥ pratiyayuḥ yattāḥ bhīmam eva mahā ratham śakti tomara nārāca gadā parigha pāṇayaḥ arjunaḥ atha bhṛśam kruddhaḥ vārṣṇeyam idam abravīt paśya mādhava sainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyuge vyūḍhāni vyūha viduṣā gāṅgeyena mahātmanā yuddha abhikāmān śūrān ca paśya mādhava daṃśitān trigarta rājam sahitam bhrātṛbhiḥ paśya keśava adya etān pātayiṣyāmi paśyataḥ te janārdana ye ime mām yadu śreṣṭha yoddhu kāmāḥ raṇa ajire vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi narādhipa gaṇān prati te api tam parama iṣvāsāḥ śara varṣaiḥ apūrayan taḍāgam iva dhārābhiḥ yathā prāvṛṣi toyadā hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt te sainye viśām pate chādyamānau bhṛśam kṛṣṇau śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā mahā raṇe devāḥ devarṣayaḥ ca eva gandharvāḥ ca mahoragāḥ vismayam paramam jagmuḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇau tathāgatau śastra vṛṣṭim paraiḥ muktām śara oghaiḥ yat avārayat na ca tatra api a nirbhinnaḥ kaḥ cit āsīt viśām pate teṣām rāja sahasrāṇām hayānām dantinām tathā dvābhyām tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ca anyān pārthaḥ vivyādha māriṣa te hanyamānāḥ pārthena bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam yayuḥ agādhe majjamānānām bhīṣmaḥ trātā bhavat tadā saṃcukṣubhe mahā rāja vātaiḥ iva mahā arṇavaḥ uvāca tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme nivṛtte ca suśarmaṇi prabhagneṣu ca vīreṣu pāṇḍavena mahātmanā kṣubhyamāṇe bale tūrṇam sāgara pratime te dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ rājan raṇe pārthasya vikramam tvaramāṇaḥ samabhyetya sarvān tān abravīt nṛpān teṣām ca pramukhe śūram suśarmāṇam mahā balam eṣa bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yoddhu kāmaḥ dhanaṃjayam sarva ātmanā kuru śreṣṭhaḥ tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ tam prayāntam para anīkam sarva sainyena bhāratam bāḍham iti evam uktvā tu tāni anīkāni sarvaśas narendrāṇām mahā rāja samājagmuḥ pitāmaham tatas prayātaḥ sahasā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ arjunam raṇe bhāratam āyāntam āsasāda mahā balam mahā śveta aśva yuktena bhīma vānara ketunā abhavat tumulaḥ nādaḥ bhayāt dṛṣṭvā kirīṭinam abhīśu hastam kṛṣṇam ca dṛṣṭvā ādityam iva aparam madhyaṃdina gatam saṃkhye na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum tathā śāṃtanavam bhīṣmam śveta aśvam śveta kārmukam na śekuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ draṣṭum śveta graham iva uditam tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam virāṭaḥ vāhinīpatiḥ śarān ca āśīviṣa ākārān jvalitān pannagān iva droṇam tribhiḥ pravivyādha caturbhiḥ ca asya vājinaḥ tasya droṇaḥ avadhīt aśvān śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ bharata śreṣṭha sūtam ekena pattriṇā āruroha ratham tūrṇam śaṅkhasya rathinām varaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa vārayām āsatuḥ balāt bhāradvājaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ śaram āśīviṣa upamam cikṣepa samare tūrṇam śaṅkham prati janeśvara sa tasya hṛdayam bhittvā pītvā śoṇitam āhave jagāma dharaṇim bāṇaḥ lohita ārdrīkṛta chaviḥ sa papāta rathāt tūrṇam bhāradvāja śara āhataḥ dhanuḥ tyaktvā śarān ca eva pituḥ eva samīpatas hatam svam ātmajam dṛṣṭvā virāṭaḥ prādravat bhayāt utsṛjya samare droṇam vyātta ānanam iva antakam bhāradvājaḥ tatas tūrṇam pāṇḍavānām mahā camūm dārayām āsa samare śataśas atha sahasraśas śikhaṇḍī api mahā rāja drauṇim āsādya saṃyuge ājaghāna bhruvoḥ madhye nārācaiḥ tribhiḥ āśugaiḥ sa babhau nara śārdūlaḥ lalāṭe saṃsthitaiḥ tribhiḥ aśvatthāmā tatas kruddhaḥ nimeṣa ardhāt śikhaṇḍinaḥ sūtam dhvajam atho rājñ turagān āyudham tathā śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ uddiśya pātayām āsa saṃyuge sa hata aśvāt avaplutya rathāt vai rathinām varaḥ khaḍgam ādāya niśitam vimalam ca śarāvaram śyena vat vyacarat kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍī śatru tāpanaḥ tatas śara sahasrāṇi bahūni bharata ṛṣabha preṣayām āsa samare drauṇiḥ parama kopanaḥ tām āpatatīm samare śara vṛṣṭim su dāruṇām asinā tīkṣṇa dhāreṇa ciccheda balinām varaḥ carma ācchinat asim ca asya khaṇḍayām āsa saṃyuge śitaiḥ su bahuśas rājan tam ca vivyādha pattribhiḥ śikhaṇḍī tu tatas khaḍgam khaṇḍitam tena sāyakaiḥ śikhaṇḍinam ca vivyādha śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ āyasaiḥ śikhaṇḍī tu bhṛśam rājan tāḍyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam mādhavasya mahātmanaḥ sātyakiḥ tu tatas kruddhaḥ rākṣasam krūram āhave māyām ca rākṣasīm kṛtvā śara varṣaiḥ avākirat na asaṃbhramat yat samare vadhyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ aindram astram ca vārṣṇeyaḥ yojayām āsa bhārata vijayāt yat anuprāptam mādhavena yaśasvinā tat astram bhasmasāt kṛtvā māyām tām rākṣasām tadā parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ tat tathā pīḍitam tena mādhavena mahātmanā pradudrāva bhayāt rakṣaḥ hitvā sātyakim āhave śaineyaḥ prāṇadat jitvā yodhānām tava paśyatām nyahanat tāvakān ca api sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja te putram janeśvaram chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ saṃchādyamānaḥ viśikhaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnena bhārata dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca samare tūrṇam vivyādha sāyakaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā ca triṃśatā ca eva tat adbhutam iva abhavat hayān ca caturaḥ śīghram nijaghāna mahā rathaḥ śaraiḥ ca enam su niśitaiḥ kṣipram vivyādha sapta sa hata aśvāt mahā bāhuḥ avaplutya rathāt balī śakuniḥ tam samabhyetya rāja gṛddhī mahā balaḥ tatas nṛpam parājitya pārṣataḥ para vīra hā kṛtavarmā raṇe bhīmam śaraiḥ ārchat mahā ratham pracchādayām āsa ca tam mahā meghaḥ ravim yathā preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇe na akampata mahā rāja bhīmam ca ārchat śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya aśvān caturaḥ hatvā bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ sārathim pātayām āsa dhvajam ca su pariṣkṛtam śakalīkṛta sarva aṅgaḥ śvāvidh vat samadṛśyata hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam vṛṣakasya ratham yayau nijaghāna ca saṃkruddhaḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ uvāca bahūni iha vicitrāṇi dvairathāni sma saṃjaya pāṇḍūnām māmakaiḥ sārdham aśrauṣam tava jalpataḥ na ca eva māmakam kam cit dhṛṣṭam śaṃsasi saṃjaya nityam pāṇḍu sutān hṛṣṭān abhagnān ca eva śaṃsasi jīyamānān vimanasaḥ māmakān vigata ojasaḥ vadase saṃyuge sūta diṣṭam etat asaṃśayam uvāca yathāśakti yathotsāham yuddhe ceṣṭanti tāvakāḥ darśayānāḥ param śaktyā pauruṣam puruṣa ṛṣabha gaṅgāyāḥ sura nadyāḥ vai svādu bhūtam yathā udakam tathā tat pauruṣam rājan tāvakānām mahātmanām prāpya pāṇḍu sutān vīrān vyartham bhavati saṃyuge ghaṭamānān yathāśakti kurvāṇān karma duṣkaram na doṣeṇa kuru śreṣṭha kauravān gantum arhasi tava aparādhāt su mahān sa putrasya viśām pate pṛthivyāḥ prakṣayaḥ ghoraḥ yama rāṣṭra vivardhanaḥ ātma doṣāt samutpannam śocitum na arhase nṛpa na hi rakṣanti rājānaḥ sarva arthān na api jīvitam yuddhe su kṛtinām lokān icchantaḥ vasudhādhipāḥ camūm vigāhya yudhyante nityam svarga parāyaṇāḥ pūrvāhṇe tu mahā rāja prāvartata jana kṣayaḥ tat mama ekamanāḥ bhūtvā śṛṇu devāsura upamam āvantyau tu mahā iṣvāsau mahātmanau mahā balau irāvantam abhiprekṣya sameyātām raṇa utkaṭau teṣām pravavṛte yuddham tumulam loma harṣaṇam irāvant tu su saṃkruddhaḥ bhrātarau deva rūpiṇaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ yudhyatām hi tathā rājan viśeṣaḥ na vyadṛśyata yatatām śatru nāśāya kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇām irāvān tu tatas rājan anuvindasya sāyakaiḥ bhallābhyām ca su tīkṣṇābhyām dhanuḥ ketum ca māriṣa tau ekasthau raṇe vīrau āvantyau rathinām varau śarān mumucatuḥ tūrṇam irāvanti mahātmani tābhyām muktāḥ mahā vegāḥ śarāḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ divākara patham prāpya chādayām āsuḥ ambaram vavarṣa śara varṣeṇa sārathim ca api apātayat tau sa jitvā mahā rāja nāga rāja sutā sutaḥ pauruṣam khyāpayan tūrṇam vyadhamat te vāhinīm sā vadhyamānā samare dhārtarāṣṭrī mahā camūḥ vegān bahuvidhān cakre viṣam pītvā iva mānavaḥ tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ rājā nāgarājam samāsthitaḥ yathā vajradharaḥ pūrvam saṃgrāme tārakā maye tatra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca samāgatāḥ yathā surapatiḥ śakraḥ trāsayām āsa dānavān tathā eva samare rājñ trāsayām āsa pāṇḍavān tena vidrāvyamāṇāḥ te pāṇḍavāḥ sarvatodiśam trātāram na abhyavindanta sveṣu anīkeṣu bhārata śeṣāḥ vimanasaḥ bhūtvā prādravanta mahā rathāḥ nivṛtteṣu tu pāṇḍūnām punar sainyeṣu bhārata naiṣṭhikīm buddhim āsthāya svargāya bharata uttamāḥ āsīt niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ tava sainyeṣu saṃyuge śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa merum girim iva ambudaḥ nihatya tān śarān rājā rākṣasasya dhanuḥ cyutān bhaimasenim raṇe tūrṇam sarva marmasu atāḍayat sa tāḍyamānaḥ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ preṣayām āsa samare tān ca ciccheda rākṣasaḥ sa tān chittvā mahā bāhuḥ tomarān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya aśvān caturaḥ saṃkhye pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ sa hata aśve rathe tiṣṭhan rākṣasa indraḥ pratāpavān tām āpatantīm sahasā hema daṇḍām su vegitām śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā haiḍimbaḥ prādravat bhayāt tam vijitya raṇe śūram vikrāntam khyāta pauruṣam pāṇḍavīm samare senām saṃmamarda sa kuñjaraḥ yathā vana gajaḥ rājan mṛdnan carati padminīm svasrīyau cakre śara oghaiḥ pāṇḍu nandanau chādyamānaḥ śara ogheṇa hṛṣṭa rūpataraḥ abhavat tayoḥ ca api abhavat prītiḥ atulā mātṛ kāraṇāt nijaghāna raṇe tam tu sūtam ca asya nyapātayat aśvān vai caturaḥ rājan caturbhiḥ sāyaka uttamaiḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ āruroha tatas yānam bhrātuḥ eva yaśasvinaḥ ekasthau tu raṇe śūrau dṛḍhe vikṣipya kārmuke madra rāja ratham kruddhau chādayām āsatuḥ kṣaṇāt sa chādyamānaḥ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ svasrīyābhyām nara vyāghraḥ na akampata yathā acalaḥ prahasan iva tām ca api śara vṛṣṭim jaghāna ha pṛṣatkānām sahasrāṇi prahasan iva tau api sṛjan rurodha samare meghaḥ vṛṣṭyā yathā acalam madra rājam abhiprekṣya preṣayām āsa bhārata niṣasāda mahā rāja kaśmalam ca jagāma ha tam visaṃjñam nipatitam sūtaḥ saṃprekṣya saṃyuge apovāha rathena ājau yamābhyām abhipīḍitam dṛṣṭvā madra īśvara ratham dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukham abhidudruvatuḥ hṛṣṭau te sainyam viśām pate uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā madhyam prāpte divākare śrutāyuṣam abhiprekṣya codayām āsa vājinaḥ abhyadhāvat tatas rājā śrutāyuṣam ariṃdamam sa saṃvārya raṇe rājā preṣitān dharmasūnunā te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave pāṇḍavaḥ tu bhṛśam viddhaḥ tena rājñā mahātmanā raṇe varāhakarṇena rājānam hṛdi vivyadhe ratha śreṣṭhaḥ rathāt tūrṇam bhūmau pārthaḥ nyapātayat ketum nipatitam dṛṣṭvā śrutāyuḥ sa tu pārthivaḥ pāṇḍavam viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ rājan vivyādha sapta yathā yuga ante bhūtāni dhakṣyan iva hutāśanaḥ kruddham tu pāṇḍavam dṛṣṭvā deva gandharva rākṣasāḥ sarveṣām ca eva bhūtānām idam āsīt manogatam trīn lokān adya saṃkruddhaḥ nṛpaḥ ayam dhakṣyati iti vai ṛṣayaḥ ca eva devāḥ ca cakruḥ svastyayanam mahat lokānām nṛpa śānti artham krodhite pāṇḍave tadā sa ca krodha samāviṣṭaḥ parilelihan tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni tāvakāni viśām pate nirāśāṇi abhavan tatra jīvitam prati bhārata sa tu dhairyeṇa tam kopam saṃnivārya mahā yaśāḥ śrutāyuṣaḥ praciccheda muṣṭideśe mahat dhanuḥ sa tvaram caraṇe rājan tasya vāhān mahātmanaḥ nijaghāna śaraiḥ kṣipram sūtam ca su mahā balaḥ hata aśvam tu ratham tyaktvā dṛṣṭvā rājñaḥ tu pauruṣam etat kṛtvā mahā rāja dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ cekitānaḥ tu vārṣṇeyaḥ gautamam rathinām varam prekṣatām sarva sainyānām chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ saṃnivārya śarān tān tu kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi cekitānam raṇe yattam rājan vivyādha pattribhiḥ hayān ca asya avadhīt rājan ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī saḥ avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam gadām jagrāha sātvataḥ sa tayā vīra ghātinyā gadayā gadinām varaḥ bhūmiṣṭhaḥ gautamaḥ tasya śarān cikṣepa ṣoḍaśa te śarāḥ sātvatam bhittvā prāviśanta dharā talam cekitānaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ punar cikṣepa tām gadām gautamasya vadha ākāṅkṣī vṛtrasya iva puraṃdaraḥ tām āpatantīm vimalām aśma garbhām mahā gadām śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ vārayām āsa gautamaḥ cekitānaḥ tatas khaḍgam kośāt uddhṛtya bhārata vegena mahatā rājan cekitānam upādravat nistriṃśābhyām su tīkṣṇābhyām anyonyam saṃtatakṣatuḥ dharaṇīm samanuprāptau sarva bhūta niṣevitām mūrchayā abhiparīta aṅgau vyāyāmena ca mohitau cekitānam tathābhūtam dṛṣṭvā samara durmadam tathā eva śakuniḥ śūraḥ syālaḥ tava viśām pati āropayat ratham tūrṇam gautamam rathinām varam saumadattim tathā kruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā balaḥ navatyā sāyakaiḥ kṣipram rājan vivyādha vakṣasi saumadattiḥ uras sthaiḥ taiḥ bhṛśam bāṇaiḥ aśobhata bhūriśravāḥ tu samare dhṛṣṭaketum mahā ratham mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa saṃyuge sa ca tam ratham utsṛjya dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā manāḥ āruroha tatas yānam śatānīkasya māriṣa virathān te putrān tu kṛtvā rājan mahā āhave tatas rājñām bahu śataiḥ gaja aśva ratha yāyibhiḥ saṃvṛtam samare bhīṣmam devaiḥ api durāsadam prayāntam śīghram udvīkṣya paritrātum sutān tava vāsudevam uvāca idam kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ codaya aśvān hṛṣīkeśa yatra ete bahulāḥ rathāḥ ete hi bahavaḥ śūrāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ yathā na hanyuḥ naḥ senām tathā mādhava codaya evam uktaḥ sa vārṣṇeyaḥ kaunteyena amita ojasā sa tvaram bāla rakṣā artham gacchau eti dhanaṃjayaḥ ratham śveta hayaiḥ yuktam preṣayām āsa saṃyuge niṣṭānakaḥ mahān āsīt te sainyasya māriṣa samāsādya tu kaunteyaḥ rājñaḥ tān bhīṣma rakṣiṇaḥ suśarmāṇam atho rājñ idam vacanam abravīt jānāmi tvām yudhi śreṣṭham atyantam pūrva vairiṇam paryāyasya adya saṃprāptam phalam paśya su dāruṇam adya te darśayiṣyāmi pūrvapretān pitāmahān evam saṃjalpataḥ tasya bībhatsoḥ śatrughātinaḥ śrutvā api paruṣam vākyam suśarmā ratha yūthapaḥ abhi gatvā arjunam vīram rājabhiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtaḥ purastāt pṛṣṭhatas ca eva pārśvatas ca eva sarvatas śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa meghaiḥ iva divākaram tatas pravṛttaḥ su mahān saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇita udakaḥ tāvakānām ca samare pāṇḍavānām ca bhārata uvāca bāṇena bāṇena mahā rathānām ciccheda cāpāni raṇe prasahya saṃchidya cāpāni ca tāni rājñām teṣām raṇe vīryavatām kṣaṇena vivyādha bāṇaiḥ yugapad mahātmā niḥśeṣa tām teṣu atha manyamānaḥ vibhinna gātrāḥ patita uttamāṅgāḥ gatāsavaḥ chinna tanutra kāyāḥ mahīm gatāḥ pārtha bala abhibhūtāḥ vicitra rūpāḥ yugapad vineśuḥ dṛṣṭvā hatān tān yudhi rāja putrān trigarta rājaḥ prayayau kṣaṇena teṣām rathānām atha pṛṣṭhagopāḥ dvātriṃśat anye abyapatanta pārtham tathā eva te saṃparivārya pārtham vikṛṣya cāpāni mahā ravāṇi avīvṛṣan bāṇa mahā ogha vṛṣṭyā yathā girim toyadharāḥ jala oghaiḥ saṃpīḍyamānaḥ tu śara ogha vṛṣṭyā dhanaṃjayaḥ tān yudhi jāta roṣaḥ ṣaṣṭyā śaraiḥ saṃyati taila dhautaiḥ jaghāna tān api atha pṛṣṭhagopān ṣaṣṭim rathān tān avajitya saṃkhye dhanaṃjayaḥ prīta manāḥ yaśasvī atha atvarat bhīṣma vadhāya jiṣṇuḥ balāni rājñām samare nihatya trigarta rājaḥ nihatān samīkṣya mahā rathān tān atha bandhu vargān raṇe puraskṛtya narādhipān tān jagāma pārtham tvaritaḥ vadhāya abhidrutam ca astrabhṛtām variṣṭham dhanaṃjayam vīkṣya śikhaṇḍi mukhyāḥ pārthaḥ api tān āpatataḥ samīkṣya trigarta rājñā sahitān nṛ vīrān vidhvaṃsayitvā samare dhanuṣmān gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ bhīṣmam yiyāsuḥ yudhi saṃdadarśa duryodhanam saindhava ādīn ca rājñaḥ āvārayiṣṇūn abhisaṃprayāya muhūrtam āyodhya balena vīraḥ utsṛjya rājānam ananta vīryaḥ jayadratha ādīn ca nṛpān mahā ojāḥ yayau tatas bhīma balaḥ manasvī gāṅgeyam ājau śara cāpa pāṇiḥ bhīṣmaḥ api dṛṣṭvā samare kṛtāstrān sa pāṇḍavānām rathinaḥ abhyudārān vihāya saṃgrāma mukhe dhanaṃjayam javena pārtham punar ājagāma sārdham sa mādrī suta bhīmasenaiḥ bhīṣmam yayau śāṃtanavam raṇāya taiḥ saṃprayuktaḥ sa mahā ratha agryaiḥ gaṅgāsutaḥ samare citra yodhī na vivyathe śāṃtanavaḥ mahātmā samāgataiḥ pāṇḍu sutaiḥ samastaiḥ ciccheda cāpāni mahā rathānām prasahya teṣām dhanuṣā vareṇa yudhiṣṭhiram bhīmasenam yamau ca pārtham tathā yudhi saṃjāta kopa duryodhanaḥ krodha viṣaḥ mahātmā jaghāna bāṇaiḥ anala prakāśaiḥ te vāri dhārāḥ ca yathā adrirājam tathā ca varṣanti mahā anubhāvāḥ chinna āyudham śāṃtanavena rājā śikhaṇḍinam prekṣya ca jāta kopaḥ ajātaśatruḥ samare mahātmā śikhaṇḍinam kruddhaḥ uvāca vākyam uktvā tathā tvam pituḥ agratas mām aham haniṣyāmi mahā vratam tam bhīṣmam śara oghaiḥ vimala arka varṇaiḥ satyam vadāmi iti kṛtā pratijñā mithyāpratijñaḥ bhava mā nṛ vīra rakṣasva dharmam ca kulam yaśaḥ ca prekṣasva bhīṣmam yudhi bhīma vegam sarvān tapantam mama sainya saṃghān śara ogha jālaiḥ ati tigma tejaiḥ kālam yathā mṛtyu kṛtam kṣaṇena nikṛt cāpaḥ samara anapekṣaḥ parājitaḥ śāṃtanavena rājan vihāya bandhūn atha sodarān ca kva yāsyase na anurūpam tava idam dṛṣṭvā hi bhīṣmam tam ananta vīryam bhagnam ca sainyam dravamāṇam evam bhītaḥ asi nūnam drupadasya putra tathā hi te mukha varṇaḥ a prahṛṣṭaḥ ājñāyamāne api dhanaṃjayena mahā āhave saṃprasakte nṛ vīra katham hi bhīṣmāt prathitaḥ pṛthivyām bhayam tvam adya prakaroṣi vīra sa dharmarājasya vacaḥ niśamya rūkṣa akṣaram vipralāpa anubaddham pratyādeśam manyamānaḥ mahātmā pratatvare bhīṣma vadhāya rājan tam āpatantam mahatā javena śikhaṇḍinam bhīṣmam abhidravantam āvārayām āsa hi śalyaḥ enam śastreṇa ghoreṇa su durjayena sa ca api dṛṣṭvā samudīryamāṇam astram yugānta agni sama prabhāvam atha ādade vāruṇam anyat astram śikhaṇḍī atha ugram pratighātāya tasya tat astram astreṇa vidāryamāṇam kha sthāḥ surāḥ dadṛśuḥ pārthivāḥ ca chittvā anadat pāṇḍu sutasya vīraḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya ajamīḍhasya rājñaḥ tatas samutsṛjya dhanuḥ sa bāṇam yudhiṣṭhiram vīkṣya bhaya abhibhūtam gadām pragṛhya abhipapāta saṃkhye jayadratham bhīmasenaḥ padātiḥ vivyādha ghoraiḥ yama daṇḍa kalpaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ pañcaśataiḥ samantāt a cintayitvā sa śarān tarasvī vṛkodaraḥ krodha parīta cetāḥ jaghāna vāhān samare samastān āraṭṭa jān sindhurājasya saṃkhye tyaktvā yayau yatra rājā kurūṇām bhayena bhīmasya sa mūḍha cetāḥ samudyatām tām yama daṇḍa kalpām dṛṣṭvā gadām te kuravaḥ samantāt vihāya sarve tava putram ugram pātam gadāyāḥ parihartu kāmāḥ amūḍha cetāḥ tu atha citrasenaḥ mahā gadām āpatatīm nirīkṣya avaplutaḥ siṃhaḥ iva acala agrāt jagāma ca anyam bhuvi bhūmi deśam gadā api sā prāpya ratham su citram sa aśvam sa sūtam vinihatya saṃkhye jagāma bhūmim jvalitā mahā ulkā bhraṣṭā ambarāt gām iva saṃpatatī āścarya bhūtam su mahat tvadīyāḥ dṛṣṭvā eva tat bhārata saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ uvāca bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tūrṇam yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ samakampanta sṛñjayāḥ yidhiṣṭhiraḥ api kauravyaḥ yamābhyām sahitaḥ prabhuḥ mahā iṣvāsam nara vyāghram bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam yayau tatas śara sahasrāṇi pramuñcan pāṇḍavaḥ yudhi bhīṣmam saṃchādayām āsa yathā meghaḥ divākaram tena samyak praṇītāni śara jālāni bhārata patijagrāha gāṅgeyaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tathā eva śara jālāni bhīṣmeṇa astāni māriṣa ākāśe samadṛśyanta khagamānām vrajāḥ iva nimeṣa ardhāt ca kaunteyam bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yudhi adṛśyam samare cakre śara jālena bhāgaśas nārācam preṣayām āsa kruddhaḥ āśīviṣa upamam a saṃprāptam tatas tam tu kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ tam tu chittvā raṇe bhīṣmaḥ nārācam kāla saṃmitam nijaghne kaurava indrasya hayān kāñcana bhūṣaṇān hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan śaktim cikṣepa dharmarāj tām āpatatīm sahasā kāla pāśa upamām śitām ciccheda samare bhīṣmaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ hata aśvam tu ratham tyaktvā dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam nakulasya mahātmanaḥ yamau api su saṃkruddhaḥ samāsādya raṇe tadā śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa bhīṣmaḥ para puraṃjayaḥ bhīṣmaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja bhīṣma bāṇa prapīḍitau jagāma atha parām cintām bhīṣmasya vadha kāṅkṣayā tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vaśyān rājñaḥ tān samacodayat bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam sarve nihata iti suhṛd gaṇān tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam cikrīda dhanuṣā rājan pātayānaḥ mahā rathān tam carantam raṇe pārthāḥ dadṛśuḥ kauravam yudhi mṛga madhyam praviśya iva yathā siṃha śiśum vane tarjayānam raṇe śūrān trāsayānam ca sāyakaiḥ dṛṣṭvā tresuḥ mahā rāja siṃham mṛga gaṇāḥ iva raṇe bharata siṃhasya dadṛśuḥ kṣatriyāḥ gatim agneḥ vāyu sahāyasya yathā kakṣam didhakṣataḥ śirāṃsi rathinām bhīṣmaḥ pātayām āsa saṃyuge patadbhiḥ ca mahā rāja śirobhiḥ dharaṇī tale babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ patatām aśmanām iva sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīt vyatikaraḥ mahān bhinneṣu teṣu vyūheṣu kṣatriyāḥ itaretaram śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānām pitāmaham abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt an ādṛtya tatas bhīṣmaḥ tam śikhaṇḍinam āhave prayayau sṛñjayān kruddhaḥ strī tvam cintya śikhaṇḍinaḥ sṛñjayāḥ tu tatas hṛṣṭāḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmam mahā ratham siṃhanādān bahuvidhān cakruḥ śaṅkha vimiśritān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ pīḍayantau bhṛśam sainyam śakti tomara vṛṣṭibhiḥ śastraiḥ ca bahuṣu rājan jaghnatuḥ tāvakān raṇe te hanyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā na tyajanti sma saṃyugam tatra ākrandaḥ mahān āsīt tāvakānām mahātmanām vadhyatām samare rājñ pārṣatena mahātmanā tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram tāvakānām mahā rathau chādayām āsatuḥ ubhau śara varṣeṇa pārṣatam avaplutya atha pāñcālyaḥ rathāt tūrṇam mahā balaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam sātyakeḥ su mahātmanaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ arjunaḥ ca api saṃkruddhaḥ kṣatriyān kṣatriya ṛṣabha ayodhayata saṃgrāme vajrapāṇiḥ iva asurān vyadhamat sarva pāñcālān tūla rāśim iva analaḥ parivārya raṇe bhīṣmam yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha yudhyatām tu tathā teṣām kurvatām karma duṣkaram astam girim atha ārūḍhe na prakāśati bhāskare prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇita ogha taraṃgiṇī gomāyu gaṇa saṃkīrṇā kṣaṇena rajanī mukhe rākṣasāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca tathā anye piśita aśanāḥ samantataḥ vyadṛśyanta śataśas atha sahasraśas āsvādya āsvādya nṛtyante nādam muñcanti bhīṣaṇam prāsam ālambya niśitam nistriṃśam nirmalam mahat arjunaḥ atha suśarma ādīn rājñaḥ tān sa padānugān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ api kauravyaḥ bhrātṛbhyām sahitaḥ tadā yayau sva śibiram rājā niśāyām senayā vṛtaḥ bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam tūrṇam prayātaḥ śibiram prati droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ parivārya camūm sarvām prayayuḥ śibiram prati tathā eva sātyakiḥ rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ parivārya raṇe yodhān yayatuḥ śibiram prati evam ete mahā rāja tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha paryavartanta sahitāḥ niśā kāle paraṃtapāḥ tatas sva śibiram gatvā pāṇḍavāḥ kuravaḥ tathā rakṣām kṛtvā ātmanaḥ śūrāḥ nyasya gulmān yathāvidhi apanīya ca śalyān te snātvā ca vividhaiḥ jalaiḥ kṛta svastyayanāḥ sarve saṃstūyantaḥ ca bandibhiḥ gīta vāditra śabdena vyakrīḍanta yaśasvinaḥ na hi yuddha kathām kām cit tatra cakruḥ mahā rathāḥ hasti aśva bahule rājan prekṣaṇīye babhūvatuḥ uvāca pariṇāmya niśām tām tu sukha suptāḥ janeśvarāḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva punar yuddhāya niryayuḥ bhīṣmaḥ ca rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ bhāradvājaḥ ca vai dvijaḥ ekībhūtāḥ su saṃyattāḥ kauravāṇām mahā camūḥ vyūhāya vidadhuḥ rājan pāṇḍavān prati daṃśitāḥ bhīṣmaḥ kṛtvā mahā vyūham pitā te viśām pate sāgara pratimam ghoram vāhana ūrmi taraṃgiṇam agratas sarva sainyānām bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yayau mālavaiḥ dākṣiṇātyaiḥ ca āvantyaiḥ ca samanvitaḥ tatas anantaram eva āsīt bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān pulindaiḥ pāradaiḥ ca eva tathā kṣudraka mālavaiḥ māgadhaiḥ ca kaliṅgaiḥ ca piśācaiḥ ca viśām pate prāgjyotiṣāt anu nṛpaḥ kausalyaḥ atha bṛhadbalaḥ bṛhadbalāt tatas śūraḥ trigartaḥ prasthala adhipaḥ kāmbojaiḥ bahubhiḥ sārdham yavanaiḥ ca sahasraśas drauṇeḥ anantaram prāyāt sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥ evam eṣa mahā vyūhaḥ prayayau sāgara upamaḥ rejuḥ tatra patākāḥ ca śveta chatrāṇi ca abhibho aṅgadāni atha citrāṇi mahārhāni dhanūṃṣi ca tam tu dṛṣṭvā mahā vyūham tāvakānām mahā rathaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abravīt tūrṇam pārṣatam pṛtanāpatim paśya vyūham mahā iṣvāsa nirmitam sāgara upamam tatas sa pārṣataḥ śūraḥ vyūham cakre su dāruṇam śṛṅgāṭakam mahā rāja para vyūha vināśanam śṛṅgebhyaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ nābhau abhūt nara śreṣṭhaḥ śvetāśvaḥ vānaradhvajaḥ madhye yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau atha itare mahā iṣvāsāḥ saha sainyāḥ narādhipāḥ vyūham tam pūrayām āsuḥ vyūha śāstra viśāradāḥ abhimanyuḥ tatas paścāt virāṭaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ draupadeyāḥ ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ evam etam mahā vyūham vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ atiṣṭhan samare śūrāḥ yoddhu kāmāḥ jaya eṣiṇaḥ bherī śabdāḥ ca tumulāḥ vimiśrāḥ śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ kṣveḍita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭaiḥ su bhīmāḥ sarvatodiśam tatas śūrāḥ samāsādya samare te parasparam tāvakānām pareṣām ca nighnatām itaretaram nārācāḥ niśitāḥ saṃkhye saṃpatanti sma bhārata vyātta ānanāḥ bhaya karāḥ uragāḥ iva saṃghaśas niṣpetuḥ vimalāḥ śaktyaḥ taila dhautāḥ su tejanāḥ ambudebhyaḥ yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahradāḥ gadāḥ ca vimalaiḥ paṭṭaiḥ pinaddhāḥ svarṇa bhūṣitāḥ patatyaḥ tatra dṛśyante giri śṛṅga upamāḥ śubhāḥ nistriṃśāḥ ca vyarājanta vimala ambara saṃnibhāḥ ārṣabhāṇi ca carmāṇi śata candrāṇi bhārata aśobhanta raṇe rājan patamānāni sarvaśas rathāḥ tu rathibhiḥ tūrṇam preṣitāḥ parama āhave yugaiḥ yugāni saṃśliṣya yuyudhuḥ pārthiva ṛṣabhāḥ dantinām yudhyamānānām saṃgharṣāt pāvakaḥ abhavat danteṣu bharata śreṣṭha sa dhūmaḥ sarvatodiśam patamānāḥ sma dṛśyante giri śṛṅgāt nagāḥ iva pādātāḥ ca api adṛśyanta nighnantaḥ hi parasparam citra rūpa dharāḥ śūrāḥ nakhara prāsa yodhinaḥ anyonyam te samāsādya kuru pāṇḍava sainikāḥ tatas śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ ratha ghoṣeṇa nādayan abhyāgamat raṇe pāṇḍūn dhanuḥ śabdena mohayan pāṇḍavānām rathāḥ ca api nadantaḥ bhairava svanam abhyadravanta saṃyattāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham te teṣām ca bhārata nara aśva ratha nāgānām vyatiṣaktam parasparam uvāca na śekuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ draṣṭum tapantam iva bhāskaram tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanāt abhyadravanta gāṅgeyam mardayantam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa tu bhīṣmaḥ raṇa ślāghī somakān saha sṛñjayān pāñcālān ca mahā iṣvāsān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ saha bhīṣmam eva abhyayus tūrṇam tyaktvā mṛtyu kṛtam bhayam sa teṣām rathinām vīraḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yudhi ciccheda sahasā rājan bāhūn atha śirāṃsi ca patitāni uttamāṅgāni hayebhyaḥ haya sādinām nirmanuṣyān ca mātaṅgān śayānān parvata upamān apaśyāma mahā rāja bhīṣma astreṇa pramohitān na tatra āsīt pumān kaḥ cit pāṇḍavānām viśām pate anyatra rathinām śreṣṭhāt bhīmasenāt mahā balāt sa hi bhīṣmam samāsādya tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge tatas niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ bhīṣma bhīma samāgame babhūva sarva sainyānām ghora rūpaḥ bhayānakaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ siṃhanādam atha anadan bhīmaḥ tu sārathim hatvā bhīṣmasya rathinām varaḥ sunābhasya śareṇa āśu śiraḥ ciccheda ca ari hā na amṛṣyanta raṇe śūrāḥ sodaryāḥ sapta saṃyuge ādityaketuḥ bahvāśī kuṇḍadhāraḥ mahodaraḥ aparājitaḥ paṇḍitakaḥ viśāla akṣaḥ su durjayaḥ pāṇḍavam citra saṃnāhāḥ vicitra kavaca dhvajāḥ navabhiḥ vajra saṃkāśaiḥ namucim vṛtrahā yathā ādityaketuḥ saptatyā bahvāśī ca api pañcabhiḥ navatyā kuṇḍadhāraḥ tu viśālākṣaḥ ca sapta aparājitaḥ mahā rāja parājiṣṇuḥ mahā rathaḥ raṇe paṇḍitakaḥ ca enam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ samardayat sa tat na mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ śatrubhiḥ vadham āhave dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇa amitra karśanaḥ śiraḥ ciccheda samare śareṇa nata parvaṇā atha apareṇa bhallena kuṇḍadhāram mahā ratham prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya sarva lokasya paśyataḥ tatas punar ameya ātmā prasaṃdhāya śilīmukham preṣayām āsa samare paṇḍitam prati bhārata sa śaraḥ paṇḍitam hatvā viveśa dharaṇī talam yathā naram nihatya āśu bhujagaḥ kāla coditaḥ viśālākṣa śiraḥ chittvā pātayām āsa bhū tale tribhiḥ śaraiḥ adīna ātmā smaran kleśam purātanam mahodaram mahā iṣvāsam nārācena stanāntare ādityaketoḥ ketum ca chittvā bāṇena saṃyuge bhallena bhṛśa tīkṣṇena śiraḥ ciccheda ca ari hā bahvāśinam tatas bhīmaḥ śareṇa nata parvaṇā manyamānāḥ hi tat satyam sabhāyām tasya bhāṣitam tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhrātṛ vyasana karśitaḥ abravīt tāvakān yodhān bhīmaḥ ayam yudhi vadhyatām evam ete mahā iṣvāsāḥ putrāḥ te viśām pate nihatāḥ bhīmasenena mahā vīryeṇa saṃyuge bhrātṝn saṃdṛśya nihatān prāsmaran te hi tat vacaḥ yat uktavān mahā prājñaḥ kṣattā hitam anāmayam lobha moha samāviṣṭaḥ putra prītyā janādhipa tathā eva hi vadha arthāya putrāṇām pāṇḍavaḥ balī nūnam jātaḥ mahā bāhuḥ yathā hanti sma kauravān tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhīṣmam āsādya māriṣa duḥkhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ vilalāpa ati karśitaḥ nihatāḥ bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ bhīmasenena mama yudhi saḥ aham kāpatham ārūḍhaḥ paśya daivam idam mama gāndhāryā ca yaśasvinyā tat tvam tāta na buddhavān samayaḥ ca mayā pūrvam kṛtaḥ vaḥ śatru karśana na aham yudhi vimoktavyaḥ na api ācāryaḥ katham cana yam yam hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām bhīmaḥ drakṣyati saṃyuge sa tvam rājan sthiraḥ bhūtvā dṛḍhām kṛtvā raṇe matim yodhayasva raṇe pārthān svargam kṛtvā parāyaṇam na śakyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jetum sa indraiḥ api sura asuraiḥ tasmāt yuddhe matim kṛtvā sthirām yudhyasva bhārata uvāca dṛṣṭvā mama hatān putrān bahūn ekena saṃjaya bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ ca eva kim akurvata saṃyuge manye aham sarvathā sūta daivena upahatāḥ bhṛśam aśvatthāmnaḥ tathā tāta śūrāṇām su mahātmanām anyeṣām ca eva vīrāṇām madhya gāḥ tanayāḥ mama vāryamāṇaḥ mayā tāta bhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa ca gāndhāryā ca eva durmedhāḥ satatam hita kāmyayā uvāca nivāraya sutān dyūtāt pāṇḍavān mā druha iti ca suhṛdām hita kāmānām bruvatām tat tat eva ca na śuśrūṣasi yat vākyam martyaḥ pathyam iva auṣadham tat eva tvām anuprāptam vacanam sādhu bhāṣitam vidura droṇa bhīṣmāṇām tathā anyeṣām hita eṣiṇām a kṛtvā vacanam pathyam kṣayam gacchanti kauravāḥ tat etat samatikrāntam pūrvam eva viśām pate loka kṣaya karaḥ rājñ tat mama nigadataḥ śṛṇu tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanāt saṃrabdhāni abhyadhāvanta bhīṣmam eva jighāṃsayā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ yukta anīkāḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥ virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ ca eva sahitāḥ sarva somakaiḥ abhyadravanta saṃgrāme bhīṣmam eva mahā rathāḥ kekayāḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca kuntibhojaḥ ca daṃśitaḥ yukta anīkāḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥ duryodhana samādiṣṭān rājñaḥ sarvān samabhyayuḥ tridhā bhūtaiḥ avadhyanta pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravāḥ yudhi droṇaḥ tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ somakān sṛñjayaiḥ saha tatra ākrandaḥ mahān āsīt sṛñjayānām mahātmanām viveṣṭantaḥ sma dṛśyante vyādhi kliṣṭāḥ narāḥ iva kūjatām krandatām ca eva stanatām ca eva saṃyuge aniśam śrūyate śabdaḥ kṣudh kṛśānām nṛṇām iva tathā eva kauraveyāṇām bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ cakāra kadanam ghoram kruddhaḥ kālaḥ iva aparaḥ sa saṃgrāmaḥ mahā rāja ghora rūpaḥ abhavat mahān kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca yama rāṣṭra vivardhanaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ rabhasaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ gajānīkam samāsādya preṣayām āsa mṛtyave tatra bhārata bhīmena nārāca abhihatāḥ gajāḥ petuḥ seduḥ ca neduḥ ca diśaḥ ca paribabhramuḥ chinna hastāḥ mahā nāgāḥ chinna pādāḥ ca māriṣa krauñca vat vyanadan bhītāḥ pṛthivīm adhiśiśyire te hayāḥ kāñcana āpīḍāḥ rukma bhāṇḍa paricchadāḥ vadhyamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta śataśas atha sahasraśas nirjihvaiḥ ca śvasadbhiḥ ca kūjadbhiḥ ca gatāsubhiḥ hayaiḥ babhau nara śreṣṭha nānā rūpa dharaiḥ dharā hāraiḥ niṣkaiḥ sa keyūraiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ apaviddhaiḥ ca patākābhiḥ ca sarvaṣaḥ anukarṣaiḥ śubhaiḥ rājan yoktraiḥ cavya su raśmibhiḥ evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ pāṇḍūnām api bhārata tathā itareṣu kruddheṣu tāvakānām api kṣayaḥ uvāca śakuniḥ saubalaḥ śrīmān pāṇḍavān samupādravat tathā eva sātvataḥ rājan hārdikyaḥ para vīra hā abhyadravata saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm tatas kāmboja mukhyānām nadījānām ca vājinām āraṭṭānām mahī jānām sindhu jānām ca sarvaśas vanāyu jānām śubhrāṇām tathā parvata vāsinām vājinām bahubhiḥ saṃkhye samantāt paryavārayan ye ca apare tittira jāḥ javanāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ abhyavartata tat sainyam hṛṣṭa rūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥ arjunasya atha dāyādaḥ irāvān nāma vīryavān sutāyām nāga rājasya jātaḥ pārthena dhīmatā airāvatena sā dattā anapatyā mahātmanā patau hate suparṇena kṛpaṇā dīna cetanā bhāryā artham tām ca jagrāha pārthaḥ kāma vaśa anugām sa nāga loke saṃvṛddhaḥ mātrā ca parirakṣitaḥ pitṛvyeṇa parityaktaḥ pārtha dveṣāt durātmanā rūpavān vīrya saṃpannaḥ guṇavān satya vikramaḥ indra lokam jagāma āśu śrutvā tatra arjunam gatam uvāca vacanam rājan ulūpī tanayaḥ tadā irāvān asmi bhadram te putraḥ ca aham te abhibho tat ca sarvam yathāvṛttam anusasmāra pāṇḍavaḥ pariṣvajya sutam ca api saḥ sadṛśam guṇaiḥ prīti pūrvam mahā bāhuḥ sva kāryam prati bhārata sa ca api nara śārdūlaḥ śārdūla sama vikramaḥ sthitaḥ preṣyaḥ ca putraḥ ca sarvathā hi anuśādhi mām kim karomi ca te kāmam kam vā kāmam tvam icchasi pariṣvajya sutam premṇā vāsaviḥ pratyuvāca tam prīti pūrvam ca kāryam ca kāryam prati ca mānada bāḍham iti evam uktvā ca yuddha kāle upāgataḥ kāma varṇa javaiḥ aśvaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ bahubhiḥ nṛpa te hayāḥ kāñcana āpīḍāḥ nānā varṇāḥ manojavāḥ te tvadīyān samāsādya haya saṃghān mahā javān kroḍaiḥ kroḍān abhighnantaḥ ghoṇābhiḥ ca parasparam śuśruve dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ suparṇa patane yathā ubhayayoḥ api saṃśāntāḥ haya saṃghāḥ samantataḥ prakṣīṇa sāyakāḥ śūrāḥ nihata aśvāḥ śrama āturāḥ vilayam samanuprāptāḥ takṣamāṇāḥ parasparam tatas kṣīṇe haya anīke kiṃcid śeṣe ca bhārata saubalasya ātmajāḥ śūrāḥ nirgatāḥ raṇa mūrdhani vāyu vega sama sparśāḥ jave vāyu samān tathā āruhya śīla saṃpannān vayaḥsthān turaga uttamān gajaḥ gavākṣaḥ vṛṣakaḥ carmavān ārjavaḥ śukaḥ vāryamāṇāḥ śakuninā svaiḥ ca yodhaiḥ mahā balaiḥ saṃnaddhāḥ yuddha kuśalāḥ raudra rūpāḥ mahā balāḥ balena mahatā yuktāḥ svargāya vijaya eṣiṇaḥ viviśuḥ te tadā hṛṣṭāḥ gāndhārāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ tān praviṣṭān tadā dṛṣṭvā irāvant api vīryavān abravīt samare yodhān vicitra ābharaṇa āyudhān yathā ete dhārtarāṣṭrasya yodhāḥ sa anuga vāhanāḥ bāḍham iti evam uktvā te sarve yodhāḥ irāvataḥ amṛṣyamāṇāḥ te sarve subalasya ātmajāḥ raṇe tāḍayantaḥ śitaiḥ prāsaiḥ codayantaḥ parasparam te śūrāḥ paryadhāvanta kurvantaḥ mahat ākulam irāvān atha nirbhinnaḥ prāsaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ urasi api ca pṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoḥ ca bhṛśa āhataḥ irāvant atha saṃkruddhaḥ sarvān tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ prāsān uddhṛtya sarvān ca sva śarīrāt ariṃdamaḥ taiḥ eva tāḍayām āsa subalasya ātmajān raṇe nikṛṣya niśitam khaḍgam gṛhītvā ca śarāvaram padātiḥ tūrṇam āgacchat jighāṃsuḥ saubalān yudhi tatas pratyāgata prāṇāḥ sarve te subala ātmajāḥ bhūyas krodha samāviṣṭāḥ irāvantam atha adravan irāvān api khaḍgena darśayan pāṇi lāghavam lāghavena atha carataḥ sarve te subala ātmajāḥ antaram na adhyagacchanta carantaḥ śīghra gāminaḥ bhūmiṣṭham atha tam saṃkhye saṃpradṛśya tatas punar parivārya bhṛśam sarve grahītum upacakramuḥ atha abhyāśa gatānām sa khaḍgena amitra karśanaḥ upahasta avahastābhyām teṣām gātrāṇi akṛntata āyudhāni ca sarveṣām bāhūn api ca bhūṣitān apatanta nikṛtta aṅgāḥ gatāḥ bhūmim gatāsavaḥ vṛṣakaḥ tu mahā rāja bahudhā parivikṣataḥ amucyata mahā raudrāt tasmāt vīrāvakartanāt tān sarvān patitān dṛṣṭvā bhītaḥ duryodhanaḥ tatas abhyabhāṣata saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasam ghora darśanam ārśyaśṛṅgim mahā iṣvāsam māyāvinam ariṃdamam māyāvī vipriyam ghoram akārṣīt me bala kṣayam tvam ca kāma gamaḥ tāta māyā astre ca viśāradaḥ kṛta vairaḥ ca pārthena tasmāt enam raṇe jahi bāḍham iti evam uktvā tu rākṣasaḥ ghora darśanaḥ vīraiḥ prahāribhiḥ yuktaḥ svaiḥ anīkaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ irāvān api saṃkruddhaḥ tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya rākṣasaḥ su mahā balaḥ tena māyā mayāḥ kḷptāḥ hayāḥ tāvantaḥ eva hi su ārūḍhāḥ rākṣasaiḥ ghoraiḥ śūla paṭṭiśa pāṇibhiḥ te saṃrabdhāḥ samāgamya dvi sāhasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ saṃgrāme vyavatiṣṭhetām yathā vai vṛtra vāsavau irāvant krodha saṃrabdhaḥ pratyadhāvat mahā balaḥ ciccheda kārmukam dīptam śarāvāpam ca pañcakam sa nikṛttam dhanuḥ dṛṣṭvā kham javena samāviśat vimohayitvā māyābhiḥ tasya gātrāṇi sāyakaiḥ ciccheda sarva marma jñaḥ kāmarūpaḥ durāsadaḥ tathā sa rākṣasa śreṣṭhaḥ śaraiḥ kṛttaḥ punar punar māyā hi sahajā teṣām vayaḥ rūpam ca kāma jam evam tat rākṣasasya aṅgam chinnam chinnam vyarohata irāvant api saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasam tam mahā balam paraśvadha kṣatam rakṣaḥ susrāva rudhiram bahu ārśyaśṛṅgiḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā samare śatrum ūrjitam kṛtvā ghoram mahat rūpam grahītum upacakrame saṃgrāma śirasaḥ madhye sarveṣām tatra paśyatām tām dṛṣṭvā tādṛśīm māyām rākṣasasya mahātmanaḥ irāvān api saṃkruddhaḥ māyām sraṣṭum pracakrame sa nāgaiḥ bahuśas rājan sarvatas saṃvṛtaḥ raṇe tatas bahuvidhaiḥ nāgaiḥ chādayām āsa rākṣasam chādyamānaḥ tu nāgaiḥ sa dhyātvā rākṣasa puṃgavaḥ sauparṇam rūpam āsthāya bhakṣayām āsa pannagān sa kuṇḍalam sa mukuṭam padma indu sadṛśa prabham irāvataḥ śiraḥ rakṣaḥ pātayām āsa bhū tale tasmin tu nihate vīre rākṣaseṇa arjuna ātmaje viśokāḥ samapadyanta dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sa rājakāḥ tasmin mahati saṃgrāme tādṛśe bhairave punar hayāḥ gajāḥ padātāḥ ca vimiśrāḥ dantibhiḥ hatāḥ tathā patti ratha oghāḥ ca hayāḥ ca bahavaḥ raṇe rathibhiḥ nihatāḥ rājñ te teṣām ca saṃkule jaghāna samare śūrān rājñaḥ tān bhīṣma rakṣiṇaḥ tathā eva tāvakāḥ rājan sṛñjayāḥ ca mahā balāḥ mukta keśāḥ vikavacāḥ virathāḥ chinna kārmukāḥ tathā marma atigaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ nijaghāna mahā rathān kampayan samare senām pāṇḍavānām mahā balaḥ tena yaudhiṣṭhire sainye bahavaḥ mānavāḥ hatāḥ tatra bhārata bhīṣmasya raṇe dṛṣṭvā parākramam dṛṣṭvā droṇasya vikrāntam pāṇḍavān bhayam āviśat kim punar pṛthivī śūraiḥ yodha vrātaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ iti abruvan mahā rāja raṇe droṇena pīḍitāḥ ubhayoḥ senayoḥ śūrāḥ na amṛṣyanta parasparam āviṣṭāḥ iva yudhyante rakṣaḥ bhūtāḥ mahā balāḥ tāvakāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ ca saṃrabdhāḥ tāta dhanvinaḥ na sma paśyāmahe kam cit yaḥ prāṇān parirakṣati saṃgrāme daitya saṃkāśe tasmin yoddhā narādhipa uvāca irāvantam tu nihatam dṛṣṭvā pārthāḥ mahā rathāḥ uvāca irāvantam tu nihatam saṃgrāme vīkṣya rākṣasaḥ nadataḥ tasya śabdena pṛthivī sāgarāmbarā sa parvata vanā rājñ cacāla su bhṛśam tadā antarikṣam diśaḥ ca eva sarvāḥ ca pradiśaḥ tathā celuḥ ca sahasā tatra tena nādena nāditāḥ tam śrutvā su mahā nādam te sainyasya bhārata sarpa vat samaveṣṭanta siṃha bhītāḥ gajāḥ iva ninadat su mahā nādam nirghātam iva rākṣasaḥ jvalitam śūlam udyamya rūpam kṛtvā vibhīṣaṇam nānā praharaṇaiḥ ghoraiḥ vṛtaḥ rākṣasa puṃgavaiḥ ājagāma su saṃkruddhaḥ kāla antaka yama upamaḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya saṃkruddham bhīma darśanam kuñjaraiḥ daśa sāhasraiḥ vaṅgānām adhipaḥ svayam tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya gaja anīkena saṃvṛtam putram te mahā rāja cukopa sa niśācaraḥ rākṣasānām ca rāja indra duryodhana balasya ca abhyadhāvanta saṃkruddhāḥ rākṣasāḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ śara śakti ṛṣṭi nārācaiḥ nighnantaḥ gaja yodhinaḥ bhindipālaiḥ tathā śūlaiḥ mudgaraiḥ sa paraśvadhaiḥ parvata agraiḥ ca vṛkṣaiḥ ca nijaghnuḥ te mahā gajān bhinna kumbhān virudhirān bhinna gātrān ca vāraṇān apaśyāma mahā rāja vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥ teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu bhagneṣu gaja yodhiṣu duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja rākṣasān samupādravat amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ mumoca niśitān bāṇān rākṣaseṣu mahā balaḥ jaghāna ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ pradhānān tatra rākṣasān tatas punar ameya ātmā śara varṣam durāsadam mumoca bharata śreṣṭha niśācara balam prati tat tu dṛṣṭvā mahat karma putrasya te māriṣa tam āpatantam udvīkṣya kāla sṛṣṭam iva antakam adya ānṛṇyam gamiṣyāmi pitṝṇām mātuḥ eva ca ye tvayā su nṛśaṃsena dīrgha kālam pravāsitāḥ yat ca te pāṇḍavāḥ rājñ chala dyūte parājitāḥ yat ca eva draupadī kṛṣṇā eka vastrā rajasvalā sabhām ānīya durbuddhe bahudhā kleśitā tvayā tava ca priya kāmena āśrama sthā durātmanā eteṣām avamānānām anyeṣām ca kula adhama saṃdaśya daśanaiḥ oṣṭham parisaṃlihan parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ uvāca tatas tat bāṇa varṣam tu duḥsaham dānavaiḥ api dadhāra yudhi rāja indraḥ yathā varṣam mahā dvipaḥ tatas krodha samāviṣṭaḥ niḥśvasan iva pannagaḥ saṃśayam paramam prāptaḥ putraḥ te bharata ṛṣabha mumoca niśitān tīkṣṇān nārācān pañcaviṃśatim te apatan sahasā rājñ tasmin rākṣasa puṃgave āśīviṣāḥ iva kruddhāḥ parvate gandhamādane dadhre matim vināśāya rājñaḥ sa piśitāśanaḥ jagrāha ca mahā śaktim girīṇām api dāraṇām saṃpradīptām mahā ulkā ābhām aśanīm maghavān iva kuñjaram giri saṃkāśam rākṣasam pratyacodayat sa nāga pravareṇa ājau balinā śīghra gāminā ratham ca vārayām āsa kuñjareṇa sutasya te mārgam āvāritam dṛṣṭvā rājñā vaṅgena dhīmatā udyatām tām mahā śaktim tasmin cikṣepa vāraṇe saṃjāta rudhira utpīḍaḥ papāta ca mamāra ca patati atha gaje ca api vaṅgānām īśvaraḥ balī prabhagnam ca balam dṛṣṭvā jagāma paramām vyathām aśaktaḥ pratiyoddhum vai dṛṣṭvā tasya parākramam kṣatra dharmam puraskṛtya ātmanaḥ ca abhimāni tām prāpte apakramaṇe rājā tasthau giriḥ iva acalaḥ saṃdhāya ca śitam bāṇam kālāgni sama tejasam tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya bāṇam indra aśani prabham lāghavāt vañcayām āsa mahā kāyaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram tasya bhīṣmasya rakṣasaḥ ācāryam upasaṃgamya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ abravīt yathā eṣa ninadaḥ ghoraḥ śrūyate rākṣasa īritaḥ na eṣa śakyaḥ hi saṃgrāme jetum bhūtena kena cit abhidrutam mahābhāgam rākṣaseṇa durātmanā etat hi paramam kṛtyam sarveṣām naḥ paraṃtapāḥ pitāmaha vacaḥ śrutvā tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ kṛpaḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalyaḥ citrasenaḥ viviṃśatiḥ aśvatthāmā vikarṇaḥ ca āvantyaḥ ca bṛhadbalaḥ rathāḥ ca aneka sāhasrāḥ ye teṣām anuyāyinaḥ tat anīkam anādhṛṣyam pālitam loka sattamaiḥ ātatāyinam āyāntam prekṣya rākṣasa sattamaḥ pragṛhya vipulam cāpam jñātibhiḥ parivāritaḥ śūla mudgara hastaiḥ ca nānā praharaṇaiḥ api dhanuṣām kūjatām śabdaḥ sarvatas tumulaḥ abhavat aśrūyata mahā rāja vaṃśānām dahyatām iva śastrāṇām pātyamānānām kavaceṣu śarīriṇām śabdaḥ samabhavat rājan adrīṇām iva dīryatām vīra bāhu visṛṣṭānām tomarāṇām viśām pate rūpam āsīt viyat sthānām sarpāṇām sarpatām iva pūrṇa āyata visṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena ca jatru deśe samāsādya vikarṇam samatāḍayat tatas punar ameya ātmā nārācān daśa pañca ca bhūriśravasi saṃkruddhaḥ prāhiṇot bharata ṛṣabha viviṃśateḥ ca drauṇeḥ ca yantārau samatāḍayat sindhu rājñaḥ ardhacandreṇa vārāham svarṇa bhūṣitam unmamātha mahā rāja dvitīyena ācchinat dhanuḥ pūrṇa āyata visṛṣṭena pītena niśitena ca bhṛśam krodhena ca āviṣṭaḥ ratha sthaḥ rākṣasa adhipaḥ cikṣepa niśitān tīkṣṇān śarān āśīviṣa upamān bibhiduḥ te mahā rāja śalyam yuddha viśāradam prāviśan bhū talam rājñ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ uvāca vimukhīkṛtya tān sarvān tāvakān yudhi rākṣasaḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya rājānam prati vegitam abhyadhāvat jighāṃsantaḥ tāvakāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā balāḥ atha enam śara varṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ śaradi iva balāhakāḥ utpapāta tadā ākāśam samantāt vainateya vat vyanadat su mahā nādam jīmūtaḥ iva śāradaḥ diśaḥ kham pradiśaḥ ca eva nādayan bhairava svanaḥ rākṣasasya tu tam śabdam śrutvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca bharata śreṣṭhaḥ bhīmasenam idam vacaḥ yudhyate rākṣasaḥ nūnam dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ atibhāram ca paśyāmi tatra tāta samāhitam pitāmahaḥ ca saṃkruddhaḥ pāñcālān hantum udyataḥ teṣām ca rakṣaṇa arthāya yudhyate phalgunaḥ paraiḥ gaccha rakṣasva haiḍimbam saṃśayam paramam gatam bhrātuḥ vacanam ājñāya tvaramāṇaḥ vṛkodaraḥ śreṇimant vasudānaḥ ca putraḥ kāśyasya anūpa adhipatiḥ ca eva nīlaḥ sva balam āsthitaḥ mahatā ratha vaṃśena haiḍimbam paryavārayan kuñjaraiḥ ca sadā mattaiḥ ṣaṣ sahasraiḥ prahāribhiḥ teṣām āpatatām śrutvā śabdam tam tāvakam balam tāvakānām pareṣām ca saṃgrāmeṣu anivartinām nānā rūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjantaḥ mahā rathāḥ vyatiṣaktam mahā raudram yuddham bhīru bhaya āvaham hayāḥ gajaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātāḥ rathibhiḥ saha rathāḥ rathaiḥ samāgacchan nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ ca saṃyuge anyonyam samare rājan prārthayānāḥ mahat yaśaḥ sahasā ca abhavat tīvram saṃnipātāt mahat rajaḥ dhūmra aruṇam rajaḥ tīvram raṇa bhūmim samāvṛṇot pitā putram na jānīte putraḥ vā pitaram tathā nirmaryāde tathā bhūte vaiśase loma harṣaṇe śastrāṇām bharata śreṣṭha manuṣyāṇām ca garjatām su mahān abhavat śabdaḥ vaṃśānām iva dahyatām gaja vāji manuṣyāṇām śoṇita antra taraṅgiṇī prāvartata nadī tatra keśa śaivala śādvalā narāṇām ca eva kāyebhyaḥ śirasām patatām raṇe śuśruve su mahān śabdaḥ patatām aśmanām iva viśiraskaiḥ manuṣyaiḥ ca chinna gātraiḥ ca vāraṇaiḥ aśvaiḥ saṃbhinna dehaiḥ ca saṃkīrṇā abhūt vasuṃdharā nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjantaḥ mahā rathāḥ hayāḥ hayān samāsādya preṣitāḥ haya sādibhiḥ samāhatya raṇe anyonyam nipetuḥ gata jīvitāḥ narāḥ narān samāsādya krodha rakta īkṣaṇāḥ bhṛśam preṣitāḥ ca mahāmātraiḥ vāraṇāḥ para vāraṇāḥ abhighnanti viṣāṇa agraiḥ vāraṇān eva saṃyuge te jāta rudhira āpīḍāḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ saṃsaktāḥ pratyadṛśyanta meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ ke cit bhinnāḥ viṣāṇa agraiḥ bhinna kumbhāḥ ca tomaraiḥ pārśvaiḥ tu dāritaiḥ anye vāraṇaiḥ vara vāraṇāḥ mumucuḥ śoṇitam bhūri dhātūn iva mahīdharāḥ nārāca abhihatāḥ tu anye tathā viddhāḥ ca tomaraiḥ hata ārohāḥ vyadṛśyanta viśṛṅgāḥ iva parvatāḥ ke cit krodha samāviṣṭāḥ mada andhāḥ niravagrahāḥ rathān hayān padātān ca mamṛduḥ śataśas raṇe tathā hayāḥ haya ārohaiḥ tāḍitāḥ prāsa tomaraiḥ parām śaktim samāsthāya cakruḥ karmāṇi abhīta vat prārthayānāḥ yaśaḥ rājan svargam vā yuddha śālinaḥ tasmin tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe dhārtarāṣṭram mahat sainyam prāyaśas vimukhīkṛtam uvāca sva sainyam nihatam dṛṣṭvā rājā duryodhanaḥ svayam mahatā śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam samavākirat ardhacandram ca saṃdhāya su tīkṣṇam lomavāhinam tad antaram ca saṃprekṣya tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ saṃdadhe niśitam bāṇam girīṇām api dāraṇam sa gāḍha viddhaḥ vyathitaḥ parisaṃlihan tathā vimanasam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenam ghaṭotkacaḥ abhimanyu mukhāḥ ca eva pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ samabhyadhāvan krośantaḥ rājānam jāta saṃbhramāḥ saṃprekṣya tān āpatataḥ saṃkruddhān jāta sambhramān bhāradvājaḥ abravīt vākyam tāvakānām mahā rathān kṣipram gacchata bhadram vaḥ rājānam parirakṣata saṃśayam paramam prāptam majjantam vyasana arṇave ete kruddhāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjantaḥ jaye ratāḥ nadantaḥ bhairavān nādān trāsayantaḥ ca bhum imām tat ācārya vacaḥ śrutvā somadatta purogamāḥ tāvakāḥ samavartanta pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm kṛpaḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalyaḥ droṇaputraḥ viviṃśatiḥ te viṃśati padam gatvā saṃprahāram pracakrire pāṇḍavāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca paraspara jighāṃsavaḥ bhāradvājaḥ tatas bhīmam ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat bhūyas ca enam mahā bāhuḥ śaraiḥ śīghram avākirat parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ śaradi iva balāhakaḥ tam pratyavidhyat daśabhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ tvaramāṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ savye pārśve mahā balaḥ pranaṣṭa saṃjñaḥ sahasā rathopasthe upāviśat gurum pravyathitam dṛṣṭvā rājā duryodhanaḥ svayam bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ gadām ādāya sa tvaraḥ samudyamya gadām gurum yama daṇḍa upamām raṇe tam udyata gadam dṛṣṭvā kailāsam iva śṛṅgiṇam tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya saṃkruddham bhīma darśanam samabhyadhāvan tvaritāḥ kauravāṇām mahā rathāḥ bhāradvāja mukhāḥ sarve bhīmasena jighāṃsayā nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi bhīmasya urasi apātayan sahita pāṇḍavam sarve pīḍayantaḥ samantataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā saṃśayam prāptam pīḍyamānam mahā ratham abhimanyu prabhṛtayaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ abhyadhāvan parīpsantaḥ prāṇān tyaktvā su dustyajān anūpa adhipatiḥ śūraḥ bhīmasya dayitaḥ sakhā sa visphārya mahat cāpam drauṇim vivyādha pattriṇā yathā śakraḥ mahā rāja purā vivyādha dānavam vipracittim durādharṣam devatānām bhayaṃkaram sa rudreṇa jitaḥ pūrvam nihataḥ mātariśvanā saṃjāta rudhira utpīḍaḥ drauṇiḥ krodha samanvitaḥ dadhre nīla vināśāya matim matimatām varaḥ tatas saṃdhāya vimalān bhallān karmāra pāyitān jaghāna caturaḥ vāhān pātayām āsa ca dhvajam tatas ṣaṣṭhena bhallena rathāt sūtam apātayat sūtam ca ekena bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat mohitam vīkṣya rājānam nīlam abhra caya upamam ghaṭotkacaḥ api saṃkruddhaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ bhīmasenaḥ api samare nīlam nīlāñjana prabham tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya rākṣasam ghora darśanam nijaghāna ca saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasān bhīma darśanān yaḥ abhavan agratas kruddhāḥ rākṣasasya puraḥsarāḥ vimukhān ca eva tān dṛṣṭvā drauṇi cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ prāduścakre mahā māyām ghora rūpām su dāruṇām mohayan samare drauṇim māyāvī rākṣasa adhipaḥ tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve māyayā vimukhīkṛtāḥ viceṣṭamānān kṛpaṇān śoṇitena samukṣitān droṇam duryodhanam śalyam aśvatthāmānam eva ca prāyaśas ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ ye pradhānāḥ ca kauravāḥ vidhvastāḥ rathinaḥ sarve gajāḥ ca vinipātitāḥ hayāḥ ca sa haya ārohāḥ vinikṛttāḥ sahasraśas tat dṛṣṭvā tāvakam sainyam vidrutam śibiram prati yudhyadhvam mā palāyadhvam māyā eṣā rākṣasī raṇe tān ca pradravataḥ dṛṣṭvā jayam prāptāḥ ca pāṇḍavāḥ ghaṭotkacena sahitāḥ siṃhanādān pracakrire śaṅkha dundubhi ghoṣāḥ ca samantāt sasvanuḥ bhṛśam evam te balam sarvam haiḍimbena durātmanā sūrya astamana velāyām prabhagnam vidrutam diśaḥ uvāca parājayam rākṣaseṇa na amṛṣyata paraṃtapa kathayām āsa durdharṣaḥ viniḥśvasya punar punar abravīt ca tadā rājñ bhīṣmam kuru pitāmaham bhavantam samupāśritya vāsudevam yathā paraiḥ ekādaśa samākhyātāḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca yāḥ mama nideśe tava tiṣṭhanti mayā sārdham paraṃtapa saḥ aham bharata śārdūla bhīmasena purogamaiḥ ghaṭotkacam samāśritya pāṇḍavaiḥ yudhi nirjitaḥ tat me dahati gātrāṇi śuṣka vṛkṣam iva analaḥ rākṣasa apasadam hantum svayam eva pitāmaha tvām samāśritya durdharṣam tat me kartum tvam arhasi duryodhanam idam vākyam bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ abravīt śṛṇu rājan mama vacaḥ yat tvā vakṣyāmi kaurava yathā tvayā mahā rāja vartitavyam paraṃtapa ātmā rakṣyaḥ raṇe tāta sarva avasthāsu ariṃdama dharmarājena saṃgrāmaḥ tvayā kāryaḥ sadā anagha arjunena yamābhyām vā bhīmasenena vā punar na tu kāryaḥ tvayā rājan haiḍimbena durātmanā rāja dharmam puraskṛtya rājā rājānam ṛcchati aham droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ śalyaḥ ca saumadattiḥ ca vikarṇaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ tava ca bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ duḥśāsana purogamāḥ tvad artham pratiyotsyāmaḥ rākṣasam tam mahā balam etāvat uktvā rājānam bhagadattam atha abravīt samakṣam pārthiva indrasya vākyam vākya viśāradaḥ gaccha śīghram mahā rāja haiḍimbam yuddha durmadam vārayasva raṇe yattaḥ miṣatām sarva dhanvinām rākṣasam krūra karmāṇam yathā indraḥ tārakam purā tava divyāni ca astrāṇi vikramaḥ ca paraṃtapa samāgamaḥ ca bahubhiḥ purā abhūt asuraiḥ saha tvam tasya rāja śārdūla pratiyoddhā mahā āhave sva balena vṛtaḥ rājñ jahi rākṣasa puṃgavam etat śrutvā tu vacanam bhīṣmasya pṛtanāpateḥ abhyavartanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ draupadeyāḥ satyadhṛtiḥ kṣatradevaḥ ca māriṣa cedipaḥ vasudānaḥ ca daśārṇa adhipatiḥ tathā pāṇḍūnām bhagadattena yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam pramuktāḥ rathibhiḥ bāṇāḥ bhīma vegāḥ su tejanāḥ prabhinnāḥ ca mahā nāgāḥ vinītāḥ hasti sādibhiḥ mada andhāḥ roṣa saṃrabdhāḥ viṣāṇa agraiḥ mahā āhave hayāḥ ca cāmara āpīḍāḥ prāsa pāṇibhiḥ āsthitāḥ coditāḥ sādibhiḥ kṣipram nipetuḥ itaretaram pādātāḥ ca padāti oghaiḥ tāḍitāḥ śakti tomaraiḥ nyapatanta tadā bhūmau śataśas atha sahasraśas rathinaḥ ca tathā rājan karṇi nālīka sāyakaiḥ tasmin tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe kiran śara sahasrāṇi supratīka śiraḥ gataḥ airāvata sthaḥ maghavān vāri dhārāḥ iva anagha sa bhīmam śara dhārābhiḥ tāḍayām āsa pārthivaḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ bhīmasenaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ pādarakṣān paraḥśatān nijaghāna mahā iṣvāsaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān kruddhaḥ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān codayām āsa nāga indram bhīmasena ratham prati sa nāgaḥ preṣitaḥ tena bāṇaḥ jyā coditaḥ yathā tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ kekayāḥ ca abhimanyuḥ ca draupadeyāḥ ca sarvaśas daśārṇa adhipatiḥ śūraḥ kṣatradevaḥ ca māriṣa uttama astrāṇi divyāni darśayantaḥ mahā balāḥ tam ekam kuñjaram kruddhāḥ samantāt paryavārayan saṃjāta rudhira utpīḍaḥ dhātu citraḥ iva adrirāj daśārṇa adhipatiḥ ca api gajam bhūmidhara upamam vāritam prekṣya nāga indram daśārṇasya mahātmanaḥ sādhu sādhu iti sainyāni pāṇḍaveyāni apūjayan tasya varma mukha trāṇam śātakumbha pariṣkṛtam vidārya prāviśan kṣipram valmīkam iva pannagāḥ upāvṛtta madaḥ kṣipram sa nyavartata vegāt sa mardamānaḥ sva balam vāyuḥ vṛkṣān iva ojasā tasmin parājite nāge pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ kirantaḥ vividhān bāṇān śastrāṇi vividhāni ca teṣām āpatatām rājan saṃkruddhānām amarṣiṇām śrutvā sa ninadam ghoram amarṣāt gata sādhvasaḥ aṅkuśa aṅguṣṭha nuditaḥ sa gaja pravaraḥ yudhi ratha saṃghān tathā nāgān hayān ca saha sādibhiḥ pādātān ca su saṃkruddhaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas amṛdnāt samare rājan saṃpradhāvan tatas tatas tad saṃloḍay tu pāṇḍūnām tat balam mahat bhagnam tu sva balam dṛṣṭvā bhagadattena dhīmatā vikaṭaḥ puruṣaḥ rājan dīpta āsyaḥ dīpta locanaḥ rūpam vibhīṣaṇam kṛtvā roṣeṇa prajvalan iva jagrāha vipulam śūlam girīṇām api dāraṇam nāgam jighāṃsuḥ sahasā cikṣepa ca mahā balaḥ sa visphuliṅga jvālābhiḥ samantāt pariveṣṭitam tam āpatantam sahasā dṛṣṭvā jvālā ākulam raṇe cikṣepa ruciram tīkṣṇam ardhacandram sa pārthivaḥ nipapāta dvidhā chinnam śūlam hema pariṣkṛtam mahā aśaniḥ yathā bhraṣṭā śakra muktā nabhaḥ gatā śūlam nipatitam dṛṣṭvā dvidhā kṛttam sa pārthivaḥ rukma daṇḍām mahā śaktim jagrāha agni śikhā upamām cikṣepa tām rākṣasasya tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt tām āpatatīm saṃprekṣya viyat sthām aśanīm iva utpatya rākṣasaḥ tūrṇam jagrāha ca nanāda ca tat avekṣya kṛtam karma rākṣaseṇa balīyasā divi devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ munayaḥ ca api vismitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ bhīmasena purogamāḥ sādhu sādhu iti nādena pṛthivīm anunādayan tam tu śrutvā mahā nādam prahṛṣṭānām mahātmanām na amṛṣyata mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavānām mahā rathān visṛjan vimalān tīkṣṇān nārācān jvalana prabhān bhīmam ekena vivyādha rākṣasam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata visṛṣṭena svarṇa puṅkhena patriṇā bibheda dakṣiṇam bāhum kṣatradevasya ca āhave draupadeyān tatas pañca pañcabhiḥ samatāḍayat tatas bhīmaḥ mahā rāja virathaḥ rathinām varaḥ tam udyata gadam dṛṣṭvā sa śṛṅgam iva parvatam tāvakānām bhayam ghoram samapadyata bhārata etasmin eva kāle tu pāṇḍavaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ ājagāma mahā rāja nighnan śatrūn sahasraśas dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavaḥ rājñ yudhyamānān mahā rathān tvaritaḥ bharata śreṣṭha tatra ayāt vikiran śarān tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ senām acodayat kṣipram ratha nāga aśva saṃkulām tām āpatantīm sahasā kauravāṇām mahā camūm abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ vimṛdnan pāṇḍava balam yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiḥ ca eva kekayaiḥ ca udyata āyudhaiḥ āśrāvayat yathāvṛttam irāvat vadham uttamam uvāca putram tu nihatam śrutvā irāvantam dhanaṃjayaḥ duḥkhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ niḥśvasan pannagaḥ yathā idam nūnam mahā prājñaḥ viduraḥ dṛṣṭavān purā kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca kṣayam ghoram mahāmati tatas nivārayitavān dhṛtarāṣṭram janeśvaram avadhyāḥ bahavaḥ vīrāḥ saṃgrāme madhusūdana nihatāḥ kauravaiḥ saṃkhye tathā asmābhiḥ ca te hatāḥ dhik arthān yatkṛte hi evam kriyate jñāti saṃkṣayaḥ kim nu prāpsyāmahe kṛṣṇa hatvā jñātīn samāgatān idānīm ca vijānāmi sukṛtam madhusūdana kṛtam rājñā mahā bāho yācatā sma suyodhanam rājya ardham pañca vā grāmān na akārṣīt sa ca durmatiḥ dṛṣṭvā hi kṣatriyān śūrān śayānān dharaṇī tale nindāmi bhṛśam ātmānam dhik astu kṣatra jīvikām aśaktam iti mām ete jñāsyanti kṣatriyāḥ raṇe saṃcodaya hayān kṣipram dhārtarāṣṭra camūm prati pratariṣye mahā pāram bhujābhyām samara udadhim na ayam klībayitum kālaḥ vidyate mādhava kva cit codayām āsa tān aśvān pāṇḍurān vāta raṃhasaḥ aparāhṇe mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata parjanya sama nirghoṣaḥ bhīṣmasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥ parivārya raṇe droṇam vasavaḥ vāsavam yathā tatas śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaḥ ca rathinām varaḥ śeṣāḥ tu anye mahā rāja śeṣān eva mahā rathān prajajvāla raṇe kruddhaḥ haviṣā havyavāṭ iva putrāḥ tu tava kaunteyam chādayām cakrire śaraiḥ prāvṛṣi iva mahā rāja jaladāḥ parvatam yathā vilihan vīraḥ śārdūlaḥ iva darpitaḥ vyūḍha uraskam tatas bhīmaḥ pātayām āsa pārthiva kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena saḥ abhavat gata jīvitaḥ tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ apātayat kuṇḍalinam siṃhaḥ kṣudra mṛgam yathā tatas su niśitān pītān samādatta śilīmukhān su bahūn preṣayām āsa kopayānaḥ mahā balaḥ sa sapta tvarayā yuktaḥ putrān te prāpya māriṣa preṣitāḥ bhīmasenena śarāḥ te dṛḍhadhanvanā anādhṛṣṭim kuṇḍabhedam vairāṭam dīrghalocanam vasante puṣpa śabalāḥ cūtāḥ prapatitāḥ iva tatas pradudruvuḥ śeṣāḥ putrāḥ te viśām pate saṃdadhāra mahā bāhuḥ bhīmasenam mahā balam yathā adrim vāri dhārābhiḥ samantāt vyakirat śaraiḥ droṇena vāryamāṇaḥ api nijaghne yat sutān te yathā hi go vṛṣaḥ varṣam saṃdhārayati khāt patat bhīmaḥ tathā droṇa muktam śara varṣam adīdharat nimīlya netre gṛhṇīyāt tathā jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ droṇa cāpa samudbhūtam śara varṣam durāsadam nimīlya nayane agṛhṇāt tathā bāṇān vṛkodaraḥ putreṣu tava vīreṣu cikrīḍa arjuna pūrvajaḥ mṛgeṣu iva mahā rāja caran vyāghraḥ mahā balaḥ yathā vā paśu madhya sthaḥ drāvayeta paśūn vṛkaḥ vṛkodaraḥ te sutān tathā vyadrāvayat raṇe pāṇḍavam rabhasam yuddhe vārayām āsuḥ arjunam astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya teṣām saḥ atirathaḥ raṇe pravīrān tava sainyeṣu preṣayām āsa mṛtyave abhimanyuḥ ca rājānam ambaṣṭham loka viśrutam viratham rathinām śreṣṭham kārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam sa vrīḍaḥ manuja adhipaḥ āpatantam tu nistriṃśam yuddha mārga viśāradaḥ lāghavāt vyaṃsayām āsa saubhadraḥ para vīra hā vyaṃsitam vīkṣya nistriṃśam saubhadreṇa raṇe tadā sādhu sādhu iti sainyānām praṇādaḥ abhūt viśām pate nirāyudham atha ātmānam sa saṃvīkṣya janādhipa tatra ākrandaḥ mahān āsīt tava teṣām ca bhārata nighnatām bhṛśam anyonyam kurvatām karma duṣkaram anyonyam hi raṇe śūrāḥ keśeṣu ākṣipya māriṣa bāhubhiḥ ca talaiḥ ca eva nistriṃśaiḥ ca su saṃśitaiḥ vyākulīkṛta saṃkalpāḥ yuyudhuḥ tatra mānavāḥ raṇe cārūṇi cāpāni hema pṛṣṭhāni bhārata hatānām apaviddhāni kalāpāḥ ca mahādhanāḥ jātarūpa mayaiḥ puṅkhaiḥ rājataiḥ ca śitāḥ śarāḥ hasti danta tsarūn khaḍgān jātarūpa pariṣkṛtān carmāṇi ca apaviddhāni rukma pṛṣṭhāni dhanvinām suvarṇa vikṛta prāsān paṭṭiśān hema bhūṣitān jātarūpa mayāḥ ca ṛṣṭīḥ śaktyaḥ ca kanaka ujjvalāḥ apakṛttāḥ ca patitāḥ musalāni gurūṇi ca parighān paṭṭiśān ca eva bhindipālān ca māriṣa patitān tomarān ca api citrāḥ hema pariṣkṛtāḥ kuthāḥ ca bahudhākārāḥ cāmara vyajanāni ca nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjya patitāḥ narāḥ jīvantaḥ iva dṛśyante gatasattvāḥ mahā rathāḥ gaja vāji ratha kṣuṇṇāḥ śerate sma narāḥ kṣitau tathā eva aśva nṛ nāgānām śarīraiḥ ābabhau tadā samare patitaiḥ ca eva śakti ṛṣṭi śara tomaraiḥ nistriṃśaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śarīraiḥ śastra bhinnaiḥ ca samāstīryata medinī niḥśabdaiḥ alpa śabdaiḥ ca śoṇita ogha pariplutaiḥ su dhṛtaiḥ lakuṭaiḥ ca eva saṃvṛtā tatra medinī baddha cūḍāmaṇi dharaiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ patitaiḥ vṛṣabha akṣāṇām babhau bhārata medinī kavacaiḥ śoṇita ādigdhaiḥ viprakīrṇaiḥ ca kāñcanaiḥ rarāja su bhṛśam bhūmiḥ śānta arcibhiḥ iva analaiḥ vipraviddhaiḥ kalāpaiḥ ca patitaiḥ ca śarāsanaiḥ viprakīrṇaiḥ śaraiḥ ca api rukma puṅkhaiḥ samantataḥ rathaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ bhagnaiḥ kiṅkiṇī jāla mālibhiḥ vājibhiḥ ca hataiḥ kīrṇaiḥ srasta jihvaiḥ sa śoṇitaiḥ pravīrāṇām mahā śaṅkhaiḥ viprakīrṇaiḥ ca pāṇḍuraiḥ srasta hastaiḥ ca mātaṃgaiḥ śayānaiḥ vibabhau mahī śuśubhe dharaṇī rājan pradīptaiḥ iva parvataiḥ nānā rūpaiḥ alaṃkāraiḥ pramadā iva abhyalaṃkṛtā karaiḥ śabdam vimuñcadbhiḥ śīkaram ca muhur muhur nānā rāgaiḥ kambalaiḥ ca paristomaiḥ ca dantinām vaiḍūrya maṇi daṇḍaiḥ ca patitaiḥ aṅkuśaiḥ śubhaiḥ ghaṇṭābhiḥ ca gaja indrāṇām patitābhiḥ samantataḥ vighāṭita vicitrābhiḥ kuthābhiḥ rāṅkavaiḥ tathā rarāja su bhṛśam bhūmiḥ tatra viśām pate aśvānām reṇu kapilaiḥ rukma channaiḥ uraśchadaiḥ sādinām ca bhujaiḥ chinnaiḥ patitaiḥ sa aṅgadaiḥ tathā prāsaiḥ ca vimalaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ vimalābhiḥ tathā ṛṣṭibhiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ ca tathā chinnaiḥ praviddhaiḥ ca tatas tatas narendra cūḍāmaṇibhiḥ vicitraiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ kḷpta śmaśruṣu atyartham vīrāṇām samalaṃkṛtaiḥ graha nakṣatra śabalā dyauḥ iva āsīt vasuṃdharā parasparam samāsādya tava teṣām ca saṃyuge teṣu śrānteṣu bhagneṣu mṛditeṣu ca bhārata rātriḥ samabhavat ghorā na apaśyāma tatas raṇam tatas avahāram sainyānām pracakruḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ avahāram tatas kṛtvā sahitāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ nyaviśanta yathākālam gatvā sva śibiram tadā uvāca tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca putraḥ te sūtaputraḥ ca durjayaḥ katham pāṇḍu sutāḥ yuddhe jetavyāḥ sa gaṇāḥ iti tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā sarvān tān āha mantriṇaḥ sūtaputram samābhāṣya saubalam ca mahā balam droṇaḥ bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ saumadattiḥ ca saṃyuge saḥ asmi kṣīṇa balaḥ karṇa kṣīṇa śastraḥ ca saṃyuge
