nikṛtaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ avadhyaiḥ daivataiḥ api saḥ aham saṃśayam āpannaḥ prakariṣye katham raṇam mahā bala mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada mantra jñaḥ mantravān dakṣaḥ nītimān nīti kovidaḥ sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrāntaḥ sūryaputraḥ pratāpavān etat mahā bhīti karam pratariṣye raṇam katham mā śucaḥ bharata śreṣṭha prakariṣye priyam tava bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tūrṇam apayātu mahā raṇāt aham pārthān haniṣyāmi sarva somakaiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu dayām rājan sadā bhīṣmaḥ karoti vai aśaktaḥ ca raṇe bhīṣmaḥ jetum etān mahā rathān abhimānī raṇe bhīṣmaḥ nityam ca api raṇa priyaḥ sa katham pāṇḍavān yuddhe jeṣyate tāta saṃgatān sa tvam śīghram itas gatvā bhīṣmasya śibiram prati anumānya raṇe bhīṣmam śastram nyāsaya bhārata nyasta śastre tatas bhīṣme nihatān paśya pāṇḍavān mayā ekena raṇe rājan sa suhṛd gaṇa bāndhavān abravīt bhrātaram tatra duḥśāsanam idam vacaḥ duḥśāsana tathā kṣipram sarvam eva upapādaya evam uktvā tatas rājan karṇam āha janeśvaraḥ anumānya raṇe bhīṣmam itas aham dvipadām varam āgamiṣye tatas kṣipram tvad sakāśam ariṃdama niṣpapāta tatas tūrṇam putraḥ te viśām pate tatas tam nṛpa śārdūlam śārdūla sama vikramam ārohayat hayam tūrṇam bhrātā duḥśāsanaḥ tadā aṅgadī baddha mukuṭaḥ hasta ābharaṇavān nṛpaḥ bhāṇḍī puṣpa nikāśena tapanīya nibhena ca araja umbara saṃvītaḥ siṃhakhela gatiḥ nṛpaḥ śuśubhe vimala arciṣman śaradi iva divākaraḥ tam prayāntam nara vyāghram bhīṣmasya śibiram prati bhrātaraḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ tridaśāḥ iva vāsavam rathaiḥ anye nara śreṣṭhāḥ parivavruḥ samantataḥ parivavruḥ mahā iṣvāsam dhārtarāṣṭram mahā ratham ātta śastrāḥ ca suhṛdaḥ rakṣaṇa artham mahīpateḥ prādurbabhūvuḥ sahitāḥ śakrasya iva amarāḥ divi saṃpūjyamānaḥ kurubhiḥ kauravāṇām mahā rathaḥ anvīyamānaḥ sahitaiḥ sodaraiḥ sarvatas nṛpaḥ dakṣiṇam dakṣiṇaḥ kāle saṃbhṛtya sva bhujam tadā pragṛhṇan añjalīn nṝṇām udyatān sarvatodiśam śuśrāva madhurāḥ vācaḥ nānā deśa nivāsinām saṃstūyamānaḥ sūtaiḥ ca māgadhaiḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ pūjayānaḥ ca tān sarvān sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ rājā pradīpaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ śubhaiḥ kañcuka uṣṇīṣiṇaḥ tatra vetra jharjhara pāṇayaḥ saṃprāpya tu tatas rājā bhīṣmasya sadanam śubham avatīrya hayāt ca api bhīṣmam prāpya janeśvaraḥ abhivādya tatas bhīṣmam niṣaṇṇaḥ parama āsane uvāca prāñjaliḥ bhīṣmam bāṣpa kaṇṭhaḥ aśru locanaḥ tvām vayam samupāśritya saṃyuge śatru sūdana kim u pāṇḍu sutān vīrān sa suhṛd gaṇa bāndhavān tasmāt arhasi gāṅgeya kṛpām kartum mayi prabho jahi pāṇḍu sutān vīrān mahā indraḥ iva dānavān pūrvam uktam mahā bāho nihaniṣyāmi somakān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham karūṣān ca iti bhārata somakān ca mahā iṣvāsān satya vāc bhava bhārata dayayā yadi vā rājan dveṣya bhāvāt mama prabho mandabhāgya tayā vā api mama rakṣasi pāṇḍavān sa jeṣyati raṇe pārthān sa suhṛd gaṇa bāndhavān na uvāca vacanam kim cit bhīṣmam bhīma parākramam uvāca duḥkhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ na uvāca apriyam aṇu api sa dhyātvā su ciram kālam duḥkha roṣa samanvitaḥ śvasamānaḥ yathā nāgaḥ praṇunnaḥ vai śalākayā udvṛtya cakṣuṣī kopāt nirdahan iva bhārata sa deva asura gandharvam lokam loka vidām varaḥ abravīt tava putram tu sāma pūrvam idam vacaḥ ghaṭamānam yathāśakti kurvāṇam ca te priyam juhvānam samare prāṇān te eva hita kāmyayā yadā tu pāṇḍavaḥ śūraḥ khāṇḍave agnim atarpayat parājitya raṇe śakram paryāptam tat nidarśanam yadā ca tvām mahā bāho gandharvaiḥ hṛtam ojasā amocayat pāṇḍu sutaḥ paryāptam tat nidarśanam dravamāṇeṣu śūreṣu sodareṣu tathā abhibho yat ca naḥ sahitān sarvān virāṭa nagare tadā droṇam ca yudhi saṃrabdham mām ca nirjitya saṃyuge karṇam ca tvām ca drauṇim ca kṛpam ca su mahā ratham vāsāṃsi sa samādatta paryāptam tat nidarśanam tathā drauṇim mahā iṣvāsam śāradvatam atha api ca vijitya ca yadā karṇam sadā puruṣa māninam avaśyam hita kāmena pārṣatena ca dhīmatā kaḥ hi śaktaḥ raṇe jetum pāṇḍavam rabhasam raṇe vāsudevaḥ ananta śaktiḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kārakaḥ sarveśvaraḥ devadevaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ vaktaḥ asi bahuśas rājan nārada ādyaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ tvam tu mohāt na jānīṣe vācya avācyam suyodhana mumūrṣuḥ hi naraḥ sarvān vṛkṣān paśyati kāñcanān tathā tvam api gāndhāre viparītāni paśyasi svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ yudhyasva tān adya raṇe paśyāmaḥ puruṣaḥ bhava aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jetum devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ aham tu somakān sarvān sa pāñcālān samāgatān tān vā nihatya saṃgrāme prītim dāsyāmi vai tava pūrvam hi strī samutpannā śikhaṇḍī rāja veśmani vara dānāt pumān jātaḥ sā eṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinī tām aham na haniṣyāmi prāṇatyāge api bhārata yā asau prāk nirmitā dhātrā sā eṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinī sukham svapihi gāndhāre śvas asmi kartā mahā raṇam praviveśa tatas tūrṇam kṣayam śatru kṣayaṃkaraḥ praviṣṭaḥ sa niśām tām ca gamayām āsa pārthivaḥ uvāca prabhātāyām tu śarvaryām prātar utthāya vai nṛpaḥ rājñaḥ samājñāpayata senām yojayata iti ha manyamānaḥ sa tam rājan pratyādeśam iva ātmanaḥ dīrgham dadhyau śāṃtanavaḥ yoddhu kāmaḥ arjunam raṇe iṅgitena tu tat jñātvā gāṅgeyena vicintitam duḥśāsana rathāḥ tūrṇam yujyantām bhīṣma rakṣiṇaḥ dvātriṃśat tvam anīkāni sarvāṇi eva abhicodaya idam hi samanuprāptam varṣa pūga abhicintitam pāṇḍavānām sa sainyānām vadhaḥ rājyasya ca āgamaḥ tatra kāryam aham manye bhīṣmasya eva abhirakṣaṇam sa naḥ guptaḥ sukhāya syāt dhanyāt pārthān ca saṃyuge abravīt ca viśuddha ātmā na aham hanyām śikhaṇḍinam rājyam sphītam mahā bāho striyaḥ ca tyaktavan purā na eva ca aham striyam jātu na strī pūrvam katham cana ayam strī pūrvakaḥ rājan śikhaṇḍī yadi te śrutaḥ udyoge kathitam yat tat tathā jātā śikhaṇḍinī kanyā bhūtvā pumān jātaḥ sa ca yotsyati bhārata tasya aham pramukhe bāṇān na muñceyam katham cana yuddhe tu kṣatriyān tāta pāṇḍavānām jaya eṣiṇaḥ sarvān anyān haniṣyāmi saṃprāptān bāṇa gocarān evam mām bharata śreṣṭhaḥ gāṅgeyaḥ prāha śāstra vid a rakṣyamāṇam hi vṛkaḥ hanyāt siṃham mahā vane mā vṛkeṇa iva śārdūlam ghātayema śikhaṇḍinā mā siṃham iva kākena hatam bhīṣmam śikhaṇḍinā paśyema puruṣa vyāghra tathā nītiḥ vidhīyatām mātulaḥ śakuniḥ śalyaḥ kṛpaḥ droṇaḥ viviṃśatiḥ sarvatas ratha vaṃśena gāṅgeyam paryavārayan putrāḥ ca tava gāṅgeyam parivārya yayuḥ mudā kampayantaḥ bhuvam divam ca kṣobhayantaḥ ca pāṇḍavān parivārya raṇe bhīṣmam daṃśitāḥ samavasthitāḥ yathā devāsure yuddhe tridaśāḥ vajra dhāriṇam savyam cakram yudhāmanyuḥ uttamaujāḥ ca dakṣiṇam goptārau arjunasya etau arjunaḥ api śikhaṇḍinaḥ sa rakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena tathā asmābhiḥ vivarjitaḥ yathā bhīṣmam na naḥ hanyāt duḥśāsana tathā kuru bhrātuḥ tat vacanam śrutvā putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ te bhīṣmam pramukhatas kṛtvā prayayau senayā saha bhīṣmam tu ratha vaṃśena dṛṣṭvā tam abhisaṃvṛtam arjunaḥ rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam uvāca ha śikhaṇḍinam nara vyāghra bhīṣmasya pramukhe anagha tatas śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ niryayau senayā saha kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca śaibyaḥ ca eva mahā rathaḥ śakuniḥ saindhavaḥ ca eva kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ bhīṣmeṇa sahitāḥ sarve putraiḥ ca te bhārata agratas sarva sainyānām vyūhasya pramukhe sthitāḥ droṇaḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalyaḥ bhagadattaḥ ca māriṣa dakṣiṇam pakṣam āśritya sthitāḥ vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ mahatyā senayā yuktāḥ vāmam pakṣam apālayan vyūha madhye sthitaḥ rājan pāṇḍavān prati bhārata alambuṣaḥ ratha śreṣṭhaḥ śrutāyuḥ ca mahā rathaḥ pṛṣṭhatas sarva sainyānām sthitau vyūhasya daṃśitau evam ete tadā vyūham kṛtvā bhārata tāvakāḥ saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta pratapantaḥ iva agnayaḥ tathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca mādrī putrau ubhau api agratas sarva sainyānām sthitāḥ vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ virāṭaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ sthitāḥ sainyena mahatā para anīka vināśanāḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas nānāvidha āyudhāḥ vīrāḥ nānā śastra upaśobhitāḥ śikhaṇḍī vijayaḥ ca eva rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ cekitānaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kuntibhojaḥ ca vīryavān sthitāḥ raṇe mahā rāja mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ yuyudhānaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ yudhāmanyuḥ ca vīryavān kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca sthitāḥ yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samare śūrāḥ sthitāḥ yuddhāya māriṣa tāvakāḥ tu raṇe yattāḥ saha senāḥ narādhipāḥ abhyudyayuḥ raṇe pārthān bhīṣmam kṛtvā agratas nṛpa tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan bhīmasena purogamāḥ bhīṣmam yuddha pariprepsum saṃgrāme vijigīṣavaḥ kṣveḍāḥ kilikilā śabdān krakacān goviṣāṇikāḥ bherī mṛdaṅga paṇavān nādayantaḥ ca puṣkarān pāṇḍavāḥ abhyadhāvanta nadantaḥ bhairavān ravān bherī mṛdaṅga śaṅkhānām dundubhīnām ca nisvanaiḥ utkruṣṭa siṃhanādaiḥ ca valgitaiḥ ca pṛthagvidhaiḥ pakṣiṇaḥ ca mahā ghoram vyāharantaḥ vibabhramuḥ vavuḥ ca tumulāḥ vātāḥ śaṃsantaḥ su mahat bhayam ghorāḥ ca ghora nirhrādāḥ śivāḥ tatra vavāśire diśaḥ prajvalitāḥ rājan pāṃsu varṣam papāta ca rudatām vāhanānām ca netrebhyaḥ prāpatat jalam susruvuḥ ca śakṛt mūtram pradhyāyantaḥ viśām pate antarhitāḥ mahā nādāḥ śrūyante bharata ṛṣabha rakṣasām puruṣādānām nadatām bhairavān ravān saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante gomāyu baka vāyasāḥ mahanti anīkāni mahā samucchraye samāgame pāṇḍava dhārtarāṣṭrayoḥ śaṅkha mṛdaṅga nisvanaiḥ prakampitāni iva vanāni vāyunā narendra nāga aśva samākulānām abhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrte babhūva ghoṣaḥ tumulaḥ camūnām vāta uddhutānām iva sāgarāṇām uvāca vikiran śara varṣāṇi vāri dhārāḥ iva ambudaḥ śastra oghinam gāhamānam senā sāgaram akṣayam nivārayitum api ājau tvadīyāḥ kuru puṃgavāḥ tena muktāḥ raṇe rājñ śarāḥ śatru nibarhaṇāḥ kṣatriyān anayan śūrān pretarāja niveśanam yama daṇḍa upamān ghorān jvalana āśīviṣa upamān saubhadraḥ samare kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa sāyakān rathinam ca rathāt tūrṇam haya pṛṣṭhāt ca sādinam gaja ārohān ca sa gajān pātayām āsa phālguniḥ pūjayām cakrire hṛṣṭāḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ ca phālgunim tūla rāśim iva ādhūya mārutaḥ sarvatodiśam tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni bhārata trātāram na adhyagacchanta paṅke magnāḥ iva dvipāḥ na ca enam tāvakāḥ sarve viṣehuḥ ari ghātinam pradīptam pāvakam yadvat pataṃgāḥ kāla coditāḥ praharan sarva śatrubhyaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathaḥ adṛśyata mahā iṣvāsaḥ sa vajraḥ iva vajrabhṛt hema pṛṣṭham dhanuḥ ca asya dadṛśe carataḥ diśaḥ toyadeṣu yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahvadāḥ śarāḥ ca niśitāḥ pītāḥ niścaranti sma saṃyuge vanāt phulla drumāt rājan bhramarāṇām iva vrajāḥ rathena megha ghoṣeṇa dadṛśuḥ na antaram janāḥ mohayitvā kṛpam droṇam drauṇim ca sa bṛhadbalam maṇḍalīkṛtam eva asya dhanuḥ paśyāma māriṣa sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśam tapataḥ te vāhinīm tam dṛṣṭvā kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ pratapantam śara arcibhiḥ tena arditā mahā rāja bhāratī sā mahā camūḥ nandayām āsa suhṛdaḥ mayam jitvā iva vāsavaḥ tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni saṃyuge tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram te sainyasya māriṣa duryodhanaḥ tadā rājā ārśyaśṛṅgim abhāṣata eṣa kārṣṇiḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ dvitīyaḥ iva phalgunaḥ camūm drāvayate krodhāt vṛtraḥ deva camūm iva tasya na anyam prapaśyāmi saṃyuge bheṣajam mahat ṛte tvām rākṣasa śreṣṭha sarva vidyāsu pāragam vayam pārthān haniṣyāmaḥ bhīṣma droṇa puraḥsarāḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ balavān rākṣasa indraḥ pratāpavān prayayau samare tūrṇam te putrasya śāsanāt nardamānaḥ mahā nādam prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ tasya śabdena mahatā pāṇḍavānām mahat balam prācalat sarvatas rājan pūryamāṇaḥ iva arṇavaḥ bahavaḥ ca narāḥ rājan tasya nādena bhīṣitāḥ kārṣṇiḥ ca api mudā yuktaḥ pragṛhīta śarāsanaḥ tatas sa rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ saṃprāpya eva ārjunim raṇe na atidūre sthitaḥ tasya drāvayām āsa vai camūm sā vadhyamānā samare pāṇḍavānām mahā camūḥ na adhyagacchata vai trāṇam pīḍyamānā durātmanā vimardaḥ su mahān āsīt tasya sainyasya māriṣa rakṣasā ghora rūpeṇa vadhyamānasya saṃyuge tatas śara sahasraiḥ tām pāṇḍavānām mahā camūm sā vadhyamānā ca tathā pāṇḍavānām anīkinī rakṣasā ghora rūpeṇa pradudrāva raṇe bhayāt tām pramṛdya tatas senām padminīm vāraṇaḥ yathā te tu kruddhāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ draupadeyāḥ prahāriṇaḥ rākṣasam dudruvuḥ sarve grahāḥ pañca yathā ravim sarva pāraśavaiḥ tūrṇam akuṇṭha agraiḥ mahā balaḥ sa taiḥ bhinna tanutrāṇaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasa uttamaḥ viṣaktaiḥ sa śaraiḥ ca api tapanīya paricchadaiḥ ārśyaśṛṅgiḥ babhau rājan dīpta śṛṅgaḥ iva acalaḥ tatas te bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasa indram mahā āhave vivyadhuḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ tapanīya vibhūṣitaiḥ nirbhiṇṇaḥ tu śaraiḥ ghoraiḥ dīpyamānaḥ samantataḥ alaṃbuṣaḥ bhṛśam bhāti ulkābhiḥ iva kuñjaraḥ praviveśa tamaḥ dīrgham pīḍitaḥ taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām krodhena dviguṇīkṛtaḥ ciccheda sāyakaiḥ teṣām dhvajān ca eva dhanūṃṣi ca tvaramāṇaḥ ca saṃkruddhaḥ hayān teṣām mahātmanām jaghāna rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ sārathīn ca mahā balaḥ bibheda ca su saṃhṛṣṭaḥ punar ca enān su saṃśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bahuvidha ākāraiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas virathān ca mahā iṣvāsān kṛtvā tatra sa rākṣasaḥ tān arditān raṇe tena rākṣaseṇa durātmanā dṛṣṭvā arjuna sutaḥ saṃkhye rākṣasam samupādravat dadṛśuḥ tāvakāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ udvṛtya cakṣuṣī rājan krodhāt prasphurita adharau āśīviṣau iva kruddhau netrābhyām itaretaram uvāca ārjunim samare śūram vinighnantam mahā ratham ārśyaśṛṅgim katham ca api saubhadraḥ para vīra hā bhīmaḥ vā balinām śreṣṭhaḥ rākṣasaḥ vā ghaṭotkacaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ vā sātyakiḥ vā mahā rathaḥ uvāca hanta te aham pravakṣyāmi saṃgrāmam loma harṣaṇam arjunaḥ ca yathā saṃkhye bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ tathā eva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣma droṇa purogamāḥ adbhutāni vicitrāṇi cakruḥ karmāṇi abhīta vat abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt ārśyaśṛṅgim mahā iṣvāsam pituḥ atyanta vairiṇam rathābhyām rathinām śreṣṭhau yathā vai deva dānavau māyāvī rākṣasa śreṣṭhaḥ divya astra jñaḥ ca phālguniḥ tatas kārṣṇiḥ mahā rāja niśitaiḥ sāyakaiḥ tribhiḥ ārśyaśṛṅgim raṇe viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ alambuṣaḥ api saṃkruddhaḥ kārṣṇim navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ tatas śara sahasreṇa kṣiprakārī niśācaraḥ arjunasya sutam saṃkhye pīḍayām āsa bhārata cikṣepa niśitān bāṇān rākṣasasya mahā urasi te tasya viviśuḥ tūrṇam kāyam nirbhidya marmaṇi sa taiḥ vibhinna sarva aṅgaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasa uttamaḥ puṣpitaiḥ kiṃśukaiḥ rājan saṃstīrṇaḥ iva parvataḥ sa dhārayan śarān hema puṅkhān api mahā balaḥ vibabhau rākṣasa śreṣṭhaḥ sa jvālaḥ iva parvataḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja ārśyaśṛṅgiḥ mahā balaḥ mahā indra pratimam kārṣṇim chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ tena te viśikhāḥ muktāḥ yama daṇḍa upamāḥ śitāḥ tathā eva ārjuni nirmuktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ saubhadraḥ tu raṇe rakṣaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vimukha ca tatas rakṣaḥ vadhyamāna raṇe ari prāduścakre mahā māyām tāmasīm para tāpanaḥ abhimanyuḥ ca tat dṛṣṭvā ghora rūpam mahat tamaḥ tām ca api jaghnivāḥ māyām rākṣasasya durātmanaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ ca mahā vīryaḥ rākṣasa indram nara uttamaḥ chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ bahvīḥ tathā anyāḥ māyāḥ ca prayuktāḥ tena rakṣasā sarva astra vid ameya ātmā vārayām āsa phālguniḥ hata māyam tatas rakṣaḥ vadhyamānam ca sāyakaiḥ tasmin vinirjite tūrṇam kūṭa yodhini rākṣase saubhadraḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ samare ca jita śramaḥ parākramī mahā tejāḥ pituḥ tulya parākramaḥ ārjuniḥ samare sainyam tāvakam saṃmamarda ha tatas śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ sainyam dṛṣṭvā abhividru koṣṭhakīkṛtya tam vīram dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ mahā rathāḥ sa teṣām rathinām vīraḥ pituḥ tulya parākramaḥ raṇe bahuvidham cakre sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ āsasāda raṇe bhīṣmam putra prepsuḥ amarṣaṇaḥ āsasāda raṇe pārtham svarbhānuḥ iva bhāskaram tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ putrāḥ te viśām pate parivavruḥ raṇe bhīṣmam jugupuḥ ca samantataḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan parivārya dhanaṃjayam raṇāya mahate yuktāḥ daṃśitāḥ bharata ṛṣabha arjunam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samācinot vivyādha sātyakiḥ tam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍava priya kāma artham śārdūlaḥ iva kuñjaram śaineyaḥ api tatas kruddhaḥ bhṛśam viddhaḥ mahā rathaḥ abhyadravat raṇe drauṇim rāhuḥ khe śaśinam yathā atha enam chinna dhanvānam tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya śatru ghnam bhāra sādhanam drauṇim ṣaṣṭyā mahā rāja bāhuvoḥ urasi ca arpayat niṣasāda rathopasthe dhvaja yaṣṭim upāśritaḥ pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān vasanta kāle balavān bilam sarpa śiśuḥ yathā ciccheda samare drauṇiḥ siṃhanādam nanāda ca punar ca enam śaraiḥ ghoraiḥ chādayām āsa bhārata nidāgha ante mahā rāja yathā meghaḥ divākaram sātyakiḥ ca mahā rāja śara jālam nihatya tat drauṇim abhyapatat tūrṇam śara jālaiḥ anekadhā tāpayām āsa ca drauṇim śaineyaḥ para vīra hā śarāṇām ca sahasreṇa punar enam samudyam sātyakiḥ chādayām āsa nanāda ca mahā balaḥ dṛṣṭvā putram tathā grastam rāhuṇā iva niśākaram abhyadravata śaineyam bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān vivyādha ca pṛṣatkena su tīkṣṇena mahā mṛdhe parīpsan sva sutam rājan vārṣṇeyena abhitāpitam droṇam vivyādha viṃśatyā sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ tad antaram ameya ātmā kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ tatas droṇaḥ ca pārthaḥ ca sameyātām mahā mṛdhe yathā budhaḥ ca śukraḥ ca mahā rāja nabhastale uvāca katham droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ samīyatuḥ raṇe śūrau tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya priyaḥ hi pāṇḍavaḥ nityam bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ ācāryaḥ ca raṇe nityam priyaḥ pārthasya saṃjaya uvāca na droṇaḥ samare pārtham jānīte priyam ātmanaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavaḥ droṇam vetti eva priyam ātmanaḥ raṇe bhārata pārthena droṇaḥ viddhaḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ na acintayata tān bāṇān pārtha cāpa cyutān yudhi śara vṛṣṭyā punar pārthaḥ chādayām āsa tam raṇe tatas arjunam raṇe droṇaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vārayām āsa rāja indra nacirāt iva bhārata droṇasya samare rājan pārṣṇigrahaṇa kāraṇāt chādayām āsa samare pārtham bāṇaiḥ ayomukhaiḥ tābhyām muktāḥ śarāḥ rājan antarikṣe virejire haṃsāḥ iva mahā rāja śarad kāle nabhastale te śarāḥ prāpya kaunteyam samastāḥ viviśuḥ prabho phala bhāra natam yadvat svādu vṛkṣam vihaṃgamāḥ arjunaḥ tu raṇe nādam vinadya rathinām varaḥ te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kālena iva yuga kṣaye pārtham eva abhyavartanta maraṇe kṛta niścayāḥ mumucuḥ śara vṛṣṭim ca pāṇḍavasya ratham prati śara vṛṣṭim tatas tām tu śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ pratijagrāha rāja indra toya vṛṣṭim iva acalaḥ vimuktām bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ śastra vṛṣṭim durāsadām yat ekaḥ vārayām āsa mārutaḥ abhra gaṇān iva karmaṇā tena pārthasya tutuṣuḥ deva dānavāḥ mumoca astram mahā rāja vāyavyam pṛtanā mukhe prādurāsīt tatas vāyuḥ kṣobhayāṇaḥ nabhastalam tatas droṇaḥ abhivīkṣya eva vāyavya astram su dāruṇam praśaśāma tatas vāyuḥ prasannāḥ ca abhavan diśaḥ nirutsāhān raṇe cakre vimukhān viparākramān tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā kṛpaḥ ca rathinām varaḥ aśvatthāmā tatas śalyaḥ kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau bāhlikaḥ ca sa bāhlikaḥ mahatā ratha vaṃśena pārthasya avārayan diśaḥ gaja anīkena bhīmasya tau avārayatām diśaḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ ca eva saubalaḥ ca viśām pate śara oghaiḥ vividhaiḥ tūrṇam mādrī putrau avārayan bhīṣmaḥ tu sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikaiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram samāsādya sarvatas paryavārayat āpatantam gaja anīkam dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ vṛkodaraḥ lelihan vīraḥ mṛgarāj iva kānane tatas tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ gadām gṛhya mahā āhave tasthau sa sa gadaḥ bhīmaḥ sa śṛṅgaḥ iva parvataḥ siṃhaḥ dṛṣṭvā mṛgam yadvat tam udvīkṣya gadā hastam tatas te gaja sādinaḥ parivavruḥ raṇe yattāḥ bhīmasenam samantataḥ gaja madhyam anuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca vyarājata vyadhamat sa gaja anīkam gadayā pāṇḍava ṛṣabhaḥ mahā abhra jālam atulam mātariśvā iva saṃtatam bahudhā dāritaḥ ca eva viṣāṇaiḥ tatra dantibhiḥ phulla aśoka nibhaḥ pārthaḥ śuśubhe raṇa mūrdhani sādinām śastra vṛṣṭim ca vyadhamat gadayā tatas viṣāṇa ullikhitaiḥ gātraiḥ viṣāṇa abhihataḥ bhṛśam viṣāṇe dantinam gṛhya nirviṣāṇam atha akarot pātayām āsa samare daṇḍa hastaḥ iva antakaḥ śoṇita aktām gadām bibhran medaḥ majjā kṛta chaviḥ kṛta aṅgadaḥ śoṇitena rudra vat pratyadṛśyata evam te vadhyamānāḥ tu hata śeṣāḥ mahā gajāḥ uvāca madhyāhne tu mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata gāṅgeyaḥ rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm vyadhamat niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas dhānyānām iva lūnānām prakaram go gaṇāḥ iva dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ tathā dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas viddhvā virāṭam ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ drupadasya ca nārācam preṣayām āsa bhārata tena viddhāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ bhīṣmeṇa amitra karśiṇā cukrudhuḥ samare rājan pāda spṛṣṭāḥ iva uragāḥ śikhaṇḍī tam ca vivyādha bharatānām pitāmaham strī mayam manasā dhyātvā na asmai prāharat acyutaḥ drupadaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā virāṭaḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ śikhaṇḍī pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmam vivyādha sāyakaiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmaḥ saṃkhye mahātmabhiḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya bhīṣmam vivyādha pañcabhiḥ sārathim ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ su śitaiḥ raṇa mūrdhani tatas bhīmaḥ mahā rāja draupadyāḥ pañca ca ātmajāḥ kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca sātyakiḥ ca eva sātvataḥ rirakṣiṣantaḥ pāñcālyam raṇe tathā eva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣma rakṣā artham udyatāḥ pratyudyayuḥ pāṇḍu senām saha sainyāḥ narādhipa tatra āsīt su mahat yuddham tava teṣām ca saṃkulam nara aśva ratha nāgānām yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam rathī rathinam āsādya prāhiṇot yama sādanam tathā itarān samāsādya nara nāga aśva sādinaḥ vipradruta aśvāḥ samare diśaḥ jagmuḥ samantataḥ mardamānāḥ narān rājñ hayān ca su bahūn raṇe vātāyamānāḥ dṛśyante gandharvanagara upamāḥ rathinaḥ ca rathaiḥ hīnāḥ varmiṇaḥ tejasā yutāḥ kuṇḍala uṣṇīṣiṇaḥ sarve niṣka aṅgada vibhūṣitāḥ ṛddhyā vaiśravaṇam ca ati nayena ca bṛhaspatim sarva loka īśvarāḥ śūrāḥ tatra tatra viśām pate vipradrutāḥ vyadṛśyanta prākṛtāḥ iva mānavāḥ dantinaḥ ca nara śreṣṭha vihīnāḥ vara sādibhiḥ mṛdnantaḥ svāni anīkāni saṃpetuḥ sarva śabda gāḥ varmabhiḥ cāmaraiḥ chatraiḥ patākābhiḥ ca māriṣa viśīrṇaiḥ vipradhāvantaḥ dṛśyante sma diśaḥ daśa tathā eva dantibhiḥ hīnān gaja ārohān viśām pate pradhāvantaḥ anvapaśyāma tava teṣām ca saṃkule nānā deśa samutthān ca turagān hema bhūṣitān vātāyamānān adrākṣam śataśas atha sahasraśas aśva ārohān hataiḥ aśvaiḥ gṛhīta asīn samantataḥ dravamāṇān apaśyāma drāvyamāṇān ca saṃyuge tatas antare mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān gajaḥ gajam samāsādya dravamāṇam mahā raṇe yayau vimṛdnan tarasā padātīn vājinaḥ tathā aśvān aśvaiḥ ca saṃmardya rathaiḥ ca rathinaḥ tathā rathaḥ ca eva samāsādya padātim turagam tathā vyamṛdnāt samare rājñ turagān ca narān raṇe dṛśyante sma mahā bāho tatra tatra mahā balāḥ prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇita antra taraṃgiṇī asthi saṃcaya saṃghāṭā keśa śaivala śādvalā ratha hradā śara āvartā haya mīnā durāsadā śīrṣa upala samākīrṇā hasti grāha samākulā kavaca uṣṇīṣa phena āḍhyā dhanuḥ dvīpā asi kacchapā śaṅkha cakra ogha saṃpūrṇā chattra kūrmā ratha uḍupā patākā dhvaja vṛkṣa āḍhyā martya kūla apahāriṇī kravyāda saṃgha saṃkīrṇā yama rāṣṭra vivardhinī tām nadīm kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ haya nāga ratha plavaiḥ apovāha raṇe bhīrūn kaśmalena abhisaṃvṛtān yathā vaitaraṇī pretān pretarāja puram prati prākrośan kṣatriyāḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā tat vaiśasam mahat guṇavatsu katham dveṣam dhārtarāṣṭraḥ janeśvaraḥ kṛtavān pāṇḍu putreṣu pāpa ātmā lobha mohitaḥ evam bahuvidhāḥ vācaḥ śrūyante sma atra bhārata pāṇḍava stava saṃyuktāḥ putrāṇām te su dāruṇāḥ tāḥ niśamya tadā vācaḥ sarva yodhaiḥ udāhṛtāḥ bhīṣmam droṇam kṛpam ca eva śalyam ca uvāca bhārata iti duryodhana utsṛṣṭāḥ sarve yuyudhire nṛpāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham kurūṇām pāṇḍavaiḥ saha akṣa dyūta kṛtam rājan su ghoram vaiśasam tadā yat purā na nigṛhṇīṣe vāryamāṇaḥ mahātmabhiḥ na hi pāṇḍu sutāḥ rājan sa sainyāḥ sa padānugāḥ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ rakṣanti samare prāṇān kauravāḥ vā viśām pate etasmāt kāraṇāt ghoraḥ vartate sma jana kṣayaḥ daivāt vā puruṣa vyāghra te ca apanayāt nṛpa uvāca suśarmā api tatas bāṇaiḥ pārtham vivyādha saṃyuge vāsudevam ca saptatyā pārtham ca navan punar tān nivārya śara ogheṇa śakra sūnuḥ mahā rathaḥ suśarmaṇaḥ raṇe yodhān prāhiṇot yama sādanam te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kālena iva yuga kṣaye vyadravanta raṇe rājñ bhaye jāte mahā rathāḥ apare tudyamānāḥ tu vāji nāga rathāḥ raṇāt tvarayā parayā yuktāḥ prādravanta viśām pate kaśābhiḥ tāḍayām āsuḥ pārṣṇibhiḥ ca mahur muhur tathā tottra nipātaiḥ ca aṅkuśānām ca vibhramaiḥ gaja ārohāḥ gajān tūrṇam tvarayantaḥ pradudruvuḥ pādātāḥ ca api śastrāṇi samutsṛjya mahā raṇe vāryamāṇāḥ sma bahuśas traigartena suśarmaṇā tathā anyaiḥ pārthiva śreṣṭhaiḥ na vyatiṣṭhanta saṃyuge putrān ca patitān bhūmau mātulān ca pitṝn tathā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ śeṣāḥ vipradrutāḥ narāḥ tathā eva paṇḍavāḥ rājan sarva udyogena daṃśitāḥ jānantaḥ api raṇe śauryam ghoram gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ hāhākāra kṛta utsāhāḥ bhīṣmam jagmuḥ samantataḥ tatas tāladhvajaḥ śūraḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ekībhūtāḥ tatas sarve kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ atiṣṭhat āhave śūraḥ kiran bāṇān sahasraśas tathā eva drupadaḥ rājā droṇam viddhvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenaḥ tu rājānam bāhlikam prapitāmaham viddhvā anadat mahā nādam śārdūlaḥ iva kānane citrasenam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam tasya aśvān caturaḥ hatvā sūtam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ nanāda balavat nādam saubhadraḥ para vīra hā hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam durmukhasya viśām pate droṇaḥ ca drupadam viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sārathim ca asya vivyādha tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī pīḍyamānaḥ tatas rājā drupadaḥ vāhinī mukhe bhīmasenaḥ tu rājānam muhūrtāt iva bāhlikam sa saṃbhramaḥ mahā rāja saṃśayam paramam gataḥ avaplutya tatas vāhāt bāhlikaḥ puruṣa uttamaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam lakṣmaṇasya mahā rathaḥ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam vārayitvā mahā rathaḥ sa viddhvā bhāratam ṣaṣṭyā niśitaiḥ lomavāhibhiḥ tasya āyasam mahā śaktim cikṣepa atha pitāmahaḥ hema citrām mahā vegām nāga kanyā upamām śubhām tām āpatantīm sahasā mṛtyu kalpām su tejanām dhvaṃsayām āsa vārṣṇeyaḥ lāghavena mahā yaśāḥ an āsādya tu vārṣṇeyam śaktiḥ parama dāruṇā vārṣṇeyaḥ tu tatas rājan svām śaktim ghora darśanām vārṣṇeya bhuja vegena praṇunnā sā mahā āhave tām āpatatīm sahasā dvidhā ciccheda bhārata kṣuraprābhyām su tīkṣṇābhyām sā anvakīryata bhū tale chittvā tu śaktim gāṅgeyaḥ sātyakim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ prahasan śatru karśanaḥ tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja parivavruḥ raṇe bhīṣmam mādhava trāṇa kāraṇāt pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca samare vijaya eṣiṇām uvāca dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmam raṇe kruddham pāṇḍavaiḥ abhisaṃvṛtam duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja duḥśāsanam abhāṣata eṣa śūraḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhīṣmaḥ śatru niṣūdanaḥ chāditaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samantāt bharata ṛṣabha tasya kāryam tvayā vīra rakṣaṇam su mahātmanaḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ hi samare bhīṣmaḥ mad pitāmahaḥ nihanyāt samare yattān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha tatra kāryam aham manye bhīṣmasya eva abhirakṣaṇam goptā hi eṣa mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhīṣmaḥ naḥ pitāmahaḥ samare duṣkaram karma kurvāṇam parirakṣatu parivārya sthitaḥ bhīṣmam sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ tatas śata sahasreṇa hayānām subala ātmajaḥ vimala prāsa hastānām ṛṣṭi tomara dhāriṇām darpitānām su vegānām balasthānām patākinām śikṣitaiḥ yuddha kuśalaiḥ upetānām nara uttamaiḥ nānā śastra samākīrṇaḥ yuddhāya eva abhidaṃśitaḥ nakulam sahadevam ca dharmarājam ca pāṇḍavam nyavārayat nara śreṣṭham parivārya samantataḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā śūrāṇām haya sādinām ayutam preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavānām nivāraṇe khura āhatā dharā rājan cakampe ca nanāda ca khura śabdaḥ ca su mahān vājinām śuśruve tadā divākara patham prāpya chādayām āsa bhāskaram heṣatām ca eva śabdena na prājñāyata kim cana tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau udvṛttasya mahā rāja prāvṛṣ kālena pūryataḥ paurṇamāsyām ambu vegam yathā velā mahā udadheḥ nyakṛntan uttamāṅgāni kāyebhyaḥ haya sādinām te nipetuḥ mahā rāja nihatāḥ dṛḍha dhanvibhiḥ te api prāsaiḥ su niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nyakṛntan uttamāṅgāni vicarantaḥ diśaḥ daśa ati āsannāḥ haya ārohāḥ ṛṣṭibhiḥ bharata ṛṣabha acchinan uttamāṅgāni phalāni iva mahā drumāt sa sādinaḥ hayāḥ rājan tatra tatra niṣūditāḥ patitāḥ pātyamānāḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas vadhyamānāḥ hayāḥ te tu prādravanta bhaya arditāḥ yathā siṃhān samāsādya mṛgāḥ prāṇa parāyaṇāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tu mahā rāja jitvā śatrūn mahā āhave dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān ca bherīḥ ca tāḍayām āsuḥ āhave abravīt bharata śreṣṭha madra rājam idam vacaḥ vac madra adhipatim rājā duryodhanaḥ tadā eṣa pāṇḍu sutaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ jitvā mātula māmakān paśyatām naḥ mahā bāho senām drāvayate balī putrasya tava tat vākyam śrutvā śalyaḥ pratāpavān prayayau ratha vaṃśena yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahā ogha vegam samare vārayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ daśabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntare yudhiṣṭhiram punar ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ mādrī putrau ca saṃrabdhau dvābhyām dvābhyām atāḍayat tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave madra rāja vaśam prāptam mṛtyoḥ āsya gatam yathā sarva pāraśavaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ nārācaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ tatas bhīṣmaḥ ca droṇaḥ ca sainyena mahatā vṛtau rājānam abhyapadyetām añjasā śara varṣiṇau aparām diśam āsthāya dyotamāne divākare uvāca ājaghāna raṇe pārthān saha senān samantataḥ bhīmam dvādaśabhiḥ viddhvā sātyakim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram dvādaśabhiḥ bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas viddhvā vinanāda mahā balaḥ tam dvādaśa ardhaiḥ nakulaḥ mādhavaḥ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sahadevaḥ ca saptatyā pārthaḥ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca saptatyā bhīmasenaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ ekaikam pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yama daṇḍa upamaiḥ śitaiḥ tottraiḥ iva mahā nāgam droṇam brāhmaṇa puṃgavam sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcya udīcya mālavāḥ abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ saṃgrāme na ajahuḥ bhīṣmam vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tathā eva anye vadhyamānāḥ pāṇḍaveyaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta vividha āyudha pāṇayaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan parivavruḥ pitāmaham ratha agni agāraḥ cāpa arciḥ asi śakti gadā indhanaḥ śara sphuliṅgaḥ bhīṣma agniḥ dadāha kṣatriya ṛṣabhān yathā hi su mahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sa anilaḥ tathā bhīṣmaḥ mahā rāja divyam astram udīrayan karṇi nālīka nārācaiḥ chādayām āsa tat balam apātayat dhvajān ca eva rathinaḥ ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ muṇḍa tāla vanāni iva cakāra sa ratha vrajān nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvān ca saṃyuge akarot sa mahā bāhuḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tasya jyā tala nirghoṣam visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ amoghāḥ hi apatan bāṇāḥ pituḥ te bharata ṛṣabha na asajjanta tanutreṣu bhīṣma cāpa cyutāḥ śarāḥ hata vīrān rathān rājan saṃyuktān javanaiḥ hayaiḥ apaśyāma mahā rāja hriyamāṇān raṇa ajire matsya pāñcāla kaikeyān pātayām āsa saṃyuge cedi kāśi karūṣāṇām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa mahā rathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kula putrāḥ tanutyajaḥ aparāvartinaḥ sarve suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya vyādita āsyam iva antakam nimagnāḥ para lokāya sa vāji ratha kuñjarāḥ bhagna akṣa upaskarān kān cit bhagna cakrān ca sarvaśas apaśyāma rathān rājan śataśas atha sahasraśas śaraiḥ su kavacaiḥ chinnaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ ca viśām pate gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva nistriṃśaiḥ ca śilīmukhaiḥ anukarṣaiḥ upāsaṅgaiḥ cakraiḥ bhagnaiḥ ca māriṣa bāhubhiḥ kārmukaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ cāpaiḥ ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ samāstīryata medinī hata ārohāḥ gajāḥ rājan hayāḥ ca hata sādinaḥ yatamānāḥ ca te vīrāḥ dravamāṇān mahā rathān na aśaknuvan vārayitum bhīṣma bāṇa prapīḍitān mahā indra sama vīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahā camūḥ āviddha ratha nāga aśvam patita dhvaja kūbaram anīkam pāṇḍu putrāṇām hāhā bhūtam acetanam jaghāna atra pitā putram putraḥ ca pitaram tathā priyam sakhim ca ākrande sakhiḥ daiva balātkṛtaḥ vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍu putrasya sainikāḥ prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārata dadṛśe pāṇḍu putrasya sainyam ārta svaram tadā prabhajyamānam sainyam tu dṛṣṭvā yādava nandanaḥ ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pārtha yaḥ kāṅkṣitaḥ tava yat purā kathitam vīra tvayā rājñām samāgame virāṭa nagare pārtha saṃjayasya samīpatas bhīṣma droṇa mukhān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikān sa anubandhān haniṣyāmi ye mām yotsyanti saṃyuge avadhyānām vadham kṛtvā rājyam vā naraka uttaram duḥkhāni vana vāse vā kim nu me su kṛtam bhavet codaya aśvān yatas bhīṣmaḥ kariṣye vacanam tava pātayiṣyāmi durdharṣam vṛddham kuru pitāmaham tatas aśvān rajata prakhyān codayām āsa mādhavaḥ yatas bhīṣmaḥ tatas rājan duṣprekṣyaḥ raśmivant iva dṛṣṭvā pārtham mahā bāhum bhīṣmāya udyantam āhave tatas bhīṣmaḥ kuru śreṣṭhaḥ siṃha vat vinadan muhur dhanaṃjaya ratham śīghram śara varṣaiḥ avākirat śara varṣeṇa mahatā na prājñāyata kim cana vāsudevaḥ tu asambhrāntaḥ dhairyam āsthāya sātvataḥ codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣma sāyakaiḥ pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuḥ chittvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nimeṣa antara mātreṇa sajyam cakre pitā tava tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavam śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥ sādhu pārtha mahā bāho sādhu kuntī suta iti ca samābhāṣya enam aparam pragṛhya ruciram dhanuḥ mumoca samare bhīṣmaḥ śarān pārtha ratham prati moghān kurvan śarān tasya maṇḍalāni vidarśayan śuśubhāte nara vyāghrau bhīṣma pārthau śara kṣatau go vṛṣau iva saṃrabdhau viṣāṇa ullikhita aṅkitau tatas pravavṛte raudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ pāṇḍavānām ca mukhyasya kurūṇām pravarasya ca dhanuṣī dṛḍha muṣṭī tau ubhau pautra pitāmahau pārtha nāma aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ petuḥ bhīṣmasya vakṣasi nirguṇānām kṛtaghnānām manāṃsi iva hi sādhuṣu bhīṣmasya api tatas bāṇāḥ petuḥ arjuna vakṣasi mahādeva pariprāpta dhanurvidyām jigīṣavaḥ bhīṣmam ca śara varṣāṇi sṛjantam aniśam yudhi varān varān vinighnantam pāṇḍu putrasya sainikān yuga antam iva kurvāṇam bhīṣmam yaudhiṣṭhire bale na amṛṣyata mahā bāhuḥ mādhavaḥ para vīra hā abhidudrāva bhīṣmam sa bhuja praharaṇaḥ balī dārayan iva padbhyām sa jagatīm jagatī īśvaraḥ krodha tāmra īkṣaṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ jighāṃsuḥ amita dyutiḥ grasan iva ca cetāṃsi tāvakānām mahā āhave dṛṣṭvā mādhavam ākrande bhīṣmāya udyantam āhave hataḥ bhīṣmaḥ hataḥ bhīṣmaḥ iti tatra sma sainikāḥ krośantaḥ prādravan sarve vāsudeva bhayāt narāḥ pīta kauśeya saṃvītaḥ maṇi śyāmaḥ janārdanaḥ śuśubhe vidravan bhīṣmam vidyut mālī yathā ambudaḥ sa siṃhaḥ iva mātaṅgam yūtha ṛṣabhaḥ iva ṛṣabham pratoda pāṇiḥ bhagavān śuśubhe yādava ṛṣabhaḥ yathā aṃśunā ardayat candram amāvāsyām divākaraḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya puṇḍarīkākṣam āhave asaṃbhramam raṇe bhīṣmaḥ vicakarṣa mahat dhanuḥ mām adya sātvata śreṣṭha pātayasva mahā āhave śreyaḥ eva param kṛṣṇa loke amuṣmin iha eva ca nirguṇena api tottreṇa vāsudeva kṛtam mama yaḥ yogibhiḥ ca duṣprāpyaḥ sa ghāta artham iha āgataḥ nijagrāha mahā bāhuḥ bāhubhyām parigṛhya vai nigṛhyamāṇaḥ pārthena kṛṣṇaḥ rājīva locanaḥ pārthaḥ tu viṣṭabhya balāt caraṇau para vīra hā nijaghrāha hṛṣīkeśam katham cit daśame pade tatas enam uvāca ārtaḥ krodha paryākula īkṣaṇam niḥśvasantam yathā nāgam arjunaḥ para vīra hā yat tvayā kathitam pūrvam na yotsyāmi iti keśava mithyāvādi iti lokaḥ tvām kathayiṣyati mādhava antam yathā gamiṣyāmi śatrūṇām śatru karśana adya eva paśya durdharṣam pātyamānam mahā vratam tārāpatim iva apūrṇam antakāle yadṛcchayā tau ratha sthau nara vyāghrau bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punar vavarṣa śara varṣeṇa meghaḥ vṛṣṭyā yathā acalau prāṇān ca adatta yodhānām pitā devavrataḥ tava gabhastibhiḥ iva ādityaḥ tejāṃsi śiśirātyaye yathā kurūṇām sainyāni babhañja yudhi pāṇḍavaḥ tathā pāṇḍava sainyāni babhañja yudhi te pitā nirīkṣitum na śekuḥ te bhīṣmam apratimam raṇe kurvāṇam samare karmāṇi ati mānuṣa vikramam te vadhyamānāḥ bhīṣmeṇa kālena iva yuga kṣaye vīkṣām cakruḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavāḥ bhaya pīḍitāḥ tathā pāṇḍava sainyāni drāvyamāṇāni bhārata vadhyamānāḥ raṇe ca api bhīṣmeṇa amitra karśiṇā trātāram na adhyagacchanta gāvaḥ paṅka gatāḥ iva pipīlikāḥ iva kṣuṇṇāḥ durbalāḥ balinā raṇe tathā eva yodhāḥ rāja indra bhīṣmeṇa amitra ghātinā samare mṛditāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ mahā ratham bhārata duṣpradharṣam śara oghinam pratapantam narendrān bhīṣmam na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum te śara arciṣam sūryam iva ātapantam vimṛdnataḥ tasya tu pāṇḍu senām astam jagāma atha sahasraraśmiḥ tatas api bhīṣmaḥ sa balaḥ sa sainyān nyavārayat pāṇḍu sutān śara oghaiḥ jaghāna ca etān su bhṛśam mahā balaḥ mahāvrataḥ pāṇḍu sutān mahātmā vṛtān sadā cakradharasya paśyataḥ tatas balānām śrama karśitānām manaḥ avahāram prati saṃbabhūva mṛdutara kiraṇa agraiḥ tāḥ svayam ca upabhujya malina madhupa saṅgāt tāsu saṃjāta kopaḥ uvāca yudhyatām eva teṣām tu bhāskare astam upāgate saṃdhyā samabhavat ghorā na apaśyāma tatas raṇam tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā saṃdhyām saṃdṛśya bhārata vadhyamānam balam ca api bhīṣmeṇa amitra ghātinā mukta śastram parāvṛttam palāyana parāyaṇam bhīṣmam ca yudhi saṃrabdham anuyāntam mahā rathān somakān ca jitān dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān mahā rathān niśā mukham ca saṃprekṣya ghora rūpam bhayānakam tatas avahāram sainyānām cakre rājan yudhiṣṭhira tatas avahāram sainyānām kṛtvā tatra mahā rathāḥ nyaviśanta kuru śreṣṭha saṃgrāme kṣata vikṣatāḥ bhīṣmasya samare karma cintayānāḥ tu pāṇḍavāḥ na alabhanta tadā śāntim bhṛśam bhīṣmeṇa pīḍitāḥ bhīṣmaḥ api samare jitvā pāṇḍavān saha sṛñjayaiḥ nyaviśat kurubhiḥ sārdham hṛṣṭa rūpaiḥ samantataḥ tasmin rātri mukhe ghore pāṇḍavāḥ vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha sṛñjayāḥ ca durādharṣāḥ mantrāya samupāviśan ātma niḥśreyasam sarve prāpta kālam mahā balāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā mantrayitvā ciram nṛpa vāsudevam samudvīkṣya vākyam etat uvāca ha paśya kṛṣṇa mahātmānam bhīṣmam bhīma parākramam gajam nala vanāni iva vimṛdnantam balam mama na ca eva enam mahātmānam utsahāmaḥ nirīkṣitum yathā ghoraḥ mahā nāgaḥ takṣakaḥ vai viṣa ulbaṇaḥ tathā bhīṣmaḥ raṇe kṛṣṇa tīkṣṇa śastraḥ pratāpavān gṛhīta cāpaḥ samare vimuñcan ca śitān śarān śakyaḥ jetum yamaḥ kruddhaḥ vajrapāṇiḥ ca devarāj varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛt vā api sa gadaḥ vā dhana īśvaraḥ na tu bhīṣmaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ śakyaḥ jetum mahā āhave saḥ aham evam gate kṛṣṇa nimagnaḥ śoka sāgare ātmanaḥ buddhi daurbalyāt bhīṣmam āsādya saṃyuge na yuddham rocaye kṛṣṇa hanti bhīṣmaḥ hi naḥ sadā ekatas mṛtyum abhyeti tathā aham bhīṣmam īyivāḥ kṣayam nītaḥ asmi vārṣṇeya rājya hetoḥ parākramī bhrātaraḥ ca eva me śūrāḥ sāyakaiḥ bhṛśa pīḍitāḥ mad kṛte bhrātṛ sauhārdāt rājyāt prabhraṃśanam gatāḥ parikliṣṭā tathā kṛṣṇā mad kṛte madhusūdana jīvitasya adya śeṣeṇa cariṣye dharmam uttamam pratyuvāca tatas kṛṣṇaḥ sāntvayānaḥ yudhiṣṭhiram dharmaputra viṣādam tvam mā kṛthāḥ satya saṃgara yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ durjayāḥ śatru sūdanāḥ mādrī putrau ca vikrāntau tridaśānām iva īśvarau mām vā niyuṅkṣva sauhārdāt yotsye bhīṣmeṇa pāṇḍava haniṣyāmi raṇe bhīṣmam āhūya puruṣa ṛṣabham paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām yadi na icchati phalgunaḥ yadi bhīṣme hate rājan jayam paśyasi pāṇḍava vimuñcantam mahā astrāṇi pātayiṣyāmi tam rathāt yaḥ śatruḥ pāṇḍu putrāṇām mad śatruḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ tava bhrātā mama sakhā saṃbandhī śiṣyaḥ eva ca māṃsāni utkṛtya vai dadyām arjuna arthe mahīpate eṣa ca api nara vyāghraḥ mad kṛte jīvitam tyajet sa mām niyuṅkṣva rāja indra yāvat dvīpaḥ bhavāmi aham ghātayiṣyāmi gāṅgeyam iti ulūkasya saṃnidhau anujñātam tu pārthena mayā kāryam na saṃśayaḥ nihaniṣyati saṃgrāme bhīṣmam parapuraṃjayam tridaśān vā samudyuktān sahitān daitya dānavaiḥ nihanyāt arjunaḥ saṃkhye kim u bhīṣmam narādhipa bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ nūnam kartavyam na avabudhyate uvāca sa indrān api raṇe devān jayeyam jayatām vara tvayā nāthena govinda kim u bhīṣmam mahā āhave ayudhyamānaḥ sāhāyyam yathoktam kuru mādhava samayaḥ tu kṛtaḥ kaḥ cit bhīṣmeṇa mama mādhava tasmāt devavratam bhūyas vadha upāya artham ātmanaḥ bhavatā sahitāḥ sarve pṛcchāmaḥ madhusūdana tat vayam sahitāḥ gatvā bhīṣmam āśu nara uttamam yathā sa vakṣyate kṛṣṇa tathā kartāsmi saṃyuge bālāḥ pitrā vihīnāḥ ca tena saṃvardhitāḥ vayam tam ced pitāmaham vṛddham hantum icchāmi mādhava yasya aṅge krīḍitam nityam bālye ca parivardhitāḥ astrāṇi vidhivat ca eva śikṣitāni janārdana tam hantum udyatāḥ kṛṣṇa rājya hetoḥ vayam yudhi pituḥ pitaram iṣṭam vai dhik astu kṣatra jīvikām satyam bṛhaspateḥ vākyam devānām agratas kila bhāṣitam guruṇā pūrvam tat nibodha janārdana putraḥ pitaram āsādya pitā putram ca mānada rājya arthe ghātayet evam kṣatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca tatas abravīt mahā rāja vārṣṇeyaḥ kuru nandanam devavrataḥ kṛtī bhīṣmaḥ prekṣitena api nirdahet gamyatām sa vadha upāyam praṣṭum sāgaragā sutaḥ vaktum arhati satyam sa tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ viśeṣataḥ te vayam tatra gacchāmaḥ praṣṭum kuru pitāmaham praṇamya śirasā ca enam mantram pṛcchāma mādhava evam saṃmantrya vai vīrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja jagmuḥ te sahitāḥ sarve vāsudevaḥ ca vīryavān praviśya ca tadā bhīṣmam śirobhiḥ pratipedire pūjayantaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavāḥ bharata ṛṣabha praṇamya śirasā ca enam bhīṣmam śaraṇam anvayuḥ caraṇa upagatān gṛhya pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavān mūrdhni ca etān upāghrāya aṅkam āropayat tadā bāṣpa paryākula mukhaḥ smṛtvā pāṇḍum punar punar tān uvāca mahā bāhuḥ bhīṣmaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ svāgatam te vārṣṇeya svāgatam te dhanaṃjaya yuddhāt anyatra he vatsāḥ prīyantām mā viśaṅkatha tathā bruvāṇam gāṅgeyam prīti yuj punar punar uvāca vākyam dīna ātmā dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prajānām saṃkṣayaḥ na syāt katham tat me vada abhibho maṇḍalena eva dhanuṣā sadā dṛśyaḥ asi saṃyuge na ādadānam saṃdadhānam vikarṣantam dhanuḥ na ca nara aśva ratha nāgānām hantāram para vīra han varṣatā śara varṣāṇi mahānti puruṣa uttama kṣayam nītā hi pṛtanā bhavatā mahatī mama yathā yudhi jayeyam tvām yathā rājyam bhavet mama tatas abravīt śāṃtanavaḥ pāṇḍavān pāṇḍu pūrvaja yuṣmāsu dṛśyate vṛddhiḥ satyam etat bravīmi vaḥ anujānāmi vaḥ pārthāḥ praharadhvam yathāsukham hate mayi hatam sarvam tasmāt evam vidhīyatām uvāca bhavantam samare kruddham daṇḍa pāṇim iva antakam uvāca satyam etat mahā bāho yathā vadasi pāṇḍava na aham śakyaḥ raṇe jetum sa indraiḥ api sura asuraiḥ ātta śastraḥ raṇe yattaḥ gṛhīta vara kārmukaḥ nyasta śastram tu mām rājñ hanyuḥ yudhi mahā rathāḥ dravamāṇe ca bhīte ca tava asmi iti ca vādini imam ca śṛṇu mama pārtha saṃkalpam pūrva cintitam amaṅgalya dhvajam dṛṣṭvā na yudhyeyam katham cana a pumān tasya putraḥ tu pūrvam āsīt viśām pate śikhaṇḍī samara ākāṅkṣī śūraḥ ca samitiṃjayaḥ yathā bhavat ca strī pūrvam paścāt puṃs tvam upāgataḥ arjunaḥ samare śūraḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam mām eva viśikhaiḥ tūrṇam abhidravatu daṃśitaḥ na prahartum abhīpsāmi gṛhīta iṣum katham cana tat antaram samāsādya pāṇḍavaḥ mām dhanaṃjayaḥ na tam paśyāmi lokeṣu yaḥ mām hanyāt samudyatam ṛte kṛṣṇāt mahābhāgāt pāṇḍavāt vā dhanaṃjayāt eṣa tasmāt purodhāya kam cit anyam mama agratas tatas jeṣyasi saṃgrāme dhārtarāṣṭrān samāgatān uvāca te anujñātāḥ tatas pārthāḥ jagmuḥ sva śibiram prati abhivādya mahātmānam bhīṣmam kuru pitāmaham guruṇā kula vṛddhena kṛtaprajñena dhīmatā pitāmahena saṃgrāme katham yotsyāmi mādhava krīḍatā hi mayā bālye vāsudeva mahā manāḥ pāṃsu rūṣita gātreṇa mahātmā paruṣīkṛtaḥ yasya aham adhiruhya aṅkam bālaḥ kila gadāgraja tāta iti avocam pitaram pituḥ pāṇḍoḥ mahātmanaḥ iti mām abravīt bālye yaḥ sa vadhyaḥ katham mayā kāmam vadhyatu mama sainyam na aham yotsye mahātmanā jayaḥ vā astu vadhaḥ vā me katham vā kṛṣṇa manyase katham asmadvidhaḥ kṛṣṇa jānan dharmam sanātanam śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca pratijñāya vadham jiṣṇo purā bhīṣmasya saṃyuge na a hatvā yudhi gāṅgeyam vijayaḥ te bhaviṣyati na hi bhīṣmam durādharṣam vyātta ānanam iva antakam jahi bhīṣmam mahā bāho śṛṇu ca idam vacaḥ mama yathā uvāca purā śakram mahā buddhiḥ bṛhaspatiḥ ātatāyinam āmantrya hanyāt ghātakam āgatam śāśvataḥ ayam sthitaḥ dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇām dhanaṃjaya yoddhavyam rakṣitavyam ca yaṣṭavyam ca anasūyubhiḥ śikhaṇḍī nidhanam kṛṣṇa bhīṣmasya bhavitā dhruvam dṛṣṭvā eva hi sadā bhīṣmaḥ pāñcālyam vinivartate gāṅgeyam pātayiṣyāmaḥ upāyena iti mama matiḥ aham anyān mahā iṣvāsān vārayiṣyāmi sāyakaiḥ śikhaṇḍī api yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ bhīṣmam eva abhiyāsyatu śrutam te kuru mukhyasya na aham hanyām śikhaṇḍinam kanyā hi eṣā purā jātā puruṣaḥ samapadyata uvāca jahṛṣuḥ hṛṣ romāṇaḥ sa kṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tadā uvāca iti evam niścayam kṛtvā pāṇḍavāḥ saha mādhavāḥ anumānya mahātmānam prayayuḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ śayanāni yathāsvāni bhejire puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ svān svān gṛhān abhigatāḥ tām rātrim avasan sukham uvāca katham śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyavartata saṃyuge pāṇḍavāḥ ca tathā bhīṣmam tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca vādyamānāsu bherīṣu mṛdaṅgeṣu ānakeṣu ca śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya niryātāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ yudhi kṛtvā vyūham mahā rāja sarva śatru nibarhaṇam śikhaṇḍī sarva sainyānām agre āsīt viśām pate pṛṣṭhatas draupadeyāḥ ca saubhadraḥ ca eva vīryavān sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca teṣām goptā mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas paścāt pāñcālaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā yamābhyām sahitaḥ prabhuḥ virāṭaḥ tu tatas paścāt svena sainyena saṃvṛtaḥ drupadaḥ ca mahā rāja tatas paścāt upādravat kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca vīryavān jaghanam pālayām āsa pāṇḍu sainyasya bhārata evam vyūhya mahat sainyam pāṇḍavāḥ te vāhinīm tathā eva kuravaḥ rājan bhīṣmam kṛtvā mahā balam agratas sarva sainyānām prayayuḥ pāṇḍavān prati tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ putraḥ ca asya mahā rathaḥ bhagadattaḥ tatas paścāt gaja anīkena saṃvṛtaḥ kāmboja rājaḥ balavān tatas paścāt sudakṣiṇaḥ tathā itare mahā iṣvāsāḥ suśarma pramukhāḥ nṛpāḥ divase divase prāpte bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yudhi āsurān akarot vyūhān paiśācān atha rākṣasān tatas pravavṛte yuddham te teṣām ca bhārata anyonyam nighnatām rājan yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam arjuna pramukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam bhīṣmam yuddhe abhyavartanta kirantaḥ vividhān śarān tatra bhārata bhīmena pīḍitāḥ tāvakāḥ śaraiḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ te sainyam samāsādya pīḍayām āsuḥ ojasā te vadhyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha na aśaknuvan vārayitum pāṇḍavānām mahat balam saṃprādravat diśaḥ rājan kālyamānam mahā rathaiḥ trātāram na adhyagacchanta tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ uvāca pīḍyamānam balam pārthaiḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ parākramī yat akārṣīt raṇe kruddhaḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya katham vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe pratyudyātaḥ paraṃtapaḥ vinighnan somakān vīrān tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca ācakṣe te mahā rāja yat akārṣīt pitāmahaḥ pīḍite te putrasya sainye pāṇḍava sṛñjayaiḥ prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja tam vināśam manuṣya indra nara vāraṇa vājinām na amṛṣyata tadā bhīṣmaḥ sainya ghātam raṇe paraiḥ sa pāṇḍavān mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān ca sa sṛñjayān sa pāṇḍavānām pravarān pañca rājan mahā rathān ātta śastrān raṇe yattān vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ parama saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nānā śastra astra varṣaiḥ tān vīrya āmarṣa praveritaiḥ sādinaḥ ca aśva pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ padātīn ca samāgatān tam ekam samare bhīṣmam tvaramāṇam mahā ratham pāṇḍavāḥ samavartanta vajrapāṇim iva asurāḥ śakra aśani sama sparśān vimuñcan niśitān śarān dikṣu adṛśyata sarvāsu ghoram saṃdhārayan vapuḥ maṇḍalīkṛtam eva asya nityam dhanuḥ adṛśyata tat dṛṣṭvā samare karma tava putrāḥ viśām pate vismayam paramam prāptāḥ pitāmaham apūjayan yudhyamānam raṇe śūram vipracittim iva amarāḥ na ca enam vārayām āsuḥ vyātta ānanam iva antakam daśame ahani saṃprāpte ratha anīkam śikhaṇḍinaḥ adahat niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kṛṣṇavartmā iva kānanam tam śikhaṇḍī tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ abhyavidhyat stanāntare āśīviṣam iva kruddham kāla sṛṣṭam iva antakam sa tena ati bhṛśam viddhaḥ prekṣya bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinam kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na tvām yotsye katham cana yā eva hi tvam kṛtā dhātrā sā eva hi tvam śikhaṇḍinī tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śikhaṇḍī krodha mūrchitaḥ uvāca bhīṣmam samare parilelihan sarvam eva mahā yuddham śrutavantam mahā raṇe jānāmi tvām mahā bāho kṣatriyāṇām kṣayaṃkaram divyaḥ ca te prabhāvaḥ ayam sa mayā bahuśas śrutaḥ pāṇḍavānām priyam kurvan ātmanaḥ ca nara uttama kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na me jīvan vimokṣyase su dṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām bhīṣma lokaḥ ayam samitiṃjaya avidhyata raṇe rājan praṇunnam vākya sāyakaiḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ aham tvām anuyāsyāmi parān vidrāvayan śaraiḥ na hi te saṃyuge pīḍām śaktaḥ kartum mahā balaḥ tasmāt adya mahā bāho vīra bhīṣmam abhidrava a hatvā samare bhīṣmam yadi yāsyasi māriṣa na avahāsyāḥ yathā vīra bhavema parama āhave aham te rakṣaṇam yuddhe kariṣyāmi paraṃtapa droṇam ca droṇa putram ca kṛpam ca atha suyodhanam vinda anuvindau āvantyau kāmbojam ca sudakṣiṇam bhagadattam tathā śūram māgadham ca mahā ratham saumadattim raṇe śūram ārśyaśṛṅgim ca rākṣasam kurūn ca sahitān sarvān ye ca eṣām sainikāḥ sthitāḥ nivārayiṣyāmi raṇe sādhayasva pitāmaham uvāca katham śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyadhāvat pitāmaham pāñcālyaḥ samare kruddhaḥ dharma ātmānam yata vratam ke arakṣan pāṇḍava anīke śikhaṇḍinam udāyudham tvaramāṇāḥ tvarā kāle jigīṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ katham śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ sa tasmin daśame ahani ayudhyata mahā vīryaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ na mṛṣyāmi raṇe bhīṣmam pratyudyātam śikhaṇḍinam uvāca nighnataḥ samare śatrūn śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ aneka śata sāhasrāḥ tāvakānām mahā rathāḥ ratha danti gaṇāḥ rājñ hayāḥ ca eva su sajjitāḥ pārthānām akarot bhīṣmaḥ satatam samiti kṣayam yudhyamānam mahā iṣvāsam vinighnantam parān śaraiḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham sarve eva abhyavārayan daśame ahani saṃprāpte tatāpa ripu vāhinīm kīryamāṇām śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas na hi bhīṣmam mahā iṣvāsam pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja aśaknuvan raṇe jetum pāśa hastam iva antakam atha upāyāt mahā rāja savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ jayantam pāṇḍavam dṛṣṭvā tvad sainyam ca abhipīḍitam duryodhanaḥ tatas bhīṣmam abravīt bhṛśa pīḍitaḥ eṣa pāṇḍu sutaḥ tāta śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ dahate māmakān sarvān kṛṣṇavartmā iva kānanam paśya sainyāni gāṅgeya dravamāṇāni sarvaśas pāṇḍavena yudhām śreṣṭha kālyamānāni saṃyuge yathā paśu gaṇān pālaḥ saṃkālayati kānane tathā idam māmakam sainyam kālyate śatru tāpana sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tathā śūraḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ vyadrāvayetām sahasā sainyam mama mahā balau na anyām gatim prapaśyāmi sthāne yuddhe ca bhārata ṛte tvām puruṣa vyāghra deva tulya parākrama paryāptaḥ ca bhavān kṣipram pīḍitānām gatiḥ bhava cintayitvā muhūrtam tu kṛtvā niścayam ātmanaḥ pātayiṣye ripūn anyān pāṇḍavān pratipālayan pratijñātaḥ jayaḥ hi adya pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām pūrva kālam te mayā pratijñātam mahā bala hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kṣatriyāṇām mahātmanām iti tat kṛtavan ca aham yathoktam bharata ṛṣabha aham vā nihataḥ śeṣye haniṣye vā adya pāṇḍavān aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jetum devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ adya te puruṣa vyāghra pratimokṣye ṛṇam mahat bhartṛ piṇḍa kṛtam rājan nihataḥ pṛtanā mukhe iti uktvā bharata śreṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyān pratapan śaraiḥ āsasāda durādharṣaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm anīka madhye tiṣṭhantam gāṅgeyam bharata ṛṣabha āśīviṣam iva kruddham pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayan daśame ahani tasmin tu darśayan śaktim ātmanaḥ rājñ śata sahasrāṇi saḥ avadhīt kuru nandana pañcālānām ca ye śreṣṭhāḥ rāja putrāḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām ādatta tejāṃsi jalam sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kuñjarāṇām tarasviṇām sa ārohānām mahā rāja hayānām ca ayutam punar pūrṇe śata sahasre dve padātīnām nara uttamaḥ prajajvāla raṇe bhīṣmaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ na ca enam pāṇḍaveyānām ke cid śekuḥ nirīkṣitum te pāṇḍaveyāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ mahā iṣvāsena pīḍitāḥ vadhāya abhyadravan bhīṣmam sṛñjayāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ sa yudhyamānaḥ bahubhiḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā avakīrṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śailaḥ meghaiḥ iva asitaiḥ uvāca arjunaḥ tu raṇe rājan dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam na ca api bhī tvayā kāryā bhīṣmāt adya katham cana aham enam śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayiṣye ratha uttamāt abhyadravata gāṅgeyam śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tathā rājñ saubhadraḥ ca mahā rathaḥ hṛṣṭau ādravatām bhīṣmam śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam virāṭa drupadau vṛddhau kuntibhojaḥ ca daṃśitaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca vīryavān tathā itarāṇi sainyāni sarvāṇi eva viśām pate samādravanta gāṅgeyam śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam pratyudyayuḥ tāvakāḥ ca sametāḥ tān mahā rathān yathāśakti yathotsāham tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu bhīṣma prepsum raṇe yāntam vṛṣam vyāghra śiśuḥ yathā dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā rāja bhīṣma antikam upāgatam tvaramāṇaḥ raṇe yattam kṛtavarmā nyavārayat tvaramāṇam raṇe yattam saumadattiḥ avārayat bhīmasenam su saṃkruddham gāṅgeyasya vadha eṣiṇam tathā eva nakulam vīram kirantam sāyakān bahūn vikarṇaḥ vārayām āsa icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitam sahadevam tathā yāntam yattam bhīṣma ratham prati vārayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi rākṣasam krūra karmāṇam bhaimasenim mahā balam sātyakim samare kruddham ārśyaśṛṅgiḥ avārayat bhīṣmasya vadham icchantam pāṇḍava prīti kāmyayā abhimanyum mahā rāja yāntam bhīṣma ratham prati sudakṣiṇaḥ mahā rāja kāmbojaḥ pratyavārayat aśvatthāmā tatas kruddhaḥ vārayām āsa bhārata tathā pāṇḍu sutam jyeṣṭham bhīṣmasya vadha kāṅkṣiṇam bhīṣma prepsum mahā rāja tāpayantam diśaḥ daśa duḥśāsanaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ vārayām āsa saṃyuge anye ca tāvakāḥ yodhāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathān bhīṣmāya abhimukham yātān vārayām āsuḥ āhave dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu sainyāni prākrośata punar punar eṣaḥ arjunaḥ raṇe bhīṣmam prayāti kuru nandanaḥ abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa bhīṣmaḥ na prāpsyate hi vaḥ kim u bhīṣmaḥ raṇe vīrāḥ gata sattvaḥ alpa jīvitaḥ iti senāpateḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ gāṅgeyasya ratham prati nyavārayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ tāvakāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja bhayam tyaktvā mahā rathaḥ bhīṣmasya jīvita ākāṅkṣī dhanaṃjayam upādravat tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ gāṅgeyasya ratham prati tatra adbhutam apaśyāma citra rūpam viśām pate duḥśāsana ratham prāptaḥ yat pārthaḥ na atyavartata yathā vārayate velā kṣubhitam vai mahā arṇavam ubhau hi rathinām śreṣṭhau ubhau bhārata durjayau ubhau candra arka sadṛśau kāntyā dīptyā ca bhārata tau tathā jāta saṃrambhau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ samīyatuḥ mahā saṃkhye maya śakrau yathā purā duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavam viśikhaiḥ tribhiḥ vāsudevam ca viṃśatyā tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge tatas arjunaḥ jāta manyuḥ vārṣṇeyam vīkṣya pīḍitam duḥśāsanam śatena ājau nārācānām samārpayat te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave yathā eva pannagāḥ rājan taṭākam tṛṣitāḥ yathā duḥśāsanaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ pārtham vivyādha pañcabhiḥ lalāṭe bharata śreṣṭha śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ lalāṭa sthaiḥ tu taiḥ bāṇaiḥ śuśubhe pāṇḍava uttamaḥ yathā meruḥ mahā rāja śṛṅgaiḥ atyartham ucchritaiḥ vyarājata raṇe pārthaḥ kiṃśukaḥ puṣpavān iva duḥśāsanam tatas kruddhaḥ pīḍayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ parvaṇi iva su saṃkruddhaḥ rāhuḥ ugraḥ niśākaram pīḍyamānaḥ balavatā putraḥ te viśām pate vivyādha samare pārtham kaṅka pattraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī ājaghāna tatas paścāt putram te navabhiḥ śaraiḥ arjunam pañcaviṃśatyā bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat tasya kruddhaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavaḥ śatru karśanaḥ apraiṣīt viśikhān ghorān yama daṇḍa upamān bahūn aprāptān eva tān bāṇān ciccheda tanayaḥ tava tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ śarān saṃdhāya kārmuke preṣayām āsa samare svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān nyamajjan te mahā rāja tasya kāye mahātmanaḥ yathā haṃsāḥ mahā rāja taḍāgam prāpya bhārata pīḍitaḥ ca eva putraḥ te pāṇḍavena mahātmanā hitvā pārtham raṇe tūrṇam bhīṣmasya ratham āśrayat pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām putraḥ te viśām pate avārayat tatas śūraḥ bhūyas eva parākramī śaraiḥ su niśitaiḥ pārtham yathā vṛtraḥ puraṃdaram uvāca sātyakim daṃśitam yuddhe bhīṣmāya abhyudyantam tadā ārśyaśṛṅgiḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ vārayām āsa saṃyuge mādhavaḥ tu su saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tathā eva rākṣasaḥ rājan mādhavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ardayām āsa rāja indra saṃkruddhaḥ śini puṃgavam śaineyaḥ śara saṃgham tu preṣayām āsa saṃyuge rākṣasāya su saṃkruddhaḥ mādhavaḥ para vīra hā tatas rakṣaḥ mahā bāhum sātyakim satya vikramam vivyādha viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ siṃhanādam nanāda ca mādhavaḥ tu bhṛśam viddhaḥ rākṣaseṇa raṇe tadā bhagadattaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mādhavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vihāya rākṣasam yuddhe śaineyaḥ rathin varaḥ prāgjyotiṣāya cikṣepa śarān saṃnata parvṇaḥ bhagadattam raṇe kruddhaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sṛkkiṇī saṃlihan muhur śaktim kanaka vaiḍūrya bhūṣitām āyasīm dṛḍhām yama daṇḍa upamām ghorām prāhiṇot sātyakāya vai tām āpatatīm sahasā tasya bāhoḥ bala īritām sātyakiḥ samare rājñ tridhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥ śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā putraḥ te viśām pate mahatā ratha vaṃśena vārayām āsa mādhavam tathā parivṛtam dṛṣṭvā vārṣṇeyānām mahā ratham duryodhanaḥ bhṛśam hṛṣṭaḥ bhrātṝn sarvān uvāca ha ismin hate hatam manye pāṇḍavānām mahat balam śaineyam yodhayām āsuḥ bhīṣmasya pramukhe tadā abhimanyum tadā āyāntam bhīṣmāya abhyudyatam mṛdhe kāmboja rājaḥ balavān vārayām āsa saṃyuge ārjuniḥ nṛpatim viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ punar eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā rājan vivyādha tam nṛpam sudakṣiṇaḥ tu samare kārṣṇim vivyādha pañcabhiḥ yat abhyadhāvat gāṅgeyam śikhaṇḍī śatru tāpanaḥ bhīṣmam ca yudhi saṃrabdhau ādravantau mahā rathau aśvatthāmā tatas kruddhaḥ samāyāt ratha sattamaḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham te teṣām ca bhārata virāṭaḥ daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ ājaghāna paraṃtapa tatas droṇa sutam yodhān dravamāṇam mahā raṇe yatamānam mahā iṣvāsam drauṇim āhava śobhinam visṛjantam śarān dṛṣṭvā aśvatthāmā tatas tau tu vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ yat drauṇeḥ sāyakān ghorān pratyavārayatām yudhi sahadevam tathā yāntam kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ abhyayāt kṛpaḥ ca samare rājan mādrī putram mahā ratham ājaghāna śaraiḥ tūrṇam saptatyā rukma bhūṣaṇaiḥ tasya mādrī sutaḥ cāpam dvidhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ mādrī putram su saṃhṛṣṭaḥ daśabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavaḥ rājan śāradvatam amarṣaṇam ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ bhīṣmasya vadha kāṅkṣayā nakulam tu raṇe kruddham vikarṇaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitam tatra tau nara śārdūlau bhīṣma hetoḥ paraṃtapau anyonyam jaghnatuḥ vīrau goṣṭhe go vṛṣabhau iva ghaṭotkacam raṇe yattam nighnantam te vāhinīm durmukhaḥ samare prāyāt bhīṣma hetoḥ parākramī ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasena sutam ca api durmukhaḥ su mukhaiḥ śaraiḥ ṣaṣṭyā vīraḥ nadan hṛṣṭaḥ vivyādha raṇa mūrdhani dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe yāntam bhīṣmasya vadha kāṅkṣiṇam hārdikyaḥ vārayām āsa rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitam vārṣṇeyaḥ pārṣatam śūram viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ punar pañcāśatā tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntare tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt ājaghāna mahā bāhuḥ pārṣatam tam mahā ratham tathā eva pārṣataḥ rājan hārdikyam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka pattra paricchadaiḥ bhīmasenam atha āyāntam bhīṣmam prati mahā balam tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt nārācena su tīkṣṇena rukma puṅkhena saṃyuge skanda śaktyā yathā krauñcaḥ purā nṛpati sattama tau śarān sūrya saṃkāśān karmāra parimārjitān bhīmaḥ bhīṣma vadha kānṣkī saumadattim mahā ratham tathā bhīṣma jaye gṛdhnuḥ saumadattiḥ ca pāṇḍavam kṛta pratikṛte yattau yodhayām āsatuḥ raṇe yudhiṣṭhiram mahā rāja mahatyā senayā vṛtam bhīṣmāya abhimukham yāntam bhāradvājaḥ nyavārayat sā senā mahatī rājan pāṇḍu putrasya saṃyuge droṇena vāritā yattā na cacāla padāt padam cekitānam raṇe kruddham bhīṣmam prati janeśvara bhīṣma hetoḥ parākrāntaḥ citrasenaḥ mahā rathaḥ cekitānam param śaktyā yodhayām āsa bhārata duḥśāsanaḥ api parayā śaktyā pārtham avārayat katham bhīṣmam paraḥ hanyāt iti niścitya bhārata uvāca atha vīraḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ matta vāraṇa vikramaḥ samādāya mahat cāpam matta vāraṇa vāraṇam vidhunvānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham drāvayāṇaḥ mahā rathān pṛtanām pāṇḍaveyānām pātayānaḥ mahā rathaḥ yuktaḥ prītyā pāṇḍavānām gāhamānaḥ mahā camūm nimittāni nimitta jñaḥ sarvatas vīkṣya vīryavān pratapantam anīkāni droṇaḥ putram abhāṣata jighāṃsuḥ samare bhīṣmam param yatnam kariṣyati dikṣu śāntāsu ghorāṇi vyāharanti mṛga dvijāḥ nīcais gṛdhrāḥ nilīyante bhāratānām camūm prati naṣṭa prabhaḥ iva ādityaḥ sarvatas lohitāḥ diśaḥ kaṅkāḥ gṛdhrāḥ balākāḥ ca vyāharanti muhur muhur śivāḥ ca aśiva nirghoṣāḥ vedayatyaḥ mahat bhayam papāta mahatī ca ulkā madhyena āditya maṇḍalāt vedayānaḥ bhayam ghoram rājñām deha avakartanam apasavyam grahāḥ cakruḥ alakṣmāṇam niśākaram avākśirāḥ ca bhagavān udatiṣṭhata candramāḥ vapūṃṣi ca narendrāṇām vigatāni iva lakṣaye dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu na ca bhrājanti daṃśitāḥ pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaḥ gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanaḥ tathā kilakilā śabdaḥ śrūyate vānarasya ca yasya lāṅgūla śabdena sphuṭati iva nabhastalam dhruvam āsthāya bībhatsuḥ uttama astrāṇi saṃyuge apāsya anyān raṇe yodhān abhyasyati pitāmaham hṛṣyanti romakūpāni sīdati iva ca me manaḥ cintayitvā mahā bāho bhīṣma arjuna samāgamam tam ca eva nikṛti prajñam pāñcālyam pāpa cetasam puraskṛtya raṇe pārthaḥ bhīṣmasya āyodhanam gataḥ abravīt ca purā bhīṣmaḥ na aham hanyām śikhaṇḍinam strī hi eṣā vihitā dhātrā daivāt ca sa punar pumān na ca amaṅgala ketoḥ sa praharet āpagāsutaḥ etat vicintayānasya prajñā sīdati me bhṛśam abhyudyatam raṇe dṛṣṭvā bhairava astram ca pāṇḍavam yudhiṣṭhirasya ca krodhaḥ bhīṣma arjuna samāgamaḥ mama ca astra abhisaṃrambhaḥ prajānām aśubham dhruvam manasvī balavān śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ dṛḍha vikramaḥ dūra pātī dṛḍha iṣuḥ ca nimitta jñaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ balavān buddhimān ca eva jita kleśaḥ yudhām varaḥ vijayī ca raṇe nityam bhairava astraḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ hema citrāṇi śūrāṇām mahānti ca śubhāni ca chidyante ca dhvaja agrāṇi tomarāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca prāsāḥ ca vimalāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ śaktyaḥ ca kanaka ujjvalāḥ vaijayantyaḥ ca nāgānām saṃkruddhena kirīṭinā na ayam saṃrakṣitum kālaḥ prāṇān putra upajīvibhiḥ haya nāga ratha āvartām mahā ghorām su dustarām pūrvam ca eva mayā aśrāvi tapasā ghora rūpiṇā brahmaṇya tā damaḥ dānam tapaḥ ca caritam mahat iha eva dṛśyate rājñaḥ bhrātā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca balavān mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau vāsudevaḥ ca vārṣṇeyaḥ yasya nāthaḥ vyavasthitaḥ eṣa saṃdṛśyate pārthaḥ vāsudeva vyapāśrayaḥ dārayan sarva sainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrāṇi sarvaśas etat ālokyate sainyam kṣobhyamāṇam kirīṭinā hāhā kilakilā śabdāḥ śrūyante ca camū mukhe yāhi pāñcāla dāyādam aham yāsye yudhiṣṭhiram durlabham hi antaram rājñaḥ vyūhasya amita tejasaḥ sātyakiḥ ca abhimanyuḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumna vṛkodarau upendra sadṛśaḥ śyāmaḥ mahā śālaḥ iva udgataḥ uttama astrāṇi ca ādatsva gṛhītvā anyat mahat dhanuḥ pārśvatas yāhi rājānam yudhyasva ca vṛkodaram kaḥ hi na icchet priyam putram jīvantam śāśvatīḥ samāḥ eṣa ca api raṇe bhīṣmaḥ dahate vai mahā camūm saṃjayaḥ putram samanuśāsya eva bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān mahā raṇe mahā rājam dharmarājam ayodhayat uvāca bhagadattaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ citrasenaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca tathā durmarṣaṇaḥ yuvā mahatyā senayā yuktāḥ nānā deśa samutthayā bhīṣmasya samare rājan prārthayānāḥ mahat yaśaḥ kṛtavarmā tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ kṛpaḥ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ durmarṣaṇaḥ ca viṃśatyā pāṇḍavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa tān sarvān mahā rāja bhrājamānān pṛthak pṛthak pravīrān sarva lokasya dhārtarāṣṭrān mahā rathān śalyam pañcāśatā viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ durmarṣaṇam ca viṃśatyā citrasenam ca pañcabhiḥ vikarṇam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pañcabhiḥ ca jayadratham viddhvā bhīmaḥ anadat dhṛṣṭaḥ saindhavam ca punar tribhiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya gautamaḥ rathinām varaḥ bhīmam vivyādha saṃrabdhaḥ daśabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān gautamam tāḍayām āsa śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ āhave saindhavasya tathā aśvān ca sārathim ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kāla antaka sama dyutiḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ śarān cikṣepa niśitān bhīmasenasya saṃyuge bhallābhyām bharata śreṣṭha saindhavasya mahātmanaḥ ati adbhutam raṇe karma kṛtavan tatra pāṇḍavaḥ mahā rathān śaraiḥ viddhvā vārayitvā mahā rathaḥ na atīva mamṛṣe śalyaḥ bhīmasenasya vikramam sa saṃdhāya śarān tīkṣṇān karmāra parimārjitān bhīmam vivyādha saptatyā tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca bhagadattaḥ ca māriṣa durmarṣaṇaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca sindhu rājaḥ ca vīryavān bhīmam te vivyadhuḥ tūrṇam śalya hetoḥ ariṃdamāḥ sa tu tān prativivyādha pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ śalyam vivyādha saptatyā punar ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena gāḍham vivyādha marmaṇi viśokam vīkṣya nirbhinnam bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān tāḍayām āsa samare siṃha vat ca nanāda ca te hi yattāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavam yuddha durmadam tribhiḥ tribhiḥ akuṇṭha agraiḥ bhṛśam marmasu atāḍayan parvataḥ vāri dhārābhiḥ varṣamāṇaiḥ iva ambudaiḥ sa tu krodha samāviṣṭaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ madra īśvaram tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhṛśam viddhvā mahā yaśāḥ śalyam ca navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhṛśam viddhvā mahā yaśāḥ prāgjyotiṣam śatena ājau rājan vivyādha vai dṛḍham tatas tu sa śaram cāpam sātvatasya mahātmanaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya kṛtavarmā vṛkodaram virarāja mahā bāhuḥ lalāṭa sthena pattriṇā ekaśṛṅgaḥ mahā rāja yathā parvata sattamaḥ atha bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kruddhaḥ sarvān mahā rathān bhagadattam tribhiḥ ca eva kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ dvābhyām dvābhyām ca vivyādha gautama prabhṛtīn rathān matvā tṛṇena tān tulyān vicacāra gata vyathaḥ te ca api rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ bhīmāya niśitān śarān preṣayām āsuḥ avyagrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tasya śaktim mahā vegām bhagadattaḥ mahā rathaḥ cikṣepa samare vīraḥ svarṇa daṇḍām mahādhanām tomaram saindhavaḥ rājā paṭṭiśam ca mahā bhujaḥ śataghnīm ca kṛpaḥ rājñ śaram śalyaḥ ca saṃyuge atha itare mahā iṣvāsāḥ pañca pañca śilīmukhān bhīmasenam samuddiśya preṣayām āsuḥ ojasā tatas kruddhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ hārdikya prahitam ca api paṭṭasam tila kāṇḍa vat sa ciccheda śataghnīm ca saindhavena īritām bhṛśam bhīmasenaḥ raṇa ślāghī navabhiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ tomaram sa dvidhā cakre kṣurapreṇa anilātmajaḥ paṭṭiśam ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ciccheda tila kāṇḍa vat madra rāja prayuktam ca śaram chittvā mahā balaḥ śaktim ciccheda sahasā bhagadatta īritām raṇe tathā itarān śarān ghorān śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ raṇa ślāghī tridhā ekaikam samācchinat tān ca sarvān mahā iṣvāsān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ atāḍayat jagāma sa rathena ājau bhīmam dṛṣṭvā mahā ratham nighnantam samare śatrūn yodhayānam ca sāyakaiḥ tau tu tatra mahātmanau sametau vīkṣya pāṇḍavau na āśaśaṃsuḥ jayam tatra tāvakāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha bhīṣmasya nidhana ākāṅkṣī puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam āsasāda raṇe yodhān tāvakān daśa bhārata suśarman gaccha śīghram tvam bala oghaiḥ parivāritaḥ jahi pāṇḍu sutau etau dhanaṃjaya vṛkodarau uvāca arjunaḥ tu raṇe śalyam yatamānam mahā ratham chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ citrasenam vikarṇam ca kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca śaraiḥ atirathaḥ yuddhe pīḍayan vāhinīm te jayadrathaḥ raṇe pārtham bhittvā bhārata sāyakaiḥ śalyaḥ ca samare jiṣṇum kṛpaḥ ca rathinām varaḥ citrasena ādayaḥ ca eva putrāḥ te viśām pate pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ tūrṇam saṃyuge niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghnuḥ arjunam saṃkhye bhīmasenam ca māriṣa apīḍayetām samare trigartānām mahat balam suśarmā api raṇe pārtham viddhvā bahubhiḥ āyasaiḥ anye ca rathinaḥ śūrāḥ bhīmasena dhanaṃjayau teṣām tu rathinām madhye kaunteyau rathinām varau āmiṣa īpsū gavām madhye siṃhau iva bala utkaṭau chittvā dhanūṃṣi vīrāṇām śarān ca bahudhā raṇe pātayām āsatuḥ vīrau śirāṃsi śataśas nṛṇām rathāḥ ca bahavaḥ bhagnāḥ hayāḥ ca śataśas hatāḥ gajāḥ ca sa gaja ārohāḥ petuḥ urvyām mahā mṛdhe rathinaḥ sādinaḥ ca eva tatra tatra nisūditāḥ dṛśyante bahudhā rājan veṣṭamānāḥ samantataḥ cāmaraiḥ hema daṇḍaiḥ ca samāstīryata medinī ghaṇṭābhiḥ ca kaśābhiḥ ca samāstīryata medinī keyūraiḥ aṅgadaiḥ hāraiḥ rāṅkavaiḥ mṛditaiḥ tathā kuṇḍalaiḥ maṇi citraiḥ ca samāstīryata medinī uṣṇīṣaiḥ apaviddhaiḥ ca cāmara vyajanaiḥ api ūrubhiḥ ca narendrāṇām samāstīryata medinī śaraiḥ saṃvārya tān vīrān nijaghāna balam te putraḥ tu tava tam dṛṣṭvā bhīma arjuna samāgamam gāṅgeyasya ratha abhyāśam upajagme mahā bhaye vinda anuvindau āvantyau ājagmuḥ saṃyugam tadā tatas bhīmaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ phalgunaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ kauravāṇām camūm ghorām bhṛśam dudruvatuḥ raṇe tatas barhiṇavājānām ayutāni arbudāni ca tatas tān śara jālena saṃnivārya mahā rathān pārthaḥ samantāt samare preṣayām āsa mṛtyave śalyaḥ tu samare jiṣṇum krīḍan iva mahā rathaḥ tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā hasta āvāpam ca pañcabhiḥ atha enam sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhṛśam vivyādha marmaṇi madra īśvaraḥ raṇe jiṣṇum tāḍayām āsa roṣitaḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ mahā rāja vāsudevam ca pañcabhiḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja māgadhaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ duryodhana samādiṣṭau tam deśam upajagmatuḥ yatra pārthaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ jayatsenaḥ tu samare bhīmam bhīma āyudham yuvā vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ bharata ṛṣabha sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat māgadhaḥ apahṛtaḥ rājā sarva sainyasya paśyataḥ droṇaḥ tu vivaram labdhvā bhīmasenam śilīmukhaiḥ vivyādha bāṇaiḥ su śitaiḥ pañcaṣaṣṭyā tam āyasaiḥ tam bhīmaḥ samara ślāghī gurum pitṛ samam raṇe vivyādha navabhiḥ bhallaiḥ tathā ṣaṣṭyā ca bhārata arjunaḥ tu suśarmāṇam viddhvā bahubhiḥ āyasaiḥ tatas bhīṣmaḥ ca rājā ca saubalaḥ ca bṛhadbalaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ abhyadravan raṇe bhīṣmam vyādita āsyam iva antakam śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bhāratānām pitāmaham yudhiṣṭhira mukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam ayodhayan raṇe bhīṣmam saṃhatāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ śikhaṇḍi pramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyuge tatas pravavṛte yuddham kauravāṇām bhaya āvaham tatra pāṇḍu sutaiḥ sārdham bhīṣmasya vijayam prati tāvakānām raṇe bhīṣmaḥ glahe asīt viśām pate tatra hi dyūtam āyātam vijayāya itarasmai vā abhidravata gāṅgeyam mā bhaiṣṭa nara sattamāḥ senāpati vacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānām varūthinī bhīṣmam eva abhyayāt tūrṇam prāṇān tyaktvā mahā āhave bhīṣmaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ pratijagrāha tām camūm āpatatīm mahā rāja velām iva mahā udadhiḥ uvāca katham śāṃtanavaḥ bhīṣmaḥ daśame ahani saṃjaya ayudhyata mahā vīryaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ kuravaḥ ca katham yuddhe pāṇḍavān pratyavārayan ācakṣva me mahā yuddham bhīṣmasya āhava śobhinaḥ uvāca kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham yathā ayudhyanta bhārata yathā ca tat abhūt yuddham tat te vakṣyāmi śṛṇvataḥ preṣitāḥ para lokāya parama astraiḥ kirīṭinā ahani ahani saṃprāptāḥ tāvakānām ratha vrajāḥ yathāpratijñam kauravyaḥ sa ca api samitiṃjayaḥ pārthānām akarot bhīṣmaḥ satatam samiti kṣayam kurubhiḥ sahitam bhīṣmam yudhyamānam mahā ratham arjunam ca sa pāñcālyam dṛṣṭvā saṃśayitāḥ janāḥ daśame ahani tasmin tu bhīṣma arjuna samāgame tasmin ayutaśas rājan bhūyas ca sa paraṃtapaḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ yodhān jaghāna parama astra vid yeṣām a jñāta kalpāni nāma gotrāṇi pārthiva te hatāḥ tatra bhīṣmeṇa śūrāḥ sarve anivartinaḥ daśa ahāni tatas taptvā bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍava vāhinīm na hanyām mānava śreṣṭhān saṃgrāme abhimukhān iti abhyāśa stham mahā rāja pāṇḍavam vākyam abravīt yudhiṣṭhira mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada śṛṇu mama vacanam tāta dharmyam svargyam ca jalpataḥ nirviṇṇaḥ asmi bhṛśam tāta dehena anena bhārata ghnataḥ ca me gataḥ kālaḥ su bahūn prāṇinaḥ raṇe tasmāt pārtham purodhāya pāñcālān sṛñjayān tathā tasya tat matam ājñāya pāṇḍavaḥ satya darśanaḥ bhīṣmam pratiyayau yattaḥ saṃgrāme saha sṛñjayaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas rājan pāṇḍavaḥ ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śrutvā bhīṣmasya tām vācam codayām āsatuḥ balam rakṣitāḥ satya saṃdhena jiṣṇunā ripu jiṣṇunā ayam ca api mahā iṣvāsaḥ pārṣataḥ vāhinīpatiḥ na vai bhīṣmāt bhayam kim cit kartavyam yudhi sṛñjayāḥ dhruvam bhīṣmam vijeṣyāmaḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam tathā tu samayam kṛtvā daśame ahani pāṇḍavāḥ brahma loka pare bhūtvā saṃjagmuḥ krodha mūrchitāḥ śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam bhīṣmasya pātane yatnam paramam te samāsthitāḥ tatas tava suta ādiṣṭāḥ nānā janapada īśvarāḥ droṇena saha putreṇa saha senāḥ mahā balāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca balavān saha sarvaiḥ sahodaraiḥ bhīṣmam samara madhya stham pālayām cakrire tadā tatas tu tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ puraskṛtya yata vratam śikhaṇḍi pramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyuge cedibhiḥ ca sa pāñcālaiḥ sahitaḥ vānaradhvajaḥ yayau śāṃtanavam bhīṣmam puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam droṇaputram śineḥ naptā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ tu pauravam virāṭaḥ tu saha anīkaḥ saha senam jayadratham vṛddhakṣatrasya dāyādam āsasāda paraṃtapaḥ madra rājam mahā iṣvāsam saha sainyam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasena abhiguptaḥ ca nāga anīkam upādravat apradhṛṣyam anāvāryam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam droṇam prati yayau yattaḥ pāñcālyaḥ saha somakaiḥ karṇikāra dhvajam ca api siṃhaketuḥ ariṃdamaḥ śikhaṇḍinam ca putrāḥ te pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam tāni anīkāni anīkeṣu samasajjanta bhārata tāvakānām pareṣām ca dṛṣṭvā śāṃtanavam raṇe prādurāsīt mahān śabdaḥ dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata śaṅkha dundubhi ghoṣaiḥ ca vāraṇānām ca bṛṃhitaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca sainyānām dāruṇaḥ samapadyata sā ca sarva narendrāṇām candra arka sadṛśī prabhā vīra aṅgada kirīṭeṣu niṣprabhā samapadyata rajaḥ meghāḥ ca saṃjajñuḥ śastra vidyudbhiḥ āvṛtāḥ dhanuṣām ca eva nirghoṣaḥ dāruṇaḥ samapadyata bāṇa śaṅkha praṇādāḥ ca bherīṇām ca mahā svanāḥ prāsa śakti ṛṣṭi saṃghaiḥ ca bāṇa oghaiḥ ca samākulam niṣprakāśam iva ākāśam senayoḥ samapadyata kuñjarāḥ kuñjarān jaghnuḥ padātīn ca padātayaḥ tat āsīt su mahat yuddham kurūṇām pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhīṣma hetoḥ nara vyāghra śyenayoḥ āmiṣe yathā anyonyasya vadha arthāya jigīṣūṇām raṇa ajire uvāca mahatyā senayā yuktaḥ bhīṣma hetoḥ parākramī ājaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ punar ca enam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya śaktim raṇe kārṣṇiḥ mṛtyoḥ ghorām iva svasām tām āpatatīm sahasā ghora rūpām viśām pate tām śaktim patitām dṛṣṭvā kārṣṇiḥ parama kopanaḥ īkṣitṛ prīti jananam sarva pārthiva pūjitam sātyakim rabhasam yuddhe drauṇiḥ brāhmaṇa puṃgavaḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ nārācena paraṃtapaḥ atāḍayat ameya ātmā navabhiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ aśvatthāmā tu samare sātyakim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ triṃśatā ca punar tūrṇam bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ droṇaputreṇa sātvataḥ droṇaputram tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna mahā yaśāḥ pauravaḥ dhṛṣṭaketum ca śaraiḥ āsādya saṃyuge bahudhā cakre mahā iṣvāsam mahā ratham triṃśatā niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vivyādha su mahā balaḥ pauravaḥ tu dhanuḥ chittvā dhṛṣṭaketoḥ mahā rathaḥ nanāda balavat nādam vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya pauravam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna mahā rāja trisaptatyā śilīmukhaiḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa parasparam avarṣatām ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre śata candra pariṣkṛte vāśitā saṃgame yattau siṃhau iva mahā vane maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gata pratyāgatāni ca pauravaḥ dhṛṣṭaketum tu śaṅkha deśe mahā asinā tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt ājaghāna śita agreṇa jatru deśe mahā asinā tau anyonyam mahā rāja samāsādya mahā āhave dhṛṣṭaketum ca samare mādrī putraḥ paraṃtapaḥ apovāha raṇe rājan sahadevaḥ pratāpavān citrasenaḥ suśarmāṇam viddhvā navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha tam ṣaṣṭyā punar ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ suśarmā tu raṇe kruddhaḥ tava putram viśām pate daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ ca eva vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ citrasenaḥ ca tam rājan triṃśatā nata parvaṇām pārtha hetoḥ parākrāntaḥ bhīṣmasya āyodhanam prati punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ na akampayata saṃgrāme vivyādha ca punar punar ājaghāna śaraiḥ ca eva triṃśatā kaṅka pattribhiḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya rāja putraḥ bṛhadbalaḥ te vadhyamānāḥ bhīmena mātaṃgāḥ giri saṃnibhāḥ nipetuḥ urvyām sahitāḥ nādayantaḥ vasuṃdharām giri mātrāḥ hi te nāgāḥ bhinnāñjana caya upamāḥ virejuḥ vasudhām prāpya vikīrṇāḥ iva parvatāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ madra rājānam āhave mahatyā senayā guptam pīḍayām āsa saṃgataḥ pīḍayām āsa saṃrabdhaḥ bhīṣma hetoḥ parākramī virāṭam saindhavaḥ rājā viddhvā saṃnata parvabhiḥ navabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ triṃśatā punar ardayat virāṭaḥ ca mahā rāja saindhavam vāhinī mukhe triṃśatā niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare droṇaḥ pāñcāla putreṇa samāgamya mahā raṇe tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja pārṣatasya mahat dhanuḥ chittvā pañcāśatā iṣūṇām pārṣatam samavidhyata saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya pārṣataḥ para vīra hā droṇasya miṣataḥ yuddhe preṣayām āsa sāyakān tān śarān śara saṃghaiḥ tu saṃnivārya mahā rathaḥ droṇaḥ drupada putrāya prāhiṇot pañca sāyakān tasya kruddhaḥ mahā rāja pārṣataḥ para vīra hā droṇāya cikṣepa gadām yama daṇḍa upamām raṇe tām āpatantīm sahasā hema paṭṭa vibhūṣitām śaraiḥ pañcāśatā droṇaḥ vārayām āsa saṃyuge sā chinnā bahudhā rājan droṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ cūrṇīkṛtā viśīryantī papāta vasudhā tale gadām vinihan dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ śatru sūdanaḥ droṇāya śaktim cikṣepa sarva pāraśavām śubhām tām droṇaḥ navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ciccheda yudhi bhārata pārṣatam ca mahā iṣvāsam pīḍayām āsa saṃyuge bhīṣmam prati mahā rāja ghora rūpam bhayānakam arjunaḥ prāpya gāṅgeyam pīḍayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ arjunam śara varṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyuge śikhaṇḍinam ca kaunteyaḥ yāhi yāhi iti acodayat bhīṣmam prati mahā rāja jahi enam iti ca abravīt prāgjyotiṣaḥ tatas hitvā pāṇḍavam pāṇḍu pūrvaja tatas te tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavam rabhasam raṇe nānāvidhāni anīkāni putrāṇām te janādhipa arjunaḥ vyadhamat kāle divi iva abhrāṇi mārutaḥ śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānām pitāmaham somakān ca raṇe bhīṣmaḥ jaghne pārtha padānugān nyavārayata sainyam ca pāṇḍavānām mahat rathaḥ ratha agni agāraḥ cāpa arcīḥ asi śakti gadā indhanaḥ śara saṃgha mahā jvālaḥ kṣatriyān samare adahat yathā hi su mahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sa anilaḥ tathā jajvāla bhīṣmaḥ api divyāni astrāṇi udīrayan suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ śitaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nādayan sa diśaḥ bhīṣmaḥ pradiśaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ pātayan rathinaḥ rājan gajān ca saha sādibhiḥ muṇḍa tāla vanāni iva cakāra sa ratha vrajān nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvān ca saṃyuge cakāra sa tadā bhīṣmaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tasya jyā tala nirghoṣam visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ amoghāḥ hi apatan bāṇāḥ pituḥ te manuja īśvara na asajjanta śarīreṣu bhīṣma cāpa cyutāḥ śarāḥ nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan su yuktān javanaiḥ hayaiḥ vātāyamānān paśyāma hriyamāṇān viśām pate cedi kāśi karūṣāṇām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa mahā rathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kula putrāḥ tanutyajaḥ aparāvartinaḥ śūrāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya sa vāji ratha kuñjarāḥ na tatra āsīt mahā rāja somakānām mahā rathaḥ yaḥ saṃprāpya raṇe bhīṣmam jīvite sma manaḥ dadhe tān ca sarvān raṇe yodhān pretarāja puram prati nītān amanyanta janāḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam ṛte pāṇḍu sutam vīram śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim śikhaṇḍinam ca samare pāñcālyam amita ojasam śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe bhīṣmam āsādya bharata ṛṣabha daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna mahā āhave śikhaṇḍinam tu gāṅgeyaḥ krodha dīptena cakṣuṣā avaikṣata kaṭākṣeṇa nirdahan iva bhārata na jaghāna raṇe bhīṣmaḥ sa ca tam na avabuddhavān arjunaḥ tu mahā rāja śikhaṇḍinam abhāṣata kim te vivakṣayā vīra hā bhīṣmam mahā ratham yaḥ śaktaḥ samare bhīṣmam yodhayeta pitāmaham ṛte tvām puruṣa vyāghra satyam etat bravīmi te śaraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ tūrṇam pitāmaham upādravat a cintayitvā tān bāṇān pitā devavrataḥ tava arjunam samare kruddham vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ tathā eva ca camūm sarva pāṇḍavānām mahat ratha apraiṣīt samare tīkṣṇaiḥ para lokāya māriṣa tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥ bhīṣmam pracchādayām āsuḥ meghāḥ iva divākaram nirdadāha raṇe śūrān vanam vahniḥ iva jvalan duḥśāsanasya tutuṣuḥ sarve lokāḥ mahātmanaḥ na ca enam pāṇḍavāḥ yuddhe āsuḥ ulbaṇam duḥśāsanena samare rathinaḥ virathīkṛtāḥ sādinaḥ ca mahā rāja dantinaḥ ca mahā balāḥ vinirbhinnāḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ nipetuḥ dharaṇī tale śara āturāḥ tathā eva anye dantinaḥ vidrutāḥ diśaḥ yathā agniḥ indhanam prāpya jvalet dīpta arciḥ ulbaṇaḥ tam bhārata mahāmātram pāṇḍavānām mahā rathaḥ ṛte mahā indra tanayam śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim vijitaḥ tava putraḥ api bhīṣma bāhu vyapāśrayaḥ punar punar samāśvasya prāyudhyata raṇa utkaṭa śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe rājan vivyādha eva pitāmaham śaraiḥ aśani saṃsparśaiḥ tathā sarpa viṣa upamaiḥ jaghāna bāṇān gāṅgeyaḥ tathā muktān śikhaṇḍinaḥ smayamānaḥ ca gāṅgeyaḥ tān bāṇān jagṛhe tadā uṣṇa ārtaḥ hi naraḥ yadvat jala dhārāḥ pratīcchati tathā jagrāha gāṅgeyaḥ śara dhārāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ tam kṣatriyāḥ mahā rāja dadṛśuḥ ghoram āhave bhīṣmam dahantam sainyāni pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām eṣa tālena dīptena bhīṣmaḥ tiṣṭhati pālayan sarva dhārtarāṣṭra raṇa śarman ca varman ca tridaśa api samudyuktāḥ na alam bhīṣmam samāsitum kim u pārthāḥ mahātmānam martya bhūtāḥ tathā abalāḥ arjunam prati saṃyattāḥ balavantaḥ mahā rathāḥ te videhāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca dāśeraka gaṇaiḥ saha abhipetuḥ niṣādāḥ ca sauvīrāḥ ca mahā raṇe bāhlikāḥ daradāḥ ca eva prācya udīcyāḥ ca mālavāḥ abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ śālva āśrayāḥ trigartāḥ ca ambaṣṭhāḥ kekayaiḥ saha abhipetuḥ raṇe pārtham pataṃgāḥ iva pāvakam śalabhāḥ iva rāja indra pārtham apratimam raṇe sa tān sarvān saha anīkān mahā rāja mahā rathān divyāni astrāṇi saṃcintya prasaṃdhāya dhanaṃjayaḥ śara pratāpaiḥ bībhatsuḥ pataṃgān iva pāvakaḥ tasya bāṇa sahasrāṇi sṛjataḥ dṛḍha dhanvinaḥ dīpyamānam iva ākāśe gāṇḍīvam samadṛśyata te śara ārtāḥ mahā rāja viprakīrṇa ratha dhvajāḥ na abyavartanta rājānaḥ sahitāḥ vānaradhvajam gajāḥ saha gaja ārohaiḥ kirīṭi śara tāḍitāḥ tatas arjuna bhuja utsṛṣṭaiḥ āvṛtā āsīt vasuṃdharā vidravadbhiḥ ca bahudhā balaiḥ rājñām samantataḥ atha pārthaḥ mahā bāhuḥ drāvayitvā varūthinīm duḥśāsanāya samare preṣayām āsa sāyakān te tu bhittvā tava sutam duḥśāsanam ayomukhāḥ dharaṇīm viviśuḥ sarve valmīkam iva pannagāḥ hayān ca asya tatas jaghne sārathim ca nyapātayat viviṃśatim ca viṃśatyāḥ viratham kṛtavan prabho ājaghāna bhṛśam ca eva pañcabhiḥ nata parvabhiḥ kṛpam śalyam vikarṇam ca viddhvā bahubhiḥ āyasaiḥ cakāra virathān ca eva kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ evam te virathāḥ pañca kṛpa śalyaḥ ca māriṣa duḥśāsanaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca tathā eva ca viviṃśatiḥ saṃprādravanta samare nirjitāḥ savyasācinā pūrvāhṇe tu tathā rājan parājitya mahā rathān prajajvāla raṇe pārthaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ tathā eva śara varṣeṇa bhāskaraḥ raśmivān iva anyān api mahā rāja pātayām āsa pārthivān parāṅmukhīkṛtya tadā śara varṣaiḥ mahā rathān prāvartayata saṃgrāme śoṇita udām mahā nadīm madhya kuru sainyānām pāṇḍavānām ca bhārata gajāḥ ca ratha saṃghāḥ ca bahudhā rathibhiḥ hatāḥ rathāḥ ca nihatāḥ nāgaiḥ nāgāḥ haya padātibhiḥ antarā chidhyamānāni śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca channam āyodhanam reje kuṇḍala aṅgada dhāribhiḥ patitaiḥ pātyamānaiḥ ca rāja putraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ ratha nemi nikṛttāḥ ca gajaiḥ ca eva avapothitāḥ pādātāḥ ca api adṛśyanta sa aśvāḥ sa haya sādinaḥ gaja aśva ratha saṃghāḥ ca paripetuḥ samantataḥ viśīrṇāḥ ca rathāḥ bhūmau bhagna cakra yuga dhvajāḥ tat gaja aśva ratha oghānām rudhireṇa samukṣitam śvānaḥ kākāḥ ca gṛdhrāḥ ca vṛkāḥ gomāyubhiḥ saha praṇeduḥ bhakṣyam āsādya vikṛtāḥ ca mṛga dvijāḥ vavuḥ bahuvidhāḥ ca eva dikṣu sarvāsu mārutāḥ dṛśyamāneṣu rakṣaḥsu bhūteṣu vinadatsu ca kāñcanāni ca dāmāni patākāḥ ca mahādhanāḥ dhūmāyamānāḥ dṛśyante sahasā māruta īritāḥ śveta chattra sahasrāṇi sa dhvajāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ vinikīrṇāḥ sma dṛśyante śataśas atha sahasraśas sa patākāḥ ca mātaṃgāḥ diśaḥ jagmuḥ śara āturāḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca manuṣya indra gadā śakti dhanuḥ dharāḥ samadṛśyanta samare dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ tam śikhaṇḍī raṇe yattam abhyadhāvata daṃśitaḥ uvāca evam vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu bhūyiṣṭham anuvartiṣu na rathāḥ rathibhiḥ sārdham na padātāḥ padātibhiḥ nara nāga ratheṣu evam vyavakīrṇeṣu sarvaśas tatas śalyaḥ kṛpaḥ ca eva
